<p>1a</p>
<p>1b</p>
<p>1b.1\] ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ bud+d+ha tsa ri ta ma hA kA bya nA ma/ bod skad du/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'
<p>1b.2</p>thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal ldan yon tan tshogs kyis gang / /bdag nyid chen po sems can gyi/ /don mdzad yang dag sangs rgyas dang / /chos dang dge 'dun la phyag
<p>1b.3</p>'tshal/ /bu ram shing par mthu mnyam bu ram shing ba'i rgyud/ /thub dka' shAkya rnams la spyod pa rnam dag pa/ /'phrog byed zla ba lta bur skye dgu rnams la sdug /rgyal po zas gtsang
<p>1b.4</p>zhes bya'i ming can byung bar gyur/ /dbang po dang mtshungs de yi bdag po ldan ma yin/ /nus mthu rjes mtshungs gzi brjid lha mo bde sogs dang / /pad+mo can 'dra phun sum tshogs pa sa
<p>1b.5</p>bzhin brtan/ /sgyu ma chen mo zhes bya dpe med sgyu 'dra byung / /mi skyong rgyal po 'di ni de dang thabs cig tu/ /dga' ba nyer ldan rnam thos sras kyi dpal bzhin rol/ /de nas yang dag ting
<p>2a</p>
<p>2a.1</p>'dzin ldan pa'i rig ma bzhin/ /sdig bral ma de mngal ni rnam par gzung bar gyur/ /mngal dang nye bar ldan pa nyid kyi sngon rol du/ /de ni gnyid song glang po'i dbang po dkar po zhig /rang nyid la
<p>2a.2</p>ni rab tu zhugs sogs mthong gyur la/ /de yi mtshan ma nyam thag pa nas thob ma yin/ /lha dang rab tu mtshungs pa de yi lha mo de/ /mngal gyis rigs kyi dpal ni rab tu 'dren byed cing / /sgyu ma ngal ba dang ni mya ngan
<p>2a.3</p>sgyu med par/ /gtsang la nyon mongs med pa'i dgon par blo gros mdzad/ /de ni lum bi zhes bya'i nags mthar gyur pa'i sa/ /sna tshogs ljon shing sna tshogs shing rta mngon dga' bar/ /bsam gtan la bzod dben
<p>2a.4</p>pa'i nags kyi mtha' bzhed ma/ /'gro ba'i chad dang gnas phyir mi skyong la zhus so/ /de yi chos dang ldan la 'phags pa'i zhes 'dod dag /rnam par shes nas ya mtshan dga' ba yis gang ste/ /zhi ba'i grong nas sa
<p>2a.5</p>yi bdag po gshegs gyur te/ /de yi dga' ba'i rgyu yin rnam par rgyu phyir min/ /dpal dang ldan pa'i nags der rgyal po'i bdag ldan ma/ /rab tu bltam pa'i dus ni yang dag mngon gzigs shing / /bla re nye bar
<p>2b</p>
<p>2b.1</p>phul ba'i gzims mal rab thob ste/ /mi mo stong phrag dag gis mngon par dga' bar byed/ /de nas skar ma rgyal rab ldan par gyur pa'i tshe/ /brtul zhugs legs par 'dus byas lha mo de yi ni/ /rtsib logs dag nas 'jig rten phan phyir sras bltams te/ /tshor
<p>2b.2</p>ba dang ni bral zhing nad dang bral ba nyid/ /ji ltar brla skyes brla nas rgya chen lag pa nas/ /dbang po dang mtshungs nga la nu ni spyi bo nas/ /mtshan ldan nyid kyang lag pa'i cha shas gsang ba nas/ /rnam pa de ltar de yi skye ba byung bar gyur/ /mngal nas mngon par nges par byung ba gzugs mdzes te/ /nam
<p>2b.3</p>mkha' dag las 'phros 'dra skye gnas las ma skyes/ /bskal ba gcig min rnams su bsgoms pa'i bdag nyid ni/ /gang zhig yang dag rab tu shes na skyes gyur blun po min/ /nyi ma gzhon nu sa lam mngon par babs pa bzhin/ /gsal ba dang ni brtan pas gang zhig mdzes pa ste/ /de ltar
<p>2b.4</p>shin tu gsal yang nges par rtog pa na/ /ri bong gis mtshan ji ltar mig dag 'phrogs par gyur/ /de ni rang gi lus kyi 'od rab 'bar ba yis/ /sgron ma'i 'od kyang gsal bar byed pa ltar bcom ste/ /rin thang chen po 'dzam bu chu gser mdzes pa'i mdog /phyogs rnams thams cad rnam
<p>2b.5</p>par snang zhing gsal bar mdzad/ /'khrugs pa ma yin yon po'i skyon dag rab bsal zhing / /shin tu brtan pa dang ldan rnam par yangs pa'i 'gros/ /de ltar mi g.yo rab tu brtan pa'i gom pa bdun/ /drang srong skar ma bdun dang rab mnyam gshegs par gyur/ /byang chub phyir dang 'gro la phan
<p>2b.6</p>pa'i phyir skyes shing / /'di ni bdag gi srid pa'i skye ba tha ma zhes/ /seng ge'i 'gros 'dra phyogs bzhi dag tu rnam gzigs nas/ /snod ldan rnams kyi don byed dag kyang smras par gyur/ /nam mkha' dag las rab babs zla ba'i 'od zer dkar/ /grang dang dro ba'i chu rgyun rnam pa gnyis kyi
<p>2b.7</p>shugs/ /lus la yang dag reg pas bde ba bskyed pa'i phyir/ /mdzes shing yid 'ong de yi spyi bor babs par gyur/ /dpal ldan bla re bres par gser gyis 'bar zhing mtshan/ /bai DUR+Ya yi rkang pa'i gzims mal la gzims pa/ /de la gus phyir gser gyi pad+ma'i phyag mnga' ba'i/ /
<p>3a</p>
<p>3a.1</p>gnod sbyin bdag rnams kun nas yongs su bskor nas gnas/ /mi mngon gyur pa'i lha rnams kyis kyang nam mkha' la/ /gang gi mthu las mgo bo yis ni rab btud cing / /kun nas gdung ba skyob pa'i gdugs dkar rnams bzung ste/ /byang chub ched du mchog
<p>3a.2</p>gi bsngags pa dag kyang smras/ /'das pa'i sangs rgyas rnams la lhag par mchod byas pa'i/ /lto 'phye che rnams khyad 'phags chos la sred pa'i phyir/ /gang la rlung g.yab kyis g.yab gus pa'i mig gzir cing / /man dA ra ba'i me tog rnams kyis yang dag 'thor/ /de bzhin gshegs
<p>3a.3</p>pa bltams pa'i yon tan gyis tshim pa'i/ /gtsang mar lhag par gnas pa'i rnam dag sems can rnams/ /sdug bsngal nyid du bying ba'i 'gro la phan pa'i phyir/ /lha rnams 'dod chags bral ba na yang dga' bar gyur/ /gang gis rab tu bltams tshe ri rgyal phur pu nyid/ /rlung gis
<p>3a.4</p>bsnun pa'i gru ltar sa gzhi g.yos gyur zhing / /tsan+dan dang bcas ut+pal pad+ma'i snying po yi/ /char pa dag ni nam mkha'i sprin dang bral las babs/ /yid 'ong reg na bde ba'i rlung dag byung gyur te/ /lha yi na bza' dag ni mngon par 'bebs byed cing / /nyi ma de nyid lhag par mngon par
<p>3a.5</p>gsal ba ste/ /zhi ba'i 'od zer 'dus ma byas pa'i me 'bar ro/ /shar dang byang gi mtshams kyi khang pa'i phyogs gcig na/ /bsil ba'i chu yi khron pa rang byung gyur pa ste/ /pho brang btsun mo'i 'khor rnams ya mtshan gyur rnams kyis/ /gang la bya ba rnams ni stegs bzhin rab tu byas/ /
<p>3a.6</p>chos dang ldan pa'i lha dang 'byung po'i tshogs rnams kyis/ /de ni lta ba'i don du nags tshal rab gang ste/ /rmad byung ngo mtshar gyur pa nyid kyi shing las kyang / /me tog rnams ni dus ma yin par nges par brul/ /'tshe bar byed pa'i sems can rnams kyang de yi tshe/ /phan tshun dag tu phyin te gnod pa mi
<p>3a.7</p>byed la/ /'tsho ba'i 'jig rten dag na nad gang ji snyed pa/ /de dag rnams kyang 'bad pa med par de tshe bcom/ /mkha' 'gro'i bya ni mtho min sgra sgrogs ri dwags kyang / /chu klung dag ni chu yang zhi bar bab gyur la/ /phyogs rnams rab snang dge ba'i nam mkha' rab mdzes shing / /lha yi rnga rnams mkha'
<p>3b</p>
<p>3b.1</p>la rab tu grags par gyur/ /rgud par gyur la mgon ni nye bar thob nas bzhin/ /'jig rten dag kyang mchog tu rab zhi thob gyur la/ /'jig rten rnams kyi thar pa'i bla ma rab bltams tshe/ /'dod pa'i lha nyid kho na dga' ba med par gyur/ /shin tu ngo mtshar sras kyi skye ba mthong gyur nas/ /mi bdag brtan pa
<p>3b.2</p>yin yang rnam par 'gyur nas song / /rab dga' skyes pa nyid dang yid mi bde skyes te/ /brtse ba las ni mchi ma rnam pa gnyis byung ngo / /mi ma yin pa'i sras po nyid kyi nus pa dang / /ma yi rang bzhin kyang ni stobs chung nyid kyi phyir/ /grang dang dro ba'i chu dag 'dres pa'i chu klung bzhin/ /lha mo 'jigs pa
<p>3b.3</p>dang ni dga' bas gang bar 'gyur/ /lhag ma spangs te 'jigs pa nyid ni shes byas nas/ /yid 'ong 'dod pa'i ched du rtogs pa ma yin pa'i/ /bud med rgan mo rnams kyis bde legs gyur byas shing / /gtsang mar byas te lha rnams dag la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de yi mtshan nyid dag kyang shes shing
<p>3b.4</p>thos gyur nas/ /spyod dang thos dang tshig la grags thob bram ze rnams/ /rnam rgyas zhal ni ya mtshan dga' ba yis gang ste/ /dga' dang 'jigs par gyur pa'i mi yi lha la smras/ /mi dag sa la bu ma gtogs pa'i khyad 'phags pa/ /gzhan gang cung zad 'dod min zhi ba de yi phyir/ /khyod
<p>3b.5</p>kyi sgron ma 'di ni rigs kyi sgron ma ste/ /khyod nyid dga' bar mdzod cig dga' ston da ltar bgyi/ /de phyir brtan par rnam dpyod med par dgar mdzod dang / /rigs ni nges pa nyid du mchog tu 'phel bar 'gyur/ /'di ni khyod kyi bu zhes skyes par gyur pa ste/ /'jig rten sdug bsngal dag
<p>3b.6</p>gis mngon par bcom pa'i mgon/ /mchog gyur 'di la mchog gyur gser gyi 'od mnga' zhing / /sgron ma'i 'od zer dag gis mtshan rnams gang gyur pas/ /de nyid rtogs par gyur pa'i thub par 'gyur ba'am/ /yang na mi bdag sa stengs 'khor los sgyur bar 'gyur/ /sa yi bdag po nyid la
<p>3b.7</p>gal te dga' 'gyur na/ /stobs dang chos dag gis ni de'i tshe sa stengs su/ /rgyal po kun gyi thog tu 'di ni gnas 'gyur te/ /skar ma'i 'od rnams la ni nyi ma'i 'od bzhin no/ /de ni gal te thar bzhed nags su gshegs gyur na/ /mkhyen dang de nyid kyis ni de tshe sa stengs su/ /lugs kun
<p>4a</p>
<p>4a.1</p>zil gyis mnan nas 'di ni gnas 'gyur te/ /mtho ba kun la ri rab ri yi rgyal po bzhin/ /ji ltar lcags rnams la ni gser dag mchog yin la/ /ri rnams la ni ri rab chu bo rnams la mtsho/ /gza' rnams la ni zla ba gdung byed rnams la nyi/ /de ltar khyod kyi
<p>4a.2</p>sras ni rkang gnyis rnams kyi mchog /gang gi spyan dag mi 'dzums mig gzir rnam par spangs pa ste/ /brtan zhing shin tu ring la dkar min rdzi ma dang / /gzi brjid ldan pa yin yang 'on kyang zhi ba nyid/ /'di ni kun nas gzigs pa'i spyan mnga' ci la min/ /de nas gnyis skyes
<p>4a.3</p>rnams la mi bdag gis smras pa/ /bdag nyid chen po mi skyong snga mas ma mthong ba/ /mthong zhes khyad 'di gang yin 'di la rgyu mtshan ci/ /de nas bram ze rnams kyis de nyid la smras pa/ /blo dang thos pa las dang grags pa rnams la ni/ /mi skyong sngon dang phyi ma nyid ni tshad ma yin/ /dngos po'i
<p>4a.4</p>lugs la 'dir ni bya ba rgyu yin la/ /'dir yang bdag gi dper brjod dag ni mkhyen par mdzod/ /gang zhig rgyal po'i bstan bcos shes ldan ngan spong dag /rig byed drang srong de gnyis kyis ni ma byas pa/ /de dag gi sras zhi ba pa wa sangs dang ni/ /phur bu yis ni dus kyis de nyid bskyed par
<p>4a.5</p>gyur/ /nyams gyur snga ma rnams kyis ma mthong rig byed gang / /dbyangs can ma yi bu yis kyang ni slar smras pa/ /nus med gnas 'jog gis ni ma byas gyur pa gang / /rgyas pa yis ni de ltar rnam pa mang por brjod/ /'pho byed drang srong chen pos ma bsdebs gyur pa gang / /tshig gi rkang pa
<p>4a.6</p>grog mkhar gyis ni dang por bskyed/ /gso ba gang yang rgyun shes kyis ni ma mthong ba/ /phyi nas de ni drang srong rgyun shes bu yis byas/ /gang yang gnyis skyes nyid ni kun shas ma rnyed pa/ /de ni gting dpogs bu yis rgyal po la thob bo/ /bu ram shing pas dang por ma bsdams gyur pa gang / /
<p>4a.7</p>rgya mtsho la ni dug bcas kyis kyang mtshams bzung ngo / /slob dpon nyid du bram ze'i rnal 'byor cho ga la/ /gzhan rnams kyis ma thob pa skyed byed gshegs par gyur/ /khyab 'jug gi ni grags pa'i las rnams gang yin pa/ /de rnams la ni dpa' bo la sogs stobs med gyur/ /de phyir lang tsho dang ni
<p>4b</p>
<p>4b.1</p>rigs dag tshad ma yin/ /la la la lar mchog nyid nyer thob 'jig rten na/ /rgyal dang drang srong rnams kyis snga mas ma byas pa/ /de dang de dag rnams ni bu rnams dag gis byas/ /de ltar gnyis skyes de rnams kyis ni yid ches te/ /mi skyong dbugs 'byin dang yang mngon par dga' gyur la/ /
<p>4b.2</p>mi 'dod the tshom dag ni yid las rnam bstsal te/ /rab tu dga' ba nyid la lhag par 'dzegs par gyur/ /dga' ba yis ni gnyis skyes dam pa de rnams la/ /bkur sti sngon du 'gro ba'i nor rnams rab phul te/ /ji skad smras bzhin 'di ni sa yi bdag por gyur/ /rgas pa thos nas nags rnams
<p>4b.3</p>su ni 'gro bar shog /de nas mtshan ma rnams dang dka' thub stobs las ni/ /skye ba mthar mdzad bltams pa de ni rtogs gyur nas/ /dam pa'i chos la gus pa'i shAkya'i dbang phyug gi /gnas su dkar min drang srong chen por gshegs par gyur/ /tshangs pa'i dpal nyid kyis kyang dka' thub dpal
<p>4b.4</p>gyis ni/ /'bar ba'i tshang rig rnams kyi tshang rig de la ni/ /rgyal po'i bla mas gus pa dang ni bkur sti'i phyir/ /mi dbang pho brang du ni rab tu spyan drangs so/ /de ni sa bdag btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nye logs su/ /gzhon nu bltams pa la ni dga' ba'i shugs kyis 'ongs/ /dka' thub mchog las dang
<p>4b.5</p>ni rgas pa la brten nas/ /brtan pa nags kyi 'du shes kyis ltar rnam par zhugs/ /de nas thub pa gdan la gnas pa de la mi skyong gis/ /zhabs bsil mchod yon sngon 'gro yang dag rab mchod nas/ /sngon tshe gnas mchog la ni mtha' can lhas bzhin des/ /ji ltar nye bar spyod la snyan gsan
<p>4b.6</p>phab pa'o/ /bdag gi rigs ni rjes su bzung phyir nor ldan des/ /gang zhig bdag la gzigs phyir bcom ldan nyer gshegs la/ /bka' drin gnang bar mdzod cig zhi ba ci bgyi bgyi/ /kho bo slob ma lags so thugs rjes mdzad par rigs/ /de ltar mi skyong gis ni dngos po thams cad kyis/ /
<p>4b.7</p>nye bar gsol btab gyur pa'i thub pa ji lta bzhin/ /rab rgyas yangs pa'i spyan ni ya mtshan dang bcas pas/ /zab ba dang ni brtan pa'i chig rnams smras pa'o/ /chos 'dod gtong ba dang ldan 'gron la sdug cing phangs/ /bdag nyid chen po khyed la 'thad pa 'di yin la/ /sems
<p>5a</p>
<p>5a.1</p>pa rjes 'gro ye shes lang tsho rjes mthun pa/ /khyod kyi blo gros gnyen gang de ltar bdag la yin/ /de dang de ni gang gis mi skyong drang srong des/ /phra mo'i chos kyi nor rnams rab tu thob byas nas/ /rtag par cho ga bzhin du mchod sbyin byas gyur pa/ /dka' thub rnams
<p>5a.2</p>kyis phyug cing nor rnams dag gis dbul/ /bdag gi nye bar 'ongs la dgos pa gang yin pa/ /bdag gi de ni gson mdzod dga' bar nyer song khyed/ /byang chub rtogs pa'i ched du khyod kyi sras bltams zhes/ /lha yi ngag dag bdag gi nyi ma'i lam du thos/ /ngag de thos nas dang ni
<p>5a.3</p>yid la bsgoms nas dang / /mtshan ma rnams kyis shes nas de nas nye bar 'ongs/ /brgya byin gyi ni rgyal mtshan yang dag bsgreng ba bzhin/ /shAkya'i rigs kyi rgyal mtshan blta bar 'dod pa yis/ /zhes pa'i tshig 'di de ltar thos par gyur nas ni/ /mi dbang rab tu dga' bas kun nas g.yos
<p>5a.4</p>gyur te/ /yum gyi pang du son las gzhon nu blangs nas ni/ /dka' thub nor can la ni yang dag bstan par gyur/ /de nas drang srong che des zhabs la 'khor los mtshan/ /phyag dang zhabs kyi sor mo dra bas 'brel ba dang / /glang po bzhin du mdoms nub smin ma mdzod spur bcas/ /
<p>5a.5</p>ya mtshan dang bcas rgyal po'i sras ni mthong bar gyur/ /lha mo'i pang na zhugs pa me yi bu bzhin du/ /ma ma'i pang du bzhugs pa mngon par mthong nas ni/ /byung gyur rdzi ma'i mtha' ru mchi ma rnams byung ste/ /dbugs med gyur nas gyen du lta la zhal phyogs gyur/ /mig dag mchi
<p>5a.6</p>mas yongs gang dkar min mthong nas ni/ /bu la brtse ba'i phyir ni mi skyong 'dar gyur te/ /mchi ma dang ni gre ba kha zhing ldab ldib bcas/ /thal mo sbyar zhing yan lag btud de dris par gyur/ /gang gi lus ni lha las bar na cung zad cig /rang gi skye ba ngo mtshar mang po'i sgron ma ste/ /gang
<p>5a.7</p>gi don ni mchog tu 'gyur bar smra ba ste/ /rab tu mthong nas brtan pa gang phyir mchi ma 'ong / /bcom ldan gzhon nu brtan pa'i tshe can yin snyam mam/ /bdag gi mya ngan ched du skyes pa min nam ci/ /bdag la chu yi snyim pa ci zhig ltar rnyed de/ /'di ni dus kyis 'thung phyir nye bar 'ongs ma yin/ /
<p>5b</p>
<p>5b.1</p>bdag gi snyan grags gter ni mi zad yin snyam mam/ /nges par bdag gi rigs kyi lag nor yin snyam ci/ /bde bar pha rol du ni rab tu 'gro snyam mam/ /gnyid par gyur kyang bu ni phye ba'i mig gcig yod/ /bdag gi rigs kyi myu gu skyes pa ma rgyas par/ /yongs su skams pa'i skal ba
<p>5b.2</p>can zhig min snyam mam/ /khyab bdag myur bar gsungs shig bdag la zhi ba med/ /gnyen 'dun rnams kyis bu la brtse ba khyed kyis rig /de ltar mi 'dod blo yis 'khrul ba byung gyur pa/ /rig nas mi dbang rgyal la thub pa des smras pa/ /bdag gis smras pa gang de the tshom
<p>5b.3</p>med pa de/ /mi skyong khyed kyi blo gros gzhan gang ma gyur cig /'di yi gzhan gyur mtshon min bdag gi rnam 'gyur te/ /'on kyang rang la slu bar rab mtshon rnam par 'khrugs/ /skye ba zad pa'i rnyed par bla min rtogs pa po/ /'di skyes bdag gi 'gro ba la ni dus yin no/ /rgyal srid rnam
<p>5b.4</p>par spangs nas yul rnams la mi gnas/ /'bad pa drag po rnams kyis de nyid thob byas nas/ /'di ni 'gro la gti mug mun pa rnam 'joms phyir/ /ye shes rang bzhin nyi ma rab tu 'bar bar 'gyur/ /sdug bsngal rgya mtsho nad rnams bkram pa'i dbu ba can/ /rga ba'i dba'
<p>5b.5</p>rlabs 'chi ba'i shugs ni drag po las/ /'gro ba nyam thag bying bar gyur rnams 'di yis ni/ /ye shes gru bo chen po yis ni sgrol bar byed/ /shes rab chu yi shugs la brten pa'i tshul khrims ngogs/ /ting nge 'dzin ni bsil ba'i brtul zhugs ngang pa 'phyo/ /'di yi mchog gi chos
<p>5b.6</p>kyi chu bos rab bskor la/ /sred pas nyam thag gson pa'i 'jig rten 'thung bar byed/ /sdug bsngal gyis nyam thag dang yul gyis bsgribs rnams dang / /'khor ba'i 'brog dgon 'jigs par gnas pa rnams la ni/ /lam rab chud zos rnams la lam 'gro rnams bzhin du/ /
<p>5b.7</p>'dis ni rnam par dag pa'i lam dag 'chad par 'gyur/ /yul gyi bud shing can gyi 'dod chags me yis ni/ /'jig rten skye bo rnam par bsregs par gyur pa la/ /sos ka'i tha mar sprin chen gyis ni char bzhin du/ /'di yi chos kyi char gyis rab tu sim byed 'gyur/ /sred pa'i sgo
<p>6a</p>
<p>6a.1</p>gtan ma rig mun pa'i sgo glegs can/ /sgo la skye dgu rnams kyi 'thon pa'i rgyu las ni/ /'di yis mchog rab kun nas rnyed par dka' ba yi/ /dam pa'i chos kyi sgras ni rnam par 'byed par 'gyur/ /rang gi las kyi zhags pa rnams kyis yongs dkris shing / /
<p>6a.2</p>sdug bsngal dag gis mngon par zil non rten med pa'i/ /'jig rten rnams kyi rdzogs pa'i byang chub brnyes nas kyang / /chos kyi rgyal po 'dis ni 'ching ba mthar mdzad 'gyur/ /rmongs sam 'dod pa'i bde ba yis sam rgyags las rung / /'di yi mthar thug chos gang thos par mi
<p>6a.3</p>byed pa/ /mi yi 'jig rten 'dir de mya ngan bya ba'i gnas/ /de phyir khyed nyid 'di la mya ngan ma byed cig /yon tan rgya mtsho 'di las 'khrul gyur bdag gi ni/ /bsam gtan rnams ni thob kyang don byas med nyid de/ /de yi dam chos ma thos pa la kho bo ni/ /mtho ris dag na
<p>6a.4</p>gnas kyang phun tshogs med pa snyam/ /de ltar don thos bshes dang bcas shing btsun mor bcas/ /yid mi bde ba dor nas mi dbang dgar gyur la/ /rnam pa de ltar bdag gi bu ni 'di'o zhes/ /des ni bdag nyid la ni snying bo ldan par bsams/ /'phags pa'i chos rnams kyis
<p>6a.5</p>kyang 'gro bar 'gyur ro zhes/ /bsam pa'i rnam par gzung bya snying la byas gyur te/ /nges par 'di ni mi sdug chos kyi phyogs min la/ /rigs rgyud nyams pa las ni 'on kyang 'jigs pa mthong / /de nas bu la rnam par 'khrugs pa'i rgyal po la/ /bu yi nges pa'i de nyid rig par byas
<p>6a.6</p>nas su/ /gus bcas gyen du gzugs mthong dkar min thub pa ni/ /rlung gi lam gyis ji ltar 'ongs par gshegs par gyur/ /blo gros byas pa'i sring mo'i bu yang mthong nas ni/ /thub pa'i gsung mnyan pa dang de yi lugs la ni/ /rnam mang rjes su brtse ba yis ni legs pa des/ /
<p>6a.7</p>sdug pa'i bu bzhin du ni sbyor ba byed du bcug /sras po skyes pas tshim pa'i mi yi bdag po yang / /yul la song ba'i 'ching ba rnams ni rnam spangs te/ /sras kyi yid 'ong sras po bltams pa'i las dag ni/ /rigs dang 'dra bar ji lta ba bzhin byed du bcug /zhag bcu yongs su 'das par
<p>6b</p>
<p>6b.1</p>gyur ba nyid kyi tshe/ /mchog gi dga' ba rab ldan snyoms par gyur pa'i yid/ /sras las mchog tu 'gyur phyir lha yi mchod pa ni/ /bzlas brjod dang ni sbyin sreg bkra shis la sogs byas/ /gzhan yang brgya dang stong phrag yongs su gang ba'i grangs/ /brtan dang stobs ldan bu rnams
<p>6b.2</p>gser gyi rwar bcas shing / /rgas pa nye bar 'ongs min swa ma ldan pa'i ba/ /rang gi sras 'phel phyir na gnyis skyes rnams la byin/ /de nas snyoms pa'i bdag nyid kyis ni rnam mang yul/ /rang sems tshim bar byed pa'i bya ba rnams byas nas/ /yon tan ldan zhing dge ba'i yud tsam nges pa na/ /
<p>6b.3</p>grong khyer rab tu 'jug la dga' bas blo gros mdzad/ /de nas mche gnyis mche ba las byung rin thang che/ /dkar po'i me tog gis spras nor bu'i sgron/ /khri la dge ba'i phyir ni lha mo sras ldan ma/ /lha rnams la ni rab tu btud nas bsnyen par gyur/ /de nas gnas brtan skye mo
<p>6b.4</p>rjes 'brang sras mgon ma/ /bdag po ldan ma grong la mdun du rab zhugs nas/ /mchod ldan lha na lha rnams kyis ni brgya byin bzhin/ /mi bdag nyid kyang grong ba'i tshogs kyis gshegs par gyur/ /de nas gdong drug skyes pas yid ches dbang phyug bzhin/ /shAkya'i rgyal pos grong
<p>6b.5</p>khyer rnam par khyab mdzad de/ /zhal ni dga' bas rab gang 'di dang 'di zhes pa'i/ /srid 'phel rgyas pa dang ni grags dang snyan pa mdzad/ /de nas mi yi bdag po'i sras bltams cher skyes pas/ /ser skya zhes pa'i grong khyer ljongs dang bcas pa de/ /gnod sbyin grong na phun tshogs 'dod
<p>6b.6</p>ba skyes pa na/ /lha yi bu mo rnams kyis bkram bzhin dga' bar gyur/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ gzhon nu sku bltams pa'i le'u ste dang po'o// //skye dang rga ba mthong song bdag skyes bdag pham de'i/ /skyes pa nas
<p>6b.7</p>brtsams mi nyid nyi mas rgyal po de/ /chu yi shugs rnams kyis ni chu bo sin d+hu bzhin/ /nor dang glang po rta dang bshes rnams 'phel bar gyur/ /nor rnams dang ni rin po che dang bzang po'i gser/ /de dang de ni byas dang ma byas pa nyid kyang / /yid la re ba yi rang bzhin du khur gyur pa/ /
<p>7a</p>
<p>7a.1</p>de la gcig tu phan pa'i cha shas gter rnyed gyur/ /gang zhig pad+ma dang mtshungs gnyis 'thung rnams kyis kyang / /dkyil 'khor 'di la nye bar 'ong bar mi nus pa'i/ /gangs dang ldan pa'i glang chen chang gis dregs de rnams/ /'bad pa las kyang gzhan du de la nye
<p>7a.2</p>bar gnas/ /sna tshogs mtshan mas mtshan zhing gsar ba'i gser sga dang / /de bzhin gzhan rnams dag gis brgyan byas rngog ma 'phyang / /stobs dang byams pa dang ni nor gyis thob pa yi/ /'di yi mgyogs 'gro rnams kyis grong khyer phye mar byas/ /de bzhin 'di yi yul 'khor
<p>7a.3</p>du ni tshim dang rgyas/ /legs la rdul ldan yon tan ldan pa 'o mar ldan/ /rab mchog be'u rnams dang bcas pa'i ba rnams ni/ /'o ma mang po 'jo ba mang po byung bar gyur/ /'di yi dgra bo dbus gnas nyid du song gyur pa/ /dbus gnas gyur pa mdza' bshes nyid du rab tu song / /
<p>7a.4</p>khyad par du ni bshes gnyen brtan por song ba ste/ /'di yi phyogs dag gnyis te dgra yang yod ma yin/ /de bzhin du ni 'di yi 'jam rlung 'brug gi sgra/ /glog gi phreng ba 'khyil ba yis ni brgyan pa'i sprin/ /rdo char dang ni thog lhung nyes pa rnams kyis gzhan/ /yul du dus la
<p>7a.5</p>lha yis char pa phab par gyur/ /zhing gi las kyis ngal dub byed pa nyung ngus kyang / /'bru ni 'bras bu ldan pa dus sbyor bzhin skyes te/ /de rnams nyid kyang 'di yi sman du byung gyur la/ /bcud dang snying po yis kyang mngon par lhags pa nyid/ /g.yul du rab tu zhugs la kun du 'joms
<p>7a.6</p>pa bzhin/ /lus la the tshom za bar byed pa'i dus na yang / /rang bzhin gnas shing bde ba nyid du nad med par/ /dus kyi dbang gis mi mo rnams ni rab tu btsas/ /brtul zhugs ldan rnams ma gtogs nor rdzas dman na yang / /mi rnams pha rol rnams las don du gnyer mi byed/ /
<p>7a.7</p>mngon par don du gnyer la 'phags pa nor 'phra yang / /de tshe 'ga' zhig dag ni rgyab kyis phyogs ma gyur/ /de tshe rgyal po de yi rgyal srid la ni dga'/ /gnyen la zhe sa med min mi ster ba yang med/ /brtul zhugs med pa nyid min brdzun med 'tshe med pa/ /sgra mi bsgrags kyi sras po
<p>7b</p>
<p>7b.1</p>lta bu byung bar gyur/ /der yang skyed mos tshal dang lha gnas dka' thub gnas/ /khron pa rdzing dang dge bcu 'du ba'i gnas rnams kyi/ /bya ba rnams ni mtho ris bzhin du nyer thob nas/ /chos 'dod rnams kyis mngon sum du ni rab tu mdzad/ /mu ge dang ni 'jigs dang nad rnams las
<p>7b.2</p>grol zhing / /dgar gyur skye bo mtho ris gzhan du mngon par dga'/ /bdag mos bdag po la 'am mo yis bdag por rung / /phan tshun log par mngon par spyod pa dag kyang med/ /dga' ba'i ched du 'dod la 'ga' zhig gis ma bsnyen/ /'dod pa'i don du nor ni 'ga' zhig
<p>7b.3</p>gis ma bsrungs/ /nor gyi don du chos la 'ga' zhig gis ma spyad/ /chos kyi don du 'tshe ba 'ga' zhig gis ma byas/ /rkun po sogs dang dgra yang nyams par rang gnas med/ /pha rol mya ngan med pa ji lta ba nyid bzhin/ /rang gi 'khor lo pha rol 'khor lo las grol te/ /rgyal po
<p>7b.4</p>de la bde dang lo legs byung bar gyur/ /de yi tshe na rgyal po de yi rgyal srid la/ /de skyes pa na nyi ma'i sras po'i yid shes bzhin/ /dga' bar spyad par gyur la sdig pa rab nyams shing / /chos rnams 'bar zhing nyon mongs rnams ni zhi bar gyur/ /gang phyir rnam pa de ltar don kun
<p>7b.5</p>grub pa dang / /rgyal po'i rigs kyi phun sum tshogs pa byung gyur te/ /de phyir mi skyong gis ni sras po de yi mtshan/ /don kun grub pa zhes bya 'di ni rab tu mdzad/ /lha mo sgyu ma yang ni lha yi drang srong mtshungs/ /bu yi nus mthu rnam par spangs pa mthong nas ni/ /bltams la rab tu
<p>7b.6</p>dga' mas bzod par ma nus te/ /de nas gnas pa'i ched du ltar ni gshegs par gyur/ /de nas lha yi mngal dang mtshungs pa'i gzhon nu la/ /byams pa'i rang bzhin gyis kyang khyad par med pa yi/ /ma yi nu mo mdangs mnyam pa yi rang bzhin la/ /yang dag skyed btsud
<p>7b.7</p>bdag las skyes pa lta bur gyur/ /de nas nyi ma gzhon nu 'char rir gnas 'dra dang / /rlung gis rab tu bus par gyur pa'i me bzhin dang / /skar ma'i bdag po mun min phyogs la gnas pa ltar/ /gzhon nu de ni rim gyis yang dag 'phel bar gyur/ /de nas rin thang chen po'i tsan+dan
<p>8a</p>
<p>8a.1</p>rnams dang ni/ /rin chen phreng ba sman gyi snying por bcas rnams dang / /ri dwags rab tu sbyar ba'i gser gyi shing rta rnams/ /'di yi ched du gshegs kyi khyim rnams dag nas blangs/ /lang tsho nyid dang rjes su mthun pa'i rgyan rnams dang / /gser gyi rang bzhin
<p>8a.2</p>ri dgas glang chen rta rnams dang / /gser dang dngul gyis bris pa'i mi chung gzugs rnams dang / /shing rta ba glang byung dus yang dag sbyar rnams blangs/ /de ni lang tsho rjes mthun yul la nye spyod pa/ /de rnams kyis ni yul la nyer spyad la/ /dpa' dang brtan pa yis dang blo dang
<p>8a.3</p>dpal gyis kyang / /byis pa yin yang byis min rab mtshungs byung bar gyur/ /lang tsho gzhon nu shin tu 'das nas yang dag par/ /'du byed las ni rab tu thob nas dus su ni/ /lo mang dag gis rtogs bya nyin zhag nyung ngu yis/ /rang dang rjes su mthun pa'i rigs pa
<p>8a.4</p>rnams ni blangs/ /drang srong chen po dkar min las ni sngon rol du/ /de yi nyes legs don gyi skal ba thob nas ni/ /nags su gshegs par 'gyur zhes shAkya'i rgyal po yis/ /'dod pa rnams la chags pa skyed du bcug par gyur/ /brtan pa'i tshul khrims spyod pa can gyi
<p>8a.5</p>rigs de la/ /ngo tsha dang ni dul ba nyer ldan legs ldan ma/ /grags 'dzin ma zhes grags pa rnam par yangs pa ma/ /btsun mor mngon par brjod pa'i dpal mo 'di la blangs/ /kun 'gyed gzhon nu dang ni rab tu mtshungs pa yis/ /mchog gi lus kyis snang zhing
<p>8a.6</p>gsal ba de nyid ni/ /shAkya'i rgyal po'i mna' ma de dang thabs cig tu/ /bde sogs ma dang mig stong ldan bzhin mngon par dga'/ /yid kyang dpyod par byed la cung zhig rab log pa/ /gang gis mthong mi 'gyur zhes rjes su bsams byas nas/ /sa la rab tu spyod
<p>8a.7</p>min lding khang lto nyid du/ /gnas dag mi skyong gis ni de la rnam par bstan/ /de nas gzhal med nam mkhar sa la spyod pa bzhin/ /ston kha'i dus kyi chu gter sprin ni dkar po yi/ /dus sbyor kun du bde ba'i gzhi yi lding khang la/ /bud med rnams kyi sil snyan rgya chen rnams kyis rnam
<p>8b</p>
<p>8b.1</p>par gshegs/ /gser gyis gdams pa'i rnga shing can gyi rdza rnga'i skad/ /mi mo'i lag pa'i rtse mos mngon par brdungs pa yi/ /lha mchog ma yi gar dang mnyam pa'i gar rnams kyis/ /ti se'i gangs ltar de yi pho brang mdzes par gyur/ /ngag dang gzo dang rol dang rnam
<p>8b.2</p>'gyur rnams kyis kyang / /rgyags dang rtse dang dgod pa dngar mo rnams kyis dang / /smin ma bskyod pa yis dang phyed mig lta rnams kyis/ /de la der ni mi mo rnams ni dga' bar gyur/ /de nas de ni 'dod pa bsten par mkhas pa yi/ /dga' bas dregs pa'i bud med rnams
<p>8b.3</p>kyis bzung gyur la/ /gzhal med khang ni rgyab nas bsod nams las can bzhin/ /gzhal med khang ni rgyab nas sa la ma gshegs so/ /mi skyong gis kyang de nyid bskyed pa'i ched las ni/ /de yi 'byung bar 'gyur ba'i don gyis bskul gyur te/ /sdig pa las ni dga' bral zhi la
<p>8b.4</p>mngon dga' zhing / /legs la skal bar bgos shing dul la bsnyen par gyur/ /brtan min bzhin du 'dod pa'i bde la ma zhen la/ /ma rungs skyed ma la ni yang dag chags ma gyur/ /brtan pas dbang po'i rta ni stobs las rnam thul zhing / /gnyen dang grong khyer pa rnams yon tan rnams kyis
<p>8b.5</p>rgyal/ /gzhan gyi sdug bsngal phyir ni rig pa ma brjod la/ /ye shes dge ba gang yang de la lhag par brjod/ /des ni rang gi skye dgu rnams la ji lta bar/ /de ltar skye dgu rnams la dge ba'i bsngags pa mdzad/ /skar ma rgyal snang shes ldan sras po lhag pa'i lha/ /ji lta bar ni de yi tshe ring phyir mchod des/ /chung min me la
<p>8b.6</p>bsreg bya rnams ni bsregs gyur la/ /gnyis skyes rnams la gser dang ba lang rnams kyang byin/ /'gram stegs chab rnams kyis dang yon tan chab rnams kyis/ /gtsang sbra'i ched du lus dang yid la khrus byas te/ /rig byed du ni nye bar bstan pa'i chang rnams dang / /zhi ba bdag
<p>8b.7</p>skyes snying la zhi ba'i bde la 'thung / /gang zhig don dang mi ldan zhi ba ma smras la/ /gang zhig dga' ba dang bral de nyid ma brjod de/ /zhi ba de nyid med dang rtsub pa'i de nyid phyir/ /ngo tsha ba yis bdag nyid kho na brjod ma nus/ /don ldan 'dod pa rnams dang mi 'dod pa rnams la/ /chags
<p>9a</p>
<p>9a.1</p>pa'i skyon la brten nas rab tu 'thob min te/ /dge ba'i tha snyad gtsang ma la ni bsnyen gyur la/ /mchod sbyin la yang ma mos de ltar ji lta bzhin/ /sred pa dang ldan mngon par 'ongs pa de ma thag /sbyin bya chu 'dra rnams kyis skom pa bcad gyur la/ /
<p>9a.2</p>g.yul las ma gtogs ye shes kyi ni sta ri yis/ /dgra bo rnams kyi nga rgyal chen po bcom par gyur/ /gcig ni rnam par dul la des ni mdun bsrungs shing / /bdun po nyid ni don la lnga po dag ni bsrungs/ /sde tshan gsum po thob la sde tshan gsum rtogs
<p>9a.3</p>shing / /sde tshan gnyis po shes la sde tshan gnyis po spangs/ /nyes pa byas kyang rab tu bskyangs nas gzhom bya la/ /'tshe bar mi byed khro bas kyang ni gzigs ma yin/ /de rnams dag la 'bras bu zhi bas bcings gyur la/ /de rnams dag ni 'dor ba tshul ma yin phyir mthong / /
<p>9a.4</p>drang srong rnams kyis mchog gi brtul zhugs spyad gyur la/ /yun rings yang dag bzung ba'i sha khon zhugs rnams dor/ /yon tan dri ldan snyan dngags rnams ni thob gyur la/ /dri ma can du byed pa'i rdul rnams rnam par dor/ /rab tu mi gnas gtor ma'i dpya ni ma blangs
<p>9a.5</p>la/ /pha rol dngos po rnams la mngon par rlom ma byas/ /dgra rnams la ni chos ma yin pa ma smras la/ /khro ba rnams ni snying gis gzung ba ma yin no/ /zhi ba'i bdag nyid sems ni rnam par rab dang la/ /rnal 'byor rab tu ldan pa'i dbang po rnams ci ltar/ /der ni
<p>9a.6</p>de ltar sa bdag rab tu sgyur ba can/ /'bangs dang grong khyer ba rnams de lta nyid du byas/ /de nas mdzes pa'i 'o ma 'dzin pa dang ldan ma/ /grags 'dzin ma ni rang gi grags pa 'dzin ma la/ /zas gtsang sras po'i sras po sgra gcan sgra yi zhal/ /sgra gcan 'dzin zhes bya ba
<p>9a.7</p>dus su skyes par gyur/ /de nas 'dod pa'i bu mnga' mchog gi yid ches te/ /rigs rgyud 'phel ba rab mtshon sa skyong rgyal po ni/ /ji lta nyid du sras po rab tu skyes la dga'/ /de lta nyid du sras po'i sras po skyes la dga'/ /bdag gi bu yi bur gyur pa la brtse ba ni/ /bdag
<p>9b</p>
<p>9b.1</p>bzhin gang las yin zhes dga' ba skyes gyur te/ /dus su des ni cho ga de dang de dmigs shing / /bu la dga' ba mtho ris bzhin du 'dzegs par gyur/ /rgyal po'i khyu mchog grags dang snyan pas mtshan rnams kyis/ /dang po'i skal ba rnams kyi lam la gnas nas ni/ /
<p>9b.2</p>dkar po ma dor dka' thub rnams la dka' thub dang / /'tshe ba dor ba'i mchod sbyin rnams kyis mchod par gyur/ /rgyal po'i dpal gyis dang ni dka' thub dpal gyis kyang / /bsod nams las can de ni de nas 'bar gyur la/ /rigs dang blo dang mdzad spyod kyis kyang gsal ba ste/ /
<p>9b.3</p>gzi brjid stong gi 'od zer bzhin du rab tu 'phro/ /rang byung las byung mchod byed sngags ni mchod byas nas/ /sras gnas ched du brtan pa'i dpal gyis bzlas byas shing / /dka' thub byed pa'i las rnams byas gyur skye dgu rnams/ /skyed 'dod skye dgu'i bdag bzhin dang po'i dus su'o/ /
<p>9b.4</p>mtshon cha spangs shing bstan bcos rnam par shes gyur la/ /nye bar zhi la bsnyen zhing nges la rnam par bzod/ /dbang ldan bzhin du yul rnams gang la ma bsnyen la/ /yab mes bzhin du yul rnams kun la gzigs par gyur/ /des kyang bu yi ched du rgyal srid bzung gyur la/ /bu ni
<p>9b.5</p>rigs kyi don du rigs ni grags pa'i phyir/ /grags pa mtho ris ched du mtho ris bdag nyid phyir/ /chos kyi don du bdag nyid gnas la 'dod par 'gyur/ /de ltar des ni dam pa rnams kyis nges thob pa'i/ /thos pa las grub chos ni rnam pa sna tshogs byas/ /gang las bdag
<p>9b.6</p>gi bus ni bu yi ngo mthong nas/ /nags tshal nyid du 'gro mi 'gyur zhes mgon bslangs so/ /bdag la yang dag blangs pa'i dpal ni srung 'dod pa'i/ /sa skyong rnams kyis sa la bu ni bsrung ba ste/ /chos ni 'dod pa'i ma yi dbang po de yis kyang / /yul rnams 'dor ba
<p>9b.7</p>med par bu ni chos las bsrungs/ /byang chub sems dpa' yul la bde ba'i ro shes thams cad kyang / /sras skyed pa na dpe med sems pa nags su gshegs gyur te/ /de phyir nye bar bsags pa'i las ni rtsa nas skyed pa'i phyir/ /de ni zhi ba ma thob de srid dga' ba bsnyen par gyur/ /
<p>10a</p>
<p>10a.1</p>sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ btsun mo'i 'khor na gnas pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// //de nas re zhig dus na 'jam po'i rtswa rnams dang / /khu byug pho ni gyen du skad 'don rkang 'thung rnams/ /glu
<p>10a.2</p>rnams dang ni nges ldan skyed mos tshal rnams ni/ /pad+ma'i 'byung gnas kyis brgyan des ni thos par gyur/ /de nas bud med skye bo rnams ni dga' ba yi/ /grong khyer skyed mos tshal gyi yid 'ong dngos thos te/ /khyim gyi nang du mngon par bkag pa'i glu bzhin du/ /phyi rol rab
<p>10a.3</p>tu 'gro ba'i ched du blo mdzad do/ /de nas sras su mngon brjod yid 'ong de yi ni/ /dgongs pa mi skyong gis ni nges par thos gyur nas/ /brtse ba'i phun sum tshogs pas lang tshor 'ongs pa ru/ /ltad mo dag la rnam par gshegs par bka' stsal to/ /gzhon nu shin tu gzhon nu'i
<p>10a.4</p>sems dang ldan pa ni/ /yang dag skyo ba'i sems su ma gyur zhes sems zhing / /nyam thag tha dad skye bo kun nas 'dus pa ni/ /rgyal po'i lam du phyir la rnam par zlog pa ste/ /nying lag dman pa rnams dang dbang po ma tshang rnams/ /'khogs pa nad pa la sogs bkren rnams phyogs rnams
<p>10a.5</p>su/ /de nas mchog tu zhi bas yang dag rab ston nas/ /rgyal po'i lam rnams dag ni mchog tu mdzes par byas/ /de nas dpal ldan rgyal po'i lam ni byas pa na/ /dpal ldan rnam par dul ba rjes 'brangs gzhon nu ni/ /gzhal yas khang pa'i logs nas dus su mngon babs nas/ /
<p>10a.6</p>mngon par rjes gnang byas pa mi skyong la mngon gshegs/ /de nas mi dbang bu la mchi ma byung gyur te/ /mgo la nye bar bsnams te yun rings rnam gzigs nas/ /song cig ces ni tshig gi bka' dag stsal gyur la/ /brtse ba dag las de ni yid kyis ma btang ngo / /de nas de
<p>10a.7</p>ni 'dzam bu chu gser sga 'dzin pa'i/ /legs par bslabs pa'i mgyogs 'gro bzhi yis sbyar ba yi/ /dbang po ma nyams mkhas shing gtsang la 'od zer 'chang / /gser gyi rang bzhin shing rta la ni yang dag 'dzegs/ /de nas 'bras spos me tog 'bar ba rab bkram zhing / /phreng ba
<p>10b</p>
<p>10b.1</p>rnam dpyangs rab tu g.yo ba'i ba dan can/ /zla ba skar ma dang bcas bar snang la bzhin du/ /'dra ba rjes 'brang lam ni rab tu thob par gyur/ /ya mtshan gyur las rab tu rgyas pa'i mig rnams ni/ /ut+pal sngon po'i phyed 'dra rnams kyis bkram pa ni/ /rgyal po'i lam la dal bu
<p>10b.2</p>dal bus gshegs gyur te/ /grong khyer skye bo rnams kyis kun nas mngon par dga'/ /kha cig de la zhi ba'i yon tan gyis bstod la/ /de bzhin gzhan rnams gsal ba nyid kyis phyag 'tshal zhing / /kha cig dag ni 'di la mngon du phyogs nas kyang / /dpal dang tshe yi rnam par rgyas la
<p>10b.3</p>shis pa brjod/ /zhar ba sgur po nad pa mi'u thung rnams kyis/ /tshogs pa rnams ni rigs chen rnams la nges dral nas/ /mi mo rnams ni nges par zhugs gnas phra rnams las/ /lha yi rjes 'gro rgyal mtshan bzhin du rab tu btud/ /de nas gzhon nu nges par gshegs zhes
<p>10b.4</p>gtam dag ni/ /bsgo bya skyes las bud med rnams kyis thob gyur na/ /bkur 'os skye bos mngon par rjes gnang byas pa rnams/ /blta bar 'dod pas lding khang shod du song bar gyur/ /yon tan ska rags brul zhing gegs byas de rnams ni/ /gnyid log rab tu sad pas lta
<p>10b.5</p>byed 'khrugs pa rnams/ /gnas lugs gtam gyis rnam par brgyan rnams rnam gzhag ste/ /ya mtshan gyur pas dogs med par ni yongs su song / /gzhal yas khang gi skas kyi 'og gi sgra rab dang / /dril chung sgra rnams dang ni gdu bu'i sgra rnams kyis/ /rnam par skrag gyur khyim gyi
<p>10b.6</p>bya yi tshogs rnams ni/ /phan tshun shugs rnams las kyang yang dag kun nas gtor/ /gang zhig 'dir ni yan lag rab mchog ma rnams ni/ /myur ba rab tu skyes gyur tsam tsam skyes rnams kyis/ /lo ma 'dzin rnams rgyas shing skyed smad shing rta ni/ /yangs pa rnams kyis lci ba nyid phyir
<p>10b.7</p>'gro ba bzung / /mtha' gcig legs par rab tu sbyar ba'i rgyan rnams ni/ /rnam par sbas pa rnam par gsal bas ngo tsha bas/ /skyen por 'gro bar nus pa yin yang gzhan ma yin/ /'gro ba nges par bzung ste myur min song bar gyur/ /phan tshun rab tu bcer bas ril por gyur pa
<p>11a</p>
<p>11a.1</p>rnams/ /yang dag drud las bskyod gyur rna lung 'khyil ba can/ /de dag rnams kyi de tshe sgra bcas rgyan rnams ni/ /rlung bgrod skar khung rnams su rab tu zhi bar gyur/ /rlung bgrod skar khung rnams las rnam par 'thon pa rnams/ /phan tshun thang chen gyur pa'i rna
<p>11a.2</p>lung 'khyil ba rnams/ /bud med rnams kyi 'dam skyes 'dra ba'i 'dam skyes zhal/ /lding khang rnams su bkod pa rnams ni rnam par mdzes/ /de nas khang bzangs lang tsho ma rnams kyis khyab cing / /ya mtshan la ni rab phye skar khung rnams kyis ni/ /lha mo dang bcas gzhal med
<p>11a.3</p>rnams kyi nam mkha' bzhin/ /dpal dang ldan pa'i grong khyer kun nas mdzes par gyur/ /skar khung rnams kyis rnam par yangs pa ma yin las/ /phan tshun 'gram par bkod pa'i rna lung can rnams kyis/ /'dam skyes pad+ma rnams kyi tshogs rnams bcings pa bzhin/ /rab
<p>11a.4</p>myos mchog ma rnams kyi zhal ni mdzes par gyur/ /gzhon nu de la lam du rnam par blta ba yi/ /bud med de rnams sa la 'gro 'dod ltar mdzes shing / /gyen du gdong phyogs de la rab tu lta ba yi/ /mi rnams gnam la 'gro bar 'dod bzhin mdzes par gyur/ /lus dad dpal
<p>11a.5</p>gyis mchog tu 'bar bar gyur pa yi/ /rgyal po'i sras de mthong nas bud med de rnams ni/ /nges par dgongs pa gzhan min bsam pa dag pa yis/ /'di yi chung ma skal ba bzang zhes dal bus smra/ /gzugs kyi dngos su me tog tog can dang mtshungs shing / /rnam par ring zhing
<p>11a.6</p>rgyas pa'i dpung pa can 'di ni/ /dpal nyid dor nas chos la nye bar gshegs zhes te/ /de la de dag rnams kyis zhe sa kho na byas/ /rnam par dul la gtsang zhing brtan pa'i cha lugs can/ /grong pa rnams kyis de ltar rgyal po'i lam khyab pa/ /de ni sngon du gzhon nus mthong nas
<p>11a.7</p>dga' bas te/ /bdag gi srid pa gzhan ma cung zhig brtags pa 'dra/ /grong khyer de yang mtho ris bzhin du rab dga' ba/ /mngon par gzigs nas gtsang mar gnas pa'i lha rnams kyis/ /sa gzhi skyong ba'i sras po yang dag bskul don du/ /'khogs pa'i mi rgan rab tu 'gro bar
<p>11b</p>
<p>11b.1</p>sprul gyur to/ /de nas gzhon nu yis ni rga bas zil non zhing / /mi rnams las ni tha dad dbyibs can de gzigs nas/ /g.yo ba med cing de nyid du ni zhugs pa'i spyan/ /chags par gyur cing kha lo 'dzin pa la smras so/ /mngon par nyer 'ongs mi de su yin 'dren pa kye/ /skra rnams
<p>11b.2</p>dkar zhing dbyug pa la ni lag pas brten/ /smin mas kun nas mig g.yogs 'khogs shing yan lag drud/ /rnam 'gyur 'di ni tha mal gang 'dod yin nam ci/ /de skad ces smra shing rta rab tu 'dren pa po/ /lha mchog de rnams nyid kyi blo ni rmongs byas shing / /don ni bsrung bya
<p>11b.3</p>yin yang skyon med mthong gyur te/ /de yis sa skyong bdag nyid skyes la nges par gsol/ /gzugs kyi gnod byed stobs kyi rnam par za ba po/ /rgan pa rnams kyi 'joms byed mya ngan rnams kyi sa/ /dran pa rnams kyi nyams byed dbang po rnams kyi dgra/ /'di ni rgas pa zhes bya gang gis
<p>11b.4</p>'di bcom mo/ /'dis kyang byis pa nyid dang 'o ma 'thung gyur cing / /dus kyi sa la yongs su gnyid log gyur pa ste/ /rim gyis lus rab ldan pa'i lang tshor gyur nas kyang / /rim gyis de nyid kho nas rga bar nye bar song / /de skad ces smras rgyal po'i bdag nyid skyes pa ste/ /cung zhig 'dar
<p>11b.5</p>la kha lo sgyur la 'di skad smras/ /skyon 'di kho bo la yang 'byung ba min nam ci/ /de bzhin 'di la kha lo sgyur ba yis gsol to/ /'di ni na tshod rab mchog tshe dang ldan pa'i yang / /gdon mi za bar dus kyi dbang gis 'byung bar 'gyur/ /de bzhin rgas pa gzugs kyi rnam par nyams pa
<p>11b.6</p>bor/ /'jig rten pa yi shes pa nyid dang mthong ba nyid/ /de nas sngon gyi bsam pa dag pa'i blo mnga' ba/ /rnam rgyas bskal par bsags pa'i bsod nams las can de/ /rdo rje chen po'i sgra la nye bar ba lang bzhin/ /rgas pa thos nas gzhon nu kun nas yi mug gyur/ /dbugs ni ring du
<p>11b.7</p>brgyus nas rang gi mgo bsgul zhing / /'khogs pa de la spyan ni rnam par zhugs nas su/ /rga ba dang bcas skye ba de rnams gzigs gyur nas/ /sems ni khong du chud pa de yis tshig 'di smras/ /dran pa dang ni gzugs dang pha rol gnon pa yang / /de ltar rgas pas rnam dpyod med par
<p>12a</p>
<p>12a.1</p>'joms pas te/ /'di lta bur ni mngon sum nyid du song na yang / /'jig rten pa dag skyo med nyer 'gro kho na'o/ /de ltar song la 'dren pa rta rnams phyir zlog la/ /khyod ni khyim nyid du ni skyes par rab tu song / /rgas pa'i 'jigs pa'i sems su gnas pa kho bo
<p>12a.2</p>la/ /skyed mos tshal gyi sa la bde ba ga la yod/ /de nas rgyal po'i sras po de yi bka' lung gis/ /kha lo sgyur bas shing rta phyir la bzlog par gyur/ /de nas gzhon nus pho brang de nyid kho nar ni/ /bsam pa'i dbang gis stong pa bzhin du rab tu thob/ /gang gi tshe na de yang bde ba ma yin te/ /
<p>12a.3</p>rgas pa rgas pa zhes ni rab tu yongs su rtog /de nas mi dbang gis ni rjes gnang de ni slar/ /rim gyis de nyid kho nas phyi rol gshegs par gyur/ /de nas gzhan yang lus la nad dang yongs ldan pa/ /lha mchog de rnams nyid kyis bskyed cing sprul pa'i mi/ /zas gtsang rgyal po'i sras
<p>12a.4</p>po can der song nyid kyis/ /gzigs nas kha lo sgyur ba de nyid la smras pa/ /gsus pa sbom zhing dbugs dag skyod pa'i lus po can/ /lag pa cha shas zha zhing rid la skya bseng lus/ /a ma zhes ni snying rje'i ngag dag smra ba po/ /gzhan la brten nas gnas pa'i mi de su zhig yin/ /
<p>12a.5</p>de nas kha lo sgyur bas smras pa zhi ba kye/ /'di yi khams ni rab 'khrugs rab stobs rab tu 'phel/ /nad ces bya ba mngon brjod shin tu don med chen po ste/ /nus kyang gang gis de ni rab dbang med par byas/ /rjes su brtse bcas mi de la ni gzigs bzhin du/ /rgyal po'i
<p>12a.6</p>sras des slar yang 'di skad ces smras pa/ /skyes gyur skyon de so sor 'di nyid kho na'i 'am/ /nad kyi 'jigs la skye dgu rnams kyi spyi la yin/ /de nas shing rta rab tu 'dren pa des smras pa/ /gzhon nu nyes pa de ni thun mong gyur pa ste/ /de ltar nad rnams dag ni yongs su
<p>12a.7</p>gtser ba ni/ /nad mthar phyin na 'jig rten dga' bar nye bar gshegs/ /de ltar don thos sems ni khong du chud pa de/ /chu rlabs nang song ri bong can bzhin rab 'dar zhing / /brtse ba thugs rje mnga' bas gsung ngag tshig 'di ni/ /cung zhig dngar ba'i dbyangs kyis rab tu smras
<p>12b</p>
<p>12b.1</p>pa'o/ /skye dgu rnams la rnam par zhen pa'i nad 'di ni/ /'jig rten pa dag rang bzhin gnas shing blo gtad byed/ /mi shes rnam par rgya chen e ma mi rnams kyis/ /gang zhig nad las rnam par grol rnams bzhad gad byed/ /'dren pa phyi rol rab tu 'gro las phyir log la/ /
<p>12b.2</p>mi dbang pho brang nyid du shing rta rab tu song / /bdag gi nad kyi 'jigs pa thos nas dga' ba las/ /sems ni 'khums pa bzhin du rab tu bcom par gyur/ /de ltar lan gnyis phyir log de ni rab gzigs nas/ /sa yi bdag po yis kyang yongs su gros byas so/ /de yi phyir log nges
<p>12b.3</p>pa'i mtshan ma thos gyur nas/ /bdag cag rnams ni 'di yis yang dag 'dor snyam ste/ /lam rnams gtsang mar lhag par byed pa po rnams la/ /khros shing 'khrugs kyang chad pa drag pos gcod pa med/ /slar yang sras po de la khyad par 'phags pa dang / /ldan pa'i yul
<p>12b.4</p>la rab tu dpyod pa rnams mdzad cing / /dbang po g.yo ba nyid kyi phyir yang chags snyam ste/ /bdag cag rnam par mi 'dor zhes ni mgon blangs so/ /gang gi tshe na sgra sgrogs dbang po'i don rnams kyis/ /sras po 'di la pho brang 'khor na dga' ba med/ /de nas ro gzhan ro la gyur cig
<p>12b.5</p>zhes sems shing / /phyi rol ltad mo la ni rnam par bka' stsal to/ /brtse ba las ni sras po'i dgongs ba rtogs nas su/ /de la chags pa'i skyon rnams 'ga' zhig ma bsams nas/ /sgyu rtsal rnams la mngon par shes zhes res ma'i gtso/ /mdzangs ma rnams la des ni yang dag bka'
<p>12b.6</p>stsal to/ /de nas khyad par du yang mi yi dbang po'i lam/ /legs par brgyan byas nyid dang yongs su brtags pa la/ /'dren pa dang ni shing rta brjes nas rgyal po yis/ /gzhon nu phyi rol du ni rab tu gshegs su gzhug /de nas de ltar rgyal po'i bu ni gshegs pa na/ /lha
<p>12b.7</p>mchog de rnams nyid kyis rnam par sprul pa yi/ /srog song shi ba'i ro de lam du bteg pa ni/ /'dren pa dang ni gzhon nus mthong ste gzhan gyis min/ /de nas 'dren pa rgyal po'i sras po des smras pa/ /zhan zhing stug pa'i mi rnams dag ni rjes 'brang zhing / /rgyan gyis brgyan pa yin yang kun nas ngu ba
<p>13a</p>
<p>13a.1</p>ste/ /mi bzhi rnams kyis bteg pa pha gi su zhig yin/ /de nas gtsang ba'i bdag nyid gtsang mar gnas pa yi/ /lha rnams dag gis sems ni zil non 'dren pa po/ /nges ni brjod par bya ba min kyang don 'di ni/ /don ldan dbang phyug la ni rab tu rnam par gsol/ /
<p>13a.2</p>blo dang dbang po srog gi yon tan dang bral zhing / /gnyid log ming bral rtswa dang shing du gyur pa ste/ /brtson 'grus ldan pa rnams kyis bskyed nas bsrungs nas kyang / /sdug pa sdug pa rnams kyis spangs pa de ni su yin nam/ /de ltar tshig ni rab tu 'dren pa las thos nas/ /cung zhig
<p>13a.3</p>kun nas bskyod cing de nyid la smras pa/ /chos 'di nyid ni skye ba 'di nyid kyang gi'am/ /mthar gyur 'di 'dra skye dgu kun gyi yin nam ci/ /de nas rab tu 'dren pas 'di nyid la gsol pa/ /mthar gyur las 'di skye dgu rnams ni kun gyi ste/ /dman dang 'bring dang bdag nyid chen po
<p>13a.4</p>thams cad kyi/ /'jig rten dag ni rnam par nges par rnam par nyams par 'gyur/ /de nas mi dbang sras po de ni bstan na yang / /'chi ba thos nas de ma thag tu yi mug cing / /dpung pas shing rta'i shing gi rtse la rab 'khyud nas/ /gdangs snyan dang ldan dbyangs kyis rab tu smras
<p>13a.5</p>pa'o/ /'di ni nges par skye dgu rnams kyi mthar thug ste/ /'jig rten pa dag 'jigs pa spangs shing bag med la/ /mi rnams dag gi sems rnams sra ba snyam pa ste/ /lam la gnas rnams de ltar rang bzhin nyid du gnas/ /de phyir 'dren pa shing rta'i kha ni phyir bzlog dang / /
<p>13a.6</p>bdag cag sa la rnam par rgyu ba'i yul dus min/ /nyam thag dus su rnam par nyams pa shes nas ni/ /sems dang bcas pa gang 'dra 'di na bag med yin/ /mi bdag bdag skyes kyis ni de skad smras na yang / /de yis shing rta de ni phyir la ma bzlog ste/ /khyab par ldan pa yin
<p>13a.7</p>yang mi dbang brten pa la/ /pad+ma'i tshogs bcas nags nyid du ni gshegs par gyur/ /de nas me tog rgyas ldan gzhon nu'i rkang 'thung zhing / /yongs su bskor zhing rab dga' myos pa'i khu byug can/ /gzhal med khang ldan pad+ma dang bcas mdzes pa'i rdzing / /dga' ba'i tshal
<p>13b</p>
<p>13b.1</p>'dra dge ba'i nags de gzigs par gyur/ /lha mchog mas bskor grong khyer brgyan byed bdag po'i gzhir/ /brtul zhugs gsal ldan thub pa bgegs kyis 'jigs pa bzhin/ /yan lag mchog ma'i tshogs khyab mi skyong bdag skyes sras/ /de nas stobs las nags
<p>13b.2</p>der spyan drangs so/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ thugs skyo ba skyes pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// //de nas skyed mos tshal de nas/ /ya mtshan gyis ni mig g.yos rnams/ /bud med rnams ni khyo thob bzhin/ /mi skyong
<p>13b.3</p>sras la mdun du 'ongs/ /'ongs nas de la de rnams kyis/ /ya mtshan rab rgyas spyan ma drangs/ /pad+ma'i mdzod 'dra'i phyag rnams kyis/ /phrin las yang dag spyod pa byas/ /g.yo med dga' ba rnam gsal ba'i/ /spyan mig rnams kyis 'thung ba bzhin/ /yid dkrugs 'dod
<p>13b.4</p>pas sems g.yengs rnams/ /de la yongs su bskor nas gnas/ /lhan skyes rgyan rnams kyis bzhin du/ /mtshan ni mdzes rnams kyis brgyan pa/ /'dod lha lus dang ldan no zhes/ /de la mi mo de rnams snyam/ /zhi ba nyid phyir brtan nyid phyir/ /gsang ba'i 'od zer zla ba ni/ /sa la
<p>13b.5</p>dngos su babs pa bzhin/ /de la kha cig rnams kyis shes/ /de yi lus kyis g.yengs de rnams/ /nges bzung lus ni rnam 'gyur zhing / /phan tshun mig rnams kyis bsnun nas/ /dal bus dbugs ni rnam par brgyus/ /de ltar mi mo de rnams kyis/ /de ni mig tsam gyis mthong nyid/ /
<p>13b.6</p>smra ba med cing dga' med par/ /'di yi mthu yis non par gyur/ /de ltar de rnams rtsom bral zhing / /snying rjes rnam par 'khrugs mthong nas/ /bram ze mdun na 'don gyi sras/ /blo ldan 'char kas tshig smras so/ /kun gyi sgyu rtsal kun shes shing / /dgongs pa len la mkhas ma
<p>13b.7</p>rnams/ /gzugs dang mdzangs dang ldan pa ste/ /rang gi yon tan gtsor phyin no/ /lus ngan gyi yang skyed tshal dang / /byang gi sgra mi snyan na yang / /yon tan 'di rnams kyis mdzes te/ /nor 'dzin 'di na sngon nyid do/ /chags bral rnams dang drang srong yang / /khyed cag rnams kyis g.yo
<p>14a</p>
<p>14a.1</p>nus shing / /lha mo rnams kyis shes pa yis/ /lha rnams la yang len par ro/ /dgongs pa shes dang rtsed 'jo dang / /mdzangs dang gzugs ni phun tshogs pas/ /bud med rnams kyis chags nus na/ /skyes pa rnams kyis smos ci dgos/ /rnam pa de ltar rab sbyar ba/ /de yi rang gi spyod yul las/ /rnam pa de
<p>14a.2</p>ltar spyod pa 'di/ /khyod kyi drang po'i tshig ma gyur/ /khyod kyi 'di ni ngo tsha bas/ /mig 'khums bag ma gsar pa yi/ /spyod pa dang mtshungs yang na ni/ /ba glang skyong gi chung ma'i 'os/ /gang yang 'di ni dpa' ba ste/ /dpal gyi mthu las chen po yin/ /bud med kyi yang gzi che ste/ /de phyir
<p>14a.3</p>'di yang nges par bya/ /sngon yang ka shi'i mdzes ma ni/ /smad 'tshong ma yi drang srong che/ /lha yis thub par dka' ba yang / /drang srong rgyas pas rkang pas brdungs/ /mAn thal gau tam dge slong ni/ /smad 'tshong gtso mo byin ma yin/ /dga' 'dod de yi don ched du/ /sngon gyi tshe na ro rnams
<p>14a.4</p>bton/ /gau ta ma mun rings ming / /drang srong chen po tshe rings po/ /kha dog dbyibs mchog ma yin pa'i/ /bud med kyis ni tshim par byas/ /drang srong rwa skyes thub pa mchog /bud med yul la mi mkhas pa/ /rnam pa sna tshogs thabs rnams kyis/ /zhi mas de ltar blangs shing pham/ /
<p>14a.5</p>sna tshogs bshes gnyen drang srong che/ /brtul zhugs chen po brtan pa yang / /lha mo mar srung mas phrogs te/ /lo bcu rnams la nyi mar shes/ /drang srong de rnams de rnams sogs/ /bud med kyis sgyur blangs gyur na/ /rol zhing lang tsho snga ma yis/ /mi bdag sras po smos ci dgos/ /
<p>14a.6</p>de ltar gyur na yid ches shing / /'di ni mi skyong rigs kyi dpal/ /'di las phyir phyogs ma yin pa/ /ji ltar de ltar nan tan mdzod/ /lang tsho ldan ma 'ga' zhig rnams/ /mtshungs pa'i skye bo 'phrog pa ste/ /mchog dang mchog min dag gi sems/ /len pa gang de bud med rnams/ /
<p>14a.7</p>de ltar 'char ka'i tshig thos nas/ /bud med de rnams phug pa bzhin/ /gzhon nu len par rab mtshon te/ /bdag nyid yang dag kun nas 'dzegs/ /'jigs las 'jigs bzhin yan lag ma/ /de rnams smin dang lta dang sgeg /dgod dang rol dang 'gro ba yis/ /kun nas
<p>14b</p>
<p>14b.1</p>bskyod pa'i spyod pa byas/ /rgyal po'i bka' lung sbyar phyir dang / /gzhon nu nyid kyang 'jam phyir dang / /rgyags pa yis ni myos pa'i phyir/ /yid mi ches ba myur bar dor/ /glang mo'i tshogs dang thabs cig tu/ /glang po gangs can nags na ltar/ /de nas mi mo'i skye bo
<p>14b.2</p>yis/ /gzhon nu bskor zhing nags na spyad/ /rnam par mdzes pa'i skyed tshal na/ /lha mos bskor ba'i nyi ma bzhin/ /yid 'ong nags der gzhon nu de/ /bud med rnams ni mdun 'gro bar/ /rnam par sgeg bcas gzhon nu ma/ /rgyags pas ma spangs de rnams dga'/ /sra zhing
<p>14b.3</p>zlum rgyas lhan cig pa'i/ /nu ma rnams kyis de la reg /dpung pa las brul 'jam ring mnyen/ /lag pa'i ljon shing stobs med ma/ /kha cig bden min 'khrul pa ru/ /byas nas de la stobs las 'khyud/ /kha cig zangs mchu ma mchu can/ /kha cig chang gi dri ngag gis/ /gcig pu
<p>14b.4</p>dben par sdod cig ces/ /'di yi rna bar shab shib byed/ /kha cig bka' lung stsol ba bzhin/ /byug pa gsher mas rab smras te/ /'dir ni gus par gyis shig ces/ /dgod dang 'khyud dang 'dod pas so/ /kha cig gser gyi ska rags kyi/ /cal col rnams kyis tsam tsom dang / /
<p>14b.5</p>phra mo'i dar gyi gos gyon zhing / /'di la ro smad ston cing bskor/ /yang dang yang du myos ma'i rgyus/ /gzhan ma dar sngon nyil ba ste/ /ska rags phan tshun sdud pa ni/ /mtshan mo glog phreng bzhin du mdzes/ /tsU ta'i me tog yal ga rgyas/ /bzung nas gzhan ni 'phyang gyur la/ /gser
<p>14b.6</p>gyi bum par mtshungs pa yi/ /lo ma 'dzin pa ston par byed/ /kha cig pad+ma'i nags tshal nas/ /'ongs nas pad bcas pad+ma'i spyan/ /pad+ma'i zhal gyi logs gnas shing / /pad+ma'i dpal bzhin bsdad par gyur/ /rang gnas de la bskul ba bzhin/ /bslus par gyur zhes mig rnams
<p>14b.7</p>kyis/ /kha cig mngon par 'dren bcas lag /don ldan dngar ba'i glu len no/ /dge ba'i gdong gis gzhan mas ni/ /smin pa'i gzhu ni rnam bkang ste/ /bskor gnas brtan dang rol pa yis/ /'di yi spyod la rjes zlos byas/ /rgyas zlum nu ldan kha cig ni/ /dgod pas rna lung
<p>15a</p>
<p>15a.1</p>g.yos gyur cing / /khyod ni thob par gyur cig ces/ /mthon po rnams kyis bzhad cing smras/ /gzhan ni de bzhin 'gro 'dod pa/ /me tog phreng ba'i tshal gyis bcings/ /kha cig cod bcas dngar mo yis/ /ngag gi zhags pa rnams kyis bzung / /so sor
<p>15a.2</p>'bral ba don gnyer 'ga'/ /tsU ta'i snye ma bzung nas ni/ /me tog 'di ni gang gi zhes/ /rgyags pas rnam par 'khrugs shing dris/ /kha cig 'gros dang cha lugs ni/ /skyes pa bzhin du byas nas ni/ /sa 'dir rgyal bar gyur cig kye/ /bud med kyis 'pham de la smras/ /de nas
<p>15a.3</p>g.yo ba'i mig can 'gas/ /ut+pal sngon po snom byed cing / /cung zhig rgyags skad tshig rnams kyis/ /mi skyong bdag skyes la smras so/ /gzigs shing jo bo tsU ta'i shing / /me tog sbrang rtsi'i dris khyab la/ /khu byug 'dir ni skad 'don pa/ /gser gyi bu na bkag pa 'dra/ /mya ngan
<p>15a.4</p>med pa'i shing 'di gzigs/ /'dod pa can gyi mya ngan 'phel/ /bung ba 'dir ni sgra bsgrags pa/ /me yis tshig pa yin pa 'dra/ /tsU ta'i shing gis yang dag 'khyud/ /gzigs shing ti la ka yi shing / /bud med lus ser chags pa yis/ /skyes pa gos dkar gon pa 'dra/ /
<p>15a.5</p>rab rgyas ku ra ba ka gzigs/ /ma zos pa yi smug rtsi'i 'od/ /bud med rnams kyi sen 'od kyis/ /sma phab gyur te dud pa 'dra/ /gzhon nu mya ngan med 'di gzigs/ /'dab ma rnams kyis spras pa gang / /kho mo'i lag pa mdzes pa yis/ /ngo mtshar gyur te gnas pa 'dra/ /rdzing
<p>15a.6</p>bu gzigs shing 'gram skyes pa'i/ /lcang ma rnams kyis rab tu bskor/ /dkar po'i dar gyi gos gon pa'i/ /rab myos ma rnams nyal ba 'dra/ /bud med rnams la bdag nyid che/ /gzigs shig ngang pa chu 'di la/ /rgyab na bsgo bya'i bran bzhin du/ /ngang mo rjes 'jug rjes
<p>15a.7</p>su 'gro/ /rab tu myos pa'i khu byug ni/ /skad grag sgra ni gson mdzod cig /khu byug gzhan ni mngon sum du/ /kus 'debs brag ca'i sgra brnyan 'dra/ /mkha' la rgyu ba rnams kyi yang / /rgyags pa dpyid kyis khyer te 'ongs/ /bsam bya min sems skye bo ni/ /shes rab can du
<p>15b</p>
<p>15b.1</p>rlom pa med/ /de ltar dar la bab pa rnams/ /yid dkrugs 'dod pas sems dregs shing / /sna tshogs tshul ni de dang des/ /gzhon nu la ni nye bar brtsams/ /de ltar kun nas g.yengs na yang / /brten pas dbang po dkris pa de/ /'chi bar bya zhes skyo byas shing / /
<p>15b.2</p>dga' dang 'jigs pa med par 'gyur/ /de rnams kyi ni gnas skabs de/ /gzigs nas skyes mchog dam pa des/ /mnyam la skyo dang brtan pa yi/ /thugs kyis bsams par gyur pa'o/ /ci zhig bud med 'di rnams ni/ /lang tsho g.yo bar rtogs pa min/ /gang
<p>15b.3</p>phyir gzugs kyi myos pa ni/ /gang zhig dga' bas nyams par 'gyur/ /gang gi nang du bying ba ru/ /nges par de rnams kyis mi mthong / /'gro ba nad kyi chos can la/ /'jigs pa spangs te de ltar dga'/ /thams cad 'phrog byed 'chi ba yi/ /nges
<p>15b.4</p>par mngon par shes min zhing / /de ltar rang gnas skyo med par/ /rtsed mo dang ni bzhad gad byed/ /rga dang na dang 'chi ba yang / /shes ldan yin na sems ldan su/ /rang gnas langs dang 'dug pa 'am/ /nyal byed rgod pa smos ci dgos/ /nad dang 'chi ba nyid dang ni/ /mchog tu
<p>15b.5</p>'khogs gang de mthong nas/ /rang gnas gyur zhing skyo med pa/ /ji ltar sems med de ltar de/ /me tog rnams dang 'bras bu yis/ /rnam par spangs par gyur pa'i shing / /'gyel lam yang na bcad pa ste/ /shing gzhan mdzes par byed ma yin/ /de ltar bsam gtan mchog mthong
<p>15b.6</p>nas/ /yul rnams la ni 'dod pa thal/ /'char ka tshul lugs bstan bcos shes/ /mdza' bo nyid kyis de la smras/ /kho bo mi skyong gis byin te/ /khyod la grogs su nus pa lo/ /gang phyir khyed la smra 'dod pa/ /rab dga' ldan pa de phyir ro/ /phan pa min las rab 'gegs shing / /phan
<p>15b.7</p>pa la yang rjes rab 'jug /sdug pa na yang yongs mi gtong / /yongs rdzogs shes kyi mtshan nyid do/ /bdag de byams par dam bcas nas/ /skyes bu'i don la phyir phyogs pa/ /gal te khyod la btang snyoms byed/ /grogs po nyid kyang ma yin no/ /de phyir mdza' bor gyur nas smras/ /
<p>16a</p>
<p>16a.1</p>gzhon nu'i lus dang ldan pa ni/ /khyod kyis 'di 'dra bud med kyis/ /yul la mkhas pa'i gzugs brnyan min/ /de yi ngo tsha'i rgod don dang / /bdag nyid dga' ba'i don nyid du/ /bden min gyis kyang mi mo yi/ /rjes su 'jug pa rigs pa yin/ /yang dag 'dud dang
<p>16a.2</p>rjes 'jug gi/ /bud med rnams kyis sems 'ching ste/ /brtse ba'i yon tan skye gnas phyir/ /yid la 'dod pa bud med yin/ /de phyir rnam par spangs pa'i spyan/ /snying la gzhan du phyir bltas kyang / /'di yi yul dang rjes mthun par/ /mkhas pa rnam par dpyad par 'os/ /mkhas pa
<p>16a.3</p>sman yin bud med la/ /mkhas pa rab mchog rgyan yin no/ /mkhas pa dang bral gzugs dag ni/ /me tog med pa'i nags dang 'dra/ /yang na mkhas pa'i rang bzhin gyi/ /bsam pa rang bzhin khas len mdzod/ /yul rnams nyes par dka' thob nas/ /phyi shol byed pa 'os ma yin/ /
<p>16a.4</p>sngon tshe lha yi dbang pos kyang / /'dod pa mchog ces shes byas nas/ /gau tam thub pa'i dga' ldan ma/ /bshol med ma la 'dod pa byas/ /zla ba'i chung ma snar ma ni/ /drang srong ri byis don du gnyer/ /de nas de dang 'dra ba yi/ /brkam bya ma ni rnyed ces thos/ /u b+ha th+ya yi chung ma ni/ /rlung
<p>16a.5</p>gi bu mo mthun ma la/ /dka' thub chen po'i phur bu yis/ /ba ra dwa dza bskyed par gyur/ /drang srong phur bu'i chung ma ni/ /sbyin sreg ma la sbyin sreg mchog /zla ba yis ni lag pa yi/ /lha yi las byed bskyed par gyur/ /sngon tshe bu mo nag mo ni/ /chur skyes ma las skyes ma la/ /rtsib
<p>16a.6</p>logs skyes ni chags skyes shing / /ya nu ni yi gling du phyin/ /gnod sbyin phreng ma rigs ngan ma/ /snod ma la ni dga' 'dod pas/ /gong ma sreg ni za ba'i bu/ /thub pa gnas mchog gis bskyed do/ /'gro mgyogs rgyal po drang srong nyid/ /na tshod rnam par song ba yi/ /lha mo sna tshogs
<p>16a.7</p>mchod mar bcas/ /sna tshogs shing rta'i nags su dga'/ /bud med 'grogs min zhi ba ni/ /skya bseng gis ni shes nas kyang / /dga' ma'i gzugs yon gyis bkug ste/ /'dod las skyes pa'i bde ba bsten/ /skyed mdzad rgyal po dmar ser yang / /bram ze'i bu mo phrogs nas ni/ /
<p>16b</p>
<p>16b.1</p>na babs thob pa nyid yin kyang / /yid dkrugs 'dod pa ma bsten min/ /de la sogs pa bdag nyid ches/ /yul rnams smad pa yin na yang / /dga' ba'i ched du longs spyad de/ /yon tan ldan la sngon nyid do/ /khyod kyang rigs pa las 'thob cing / /stobs ldan gzugs ldan dar
<p>16b.2</p>la bab/ /gang du skye 'gro 'di 'chags na/ /yul rnams la ni phyi shol byed/ /de ltar 'jam zhing lung dang bcas/ /de yis tshig ni gsan gyur nas/ /'brug gi sgra skad dbyangs kyis ni/ /gzhon nu yis ni lan smras so/ /ngag tshig 'di ni 'thad pa ste/ /khyod la mdza' bo nyid du gsal/ /
<p>16b.3</p>gang du bdag la ngan par sems/ /'dir ni khyod la rjes zhi bgyi/ /yul rnams la ni phyi shol byed/ /'jig rten de'i bdag nyid du shes/ /'gro ba mi rtag par shes nas/ /'dir ni bdag yid dga' ba min/ /rga dang na dang 'chi ba ste/ /gal te 'di gsum ma yin na/ /yid du 'ong ba'i yul
<p>16b.4</p>rnams la/ /kho bo yang ni dga' bar 'gyur/ /gal te bud med rnams kyi lus/ /de nyid rtag par 'gyur na ni/ /skyon ldan 'dod pa rnams la yang / /kho bo'i sems ni 'dod la phyogs/ /gang tshe 'di dag rnams kyi gzugs/ /rgas pas 'thung ba 'byung 'gyur zhing / /bdag nyid kyi yang
<p>16b.5</p>'dod med na/ /rmongs las der ni dga' bar 'gyur/ /rga dang na dang 'chi ba'i tshes/ /rga na 'chi ba'i bdag nyid kyis/ /skyo ba med par rol pa ni/ /ri dgas dang ni bya dang mtshungs/ /bdag nyid chen po 'di rnams kyang / /'dod pa'i bdag nyid ces smras gang / /'dir ni skyo bar bya ba ste/ /gang tshe de
<p>16b.6</p>rnams kyi yang tshad/ /gang du phyi las zad pa ste/ /bdag nyid chen por mi sems te/ /yul rnams la ni chags pa 'am/ /sbyor min bdag nyid ldan nyid kyis/ /mkhas pa yis kyang dpe brjod cing / /bden min gyis kyang bud med kyi/ /skye la zhugs zhes smras pa gang / /bden min bdag gis
<p>16b.7</p>shes ma yin/ /gang du drang min rjes 'jug pa/ /de la bdag gis sred pa med/ /dngos po kun gyi tshogs ba de/ /gal te smon na med par shog/ /mi brtan pa yi dad pa dang / /skyon du mthong ba'i nus pa yis/ /chags pa skyes par gyur pa'i sems/ /slu bar bya ba ci zhig yin/ /bud
<p>17a</p>
<p>17a.1</p>med skyes pa'i chags skyes shing / /bud med skyes pa phan tshun du/ /gal te de ltar slu na ni/ /lta bar nus pa nyid ma yin/ /de ltar gyur na sdug bsngal gyis/ /nyam thag rga 'chi'i skal ba can/ /bdag ni 'phags min 'dod pa la/ /slu bar 'os pa ma yin no/ /e
<p>17a.2</p>ma shin tu brtan la stobs ldan khyod kyi sems/ /'dod pa g.yo ba rnams su snying po mthong gyur la/ /shin tu rno zhing 'jigs pa'i yul la zon mdzad cing / /rga dang rgud pa nad kyi 'jigs pa rnam sems shing / /'gro ba rnams ni me yis tshig pa bzhin thos na/ /zhi ba 'thob min brtan min dga'
<p>17a.3</p>ba ga la zhig /the tshom med par 'chi zhes rab tu shes pa yi/ /mi rnams gang gi snying la chags pa rab skyed pa/ /de yi sems ni lcags las gyur par shes pa ste/ /'jigs pa che la chags pa gang zhig du ba med/ /de nas gzhon nu yis ni 'dod pa rnams kyis bsten/ /'joms byed
<p>17a.4</p>gtam ni rnam par nges pa'i bdag nyid mdzad/ /skye bo rnams kyi mig gi 'gro bya gsal byed kyi/ /dkyil 'khor sa 'dzin ri bo la ni nub par gyur/ /de nas rgyan dang me tog phreng ba 'bras med 'dzin/ /sgyu rtsal yon tan gyis dang rab dgas 'bras med rnams/ /rang gi sems la yid dkrugs
<p>17a.5</p>'dod pa rnams smad nas/ /yid la re nyams bud med rnams ni grong du thal/ /de nas grong khyer skyed mos tshal song skye bo'i dpal/ /legs par brtags nas spyod la so sor brtul te yang / /thams cad mi rtag par gyur rnam par sems bzhin du/ /slar yang mi skyong bdag skyes grong du rnam par
<p>17a.6</p>zhugs/ /de nas de yi yid ni yul la rnam par phyir phyogs rgyal pos thos gyur nas/ /snying la song ba'i zug la glang chen bzhin du mtshan mo de la gnyid ma log /de nas sngags mang rnam pa sna tshogs lam rnams dag gis thang chad blon por bcas/ /des ni 'dod pa las gzhan sras kyi blo yi
<p>17a.7</p>nges pa gzigs ma gyur/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ bud med kyis gegs byas pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// //de ltar yul rnams dam pa'i mchod pa rnams kyis ni/ /sred du bcug kyang shAkya'i rgyal po'i sras po de/ /dug
<p>17b</p>
<p>17b.1</p>bsgos mda' yis snying la phug pa'i seng ge bzhin/ /bde ba rnyed pa ma yin brtan par gshegs ma gyur/ /de nas res 'ga' zhig na blon po'i bu mkhas shing / /grogs gyur sna tshogs gtam gyis rjes su 'brangs byas pa/ /nags kyi sa la 'gro 'dod lta bar 'dod pa yis/ /mi yi
<p>17b.2</p>lha yis rjes gnang phyi rol rab tu gshegs/ /gsar ba'i gser gyi srab dang dril bu chung ngu dang / /rab tu g.yo ba'i rnga yab mdzes pa'i gser sga dang / /stan bcas dam pa'i rta la mngon par zhon nas ni/ /tog la ljon dang chu skyes tog can bzhin du gshegs/ /de ni mchog tu rnam par
<p>17b.3</p>rgyang ring nags mtha'i sa/ /nags tshal 'dod dang sa yi yon tan las gshegs te/ /chu gnyer bzhin du rnam par bkram pa'i gshol lam can/ /nor 'dzin sa la zhing dag rmo ba gzigs par gyur/ /gshol gyi phya las rnam bkram rtswa myug ku sha dang / /shi gyur 'bu srin srog chags
<p>17b.4</p>phra mos khyab pa ste/ /rnam pa de 'dra'i sa de yang dag mngon gzigs nas/ /rang gi skye bo bsad pa la bzhin mya ngan gyur/ /zhing dag rmo ba'i skyes bu rnams ni rnam gzigs pa/ /rlung gis gtor ba'i rdul gyis rnam 'gyur kha dog can/ /khur bas thang chad rnam par 'khrugs pa'i glang rnams
<p>17b.5</p>la/ /'phags pa mchog gis mchog tu brtse ba'i snying rje mdzad/ /de nas mgyogs 'gro'i rgyab nas dal bus babs nas ni/ /sa la rnam par rgyu zhing mya ngan dang ldan pa/ /skye bo dag gi skye dang 'god pa rnam sems zhing / /nges par bkren pa 'di zhes smras shing nyam thag gyur/ /bsam pa yis
<p>17b.6</p>kyang rnam par dben pa mngon bzhed cing / /rjes su 'ongs pa'i mdza' bshes de rnams phyir bzlog nas/ /kun nas mngon par g.yo zhing mdzes pa'i lo 'dab can/ /'dzam bu'i rtsa ba skye bo med par de gshegs so/ /rin chen bai DUr+ya dang mtshungs pa'i rtswa 'jam can/ /gtsang mar ldan pa'i sa gzhi der ni
<p>17b.7</p>de zhugs te/ /'gro ba'i skye ba dang ni 'god pa rnams sems shing / /yid ni brtan pa'i lam la dmigs pa'o/ /yul la 'dod sogs sems kyi nad las rnam grol ba'i/ /sems gnas pa ni de ma thag tu thob gyur la/ /bsam gtan dang po zag pa med pa'i rab spyod pa/ /rtog pa dpyod pa dang
<p>18a</p>
<p>18a.1</p>bcas zhi ba thob par gyur/ /rnam par dben pa las skyes thob nas de nas ni/ /mchog tu dga' ba'i bde ba sems kyi ting nge 'dzin/ /yid kyis 'jig rten 'gro ba yang dag rab brtags nas/ /'di nyid de nas gzhan ni rab tu rtogs par gyur/ /kye ma skye bo bkren pa
<p>18a.2</p>gang zhig rang dbang ni/ /yod min rga dang na dang rnam par nyams pa'i chos/ /nad pa dang ni shi dang rga bas nyam thag gam/ /gzhan la rgyags pas long zhing shes pa med pas smod/ /'dir ni gal te bdag gis rang dang mtshungs gyur pa/ /gzhan gyi rang bzhin dag la de ltar smod ba ni/ /mchog gi chos
<p>18a.3</p>'di rnam par rtog pa kho bo yi/ /mtshungs par gyur pa ma yin nus pa'ang gzhan med do/ /'gro ba'i rga dang na dang rgud pa'i nyes pa rnams/ /de ltar ji lta ba bzhin rnam par gzigs de yi/ /stobs dang lang tsho dang ni srog la rab zhugs pa'i/ /bdag tu gyur pa'i rgyags pa skad cig gis med gyur/ /
<p>18a.4</p>de ni dga' ba med cing rjes su gdung med la/ /the tshom som nyir ma gyur gnyid dang rmugs pa med/ /'dod pa'i yon tan rnams la yang dag ma chags shing / /gzhan la rnam par sdang bar ma gyur phyi shol med/ /de ltar bdag nyid chen po de yi rdul med cing / /rnam par dag pa'i blo gros 'di ni 'phel
<p>18a.5</p>gyur la/ /skyes bu gzhan dag rnams kyis mthong bar ma gyur pa'i/ /dge slong cha lugs ldan pa'i skyes bu nye bar 'ongs/ /su zhig yin pa smros zhes mi yi lha sras kyis/ /de la mngon par dris gyur de la des smras pa/ /mi yi skyes mchog skye dang 'chi bas 'jigs pa yi/ /thar pa'i phyir ni rab tu
<p>18a.6</p>zhugs pa'i dge sbyong yin/ /bdag ni 'gro ba zad pa'i chos ni thar 'dod cing / /dge zhing 'gyur ba med pa'i gnas de tshol ba ste/ /rang gi skye bo dang ni skye bor mnyam pa'i blo/ /yul rnams la ni chags pa'i nyes pa phyir log pa'o/ /skye bo med pa'i gnas khang dang ni ri 'am nags/ /shing gi rtsa
<p>18a.7</p>ba 'ga' zhig tu ni gnas pa yi/ /don dam phyir ni ji ltar nyer ldan slong mo ba/ /sred bral yongs su 'dzin pa med par rnam par rgyu/ /de ltar gzigs pa'i rgyal po'i sras po de nyid la/ /'di skad smras nas nam mkha' la ni gshegs par gyur/ /de ni de yi lus kyis sangs rgyas gzhan gzigs
<p>18b</p>
<p>18b.1</p>shing / /lha na gnas pa de yi dran pa'i ched du 'ongs/ /mkha' la mkha' 'gro bzhin du gshegs pa de la ni/ /mi mchog yang dag dga' bar gyur zhing ya mtshan gyur/ /de nas chos kyi 'du shes nye bar thob gyur nas/ /mngon par nges 'byung cho ga la ni blo gros mdzad/ /de nas dbang po
<p>18b.2</p>dang mnyam dbang po'i rta thul ba/ /grong la rab tu 'jug 'dod rta la rab 'dzegs shing / /'khor gyi skye bo dag kyang mngon par 'dod pa ste/ /de nyid phyir na mngon 'dod nags ni ma bsnyen to/ /de ni rga dang 'chi ba zad par byed 'dod pa/ /nags su gnas phyir blo gros dran pa la bzung nas/ 
<p>18b.3</p>gnyis 'thung dbang po nags kyi sa nas grong du ltar/ /'dod pa las min grong la slar yang rab tu zhugs/ /de ni yang dag mthong nas shAkya'i bu mo zhig /rab zhugs lam la thal mo sbyar ba dang bcas shing / /kye ma spyan dbang gang gi bdag po 'di 'dra 'dir/ /mo de bde ma mya ngan 'das ma zhes
<p>18b.4</p>smras so/ /de nas dbyangs 'di sprin chen dbyangs dang ldan pa yis/ /yongs su thos nas mchog tu zhi ba rnyed gyur la/ /mya ngan 'das zhes sgra skad thos pa dang ldan des/ /yongs su mya ngan 'da' ba'i chos gar blo gros mdzad/ /de nas gser gyi ri bo'i rtse mo'i sku mnga' zhing / /glang chen phyag dang
<p>18b.5</p>'brug gi sgra dbyangs khyu mchog spyan/ /seng ge'i stobs dang ri bong can gyi zhal mnga' bas/ /mi zad chos la chags skyes pho brang rab tu 'thob/ /de nas mtho ris dag na lha yi 'dun sa ru/ /lha dbang 'bar ba la ni bkug 'gyed gzhon nu bzhin/ /blon po'i tshogs kyis nye bar bsnyen pa'i mi
<p>18b.6</p>bdag la/ /ri dgas dbang po'i 'gros dang ldan pa mngon par gshegs/ /rab tu btud nas thal mo dang bcas smras gyur pa/ /mi dbang bdag la legs par rjes su gnang ba byin/ /nges par skye bo 'di ni rnam par 'bral ba ste/ /thar pa'i ched du yongs su rnam par gshegs par bgyi/ /de ltar
<p>18b.7</p>de'i tshig nges par thob nas rgyal po ni/ /lag ldan gyis ni mngon snun ljon pa ltar g.yos shing / /ka ma la dang rab mtshungs thal mo dag bzung nas/ /mchi ma dang ni gre ba kha zhing tshig 'di smras/ /brtse ba'i blo gros 'di ni rab tu thong mdzod cig /khyed kyi chos la bsnyen pa'i dus ni ma yin te/ /na tshod dang
<p>19a</p>
<p>19a.1</p>po dang ni blo gros g.yo ba na/ /chos kyi spyod pa gsungs pa rnams ni skyon mang ngo / /yul rnams su ni dbang po ya mtshan glo bur zhing / /brtul zhugs g.yo ba rnams su nges par nus med la/ /khyad par du ni dben par mngon par mi shes pa/ /dar la bab pa'i yid
<p>19a.2</p>ni dgon pa nas g.yo'o/ /mtshon gyur khyod la phun sum tshogs pa gtad nas ni/ /kho bo yi yang chos dga' chos kyi dus yin te/ /rnam par gnon pa bstan pa rnam par gnon pa yis/ /bla ma spangs nas khyod kyi chos kyis chos ma yin/ /de phyir khyod kyis nan tan nges pa 'di dor la/ /
<p>19a.3</p>khyod ni re zhig khyim gnas chos la dga' bar gyis/ /dar la bab pas bde ba rnams ni longs spyad nas/ /skyes bu'i dka' thub nags su 'jug pa nyams dga'o/ /de ltar rgyal po'i tshig 'di rnam par gsan nas ni/ /ka la ping ka'i dbyangs kyis lan ni smras pa ste/ /rgyal po gal te bdag
<p>19a.4</p>gi khas len bzhi rnams su/ /khyed kyis 'gyur na dka' thub nags ni mi bsnyen to/ /bdag gi srog ni 'chi ba nyid du mi 'gyur zhing / /bdag gi rang gnas gyur 'di nad kyis mi 'phrogs la/ /bdag gi lang tsho rgas pa yis ni mi g.yeng zhing / /phun sum tshogs pa 'di ni rgud pas
<p>19a.5</p>ma gtor na'o/ /de ltar rnyed par dka' ba'i don smras gyur pa yi/ /sras po la ni shAkya'i rgyal pos tshig smras pa/ /shin tu rab tu zhugs pa'i blo 'di thong mdzod cig /shin tu yid la re ba 'phya zhing sha thang 'chad/ /de nas lhun po ltar lcis bla ma la smras pa/ /gal te rim pa de dag med
<p>19a.6</p>de shol mi thebs/ /'bar ba'i me yis tshig pa'i khang pa nas/ /phyi rol 'byung bar 'dod pa 'dzin par nus ma yin/ /gang gi tshe na 'gro ba nges par 'bral ba ste/ /chos phyir ma yin 'di ni rnam par 'bral ba mchog /'o na bdag la 'chi bas dbang med 'bral byed cing / /rang gi don
<p>19a.7</p>ma byas shing tshim pa ma yin nyid/ /de ltar mthar bzhed sras po de yis nges pa ni/ /sa yi bdag po yis ni nges par thos nas ni/ /'gro bar mi bya zhes ni mngon par brjod nas su/ /slar yang bsrung ba dag ni 'dod pa mchog rnams mdzad/ /dga' zhi zhi ba sngon 'gro bskur sti mang po las/ /
<p>19b</p>
<p>19b.1</p>blon po rnams kyis ji lta ba bzhin dpe bstan zhing / /bla mas mchi ma lhung ba rnams kyis shol btab ste/ /de nas de ni mya ngan bzhin du khyim la zhugs/ /rna lung 'khyil ba g.yo bas 'o byas gdong ldan ma/ /dbugs rlung stug pos rnam par bskyod pa'i nu ma can/ /bstan pa min pa'i mig ldan
<p>19b.2</p>bud med rnams kyis ni/ /ri dgas mo rnams kyis bzhin mngon par gyen du lta/ /gser gyi ri bo dang 'dra dkar ser mdog de ni/ /yan lag mchog ma rnams kyi snying ni myos mdzad cing / /ngag dang reg bya dang ni lus dang yon tan gyis/ /thos byed lus dang lta byed bdag gi dngos rnams
<p>19b.3</p>phrogs/ /nyin mo rnam par thal tshe de nas khang bzangs la/ /lus kyis nyi ma bzhin du mngon par gsal ba ni/ /rab rib rnam par 'joms 'dod bdag nyid snang ba yis/ /nyi ma shar ba lhun po la bzhin kun nas 'dzegs/ /gser gyis 'bar zhing gsal ba'i sgron ma'i shing dang ni/ /a ga ru
<p>19b.4</p>mchog nag po'i bdug pas gang ba'i ltor/ /mngon par 'dzegs nas rdo rjes spras shing sna tshogs pa/ /rab mchog gser gyi bzhugs gdan la ni bsnyen pa'o/ /zla ba ltar dkar gangs dang ldan pa'i rtse mo na/ /nor dbang bdag nyid skyes la lha mo'i tshogs 'dus bzhin/ /de nas lus mchog ma
<p>19b.5</p>rnams dbang po dang mtshungs mchog /de la mtshan mor sil snyan rnams kyis nye bar gnas/ /mchog rab lha yi sil snyan 'dra ba rnams kyis kyang / /de yang de yis bskyed par ma gyur dga' ba med/ /dam pa'i don gyi bde phyir legs pa de yi ni/ /mngon par nges par 'byung 'dod gang la dga'
<p>19b.6</p>ma gyur/ /de nas der ni brtul zhugs mchog gyur 'og min gyi/ /lha rnams kyis ni 'di yi nges pa rtogs nas ni/ /lus kyi rnam 'gyur rnam par 'gyur byas dus gcig la/ /myos ma'i skye bo rnams ni gnyid du 'gro bar byas/ /de la kha cig dga' ba yin yang khros pa bzhin/ /pang du son pa'i
<p>19b.7</p>gser gyi snod ni sna tshogs pa'i/ /pi wang rnam par spangs nas lag pa g.yo ba la/ /'gram pa rnam par bkod nas nyal bar gyur pa'o/ /'khyog min bung ba'i phreng ba sgra sgrogs pad+ma dang / /chu bo'i ngogs na chu sbur rab tu rgod pa bzhin/ /gzhan rnams nu mar rnam nyil dkar po'i dar gon zhing / /
<p>20a</p>
<p>20a.1</p>gling bu lag par sbyar zhing gnyid log rnam par mdzes/ /de bzhin gzhan rnams pad+ma gsar pa'i snying po ltar/ /'jam zhing gdung bya gser gyis 'bar ba'i dbu brgyan ni/ /'dus pa'i lag pa dag gis dga' ba bzhin du ni/ /rdza rnga nyid ni yongs su 'khyud
<p>20a.2</p>nas gnyid log gyur/ /de bzhin gzhan ni gsar ba'i gser gyis rnam brgyan zhing / /bgo ba'i gos ni ser po mchog dag gon pa ste/ /kar ni ka ra'i yal ga glang pos bsgyel ba bzhin/ /dbang med par ni sdug ma gnyid kyis 'gyel bar gyur/ /de bzhin gzhan ni skar khung
<p>20a.3</p>logs la sngas nas ni/ /nyal bar gyur pa'i lus kyi mchod sdong rnams 'khyog pa/ /rta babs la ni sha la b+hany+dza ka bzhin du/ /mdzes pa'i do shal rnam par 'phyang ba rnam par mdzes/ /de bzhin gzhan gyi zhal gyi pad+ma rnam rgyas shing / /'gram pa'i logs la nor bu'i rna lung gis
<p>20a.4</p>dmugs pa/ /'dab ma brgya pa'i sdong bu'i phyed ni 'khyog pa la/ /gnas pa'i kar Ni Da bas bskyod bzhin g.yos par gyur/ /gzhan ni ji ltar rnam par zhugs bzhin gnyid log cing / /nu ma'i khur gyis mngon par dud pa'i lus po rnams/ /lag pa'i zhags pa gser gyi gdu bu can rnams kyis/ /
<p>20a.5</p>phan tshun nye bar 'khyud nas rnam par gnas te mdzes pa'o/ /rnam par g.yo zhing bskyod pa'i gser gyi skud pa can/ /rna ba'i shog dril kun nas 'khrugs pa'i gdong gis ni/ /yongs su smra ldan pi wang chen po 'khyud nas ni/ /bud med kha cig grogs mo bzhin du gnyid log go/ /lang tsho ma
<p>20a.6</p>gzhan lag pa'i dpung pa'i yul las ni/ /kun nas rnam 'phyang mdzes pa'i logs can pa Na wa/ /sgyeg bcas dga' ba'i mthar ni thang chad sdug pa bzhin/ /brla gnyis dag ni dbus su blangs nas nyal ba'o/ /rab tu yang dag 'khums gyur pad+ma dmar po'i mdzod/ /nyi ma nub
<p>20a.7</p>par gyur tshe rdzing bu rnams ji ltar/ /rnam rgyas mig dang mdzes pa'i smin ma yod na yang / /gzhan rnams mig rnams btsums shing mdzes par ma gyur to/ /de bzhin gzhan ni mgo skyes lhod pa las 'khrugs shing / /rgyan dang dar rnams dpyi la rnam nyil de rnams ni/ /yan lag ma yi gzugs
<p>20b</p>
<p>20b.1</p>brnyan glang pos bcom pa bzhin/ /mgrin pa'i skud pa'i do shal rnam par bkram zhing nyal/ /brtan ldan lus ni yon tan rnams dang ldan na yang / /gzhan rnams kyang ni dbang med ngo tshas rnam spangs shing / /rnam par 'gyur zhing bskyod pa'i yan lag gya gyu dang / /dbugs ni rnam par rgyu
<p>20b.2</p>zhing lus po gsal bar gnyid/ /gzhan gyi rgyan dang me tog phreng ba rnam brul zhing / /mdud pa'i gos rnams rnam par nyil gyur 'du shes med/ /btsums pa ma yin dkar po g.yo ba dang bral mig /srog song ro ltar nyal ba rnam par mdzes ma gyur/ /kha sbyar rnam par gdangs te
<p>20b.3</p>lus po rab brkyang zhing / /kha yi chu ni rab 'dzags gsang ba rnam rab gsal/ /gzhan ma dag ni chang gis 'khrul par gyur pa nyid/ /lus rgyas rnam par 'gyur bar gnyid log mdzes ma gyur/ /de ltar sems pa dang ni rigs kyi rjes 'gro'i gzugs/ /rnam pa sna tshogs rab myos skye bo de
<p>20b.4</p>nyal ba/ /rlung gis kun nas bskyod gyur gser gyi pad+ma yi/ /rdzing bu dang ni mtshungs pa'i gzugs ni mdzes par gyur/ /de ltar rnam par 'gyur la brtan min spyod pa can/ /de ltar nyal ba'i lang tsho ldan ma de mthong nas/ /lus kyi yon tan ldan zhing smra ba'i yid 'ong yang / /mi skyong sras po des ni rnam
<p>20b.5</p>par smad par gyur/ /mi gtsang rnam par 'gyur ba gson pa'i 'jig rten te/ /bud med rnams kyi rang gi ngo bo 'di 'dra ba/ /bgo ba rnams dang rgyan rnams kyis kyang slu ba ste/ /bud med rnams kyi yul la skyes pa chags par 'gro/ /gal te skyes pas bud med rnams kyi rang bzhin ni/ /rmi lam rnam
<p>20b.6</p>par 'gyur ba bzhin du rnam dpyad na/ /nges par 'dir ni bag med 'phel ba ma yin la/ /'on kyang yon tan rtog pa bcom ste chags par 'gro/ /de ltar de yi go skabs rnam par rig nas ni/ /mtshan mor phyi ru 'gro 'dod yang dag skyes par gyur/ /'di yi sems ni kun nas rtog nas de nas ni/ /
<p>20b.7</p>lha rnams dag gis khang pa'i sgo ni phye bar gyur/ /de nas lang tsho ldan ma nyal ba de rnams ni/ /smad cing de ni lding khang logs nas babs pa ste/ /mngon par babs nas de nas som nyi rnam bral bar/ /khang pa'i rim pa dang por phyi ru rnam par gshegs/ /de ni mgyogs 'gro bsrungs la go bar
<p>21a</p>
<p>21a.1</p>byas nas ni/ /skyen par 'dun pa la ni 'di skad ces smras so/ /bsngags ldan rta ni khyer shog myur ba dang ldan pas/ /bdud rtsi thob phyir 'di las di ring bdag skom mo/ /bdag gi snying la de ring tshim pa skyes gyur zhing / /nges pa
<p>21a.2</p>yang ste ji ltar blo gros la zhugs pa/ /skye bo med pa la yang mgon dang ldan pa ste/ /nges par 'dod pa'i don ni mngon du phyogs par 'du/ /ngo tsha nyid dang yang dag 'dud pa spangs nas ni/ /long tsho ma rnams bdag gi gdong du ji bzhin nyal/ /sgo ni rang bzhin ji ltar rnam par dbye ba la/ /nges
<p>21a.3</p>par bdag ni 'di nas di ring 'gro ba'i dus/ /mi dbang brtan pa'i don ni rnam par rig na yang / /jo bo bka' lung des ni de nas rab bzung nas/ /yid la pha rol po yis yang dag bskul ba bzhin/ /mgyogs 'gro khyer te 'ong ba la ni blo gros byas/ /de nas gdong gi gser gyi srab kyis gang ba ste/ /
<p>21a.4</p>rgyab na yang ba'i stan g.yogs dag gis nye bar g.yogs/ /stobs dang sems pa mgyogs dang rjes 'gro nyer ldan pa/ /de yis rta mchog de la der ni nye bar 'ongs/ /snga ma'i rtsa ba rtsib logs gsum ga rab rgyas shing / /rgyab dang rna ba lus skyes spu ni thung zhing dul/ /rgyab kyi rtsib ma dag ni dud cing
<p>21a.5</p>rnam rgyal la/ /mchu dang dpral ba brang dang dpyi ni rab rgyas pa'o/ /zhi zhing ka ma la dang mtshungs pa'i phyag gis kyang / /sku stong rnam par spangs des de la nyer 'khyud nas/ /rgyal mtshan sde la dmag dpon rab tu 'jug pa bzhin/ /mngar mo'i yi ge'i tshig gis zhal ta mdzad pa'o/ /g.yul du khyod la
<p>21a.6</p>mngon par zhon nas sa skyong gis/ /dgra bo rnams ni lan grangs mang por nges par gtor/ /bdag kyang 'chi med go 'phang ji lta ba bzhin du/ /mgyogs 'gro'i gtso bo nye bar thob pa de ltar mdzod/ /yul thob bde ba la dang nor bsgrub pa la rung / /g.yul 'gyed pa na 'khor ni nges par rnyed bla ste/ /brgyud par
<p>21a.7</p>lhung ba la ngang chos la brten par rung / /skyes bu yi yang 'khor ni rnyed par dka' ba'o/ /'di nyid du yang gang zhig 'khor du gyur pa ni/ /sdig pa'i las la dang ni chos dang ldan la rung / /ji ltar bdag gi nang gi bdag nyid kyis rtogs pa/ /mi de rnams kyang de yi cha shas skal ba yi/ /de phyir chos dang ldan pa
<p>21b</p>
<p>21b.1</p>'di ni yongs shes nas/ /bdag ni 'di las nges 'byung 'gro la phan pa'i phyir/ /mgyogs 'gro mchog skye shugs dang rnam par gnon pa yis/ /bdag phan la dang 'gro phan la ni 'bad par gyis/ /de ltar mdza' bshes bzhin du rjes su bslabs nas ni/ /mgyogs 'gro mchog la mi mchog
<p>21b.2</p>'gro 'dod de/ /dkar la dkar min 'gros kyi 'od zer lung ldan pa/ /nyi ma ston ka'i sprin la bzhin du yang dag 'dzegs/ /de nas 'khor gyi skye bos go bar byed pa'i skad/ /mtshan mor gtum pa dam pa'i rta des yongs bkag cing / /'gram pa'i sgra med 'tsher ba'i skad ni rab zhi bar/ /
<p>21b.3</p>'jigs pa'i sgra ni dor ba'i gom pa'i 'gros kyis gshegs/ /gser gyi gdu bu'i rgyan ni lag pa'i mkhrig ma la/ /ka ma la 'dras ka ma la rnams rnam byas nas/ /lus 'dud gnod sbyin rnams ni de nas 'di yis ni/ /tshim gyur lag pa'i rtse mos rmig pa rnams bzung ngo / /lci mo'i sgo
<p>21b.4</p>gtan sgo glegs yang dag bcad pa gang / /bde bar gnyis 'thung gis kyang phyed pa ma yin pa/ /mi skyong sras po gshegs tshe skad med grong khyer dang / /sgo khang de rnams rang nyid rnam par bye bar gyur/ /mngon par gdong phyogs yab dang sras po byis pa dang / /skye bo rjes su chags dang phun
