<p>21b.5</p>tshogs mchog dag ni/ /blo gros byas shing ltos pa med par dor nas ni/ /yab kyi grong nas de ni de nas rnam par gshegs/ /de nas de ni rnam rgyal 'dam skyes yangs pa'i spyan/ /grong khyer kun nas gzigs nas seng ge'i sgra bsgrags pa/ /skye dang 'chi ba dag gi pha rol ma mthong bar/ /
<p>21b.6</p>grong khyer ser skya zhes byar rab tu mi 'jug go/ /de ltar de yi gsung ni nges par thos nas ni/ /nor gyi bdag po'i 'khor rnams dag ni dga' bar gyur/ /rab tu dga' ba'i yid can lha yi tshogs rnams ni/ /nan tan pha rol song ba de la bsngags pa byas/ /me yi lus can mtho ris gnas pa
<p>21b.7</p>gzhan rnams ni/ /'di yis nges pa shin tu dka' ba rnams rig nas/ /sprin stug gseb nas zla ba'i 'od zer 'thon pa bzhin/ /mtshan mo'i mun pa'i lam ni rab tu gsal bar byas/ /nyi ma'i mgyogs 'gro lta bu'i mgyogs 'gro de/ /yid kyis sprul pa bzhin du rnam par rgyu bzhin du/ /shing
<p>22a</p>
<p>22a.1</p>rta 'dren pas gzi nyams skar ldan bar snang la/ /de ni shin tu mang po'i dpag tshad rnams su gshegs/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ phyi rol du mngon par byung ba'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// //de nas 'gro mig nyi ma
<p>22a.2</p>ni/ /mngon par shes pa'i yud tsam na/ /ngan spong bu yi dka' thub gnas/ /mi mchog des ni gzigs par gyur/ /blo phab gnyid log ri dgas dang / /rang gnas gnas par bya gang zhig /gzigs nas ngal sos bzhin du dang / /don ni byas pa bzhin du gyur/ /de ni rgyags pa med
<p>22a.3</p>don dang / /dka' thub mchod pa'i don nyid dang / /rang gi rjes su srung ba la/ /rta yi rgyab nas babs par gyur/ /mngon par babs nas kyang reg cing / /dga' zhing mig gis 'khru ba bzhin/ /nges par 'khor zhes rta dang ni/ /'dun pa la ni smras pa'o/ /'di ni mkha' lding dper mgyogs la/ /
<p>22a.4</p>mgyogs 'gro la ni rjes su 'ongs/ /'dis ni bdag gi stobs dang ni/ /zhi ba bdag la gus pa bstan/ /thams cad nas don gzhan yin kyang / /khyod kyi snying la bzung ba ste/ /gang gi jo bo dag la dga'/ /'di ni de 'dra dag la nyid/ /gus pa med la nus pa yod/ /nus pa med la gus
<p>22a.5</p>pa ldan/ /gus pa ldan dang nus pa ste/ /khyod 'dra sa stengs rnyed par dka'/ /de phyir skal ba chen po'i las/ /khyod kyi 'dis ni bdag dga'o/ /gang zhig khyod kyis bsams pa 'di/ /'bras bu las kyang gzhan du phyogs/ /skye bo 'bras bu la gnas pa'i/ /mthun phyogs skye bo gang gis
<p>22a.6</p>min/ /zlog la rang gi skye bo yang / /phal cher pha rol skye bor gyur/ /rigs kyi don du bu bzung zhing / /gsos pa'i don du pha bskyed la/ /sred pa'i bsam pas chags skye ste/ /byed pa med par rang nyid med/ /mang po brjod cing mdor bsdus nas/ /bdag gi dga' chen legs byas te/ /
<p>22a.7</p>rta blangs nas ni phyir log dang / /bdag ni 'dod pa'i gnas rab thob/ /de skad smras nas phyag chen te/ /rjes su bsngags par byed 'dod pas/ /rgyan rnams kun nas btogs nas ni/ /gdung sems ldan pa 'di la byin/ /dbu rgyan dag nas nor bu gsal/ /sgron ma'i las la blangs nas ni/ /nyi ma
<p>22b</p>
<p>22b.1</p>'bigs byed la bzhin des/ /tshig 'di smras bzhin bzhugs par gyur/ /'dun pa nor bu 'di long la/ /lan mang btud nas mi skyong ni/ /kun nas gdung ba zlog pa'i phyir/ /blo phebs par ni gsol bar bya/ /skye dang 'chi ba nyams don du/ /dka' thub nags tshal rab thob ste/ /mtho ris
<p>22b.2</p>skom pas nges min zhing / /brtse ba med min khros pa min/ /de phyir de ltar mngon byung ba/ /bdag la mya ngan 'os ma yin/ /yun rings 'dus par gyur nas kyang / /dus kyis 'gyur ba ma yin no/ /gang phyir nges par 'bral ba ste/ /de phyir thar phyir bdag gi blo/ /slar yang rang gi skye bo las/ /
<p>22b.3</p>rnam par 'bral ba gang las min/ /mya ngan spong phyir nges 'byung ba/ /bdag la mya ngan 'os ma yin/ /mya ngan rgyud ni 'dod la chags/ /chags pa can la mya ngan bya/ /'di yang snga ma rnams la grags/ /kho bo cag la nges par gnas/ /de ltar ster byar gyur pa las/ /mya ngan 'os min lam
<p>22b.4</p>gyis 'gro/ /skyes bu rnams la phyin log tu/ /nor gyis ster byar gyur pa ste/ /sa la chos kyi bdag po yang / /rnyed dka' yang ni ma yin no/ /gang yang 'di ni dus min par/ /nags su song ba yin zhe na/ /srog kyang g.yo bar gyur pa na/ /chos la dus yod ma yin no/ /de phyir da lta nyid du
<p>22b.5</p>bdag/ /dge ba bsag ces nges pa ste/ /'chi ba'i dgra ni gnas pa na/ /gson pa la ni blo gtad cing / /zhi ba khyod kyis de la sogs/ /sa 'dzin bdag la zhu bya ste/ /ji ltar bdag ni mi dran pa/ /de ltar nyid du 'bad pa gyis/ /gzhan yang bdag la yon tan med/ /khyod kyis mi
<p>22b.6</p>bdag la smra bya/ /yon tan med las brtse ba 'dor/ /brtse ba dor las mya ngan med/ /de ltar tshig 'di thos gyur nas/ /'dun pa gdung bas rnam 'khrugs shing / /mchi mas 'dud pa'i tshig nyid kyis/ /thal mo sbyar te lan gsol ba/ /jo bo khyod kyis dgongs pa ni/ /gnyen la ngal ba ster ba
<p>22b.7</p>'dis/ /chu bo'i 'gram na gnyis 'thung bzhin/ /bdag gi sems 'di sgyur ba'o/ /khyod kyis nges pa 'di lta bus/ /su yis mchi ma 'byung ba med/ /lcags las gyur pa'i snying la'ang ste/ /brtse bas 'khrug la smos ci dgos/ /gzhal med khang gi mal 'os pa'i/ /shin tu gzhon nu 'di gang na/ /
<p>23a</p>
<p>23a.1</p>ku sha'i myu gu rno ba can/ /dka' thub nags kyi sa gang na/ /khyod kyi 'bad pa thos nas kyang / /rta gang bdag gis blangs pa 'di/ /mgon po de ni stobs kyis ni/ /lha yis byed du bcug pa 'dra/ /khyed kyi nan tan nges pa 'di/ /rang dbang shes na gang gi phyir/ /nye
<p>23a.2</p>bar len te mgyogs 'gro'i rta/ /ser skya'i gzhi yi mya ngan gnas/ /med pa po yis dam chos bzhin/ /rgyal po brtse ba bgres pa dang / /sras po sdug go 'dor ba ni/ /phyag chen de ni 'os ma yin/ /dam pa'i bya ba byed bcom yin/ /yang dag bskyed pas yongs su ni/ /thang chad gnyis
<p>23a.3</p>pa'i ma de dang / /lha mo brjod par 'os ma yin/ /ma ning gis ni dpal thob bzhin/ /sras po byis pa yon tan ldan/ /rigs btsun bdag po'i brtul zhugs ma/ /lha mo 'dor bar 'os ma yin/ /bsngags 'os sras po grags pa 'dzin/ /snyan grags chos ni 'dzin pa'i mchog/ /zhen
<p>23a.4</p>pa ldan pas grogs mchog bzhin/ /byis pa 'dor bar 'os ma yin/ /ci ste gnyen dang rgyal srid dag/ /'dor ba nyid du blo gros mdzad/ /bdag gi 'gros ni khyod zhabs la/ /khyab bdag bdag 'dor 'os ma yin/ /ma g+hu'i bu ni bshes bzang bzhin/ /khyod ni dgon par dor nas su/ /me
<p>23a.5</p>yis tshig pa'i sems kyis ni/ /grong du 'gro bar nus pa med/ /khyod 'dir grong du 'gro ba can/ /rgyal pos bdag la ci zhig gsung / /khyed kyi btsun mo'i 'khor du 'am/ /'os pa mi thong na ci zhig smra/ /gang yang yon tan med pa yang / /mi bdag la smos gsung ba yang / /skyon med thub pa'i
<p>23a.6</p>bzhin khyod kyi/ /ma gyur pa de ci zhig smra/ /ngo tsha dang bcas sems kyis ni/ /lce ni thogs par gyur pa yi/ /bdag ni gal te yang smra ba/ /de la dad par 'os pa su/ /gang zhig zla ba'i 'od rno bar/ /smra bar dad par 'dzin pa'am/ /khyed kyis skyon shes des skyon ni/ /smra ba dad par 'dzin
<p>23a.7</p>pa'am/ /rtag tu rjes su brtse bcas dang / /rtag par snying rje shes pa yi/ brtse ba spong ba tshul min te/ /phyir log bdag la bka' drin mdzod/ /de ltar mya ngan gyis non pa'i/ /'dun pa'i tshig 'di gsan gyur nas/ /rang gnas mchog tu brtan pa yis/ /smra ba'i mchog gis bka'
<p>23b</p>
<p>23b.1</p>stsal to/ /'dun pa bdag dang bral ba la/ /kun nas gdung ba 'di thong cig /lus can 'gro ba tha dad la/ /dgongs pa sna tshogs nges pa yin/ /gang yang brtse las rang gi skye/ /bdag gis rang ni mi 'dor te/ /'chi bas phan tshun dbang med par/ /bdag cag rnams ni
<p>23b.2</p>'dor bar 'gyur/ /sred pa chen po'i sdug bsngal gyi/ /mngal gang gis ni bdag bzung ste/ /'bras med 'bad pa med de yis/ /bdag su bdag gi de su yin/ /ji ltar sgong skyes gnas shing la/ /yang dag 'dus nas rnam par bral/ /de ltar 'byung po 'dus pa ni/ /
<p>23b.3</p>nges par 'bral ba'i mtha' yin no/ /ji ltar sprin rnams 'dus nas ni/ /slar yang rnam par 'byed pa'o/ /de ltar 'du dang 'bral ba ni/ /bdag dang srog chags rnams kyi lugs/ /gang gi phyir na 'jig rten 'di/ /slus nas rnam par 'bral ba de/ /de phyir rmi lam 'dus gyur la/ /
<p>23b.4</p>bdag gi ba nyid bzod ma yin/ /shing rnams 'dab ma dmar po dang / /lhan cig skyes te rnam par 'bral/ /gzhan dang gzhan gyi 'bral ba ni/ /'gyur ba ma yin smos ci dgos/ /de phyir de ltar gyur na ni/ /zhi ba gdung ba ma byed song / /gal te yang ni brtse ba 'bebs/ /song nas kyang ni
<p>23b.5</p>slar yang shog /kho bo cag la ltos byas pa'i/ /ser skya'i gzhi na skye bo la/ /der song brtse ba thong cig dang / /'di yi nges la nyon cig smos/ /rga dang 'chi ba zad byas nas/ /yang na myur du 'ong ba'i gtam/ /rtsom pa nyams shing don ma byas/ /yang na nyams par 'gyur ba smros/ /
<p>23b.6</p>de ltar 'di yi tshig thos nas/ /bsngags ldan mgyogs 'gro'i mchog gis ni/ /lce yis zhabs la rab ldags te/ /mchi ma dron mo phyung bar gyur/ /dra ba dang ni bkra shis rtags/ /'khor lo dbus ldan phyag gis ni/ /gzhon nus de la reg gyur cing / /na tshod bzhin du rnam par smras/ /
<p>23b.7</p>bsngags ldan mchi ma ma 'don cing / /dam pa'i rta nyid 'di bstan to/ /sron mdzod khyod kyi ngal ba 'dis/ /myur du 'bras bu bcas bar 'gyur/ /de nas ral gri rnon po nor bu'i yu ba can/ /gser gyi phra ni sna tshogs dang ldan 'dun pa yi/ /lag na yang dag gnas pa brtan pa des bsnams
<p>24a</p>
<p>24a.1</p>nas/ /khung bu dag nas sbrul bzhin zhugs nas rab tu drungs/ /ut+pa la yi 'dab ma sngon po de drangs nas/ /sna tshogs dbu rgyan dbu skrar bcas pa rab bcad cing / /rdzing bu dag na ngang pa bzhin du rnam bkram pa/ /'od zer dang ldan bar snang dag la de gtor ro/ /
<p>24a.2</p>mchod pa mngon par 'dod phyir rnam mang bkur sti'i phyir/ /lha ni gnas pas rab tu bkram pa de bzung ste/ /ji lta ba bzhin de ni lha ni lha tshogs rnams/ /lha yi khyad par 'phags pa rnams kyis mchod pa byas/ /rgyan ni bud med ldan pa rnam par spangs nas kyang / /dbu las dpal ni rnam par rgyang ring
<p>24a.3</p>byas nas ni/ /nags su gser gyi ngang pa'i mtshan ma gos gzigs nas/ /brtan pa des ni gos dag mngon par 'dod par gyur/ /de nas lha ni gnas par ri dgas sngon po'i lus/ /dgongs pa rnam dag 'di yi dgongs pa rnams rig nas/ /kha bsgyur ngur smrig gos can nye logs mngon par
<p>24a.4</p>'ongs/ /de la shAkya'i rgyal po skyes kyis mngon par smras/ /khyod kyi dge yi ngur smrig drang srong rgyal mtshan dang / /'tshe ba byed pa'i gzhu 'di rigs pa ma yin te/ /de phyir zhi ba gal te 'dir ni chags med na/ /bdag la rab tu byin la 'di dang 'di snoms mdzod/ /rngon pas smras pa 'dod sbyin
<p>24a.5</p>'dod pa snying po las/ /'di yis blo ni phab nas ri dgas rnams gsod do/ /brgya byin mtshungs pa gang de 'dis ni don 'gyur na/ /e ma rab tu bzhes la dkar po de gsol mdzod/ /de nas de ni mchog tu rab tu dga' ba yis/ /nags su byung ba'i na bza' blangs shing gos dor la/ /
<p>24a.6</p>rngon pa nyid kyang lha yi lus nyid rnam bzung ste/ /dkar po de nyid blangs nas lha ni gshegs par gyur/ /de nas gzhon nu dang ni rta mchog skyong ba des/ /de ltar gshegs pa de la ya mtshan skyes gyur te/ /nags nas byung ba'i na bza' nyid dang de la ni/ /slar yang ri mor bya ba mang
<p>24a.7</p>po skyen par mdzad/ /gdong ni mchi ma dang bcas 'dun pa rnams bzlog nas/ /bdag nyid chen po brtan dang grags pa 'chang ba ste/ /mtshams kyi sprin gyis g.yogs pa'i skar ma'i rgyal po bzhin/ /ngur smrig gyon zhing gdung sems gang yin de nas gshegs/ /de nas de ltar jo bo
<p>24b</p>
<p>24b.1</p>rgyal srid mi bzhed par/ /dka' thub nags su gshegs pa mdog nyams snang ba na/ /mgyogs 'gro 'chang de phyag rgyas gyen du bskyod byas nas/ /shin tu rnam par ngu zhing sa la 'gyel gyur to/ /rnam par bltas nas slar yang sgra bcas par ngu zhing / /bsngags ldan rta la lag
<p>24b.2</p>pa dag gis nyer 'khyud nas/ /de nas kho chad yang dang yang du zlos bzhin du/ /lus kyis song bar gyur kyang sems kyis ma yin no/ /la lar rab tu sems zhing la lar rnam par du/ /la lar sa la rab tu 'brad cing la lar 'gyel/ /de nas 'gro bzhin gus pa'i dbang gis sdug bsngal
<p>24b.3</p>zhing / /dbang med lam na bya ba mang po byas pa'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ bsngags ldan phyir la bzlog pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// //de nas 'dun pa ngu zhing gdong ni mchi ma can/ /bzlog nas nags su 'dun pa'i dka'
<p>24b.4</p>thub chags med pa/ /don kun grub pa'i lus kyis mngon par zil mnan nas/ /dka' thub gnas de grub pa bzhin du rab tu thob/ /de nas ri dgas rgyal po'i 'gros can rgyal po'i sras po de/ /ri dgas gnas der ri dgas bzhin du rab zhugs pa/ /phun tshogs rnams dang bral yang
<p>24b.5</p>lus kyi phun tshogs kyis/ /dka' thub gnas ldan kun gyi mig dag phrogs par gyur/ /khur ldan rnams bzhin mgo bo rnams ni phyed dud pas/ /lag na gnya' shing bcas par 'gro gyur ya mtshan la/ /de bzhin 'khor los sgyur ba chung ma dang bcas pa/ /dbang po dang mtshungs de
<p>24b.6</p>mthong song bar ma gyur to/ /sbyin sreg bud shing phyir ni bram ze rnams phyin nas/ /me tog lo 'dab rgyas pa'i lag pa gtsang ma rnams/ /dka' thub gtso bo rnams ni blo rnams byas na yang / /gshegs pa mthong ste klog glar song bar ma gyur to/ /chu gter sngon po bzhin du mthong nas rma bya
<p>24b.7</p>rnams/ /dga' zhing gyen du dud cing skad dag 'don gyur la/ /rgya skyegs ri dgas spyod ldan rnams dang ri dgas rnams/ /'bru rnams bor nas mngon par gdong phyogs gnas par gyur/ /'od zer ldan pa shar ba lta bur 'bar ba yis/ /bu ram shing pa'i rigs kyi sgron ma de mthong nas/ /
<p>25a</p>
<p>25a.1</p>sbyin sreg 'jo rnams bzhos pa yin na yang / /rab tu dga' ba skyes te rab tu 'jo gyur to/ /'di ni nor sbyin rnams kyi brgyad pa yin nam ci/ /tha skar dag gi nang nas gcig ni 'phos sam zhes/ /de mthong ba la ya mtshan skyes par gyur pa yi/ /thub pa rnams kyi
<p>25a.2</p>tshig der mthon por sgrogs bar gyur/ /lha yi khyu mchog gnyis pa'i lus po lta bu dang / /'jig rten rgyu dang mi rgyu'i snying po lta bu dang / /gang 'dod pa yis nyi ma mngon par babs 'dra ba/ /des ni nags tshal mtha' dag rab tu snang bar mdzod/ /de nas gdung gnas pa de rnams kyi ji lta
<p>25a.3</p>bzhin/ /nye bar snyan gsan phab cing mngon par mchod gyur la/ /de ni chu bcas chu 'dzin lta bu'i dbyangs kyis ni/ /chos 'dzin rnams la slar yang rab tu mchod par gyur/ /de nas rnam par thar bzhed brtan pa de yis ni/ /dka' thub sna tshogs rnams la nges par rnam gzigs shing / /mtho
<p>25a.4</p>ris mngon 'dod bsod nams byas pa'i skye bo yis/ /khyab pa'i dka' thub gnas der rjes su dpyad par gyur/ /dka' thub nor can rnams kyi dka' thub nags tshal der/ /dka' thub rnam par 'gyur ba rnams ni nges gnas nas/ /rjes su gshegs pa'i dka' thub ldan pa kha cig la/ /zhi bas
<p>25a.5</p>de nyid rnam par shes bzhed 'di gsungs so/ /gang phyir chos kyi cho ga 'di ni mi shes pa/ /bdag gis dka' thub gnas mthong de ring snga ma'o/ /de phyir khyod kyis bdag la smra bar 'os min te/ /nges pa gang zhig gang la rab tu 'jug pa'o/ /de nas dka' thub rnam par rgyu ba'i gnyis
<p>25a.6</p>skyes des/ /shAkya'i khyu mchog khyu mchog rnam par gnon pa po/ /de la rim gyis dka' thub khyad par rnams dang ni/ /dka' thub 'bras bu dang bcas gtam ngag byas pa'o/ /grong byung bza' ba ma yin chu la rab skyes pa'i/ /'dab ma rnams dang chu dang 'bras bu rtsa ba nyid/ /
<p>25a.7</p>thub pa rnams kyi spyod pa 'di ni lung ji ltar/ /dka' thub rnams kyi rnam rtog tha dad de de'o/ /kha cig ri dgas bzhin du rtswa rnams la spyod la/ /gzhan rnams bor ba yis ni mkha' la rgyu ba'i bya ltar 'tsho/ /kha cig lag 'gro rnams dang lhan cig 'tsho ba ste/ /grog mkhar gyur pa
<p>25b</p>
<p>25b.1</p>rnams ni nags na rlung gis so/ /rdo yis rab 'bad bsgrub pa'i spyod pa gzhan rnams te/ /kha cig rang gi so yis nye bar blangs shing za/ /de bzhin gzhan ni gzhan gyi don du bcos byas nas/ /gal te lhag ma yod na bya ba byed pa'o/ /chu yis gsher ba'i ral pa'i tshogs can kha
<p>25b.2</p>cig ni/ /gsang sngags sngon 'gro lan gnyis me la sbyin sreg cing / /kha cig nya dang mnyam par chu la rnams zhugs nas/ /rus sbal bzhin du lus rnams rab tu bskum pa'o/ /de ltar dus su bsags pa'i dka' thub nags tshogs kyi/ /mchog gis lhar 'gro gzhan gyis mi yi 'jig
<p>25b.3</p>rten te/ /sdug bsngal lam gyis bde ba nye bar thob phyir dang / /chos kyi rtsa ba bde ba nyid du gsungs phyir ro/ /de skad ces sogs rkang gnyis dbang po'i sras po yis/ /dka' thub nor dang ldan pa de yi tshig gsan nas/ /de nyid gzigs pa min yang ngoms par ma gyur la/ /
<p>25b.4</p>bdag tu song ba 'di ni dal bus gsungs par gyur/ /sdug bsngal bdag nyid dka' thub rnam pa du ma ste/ /dka' thub bdag gi 'bras bu mtho ris gtso bo'o/ /'jig rten thams cad yongs su 'gyur ba dang ldan la/ /nyung ngu la ngal 'di ni gdung gnas rnams kyi'o/ /phangs pa rnams
<p>25b.5</p>dang gnyen dang yul rnams bor nas ni/ /gang zhig mtho ris phyir ni rnam par spyod byed la/ /de rnams rnam par bral te nges par 'gro 'dod la/ /slar yang shin tu 'ching ba chen po nyid yin no/ /lus kyi ngal dub gdung ba'i bya ba rnams kyis ni/ /'dod pa'i rgyu las rab tu 'jug par 'dod
<p>25b.6</p>pa'o/ /'khor ba'i rgya mtsho'i skyon rnams yongs su mi rtog par/ /sdug bsngal gyis de sdug bsngal kho na rjes su tshol/ /'chi bas skye dgu rnams kyis rtag par 'jigs pa ste/ /'bad pa yis ni slar yang rab tu 'jug par 'dod/ /rab tu zhugs par gyur na nges par 'chi ba ste/ /'di nyid du ni
<p>25b.7</p>gang las 'jigs pa rnams lhung ngo / /'di yi don du gcig rnams ngal bar rab 'jug cing / /gzhan rnams mtho ris don du ngal ba 'thob pa ste/ /bde ba'i don du sred pa'i bkren pa don ma byas/ /gson pa'i 'jig rten nges par don med nyid du lhung / /gang zhig dman pa dor nas khyad 'phags
<p>26a</p>
<p>26a.1</p>'gro ba can/ /'bad pa 'di ni nges par smad pa ma yin la/ /shes ldan rnams dang mnyam pa'i yongs su gdung ba yis/ /bya ba ma yin de 'dir slar yang byed pa'o/ /lus kyi gtser bas gal te 'dir ni chos yin na/ /lus kyi bde ba chos ma yin par 'gyur ba ste/ /pha rol
<p>26a.2</p>du ni bde ba chos kyis kyang 'thob la/ /de phyir 'di yis chos kyi chos min 'bras bu'o/ /gang gi phyir na bsams pa'i dbang gis lus yin la/ /rab tu 'jug pa dang ni zlog pa dag kyang ngo / /de phyir sems kyi dul ba nyid ni rig pa ste/ /sems las gzhan pa'i lus ni shing dang mnyas ba'o/ /bza' ba gtsang
<p>26a.3</p>bas gal te bsod nams 'dod na ni/ /de phyir ri dgas rnams kyang bsod nams yod pa ste/ /phyi rol skyes bu gang dag rnams kyang 'bras bu las/ /bskal pa'i nyes pas don rnams gzhan du kha bltas so/ /bsod nams phyir ni sdug bsngal mngon par mtshams sbyor na/ /'o na sdug bsngal mngon par
<p>26a.4</p>mtshams sbyor tshad ma min/ /de ltar gang dag las ni rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ /stegs zhes rab tu zhugs te chu la reg par byed/ /de yang de yi snying la tshim pa tsam yin te/ /chu yis sdig pa dag par byed pa ma yin phyir/ /yon tan ldan bas rig pa'i chu ni gang dang gang / /de dang de ni sa la gal
<p>26a.5</p>te stegs 'dod na/ /chu yang the tshom med par chu nyid kho na ste/ /de phyir yon tan ldan rnams kho na stegs su go/ /de ltar rigs pa mang po ldan pa de dang de/ /smras te rnam par mdzes pa'i nyi ma nub bar gyur/ /de nas sbyin sreg du bas kha dog 'gyur ba'i shing / /dka' thub rab tu zhi ba'i khrus sar
<p>26a.6</p>rnam par zhugs/ /mngon par bton pa'i rab tu 'bar ba'i me yis thal ba ni/ /dbang bskur byas pa'i drang srong skye bos khyab pa ste/ /bzlas bya'i dbyangs kyis kun nas skad sgrogs lha yi tshogs/ /chos kyi lam gyi las kyi mtha' bzhin rab tu zhugs pa'o/ /de ni mtshan mo thang 'ga' mtshan mor
<p>26a.7</p>byed 'od kyis/ /dka' thub rnams la yongs su rtog cing zhugs gyur la/ /dka' thub thams cad yongs su brtags shing mkhyen gyur na/ /dka' thub zhing gi thang de las ni gshegs par gyur/ /de'i gzugs bdag nyid chen por sod ba'i yid rnams kyis/ /dka' thub gnas ldan rnams ni de nas de
<p>26b</p>
<p>26b.1</p>rjes gshegs/ /'phags min sdig pa rnams kyis zil non yul las ni/ /drang srong chen po rnams ni chos bzhin pha rol gshegs/ /de nas ral pa shing shun zur phud kyis rol ba'i/ /dka' thub nor dang ldan ba de rnams des gzigs shing / /de dag rnams kyis dka' thub rnams
<p>26b.2</p>la rjes brten te/ /dpal dang ldan la dge ba'i shing gi rtsa bar gnas/ /de nas dka' thub gnas ldan rnams ni nyer 'ongs nas/ /mi mchog de la yongs su bskor nas gnas gyur la/ /de dag rnams kyi rgyan pos mchod ma sngon btang ste/ /dus kyi zhi bas tshig 'di rab tu 'di smras so/ /khyod
<p>26b.3</p>kyis byon tshe gdung gnas gang ba bzhin gyur la/ /rab tu gshegs tshe stong pa bzhin du rab tu thob/ /de phyir brtse ba 'di ni 'bor bar 'os min te/ /'tsho bar 'dod pa'i phangs pa'i tshe yis lus bzhin no/ /lha yi drang srong tshangs pa'i drang srong rgyal po yis/ /drang srong gis bsnyen bsod nams nye bar gang
<p>26b.4</p>ldan ri/ /dka' thub nor ldan rnams kyi dka' thub de rnams ni/ /gang gi nye logs dag nas mang por 'gyur ba'o/ /de bzhin kun nas bsod nams dag gi stegs gyur la/ /nam mkha'i 'og gi them skas dag tu gyur pa ste/ /lha yi drang srong rnams dang drang srong chen po ni/ /chos kyi bdag nyid bdag nyid
<p>26b.5</p>chen po rnams kyis bsnyen/ /'di nas slar yang khyad 'phags chos kyi ched las ni/ /byang gi phyogs nyid kho nar bsnyen par nus pa ste/ /blo dang ldan pas gom pa gcig tu gyur pa yang / /lho yi phyogs su 'gro bar nus pa ma yin no/ /dka' thub nags 'dir ji ste bya ba ngan pa 'am/ /bsre ma'i
<p>26b.6</p>chos sam ltung ba min nam mi gtsang bar/ /khyed kyis mthong ste gang gis khyed 'di bzhugs 'dod min/ /de ni gsung la re zhig sred par bzhugs mdzod cig /dka' thub gter dang rab tu mtshungs par gyur pa la/ /'di rnams kyis ni dka' thub grogs su 'dod pa ste/ /dbang po dang mnyam khyed dang
<p>26b.7</p>lhan cig gnas pa ni/ /phur bu yi yang mngon par mtho ba 'dren pa yin/ /dka' thub ldan pa'i gtso bos de skad ces smras te/ /srid pa rab tu nyams phyir dam bca' byas pa yis/ /mkhas pa'i gtso bo des ni dka' thub ldan dbus su/ /nang du song ba'i rang bzhin smras par gyur pa'o/ /'gron
<p>27a</p>
<p>27a.1</p>la sdug cing rang gi skye bo dang mtshungs pa'i/ /drang po'i bdag nyid chos 'dzin thub pa rnams kyis ni/ /bdag la rnam pa de ltar bsam pa skyes pa yis/ /bdag gi dga' ba mchog dang bkur sti skyes par gyur/ /mdor bsdus gyur na brtse zhing bsnyen pa 'di rnams dag /snying la
<p>27a.2</p>song ba'i ngag rnams ngag gis khrus byas bzhin/ /kun nas 'dzin med chos can bdag gi dga' ba ni/ /de ring slar yang cung zhig g.yos par gyur pa nyid/ /de ltar rab tu zhugs pa'i khyed cag skyabs 'os rnams/ /shin tu phyogs su lhung ba yang dag bstan pa rnams/ /bor nas 'gro zhes kho
<p>27a.3</p>bo yi yang sdug bsngal te/ /ji ltar gnyen 'dun rnams ni spangs pa de ltar ro/ /khyed cag rnams kyi chos 'di mtho ris ched du ste/ /bdag gi mngon par mtho bar yang srid ma yin phyir/ /nags der gang gi bdag ni sdod 'dod ma yin te/ /chos las ldog pa rab tu 'jug pa tha dad phyir/ /
<p>27a.4</p>de phyir nags 'di dag na gang gis yongs 'gro ba/ /bdag gi ma dga' ma yin pha rol spyod log min/ /sngon gyi dus na rjes mthun chos la gnas pa yi/ /drang srong chen po thams cad rnams dang mtshungs par gyur/ /de nas don dang ldan la bde zhing yid du 'ong / /legs mthun mdangs dang ldan
<p>27a.5</p>la snying po dang ldan pa/ /gzhon nu'i tshig ni dka' thub ldan pa de rnams kyis/ /thos nas khyad 'phags dang ldan bkur sti mang pos gshegs/ /de nas gnyis skyes thal ba la nyal kha cig ni/ /lus ring gtsug tor dang ldan shing shun gos gyon zhing / /mig ni cung zad dmar ser sna ni phra la
<p>27a.6</p>rings/ /lag gcig spyi blugs ldan pas tshig 'di smras pa'o/ /khyod kyis nges pa nyid du rgya chen blo ldan zhing / /gzhon nu khyed kyi skye ba la ni nyes pa gzigs/ /mtho ris dang ni nyes pa yang dag rnam spyod phyir/ /thar pa gang gi blo gros yod pa de yin no/ /mchod sbyin dka' thub nges ba de dang de
<p>27a.7</p>rnams kyis/ /chags pa dang ldan mtho ris la ni 'gro bar 'dod/ /dgra bo bzhin du chags dang lhan cig g.yul sprad nas/ /sems pa rang ldan thar pa ru ni 'gro bar 'dod/ /de phyir gal te khyod kyi blo gros 'di nges na/ /skyen par khyed nyid 'bigs byed phug par gshegs mdzod
<p>27b</p>
<p>27b.1</p>cig/ /gang zhig mthar thug nges par legs pa thob ba'i mig/ /thub pa 'di ni de ru mtshan mo min par gnas/ /de phyir khyod kyis de nyid lam ni thob 'gyur la/ /sred par gyur na yang dag rab tu thob par 'gyur/ /bdag gi mthong ba ji ltar blo gros de de ltar/ /de nyid kyi yang blo gros bor
<p>27b.2</p>nas 'gro bar 'gyur/ /gsal zhing mtho ba'i shangs dang rnam rgyas yangs pa'i spyan/ /zangs mdog ya mchu ma mchu rno dkar mche ba can/ /ljags ni dmar zhing phra ba'i zhal dang ldan pa 'di/ /shes bya'i rgya mtsho mtha' dag la ni 'gro ba nyid/ /khyod kyi zab pa dang ni gting dpag dka' gang
<p>27b.3</p>dang / /gang zhig sgron ma nyid dang mtshan rnams gang yin pas/ /sngon gyi bskal par drang srong gis kyang ma mthong ba'i/ /slob dpon nyid de sa la mngon par dga' nas gshegs/ /dka' thub ldan pa de rnams kyis kyang de la yang / /cho ga bzhin rjes byas nas dka' thub nags der
<p>27b.4</p>gshegs/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ /dka' thub kyi nags su zhugs pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// //de nas mgyogs 'gro spyod de yid mi bde gyur te/ /de ltar jo bo nags su nga med par gshegs la/ /lam du mya ngan med pa 'bad
<p>27b.5</p>pa byas gyur te/ /de lta na yang de yi mchi ma khogs ma gyur/ /gang la jo bo'i bka' la mtshan mo gcig gis ni/ /mgyogs 'gro de dang gshegs par gyur pa'i lam/ /lam de nyid la 'gro zhag dag ni brgyad rnams kyis/ /jo bo nyid dang bral ba de yis sems shing 'ongs/ /'thon ba med pas rgyags
<p>27b.6</p>pa med par gyur pa yis/ /bsngags ldan mgyogs 'gro nyid kyang mdangs med rgyu ba ste/ /de ltar rgyan de rnams kyis brgyan par byas na yang / /de yis dor bas dpal ni song ba bzhin du gyur/ /phyir log nas kyang dka' thub nags su mngon phyogs te/ /snying rje bar ni yang dang yang du drag tu 'tsher/ /
<p>27b.7</p>lam na ltogs pa ldan pa yin yang 'bru dang chu/ /ji ltar sngon bzhin mngon par ma dga' ma bslangs so/ /de nas 'gro la phan pa'i bdag nyid bdag nyid chen po des/ /ser skya zhes bya'i grong khyer rnam par dman pa la/ /nyin mor byed pas bor ba'i nam mkha' 'bras med bzhin/ /rim gyis de gnyis
<p>28a</p>
<p>28a.1</p>stong pa bzhin du nye bar song / /pad+ma dkar po dang bcas chu yis mdzes gyur zhing / /me tog 'dzin pa'i shing rnams kyis ni brgyan pa yang / /grong khyer pa rnams rab tu dga' ba song gyur te/ /de yi nye ba'i nags de nags ltar mdzes ma gyur/ /de ltar lta byed mchi mas bcom pa'i
<p>28a.2</p>mi rnams ni/ /rab tu 'bar min zhan pa'i yid kyis phyogs su skor/ /'ong du mi ster ba bzhin gnyis po de grong du/ /dal bus log pa'i khrus bzhin mngon par song bar gyur/ /shAkya'i rigs kyi drang srong dang bral 'ongs pa yis/ /lus zags 'gros dang ldan pa de gnyis mthong nas kyang / /
<p>28a.3</p>sngon tshe shing rta bcu pa'i shing rta 'ongs pa bzhin/ /grong khyer skye bo rnams ni lam du mchi ma phyung / /de nas mya ngan nye bar ldan ba'i skye bo dag /mchi ma byung ba rnams kyis 'dun pa la smras pa/ /grong khyer yul 'khor dga' mdzad rgyal bo'i sras po de/ /khyed kyis gang du bor zhes rgyab nas rjes su
<p>28a.4</p>'gro/ /de nas gus ldan skye bo de la des smras pa/ /mi dbang sras po bdag gis yongs su bor ba min/ /ngu bzhin skye bo med pa'i nags su kho bo dang / /khyim bdag cha lugs dag kyang de yis rnam par spangs/ /de yi tshig ni skye bo de rnams kyis thos nas/ /nges par shin tu dka' ba nyid
<p>28a.5</p>ces nges par song gyur la/ /'gyel zhing mig skyes chu ni rnam par 'thor ba ste/ /yid la smod cing bdag nyid kyis ni 'bras bu long / /de nas smras pa gnyis skyes rgyal po'i shugs mnga' ste/ /gang du gshegs pa'i nags der di ring zhugs par bgyi/ /lus can dbang po ma tshang rnams
<p>28a.6</p>kyi ji lta bar/ /de dag bral bas bdag cag 'tshe bar 'dod pa med/ /de dang bral ba'i grong khyer 'di ni nags yin la/ /de dang yang dag ldan pa'i nags de grong khyer yin/ /lha ni lha min gsod tshe brgya byin gyis ji ltar/ /de dag bral bas bdag gi grong khyer mdzes ma gyur/ /de
<p>28a.7</p>nas slar yang gzhon nu phyir la log ces te/ /yan lag ma rnams skar khung phreng rnams rab thob ste/ /mgyogs 'gro'i rgyab ni rnam par dben ba mthong gyur nas/ /slar yang skar khung rnams ni rnam par bkag nas ngu / /brtul zhugs dang ni mya ngan dag gis yid dub cing / /brtul zhugs la rab zhugs
<p>28b</p>
<p>28b.1</p>pas sras po nyer thob phyir/ /bzlas byas shing gi lha yi khang par mi bdag gis/ /bsam pa ji ltar bya ba de dang de rnams byas/ /de nas mig dag mchi mas rab tu gang ba des/ /mgyogs 'gro blangs nas mgyogs 'gro rjes su 'gro ba ste/ /g.yul 'gyed pa na dgra bos jo bo khyer ba ltar/ /mya ngan dag gis
<p>28b.2</p>mngon bcom mi skyong khang par zhugs/ /mi dbang rgyal po'i khab tu rnam par zhugs pa na/ /rnam par blta zhing mig dag mchi ma 'bab pa yis/ /skye bo la ni sdug bsngal rab tu rtogs 'jug bzhin/ /bsngags ldan mgyogs 'gro gsal ba'i dbyangs kyis ngus par gyur/ /de nas khang pa'i dbus na spyod pa'i bya
<p>28b.3</p>rnams dang / /nye bar brtags pa'i mgyogs 'gro dam par byed rnams kyis/ /mi dbang sras po log par gshegs la the tshom ste/ /mgyogs 'gro de yi dbyangs la so sor ram 'degs byas/ /ji ltar bsngags ldan mgyogs 'gro 'tsher bar byed pa ste/ /nges par gzhon nu khab tu rnam par zhugs snyam
<p>28b.4</p>ste/ /dga' ba phul du byung bas bslus pa'i skye bo rnams/ /skye bo'i bdag po'i btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nye logs song / /shin tu dga' ba las ni mya ngan gyis brgyal rnams/ /gzhon nu blta ba la ni g.yo ba'i spyan ma rnams/ /ston ka'i chu gter sprin las glog ni g.yo ba bzhin/ /bud med rnams ni sred
<p>28b.5</p>pas khyim nas phyir la 'thon/ /lan bu rnam par 'phyang zhing dar gos dri ma can/ /mig rtsi dang bral mchi mas mig bcom gdong rnams kyis/ /mtshan mo zad tshe skya rengs kyis mkhar skar ma bzhin/ /byi dor dang bral bud med rid rnams mdzes ma gyur/ /rkang pa rkang gdub dang bral zangs mdog ma
<p>28b.6</p>chags rnams/ /gdong pa rna lung dang bral mgrin pa drang po rnams/ /rang bzhin gyis rgyas brla ni 'og phab dang bral rnams/ /nu ma do shal dang bral stod g.yogs tshad rnams so/ /rten dang bral ba'i 'dun pa dang ni mgyogs 'gro nyid/ /mig ni mchi ma dang ldan de rnams kyis mthong nas/ /nags mthar khyu
<p>28b.7</p>mchog dang bral ba glang rnams bzhin du/ /sems khral gdong ldan yan lag mchog ma rnams ni ngus/ /de nas rgyal po'i btsun mo mchi ma dang bcas par/ /be'u nyams pa'i ma he mo ltar mnyes gshin ma/ /gser gyi chu shing lo 'dab rnam par g.yo ba bzhin/ /gau ta ma mas ni lag pa bzung nas 'gyel/ /
<p>29a</p>
<p>29a.1</p>dpung pa lag pa mnyam zhing gzi brjid bcom pa yis/ /bud med gzhan rnams yid mi bde bas sems med bzhin/ /mchi ma ma bton 'o dod 'bod min dbugs med par/ /g.yo bral ri mo bris pa bzhin du gnas par gyur/ /brtan min bdag po'i mya ngan gyis brgyal
<p>29a.2</p>bud med gzhan/ /rnam par lta byed nas 'bab rgyun gyi gdong rnams kyis/ /sa 'dzin ri bo nas 'bab rgyun gyi rdo ba ltar/ /tsan+dan rab bskus nu ma rnams la rnam par 'thor/ /de rnams kyis ni mig chus btab pa'i gdon rnams kyis/ /rgyal po'i khab de de tshe mdzes par gyur pa ni/ /
<p>29a.3</p>chu gsar dus na chu gter char gyis btab pa yi/ /chu 'dzin pad+ma rnams kyis rdzing bu ji ltar ro/ /rgyas shing bar med legs par zlum pa'i sor mo can/ /rgyan bral rtsa mi mngon pa'i yan lag mchog ma rnams/ /rlung gis g.yos pa'i ljon shing rang gi 'dab mas ltar/ /pad+ma lta bu'i lag
<p>29a.4</p>pa rnams kyis brang rnams brdungs/ /nags rlung gis sgul pad+ma lta bur g.yos pa yis/ /ngang pa rnams kyi 'khrigs pa rnams kyis chu klung ltar/ /brang brdungs rab bskyod 'brel mtho'i nu ma rnams kyis ni/ /de lta na yang mi mo de rnams mdzes par gyur/ /ji ltar brang rnams la ni lag
<p>29a.5</p>pas zug byas pa/ /de ltar lag pa rnams la brang ni zug byed cing / /le lo can ma brtse med stobs med ma yis der/ /lag pa'i rtse dang brang rnams phan tshun zug byas so/ /de nas khros pas rab tu dmar ba'i spyan ldan ma/ /sems khral gyis sbrel mgrin pa kha zhing ldab ldib dang / /shugs ring phyung
<p>29a.6</p>bas 'o ma 'dzin g.yo brtan pa yi/ /mya ngan mchi ma 'dzin pa'i grags 'dzin mas smras pa/ /mtshan mo gnyid log dbang med bdag ni rnam spangs nas/ /'dun ba 'dod pa'i shing rta de ni gang du thal/ /gsum po mnyam du song la khyod dang bsngags ldan ni/ /nye bar 'ongs pas kho mo'i yid ni g.yos par gyur/ /kho
<p>29a.7</p>mo 'phags min brtse min bshes ma yin pa'i las/ /phul byung de 'dir byas nas da ni ci la ngu / /mchi ma ma 'don khyod kyi sems ni sim par 'gyur/ /khyod kyi mchi ma dang ni las de gtam ma yin/ /dga' dang dbang du song dang phan dang legs pa dang / /ci lta ba bzhin don byed khyod nyid dang 'grogs shing / /
<p>29b</p>
<p>29b.1</p>slar mi ldog pa'i ched du jo bo sras po thal/ /khyod kyis nga la 'bras bcas sems ni dga' bar gyis/ /mi yi dbang po'i dgra bo dag ni mchog yin la/ /sbyor min la mkhas shes rab med pa'i bshes mchog min/ /nges par mdza' bshes rnam par mi mkhas khyod kyis ni/ /'di yi rigs kyi nye bar nub pa
<p>29b.2</p>chen po byas/ /rab chags dri mas 'dres shing dmar ba'i mig can ma/ /kun nas rgyan dang bral ba 'di rnams mya ngan byed/ /gangs ldan ri bo dang mnyam bdag po gsan na yang / /bud med rnams ni yugs sa mo bzhin mdzes pa nyams/ /'di dag rnams kyang bya 'dab lag pa rnam bskyod cing / /
<p>29b.3</p>rtag par phug ron rnams kyi ring ba'i skad rnams ni/ /de dang bral bas 'bras med pho brang 'khor dang bcas/ /gzhal med khang pa'i gtsang rnams shin tu ngu ba 'dra/ /skye bo 'di ni kun nas don med 'dod pa ste/ /bsngags ldan mgyogs 'gro de yang nges pa nyid du'o/ /mtshan mo skye bo gnyid che rkun pos rin chen
<p>29b.4</p>bzhin/ /bdag gi 'di ltar 'di nas nor rdzas thams cad stor/ /mgyogs 'gro 'dis ni mda' yi rma srol byung rnams kyang / /sron par nus zhes grags na lcags rnams smos ci dgos/ /bdag gi snying dang 'dra ba'i dpal ni blangs gyur nas/ /'dis ni lcags lhung 'jigs las song ba yin nam
<p>29b.5</p>ci/ /mi dbang pho brang yongs su gang ba bzhin du ni/ /'phags pa min las da lta drag tu 'tsher bar byed/ /gang gi tshe na bdag gi dga' ba phyi rol gshegs/ /de yi tshe na mgyogs 'gro lkugs pa thang chad gyur/ /gal te skye bo dag la go bar 'tsher byed dam/ /yang na rmig pas sa
<p>29b.6</p>la rmig pa'i sgra byed dam/ /yang na 'gram pa'i sgra ni mchog tu bskyod na ni/ /bdag la sdug bsngal 'di 'dra 'byung ba ma yin no/ /de ltar 'dir ni lha mo'i smre sngags la brten zhing / /mchi mas 'dud pa yi ge'i tshig dag thos gyur nas/ /'og tu gdong phyogs mchi ma dang bcas thal sbyar te/ /
<p>29b.7</p>'dun pas lan 'di dal bus smras par gyur pa'o/ /lha mo bsngags ldan la ni smod par 'os min zhing / /kho bo la yang khro bar mdzad pa 'os ma yin/ /kho bo cag gi skyon min lha mo mkhyen par mdzod/ /mi yi lha de lha bzhin bkra shis kun gyis gshegs/ /bdag gis rgyal po'i brtan pa
<p>30a</p>
<p>30a.1</p>shes pa yin na yang / /lha nyid gang dag gis ni stobs las byas pa bzhin/ /bdag gis mgyogs 'gro 'di ni nye bar 'ongs pa de/ /lam na ngal ba med par de ltar rjes su song / /mgyogs 'gro mchog 'di nyid kyang gshegs tshe sa la ni/ /bar snang dag la
<p>30a.2</p>bzung bzhin rmig pas ma reg cing / /de bzhin lha yi ched du gdong ni sngogs byas bzhin/ /'gram pa'i sgra ni byas min 'tsher ba dag kyang med/ /gang las sa skyong bdag nyid skyes pa gshegs pa na/ /de tshe sgo ni rang nyid bye bar gyur pa ste/ /mtshan mo'i mun pa nyi mas bzhin du bsal gyur te/ /
<p>30a.3</p>de yi phyir yang lha yi cho ga de zung shig /gang phyir mi dbang bka' las skye bo stong phrag dag /khang pa dang ni grong khyer nyid du bag yod kyang / /de tshe de ni gnyid kyis phrogs shing ma sad de/ /de yi phyir yang lha yi cho ga de zung shig/ /gang phyir nags na gnas la mthun pa'i gos dag ni/ /lha na gnas
<p>30a.4</p>pas dus su 'di la byin gyur la/ /rgyan dag mkha' la rab tu gtor ba de khyer te/ /de yi phyir yang lha yi cho ga de zung shig/ /de phyir de ltar lha mo nged gnyis la skyon du/ /ji ltar song ba de la rtog par 'os ma yin/ /mgyogs 'gro 'di dang bdag gi 'dod pa mi mdzad par/ /de ni lha rnams dag gis rjes
<p>30a.5</p>'gro byas shing gshegs/ /de ltar bdag nyid chen po de yis rab gshegs pa/ /lha yi mtshar mang bud med de rnams kyis thos nas/ /rab tu gshegs las yid la 'bar ba yang 'thob ste/ /mya ngan rab tu nyams bzhin ngo mtshar ldan par thal/ /de nas yid mi bde bas yongs lding mig can ma/ /phrug
<p>30a.6</p>gu rab tu nyams pa'i 'ol ba sdug bsngal bzhin/ /rmongs gyur nyid kyang mchi ma dang ldan gdong gis smras/ /rlabs chen dang ldan 'jam zhing dkar min dge ba ste/ /so so so sor rtsa ba nas 'khrungs gyen du 'khyil/ /de yid bu skyes sa la 'thor ba de rnams ni/ /mi dbang dbu rgyan la ni yongs su dkri bar 'os/ /
<p>30a.7</p>phyag ni rab 'phyang ri dgas rgyal po'i stobs mnga' zhing / /khyu mchog chen po'i spyan ldan gser 'bar 'od mnga' ba/ /'brug dang rnga yi sgra ldan sku stod rnam par yangs/ /de ltar gyur kyang dka' thub gnas su gnas par 'os/ /sor mo legs skyes 'jam zhing dra bas 'brel pa dang / /long bu mi mngon pad+ma'i
<p>30b</p>
<p>30b.1</p>rtsa ba ltar 'jam la/ /dbus na 'khor lo dang bcas zhabs ni de dag gis/ /drang srong rnams kyi nags mtha'i sa la 'gro 'am ci/ /khang bzangs logs na khri dang gdan la 'os pa ste/ /rin chen na bza' lci min tsan+dan gyis spras shing / /de yi lus ni mdangs dang ldan pa nags dag tu/ /grang dang dro dang
<p>30b.2</p>chu 'od rnams su bskor ram ci/ /rigs dang gzugs dang stobs dang sems pa dag dang ni/ /thos dang phun sum tshogs dang na tshod kyis khengs shing / /slong bar ma yin ster ba nyid du mngon 'ongs pa/ /de ni pha rol dag la slong mo rgyu 'am ci/ /gser khri dang zhing gzims mal dag la gzims nas ni/ /
<p>30b.3</p>mtshan mo sil snyan sgra rnams dag gis rab slong ba/ /gos kyi phyogs gcig bar na sa yi logs la ni/ /bdag gi brtul zhugs ldan de de ring ji ltar gzims/ /snying rje'i smre sngags rab tu zlos pa 'di thos nas/ /bud med de rnams phan tshun lag pas yongs 'khyud de/ /ljon shing g.yos las me
<p>30b.4</p>tog las ni sbrang rtsi bzhin/ /rnam par lta byed dag nas chu dag 'thor ba'o/ /de nas ngang pa med pa'i ngang mo bzhin du ni/ /grags 'dzin ma ni nor 'dzin sa la 'gyel gyur la/ /rnam par 'khrugs shing yang dang yang du ldab ldib kyi/ /skad kyis de dang de dag rnam par smras pa'o/ /chos dang lhan
<p>30b.5</p>cig spyod pa mgon med kho mo ni/ /de yis dor nas gal te chos ni byed 'dod cing / /chos dang lhan cig spyod ma dang bral dka' thub gang / /yongs su longs spyod 'dod 'di'i chos ni ga la zhig/ /sngon gyi sa skyong rnams des nges par ma mthong ste/ /legs mthong chen po la sogs mes po chen
<p>30b.6</p>po rnams/ /bdag po ldan ma dang bcas nags su gshegs gyur la/ /kho mo dang bral chos byed 'dod pa de ltar ltos/ /mchod sbyin du 'am rig byed cho gas 'dus byas shing / /pho mo gnyis la dbang bskur de yi 'bras bu ni/ /gzhan du mnyam por longs spyod 'dod pa ma mthong ste/ /de nas
<p>30b.7</p>bdag la 'di yi chos la ser sna skyes/ /bdag nyid la ni sdud dang phan tshun phrag dog cing / /yang yang rtsod par chos 'ga' des ni nges par shes/ /khro ba kho mo spangs nas dbang chen 'jig rten du/ /'jigs med lha mo las ni dga' ba len par 'dod/ /de la lus kyi yon tan bzung ba'i
<p>31a</p>
<p>31a.1</p>btsun mo de/ /ci 'dra zhig gam 'di ni bdag gis bsam mno ste/ /bdag gi gus pa nyid dang bud med bor nas ni/ /nags su gang phyir des ni dka' thub rnams la gdung / /nges par bdag gi 'dod 'di mtho ris bde phyir min/ /sems ldan skye bo de ni rnyed par dka' ba min/ /
<p>31a.2</p>sdug pa des kyang bdag la 'di 'am gzhan du rung / /gang gis ma spangs zhes ni bdag gi yid la re/ /gal te bdag ni jo bo'i gzigs byed yangs pa'i zhal/ /gtsang zhing bzhad pa gyen du blta ba'i skal med na/ /skal ba dman par 'os min sgra gcan 'dzin de yang / /pha yi pang na
<p>31a.3</p>yongs su gnas par nam zhig 'gyur/ /e ma yid mnga' 'di yi lus ni shin tu gzhon/ /yid ni mi rnams kyis bsngags shin tu sra ba ste/ /ngag gi skad grag rab zos dgra yang dga' ba yi/ /bu ni byis pa 'di 'dra kye ma spong bar byed/ /bdag gi 'dod pa'i sems kyang shin tu sra ba
<p>31a.4</p>ste/ /rdo las gyur ram yang na lcags las byas pa'am/ /bder 'os jo bo dpal dor nags su song ba la/ /mgon med ldan pa gang zhig dum bur ma song ngo / /de lhar lha mo bdag po'i mya ngan gyis brgyal te/ sems shing rnam zlos lan cig ma yin 'di dus la/ /rang bzhin brtan yang dam
<p>31a.5</p>ba mo de mya ngan gyis/ /brtan pa dran pa ma yin ngo tsha ma byas so/ /de nas de ltar mya ngan gyis smra rnam 'khrugs pa'i/ /grags 'dzin ma ni sa la 'gyel ba mthong nas ni/ /char gyis btang bas pad+ma chen po bzhin du ni/ /mchi bcas gdong gis bud med rnams ni cho nges 'debs/ /bzlas brjod
<p>31a.6</p>rdzogs shing sbyin sreg bkra shis byas gyur te/ /mi skyong nyid kyang lta gang dag nas phyir gshegs pa/ /rdo rje'i sgra yis glang po ji bzhin skye ba yi/ /nyam thag sgra des kun nas bcom zhing g.yos par gyur/ /'dun pa dang ni bsngags ldan gnyis po mthong nas kyang / /sras kyi nges par brten pa
<p>31a.7</p>yang dag gsan nas ni/ /bde sogs bdag po'i ltad mo zin pa'i rgyal mtshan bzhin/ /mya ngan gyis bcom sa yi bdag po 'gyel bar gyur/ /de nas sras po'i mya ngan gyis rmongs yud tsam zhig/ /skye bo mtshungs mnyam mngon pa'i skye bos bzung gyur la/ /chab kyis gang ba'i spyan gyis mgyogs
<p>31b</p>
<p>31b.1</p>bgro la gzigs nas/ /sa yi logs nas sa skyong gis ni sme sngags bton/ /g.yul 'gyed pa na dga' chen mang po byas nas ni/ /bsngags ldan khyod kyis bdag gi dga' ba ma yin byas/ /bdag gi dga' ba yon tan dga' de gang gis ni/ /dga' ba yin yang dga' ba med bzhin nags
<p>31b.2</p>su bor/ /de phyir de nyid gang du gshegs pa der bdag khyer/ /yang na de ni slar yang skyen par khyer la shog /tshabs cher na ba'i sman dang bral bas de bzhin du/ /de dang bral bas bdag gi 'tsho ba med pa'o/ /rgyal bu gser 'bab 'chi bas phrogs par gyur pa na/ /dka' thub gang
<p>31b.3</p>las yang dag rgyal ba shi ma gyur/ /bdag kyang chos 'dzin sras po gshegs par gyur pa na/ /bdag nyid thar 'dod bdag nyid med pa lta bur gyur/ /rgyal rigs bcu byas khyab bdag skye dgu'i bdag bo ni/ /mchog dang mchog min shes pa nyi ma'i sras po yi/ /bu ni phangs shing sdug bsngal dam
<p>31b.4</p>pa dang bral la/ /yid mi bde byas yid kyi rmongs pa gang las min/ /rgyal bo a dza'i sras po blo dang ldan pa ni/ /mi bdag dbang po'i grogs la bdag gi 'dod pa ste/ /sras po nags su song la gang zhig lhar song la/ /mchi ma don yod ma yin bkren pas 'chos so kye/ /
<p>31b.5</p>khyod kyis bdag gi chu yi snyim pa de gang du/ /phrogs pa'i dka' thub gnas der bzang po bdag la smros/ /de la bdag gi skom pa 'dis ni yongs 'dod de/ /bdag gi srog ni yi dgas 'gro bar 'dod/ /de ltar sras dang bral ba'i sdug bsngal skyes gyur te/ /sa dang 'dra ba'i
<p>31b.6</p>lhan skyes brtan pa rnam spangs nas/ /rA ma'i mya ngan dag gis shing rta bcu pa bzhin/ /mi skyong 'du shes bral bzhin mang po rnam par labs/ /de nas de la thos dang dul dang yon tan ldan/ /rab bgres mdun na 'don dang blon po blo gros kyis/ /mnyam par gzhag 'di ji lta ba bzhin
<p>31b.7</p>smas gyur te/ /yongs su gdung ba'i gdong min mya ngan med pa'ang min/ /mi mchog brtan pa mya ngan thong la brtan par gshegs/ /mya ngan bzhin du mchi ma 'don par 'os ma yin/ /me tog phreng ba rnying bzhin phun tshogs bor nas ni/ /sa na mi skyong mang po nags su shin tu song / /gzhan yang
<p>32a</p>
<p>32a.1</p>de yi dgongs pa nges pa 'di sngon tshe/ /drang srong dkar ming de yi tshig ni dran par mdzod/ /mtho ris su yang 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal srid la/ /skad cig kyang de gnas par bde bas nus ma yin/ /gal te yang de mi mchog 'bad pas byas pa ste/ /myur bar bka' lung stsol
<p>32a.2</p>mdzod ji snyed 'dir 'gro bgyi/ /sna tshogs rnams kyi khyed kyi sras po de yi ni/ /sna tshogs mang bo'i 'thab mo de rnyed der byed shog /de nas de gnyis la ni mi bdag gis bslabs la/ /de phyir nges par 'di nas khyed gnyis mngon par song / /bu la lhag par chags pa'i nags kyi bya yi bzhin/ /bdag
<p>32a.3</p>gi sems ni dga' bar rab tu song ma yin/ /dam pa zhes ni mi dbang bstan las blon po dang / /mdun na 'don pa de gnyis nags der song bar gyur/ /byas zhes gna' ma'i skye bo dang bcas btsun mor bcas/ /mi skyong gis kyang bya ba lhag ma rab tu mdzad/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya
<p>32a.4</p>ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ btsun mo'i 'khor smre sngags bton pa'i le'u ste brgyad pa'o// //de nas de'i tshe mdun na 'don dang blon po de/ /mi skyong mchi ma'i lcag gis mngon par bsnun pa dag /phug pa'i dam pa'i rta bzhin 'bad pa thams cad las/ /
<p>32a.5</p>bsam pa bzang pos skyen par nags der song bar gyur/ /'dra ba'i rjes 'brangs ngal ba skyes pa de gnyis ni/ /dka' thub nags der dus su nye bar phyin nas ni/ /rgyal po'i rdzu 'phrul dor de dul ba'i spyod pa yis/ /drang srong shes ldan bu yi khang par nye bar song / /de dag gis ni tshul
<p>32a.6</p>bzhin bram ze de mchod nas/ /de ni de dag la yang rjes mthun mchod pa ste/ /gdan byas pa dag bdag tu lta ba bcad nas ni/ /shes ldan sras po gdan gnas pa la gtam smras so/ /mdangs gtsang gtsang zhing rnam par grags pa'i yangs pa mnga'/ /bu ram
<p>32a.7</p>shing pa'i rigs su rab 'khrungs rgyal po yis/ /shru ka rab tu 'dzin dang gsang sngags yongs 'dzin la/ /nag por skye bo 'di ni khyod kyis rig par mdzod/ /dbang po dang mtshungs de yi rgyal ba dang mtshungs sras/ /rga dang 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa dag ni sgrol 'dod de/ /
<p>32b</p>
<p>32b.1</p>'di na mngon par nye bar 'ongs grag de yi phyir/ /bdag cag nye bar 'ongs par bcom ldan mkhyen par mdzod/ /de dag la des smras pa phyag ring gyur pa de/ /rab tu thob gyur gzhon nu shes pa min pa min/ /chos 'di 'khor bar byed ces mngon par mkhyen nas ni/ /
<p>32b.2</p>mngon par gdong phyogs ma yin thar bzhed skyen par gshegs/ /de nas de las de nyid de dag nyer thob nas/ /bram ze de la snyan dngags phab nas de ma thag /dub kyang ma dub pa bzhin rgyal po la gus pas/ /de nyid gang nas gshegs pa de nas rab tu song / /song ste de nas de dag
<p>32b.3</p>gi ni rngon pa dang / /rnam par bral ba'i sku lus rab tu 'bar ba de/ /nyi ma sdug po'i longs spyod dag la zhugs pa ltar/ /lam ni shing gi rtsa bar nye bar bzhugs pa mthong / /de nas de la mdun na 'don dang sngags 'dzin bcas/ /theg pa rnam par spangs nas nye bar gshegs pa ste/ /
<p>32b.4</p>slar gnas thub pa'i bu ni g.yon gyi lhar bcas pas/ /nags gnas lhag spyod lta bar 'dod pa ji ltar ro/ /lha na pa ba sangs dang phur bus dbang chen bzhin/ /de dag gis ni de nyid bskyed cing mchod pa'o/ /lha na pa sangs phur bu dag la dbang chen bzhin/ /mchod 'os des ni de gnyis
<p>32b.5</p>dag la slar mchod do/ /sbyor bar song ba'i zla ba nye sar nab so bzhin/ /de nas kun nas mngon par rjes gnang byas pa ni/ /de dag shA kya'i rigs kyi rgyal mtshan de yi ni/ /nye logs dag tu song ba rnam par mdzes par gyur/ /shing gi rtsa bar gnas pa mngon par 'bar ba yi/ /rgyal po'i
<p>32b.6</p>sras po de la mdun na 'don gyis smras/ /lha na yongs 'dus dag la brgya byin sras po ni/ /rgyal ba nye bar gnas la phur bu ji ltar ro/ /khyod kyi mya ngan zug rngu snying la btags pa na/ /sa yi logs la rmongs shing brgyal bar gyur pa ste/ /gzhon nu mig gi chu yi char ltar rgyal po yis/ /
<p>32b.7</p>gang zhig khyod la smras pa 'di ni mkhyen par mdzod/ /khyod kyis chos la rab dmigs nges par shes pa ste/ /khyod kyi 'byung bar 'gyur pa'i don ni shes pa'o/ /khyod kyi dus ma yin par nags su bsnyen las bdag /me dang rab mtshungs mya ngan me yis tshig pa'o/ /de phyir tshur
<p>33a</p>
<p>33a.1</p>spyon chos dga' dag gi dga' ston du/ /chos kyi don du blo gros de nyid thong mdzod dang / /chu bo'i shugs kyis 'gram ngogs mngon par bcom pa bzhin/ /bdag la mya ngan shugs 'dir rab tu 'phel ba'o/ /rlung dang nyi ma me dang thog chen rnams kyi ni/ /'jug
<p>33a.2</p>pa gang zhig sprin dang chu me ri rnams su/ /rnam par 'byer dang skems dang srog dang 'byed rnams kyis/ /bdag cag rnams la mya ngan gyis 'jug pa de byed/ /de phyir re zhig nor 'dzin bdag nyid longs spyod la/ /dus su bstan bcos mthong ste nags su gshegs gyur te/ /'byung po
<p>33a.3</p>thams cad la ni brtse ba chos yin phyir/ /mi 'dod gnyen 'dun kho bo la ni ltos par mdzod/ /chos de nags nyid kho nar 'grub pa ma yin te/ /sdom brtson rnams kyis nges par grong khyer na yang 'grub/ /'dir ni blo dang 'bad pa dag ni mtshan ma ste/ /nags dang stag ni 'jigs pa dag gi
<p>33a.4</p>mtshan ma'o/ /dbu rgyan 'dzin zhing dpung par rna cha do shal dang / /dpung rgyan rnam par rengs pa'i phyag mnga' mi dbang rnams/ /phun tshogs yan lag dbus na yongs su gnas rnams kyis/ /khyim na gnas kyang thar ba'i lam ni rab tu thob/ /bstan pa'i nu bo
<p>33a.5</p>stobs dang rdo rje'i lag pa dang / /rnam mdzes bu dang chu stod de nas mthar gnas lha/ /lus 'phags rgyal po skyes byed dang ni de bzhin du/ /grong dang ljon shing can dang sde rgyal rgyal po rnams/ /nyes legs chos kyi cho ga la ni rnam dul ba'i/ /mi bdag khyim na gnas pa de rnams
<p>33a.6</p>mkhyen mdzod la/ /nor gyi bdag po dang ni mi skyong dpal dag ste/ /gnyis po dag kyang de phyir dus gcig mkhyen par mdzod/ /mngon par dbang bskur byas pa'i chu yis brlan pa nyid/ /gdung ba skyob pa'i gdugs bzung khyed la drag tu ni/ /nye bar 'khyud nas kun nas gyen du lta ba ste/ /dga'
<p>33a.7</p>ba des ni nags su rab tu 'jug par 'dod/ /de ltar mchi mas 'dud pa'i yi ge'i tshig gis ni/ /khyed nyid la ni sa yi bdag pos smras pa ste/ /thos nas de la brtse zhing de la dga' don du/ /khyed kyi brtse bas rjes su 'gro bar 'os pa'o/ /khyod las byung ba'i mya ngan chu ni gting med pa'i/ / 
<p>33b</p>
<p>33b.1</p>sdug bsngal rgya mtshor shAkya'i rgyal po nub gyur te/ /de phyir mgon po rgya mtshor bying la gru bzhin du/ /dman zhing rten dang bral ba de ni sgrol mdzod cig /chu bo gang gA'i lto nas byung ba 'jigs byed dang / /lhag spyod dang ni ngan spong sras po lhag spyod kyis/ /pha yi dga' ba'i don du
<p>33b.2</p>las byas thos nas ni/ /khyed kyang yab kyi bzhed pa mdzad par 'os pa lags/ /gnyen bshes be'u nyams par gyur pa'i ba bzhin du/ /rgyun mi 'chad par nyam thag snying rjer ngu ba mo/ /drang srong ri byi bsnyen zhing phyogs su ma song ba/ /yang dag skyed par byed pa'i lha mo mkhyen par mdzod/ /
<p>33b.3</p>ngang pa rnam par bral ba'i ngang mo lta bu dang / /nags na glang po dang bral glang mo lta bu ni/ /mgon dang bcas kyang mgon med dman zhing nyam thag pa'o/ /btsun mo gzigs pa yis ni skyob par 'os pa yin/ /sras gcig byis pa sdug bsngal 'os pa ma yin pa/ /kun nas gdung
<p>33b.4</p>ba mthar gyur pa ni 'dren pa ste/ /gang ba'i zla ba sgra gcan nye bar bsgyur las bzhin/ /sgra gcan 'dzin de gnyen gyi mya ngan las thar mdzod/ /pho brang btsun mo'i 'khor dang grong khyer mtha' dag ni/ /khyed dang bral ba'i bud shing can gyi mya ngan me/ /phyir 'byung dbugs ni du ba mun pa'i
<p>33b.5</p>rtse mo yis/ /tshig pa dag ni khyed la lta ba'i chu 'dod do/ /mdun na 'don pa de yi tshig dag gsan gyur nas/ /byang chub sems dpa' yongs su gang ba'i sems dpa' des/ /yon tan ldan zhing yon tan shes pas yud tsam zhig /bsam gtan mdzad nas rigs pa'i lan 'di
<p>33b.6</p>smras pa'o/ /pha rnams kyi ni bu la dgongs pa shes pa ste/ /gang zhig bdag la sa skyong gi ni khyad par du/ /shes pa yin yang na dang rga dang rgud pa las/ /'jigs te nags su phyin nas rang gi skye bo dor/ /mthar ni gal te dga' ba dang bral ma yin na/ /rang gi skye bo dga' ba lta 'dod cis
<p>33b.7</p>ma yin/ /gang tshe yun ring gyur kyang rnam par 'bral ba ste/ /de phyir bla ma brtse ba yin yang 'dor bar bgyi/ /gang yang bdag gi ched du mi yi bdag po yi/ /mya ngan khyod kyis smras des bdag la dga' ba med/ /gang phyir rmi lam yang dag 'dus par gyur rnams su/ /rnam par 'bral
<p>34a</p>
<p>34a.1</p>bar 'gyur la kun nas gdung bar byed/ /'gro ba'i spyod pa rnam pa sna tshogs mthong nas ni/ /de bzhin du yang khyod kyi blo gros nges par song / /bu min gnyen min kun nas gdung ba'i rgyu yin bzhin/ /'ching ba de ni shes pa med pa'i mtshan ma nyid/ /lam du 'gro rnams 'dir ni
<p>34a.2</p>'dus pa ji lta ba'i/ /skye dgu rnams ni dus su nges par 'bral ba ste/ /gnyen 'dun dam 'cha' skye bos rnam par dman pa yi/ /shes rab ldan pa'i skye bos mya ngan bsnyen nam ci/ /gzhan du rang gi skye bo dor nas 'dir 'ongs la/ /'dir yang rab tu bslus nas slar yang 'gro ba ste/ /der song nas
<p>34a.3</p>kyang pha rol gzhan du 'gro 'gyur la/ /de ltar 'dor ldan skyo la rjes su brten nam ci/ /gang tshe mngal nas bzung ste gnas skabs thams cad du/ /gsod pa'i phyir ni 'chi ba rab tu gnas pa ste/ /bu la dga' ba der ni khyed kyis smras pa yi/ /bdag gi nags su brten pa gang phyir dus ma yin/ /
<p>34a.4</p>yul la mngon par lhung tshe dus ma yin pa de/ /de bzhin nor gyi cho gar zhugs pa dus yin no/ /dus rnams kun du dus kyi 'gro ba khyab pa ste/ /dge legs nges par thob pa dus yod ma yin no/ /gang yang rgyal pos bdag la rgyal srid 'dir bzhad la/ /de yang yab kyi rgya
<p>34a.5</p>chen mtshungs shing 'dra ba ste/ /sred pa las ni nad pa'i mi 'phrod zas bzhin du/ /bdag gis rab tu 'dzin par nus pa ma yin no/ /gti mug rmongs pa'i gzhi ma mi skyong rgyal po nyid/ /rab tu 'thob par mi ni mkhas pas gang phyir nus/ /gang du skyo ba dang bcas rgyags dang
<p>34a.6</p>ngal dub dang / /pha rol log par spyod pas ches la gnod pa'o/ /'dzam bu chu gser bzhin du gsal ba'i lding khang ni/ /dug dang 'dres pa'i kha zas bzang po lta bu dang / /gza' yis 'khrugs pa'i pad+ma dang bcas chu lta bu/ /rgyal srid dang ni gser dag sdug bsngal dag gi
<p>34a.7</p>rten/ /de ltar rgyal srid chos min bde ba ma yin pa/ /ji ltar mi gtsang skyes te mi dbang snga ma rnams/ /sdug bsngal yongs su spang bya na tshod rab mchog tshe/ /rgyal srid nges par dor nas nags su song bar gyur/ /rin chen bzhin du tshim ba mchog ni nyer mkhyud nas/ /'brog
<p>34b</p>
<p>34b.1</p>dgon dag na rtswa dag zos pa mchog yin la/ /sbrul nag bzhin du mthong ba ma yin nyes pa ni/ /rnyed bla'i dpal dang lhan cig nyal ba mchog ma yin/ /rgyal srid rnam par spangs pa rgyal po rnams kyi chos/ /mngon par 'dod pas nags su rab 'jug bsngags pa ste/ /nags
<p>34b.2</p>tshal yongs su dor nas khyim du rab 'jug pa/ /dam bca' nye bar bcom pa'i 'thad pa ma yin no/ /rigs su skyes shing sems pa dang bcas mi gang gis/ /chos ni mngon par 'dod pas nags su rab zhugs la/ /ngur smrig rab tu dor nas ngo tsha rnam spangs nas/ /grong khyer 'joms pa yi
<p>34b.3</p>yang grong la bsnyen ma yin/ /sred dang rnam par rmongs dang yang na 'jigs pa yis/ /gang zhig skyugs pa'i bza' ba slar yang len byed la/ /sred pa de ni rmongs dang yang na 'jigs pa yis/ /'dod pa rnams ni dor nas slar yang len par byed/ /gang zhig rab 'bar khang pa dag nas ci zhig
<p>34b.4</p>ltar/ /byung nas slar yang de nyid kho nar rab 'jug la/ /nyes pa mthong de khyim na gnas pa dor nas ni/ /rmongs pas slar yang len par mngon par 'dod pa'o/ /gang yang mi skyong khyim na gnas pas thar pa ni/ /'thob pa dang ldan zhes thos de ni med pa ste/ /zhi ba gtso bo'i thar pa'i chos ni gang la yang / /
<p>34b.5</p>chad pa gtso bo'i rgyal po'i chos ni gang du'o/ /zhi ba dga' ba gal te rgyal srid dman pa ste/ /rgyal srid la blo gal te zhi ba rnam par nyams/ /grang dang dro dang me dang chu yi gcig nyid bzhin/ /zhi ba dang ni rno nyid 'thad pa ma yin no/ /me dang chu yi 'du ba yod pa ma yin la/ /khram dang drang
<p>34b.6</p>po'i 'du ba yod pa ma yin zhing / /'phags dang sdig pa'i 'du ba yod pa ma yin te/ /zhi dang chad pa'i 'du ba yod pa ma yin no/ /de phyir sa 'dzin bdag po de rnams nges pas sam/ /rgyal po'i srid rnams spangs te zhi ba thob pa can/ /rgyal srid dag la bsnyen nam dbang po sbas nyid las/ /
<p>34b.7</p>mthar ma thug par thar par mngon pa'i nga rgyal byas/ /de dag rnams kyi rgyal srid la zhi ji lta bzhin/ /bdag ni nags tshal rab thob nges pas ma yin zhing / /khyim dang gnyen gyi 'du shes zhags pa bcad nas ni/ /thar gyur slar yang rab tu 'jug par 'dod ma yin/ /de ltar bdag
<p>35a</p>
<p>35a.1</p>nyid rnam shes yon tan rjes mthun pa/ /re 'dod spangs shing gtan tshigs ldan pa sgrogs pa ste/ /mi dbang bdag nyid skyes kyi smra ldan thos gyur nas/ /gsang sngags 'dzin pa yis kyang lan ni smras pa'o/ /gang zhig chos kyi cho gar nges pa khyod kyi 'di/ /
<p>35a.2</p>rig pa min pa ma yin 'di ni dus rig min/ /na tshod la gnas yab ma mya ngan phyir byin nas/ /chos 'dod khyod kyi chos ma yin par gyur pa'o/ /nges par khyed kyi blo yang shin tu phra min pa/ /yang na chos dang don dang 'dod par mkhas ma min/ /gang zhig ma mthong 'bras bu'i don du khyed nyid
<p>35a.3</p>kyis/ /mngon sum don ni yongs su brnyas par mdzad nas gshegs/ /yang srid yod ces kha cig dag ni smra ba ste/ /med ces kha cig dag ni nges par dam 'cha'o/ /de ltar gang tshe don 'di the tshom gyur pa ste/ /de phyir longs spyod par nus dpal ni nye bar gnas/ /gal te
<p>35a.4</p>slar yang rab tu 'jug pa gang yang yod/ /der ni ji ltar 'bad pa dag la dga' bar bgyi/ /ci ste gzhan du rab tu 'jug pa gang yang med/ /'gro ba 'di yi 'bad rtsol med las thar pa 'grub/ /kha cig 'jig rten pha rol yod ces smra ba ste/ /thar pa'i sbyor ba la ni bsngags pa byed
<p>35a.5</p>ma yin/ /ji ltar me yi dro dang chu yi gsher ba nyid/ /de ltar rab tu 'jug par rang bzhin nyid du smra/ /dge dang mi dge nyid dang srid dang srid min la/ /kha cig rang bzhin las zhes bsngags pa byed pa ste/ /gang phyir 'di dag thams cad rang bzhin las yin te/ /de yi phyir
<p>35a.6</p>yang rab tu 'bad pa don med 'gyur/ /gang zhig dbang po rnams kyis nges par rab spyod pa/ /yul rnams la ni dga' ba dang ni mi dga' nyid/ /gang zhig dga' dang nad rnams dag gis sbyor byed de/ /de la gang gis 'bad dam de ni rang bzhin no/ /chu rnams kyis ni me rnams
<p>35a.7</p>zhi bar nye 'gro zhing / /'od zer rnams kyis chu ni skams par byed pa ste/ /lus la yang dag gnas pa'i 'byung ba tha dad rnams/ /gcig nyid gyur nas 'gro ba dag ni 'dren par byed/ /gang zhig lag pa rkang pa lto rgyab mgo rnams kyis/ /mngal du song ba'i ngo bo nges par sgrub byed la/ /
<p>35b</p>
<p>35b.1</p>gang tshe bdag nyid de yi de yis sbyor ba ste/ /rang bzhin las byung de shes rnams kyis de smra'o/ /bya dang ri dgas rnams kyi sna tshogs ngo bo dang / /tsher ma'i rnon po nyid du rab tu byed pa su/ /rab tu 'jug pa 'di kun rang bzhin las yin la/ /'dod pa byed pa yod min 'bad pa gang las
<p>35b.2</p>so/ /de bzhin gzhan rnams dbang phyug las skyes smra ba ste/ /der ni skyes bu'i rab tu 'jug pa la don ci/ /'gro ba'i rab tu 'jug la gang nyid rgyu yin zhing / /ldog pa la ni nges par de nyid rgyu yin no/ /kha cig bdag gi mtshan ma nyid du smra ba ste/ /rab tu skye ba nyid dang srid pa zad
<p>35b.3</p>pa yang / /'bad pa med las rab tu skye bar smra ba ste/ /'bad pa yis ni thar pa 'thob par smra ba'o/ /lha yi mchod sbyin drang srong rnams kyi rig byed dang / /pha yi bu lon med pa bu rnams kyis te mi/ /gang gi grol ba yod pa de yi thar pa zhes/ /bu lon gsum po de dang lhan cig skyes
<p>35b.4</p>pa'o/ /de ltar cho ga'i bya ba'i rim pa 'di yis ni/ /'bad rtsol bcas pa'i thar pa de shes rnam smra la/ /'bad rtsol ldan pa yin yang rnam par gnon pa yis/ /thar pa 'dod pa rnams ni ngal ba thob par byed/ /de phyir zhi ba gal te thar la gus yod na/ /cho gar brjod pa ji ltar
<p>35b.5</p>rigs pas bsnyen mdzod dang / /'di yi nye bar 'thad pa de ltar gyur pa ste/ /mi yi bdag po'i kun nas gdung ba nyams par 'gyur/ /dka' thub nags tshal dag nas khang par 'jug pa la/ /khyod kyi skyon gyi blo gros gang zhig rab zhugs te/ /yab gcig der yang khyod kyi bsam par ma gyur
<p>35b.6</p>dang / /snga ma rnams kyang nags nas rang gi khang par gshegs/ /dka' thub nags na gnas pa bu rnams kyis bskor te/ /rgyal po a ma ri Sha grong du zhugs gyur la/ /de bzhin 'phags min rnams kyis sa ni rnam bcom pa/ /dka' thub nags nas 'ongs nas rangs byed kyis gsungs
<p>35b.7</p>so/ /de bzhin rdo ba dang bcas bdag po'i ljon shing ming / /nags gnas bu dang bcas pa grong du bzhugs pa ste/ /tshangs pa'i drang srong gyur dang thub pa gnas 'jog las/ /sbyin sreg dang bcas mtha' can lha yis dpal bzung ngo / /rnam pa de ltar chos dang grags par rab bzhugs pa/ /
<p>36a</p>
<p>36a.1</p>nags rnams bor nas khang khyim rnams su song ba ste/ /de phyir dka' thub nags nas chos kyi ched du nyid/ /khyim na rab tu 'gro ba skyon yod ma yin no/ /de nas mi skyong rgyal po'i dga' dang phan pa nyid/ /byas pa'i blon po de yi tshig dag gsan
<p>36a.2</p>nas ni/ /dman min ma 'khrugs chags min brtan dang gnas pa la/ /myur min tshig ni rgyal po sras kyis smras pa'o/ /'dir ni yod dang med ces the tshom gang de ni/ /gzhan gyi tshig gis bdag la 'di na nges pa med/ /dka' thub dang ni zhi bas de nyid rtogs gyur nas/ /
<p>36a.3</p>gang 'dir nges par bdag nyid kyis ni gzung bar bgyi/ /phan tshun gnod cing mi gsal the tshom skye ba yi/ /lta ba dag ni len par bdag gis nus ma yin/ /mun par long bas long ba'i lam mkhan byed pa bzhin/ /mkhas pa'i skye bo su zhig gzhan gyi rkyen gyis 'gro/ /de nyid
<p>36a.4</p>ma mthong gyur kyang 'on kyang kho bo yi/ /dge dang mi dger the tshom na dge blo gros gyur/ /'bras bu med phyir la yang dge ba'i bdag nyid mchog /smod pa'i bdag nyid de nyid la yang bde ba med/ /rnam gzhag med pa'i lung 'di yang ni mthong gyur
<p>36a.5</p>nas/ /tshad ldan rnams kyis gang smras de ni legs rtogs mdzod/ /nyes la rab dman tshad ldan nyid ni rtogs mdzod dang / /nyes pa rab tu dman pas bden min smra ba yin/ /khyim la 'jug par dmigs gang bdag la khyod kyis ni/ /smras shing rangs byed la sogs rnams ni dpe
<p>36a.6</p>bstan te/ /de rnams tshad min chos des rnams su nus med cing / /tshad ma'i ched du brtul zhugs rnams ni yongs su zad/ /de lta na yang nyi ma sa la lhung gyur la/ /gangs dang ldan pa'i ri bos brtan nyid 'dor na yang / /de nyid ma mthong yul la kha bltas dbang po ni/ /khyim rnams
<p>36a.7</p>dag la so so skye bo mi bsnyen to/ /bdag ni 'bar bar gyur pa'i me la 'jug pa ste/ /don ma byas par khyim gyi gzhi la rab mi 'jug /de ltar thugs rgyal ldan des dam bca' mdzad gyur cing / /ji ltar 'dod bzhin bzhengs nas ngar 'dzin med par gshegs/ /de nas mchi ma dang bcas blon
<p>36b</p>
<p>36b.1</p>dang gnyis skyes gnyis/ /de yi bstan pa nyid dang nges pa thos gyur nas/ /gti mug bzhin ldan rjes su song nas sdug bsngal ba/ /dal bus song nas grong khyer nyid du song bar gyur/ /de nas de la brtse dang mi skyong la gus las/ /de dag ltos byas rab tu song zhing gnas gyur
<p>36b.2</p>la/ /gsal zhing snang bas nyi ma blta bar dka' ba ltar/ /de ni lam du lta bar ma nus 'dor bar min/ /mchog tu gshegs te gshegs pa shes phyir de dag gis/ /so pa'i skyes bu gtsang ma sbas pa rnams byas nas/ /dga' zhing sras po 'dod pa'i rgyal po la song nas/ /ji
<p>36b.3</p>ltar blta'am zhes ni ji ltar yang song ngo / /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ gzhon nu rjes su tshol ba'i le'u ste dgu pa'o// //sku stod rgyas shing rgya chen rgyal po'i sras po ste/ /bsreg bya dang bsngags bdag po de dag rnams spangs te/ /dba'
<p>36b.4</p>rlabs g.yo ba'i chu bo gang gA rgal nas ni/ /dpal dang ldan pa'i rgyal po'i khab tu gshegs par gyur/ /ri rnams dag gis legs par sbas dang brgyan pa dang / /dge dang dka' thub gter bas gzung dang gtsang ba ste/ /zhi ba rang byung tshangs pa mtho ris logs su bzhin/ /ri
<p>36b.5</p>lngas mtshan pa'i grong khyer rab tu thob par gyur/ /zab mor gyur pa'i mdangs dar de yi lugs gsal ba/ /skyes bu rnams ni shin tu gnon pa mthong gyur nas/ /khyu mchog rgyal mtshan de yi brtul zhugs brtan pa bzhin/ /der ni de tshe skye bo rnams ni ya mtshan gyur/ /de rab
<p>36b.6</p>mthong nas gzhan gang ma song de gnas shing / /der ni gang zhig lam na gnas de rjes 'gro zhing / /gang zhig skyen por song ste brtan por song gyur la/ /kha cig bsdad pa gang yin de ni langs pa'o/ /skye bo kha cig de la mchod pa'i lag pa yis/ /bsti stang byas nas kha cig
<p>36b.7</p>mgo bos phyag 'tshal zhing / /kha cig gnyen po'i tshig gis mngon par stod byed cing / /kha cig de la rab tu mchod nas song bar gyur/ /de rab mthong nas sna tshogs cha lugs rnams ngo tsha/ /rab bkram tshig ni lam du smra ba med par song / /dngos su gzhan du chos rnams
<p>37a</p>
<p>37a.1</p>dag gi nye logs su/ /kha cig tshul ma yin pa'i blo gros ma gyur to/ /lha dang mtshungs pa'i mi dbang sras po de mthong nas/ /bya ba gzhan ma rnams kyang rgyal po'i lam du ni/ /mchod mang bkur sti sngon 'gro bud med rnams kyi 'am/ /skyes pa rnams kyis mig
<p>37a.2</p>dang ngoms par ma gyur to/ /dpral ba 'am smin ma dag dang zhal lam spyan dag dang / /sku 'am phyag dag dang ni 'gros sam zhabs dag ni/ /gang gis de yi gang nyid der ni mthong gyur pa/ /de nyid kyis ni de yi mig dag bcings par gyur/ /smin ma mdzod spu dang bcas spyan dag
<p>37a.3</p>yangs pa dang / /sku lus mdzes shing dge ba'i dra ba dang ldan phyag /sa skyong nyid du 'os pa'i dge slong cha lugs de/ /mthong nas rgyal po'i khab kyi phun tshogs g.yos par gyur/ /de nas khang pa'i phyi nas rnam rgyas skye bo'i tshogs/ /ma ga d+hA yi khyim gyi ngo bo bzo sbyangs kyis/ /
<p>37a.4</p>mthong bar gyur te de yi rgyu mtshan dris pa ste/ /de nas 'di la skyes bu rnams kyis de smras so/ /ye shes mchog gam yang na sa yi dpal dag ni/ /'thob par 'gyur zhes bram ze rnams kyis gang smras pa/ /rab tu gshegs par skye bos nges par mthong ba yi/ /shAkya'i bdag po'i sras po de ni
<p>37a.5</p>'di yin no/ /de nas don thos yid kyis chags shing zhen gyur pa'i/ /rgyal po yis ni skyes bu de nyid la smras pa/ /de ni gang du song zhes rnam par shes par mdzod/ /de nas de ltar bgyi zhes skyes bu rjes su song / /g.yo mi spyan ni gnya' shing gang tsam gzigs pa ste/ /gsung ni kun nas snyoms
<p>37a.6</p>shing zab mo'i 'gros mnga' ba/ /g.yo ba'i sems dang lus rnams dag ni nges bsdams nas/ /dge slong mchog nyid de yang bsod snyoms la gshegs so/ /ji ltar nye bar 'thad pa'i bsod snyoms bsnams nas ni/ /rnam par dben zhing char rab 'bab par rab gshegs la/ /der ni
<p>37a.7</p>tshul bzhin rigs pas mngon par gsol gyur nas/ /de ni sa 'dzin ri bo skya bseng la 'dzegs so/ /ro d+ha'i nags kyis nye bar sbas pa'i ri bo der/ /rma bya'i skad kyis rab gang lo ma'i spyil bo na/ /'char ri'i steng na nyi ma gzhon nu ji lta bar/ /ngur smrig gos kyis nyi ma'i nyi ma de mdzes
<p>37b</p>
<p>37b.1</p>so/ /der ni de nyid rgyal po'i 'khor de mthong gyur nas/ /bzo sbyangs rgyal po la ni gtam dag byas pa ste/ /thos nas rgyal po des kyang mchod pa mang po las/ /der ni sbas pa'i rjes su 'brang bas rab tu song / /skya bseng ri bo mchog la skya bseng na dang ni/ /brtson 'grus mnyam
<p>37b.2</p>zhing ri bo dang mnyam sku lus can/ /mi yi seng ge'i 'gros can cod pan 'dzin pa ste/ /ral pa g.yo ba'i seng ge bzhin du 'dzegs par gyur/ /de nas de yi steng na rtse mor gyur pa yi/ /byang chub sems dpa' dbang po nye bar zhi ba ni/ /ri bong gis mtshan sprin gyi sbubs nas byung ba bzhin/ /
<p>37b.3</p>skyil mo krung gis bzhugs nas rnam par mdzes pa mthong / /gzugs dang phun sum tshogs dang nye bar zhi ba yi/ /chos kyi sprul pa bzhin du nye bar bzhugs de la/ /ya mtshan dang bcas rab tu bsnyen ldan mi dbang po/ /rang byung la ni brgya byin gyis bzhin nye bar gnas/ /rigs pa
<p>37b.4</p>yis ni rigs pa rig pa rnams kyi mchog /khams mnyam gyur pa de la song nas dris pa ste/ /de nyid kyis kyang mtshungs shing zhi bas mi skyong la/ /yid ni rang bzhin gnas dang nad med smras par gyur/ /de nas gtsang la glang po'i rna ba ltar sngo ba'i/ /rdo ba'i logs la rgyal po yang
<p>37b.5</p>dag nges gnas shing / /nye sar nye bar bsdad nas rjes su mthun pa yis/ /de yi dgongs pa rnam par shes 'dod 'di smras so/ /rim pas 'ongs pa nyid dang yongs su brtags pa ste/ /khyod kyi rigs kyis bdag gi dga' ba mchog yin la/ /gang phyir bdag la rang gi na tshod smra
<p>37b.6</p>'dod pa/ /skyes te de phyir brtse ba'i tshig 'di mkhyen par mdzod/ /khyod kyi rigs ni rnam rgyas sngon du nyi ma ste/ /lus kyang na tshod gsar pa gsal la mdzes pa 'di/ /gang phyir 'di ni khyod kyi blo gros rim med pas/ /slong mo nyid la mngon dga' rgyal srid la ma yin/ /khyod kyi
<p>37b.7</p>lus 'di tsan+dan dmar po 'os pa ste/ /ngur smrig gis dkris de ni 'os pa ma yin no/ /lag pa 'di ni skye dgu skyong bar 'os pa ste/ /gzhan gyis byin pa'i bza' ba za bar 'os ma yin/ /de phyir zhi ba gal te yab kyi rgyal srid la/ /khyod kyi yab kyi brtse las stobs kyis mi 'dod cing / /
<p>38a</p>
<p>38a.1</p>khyod kyi blo gros rim par bzod par ma gyur na/ /skyen par kho bo'i yul gyi phyed la longs spyod mdzod/ /de lta na ni rang gi skye la gnod min zhing / /dus kyi rim pa yis kyang dpal gang bsngags pa ste/ /de phyir khyod kyis bdag la brtse ba mdzod cig dang / /
<p>38a.2</p>dam pa rnams dang bcas pas dam pa'i dpal 'phel lo/ /ci ste da ni rigs kyis khengs pa nyid las ni/ /bdag cag rnams la khyod la blo gtad yon tan med/ /sde rgyas rnams ni mda' yis rnam par dkrugs byas nas/ /bdag dang bcas pas pha rol rnams ni pham par mdzod/ /
<p>38a.3</p>de phyir 'dir ni gnyis dbus gcig blo tshol mdzod la/ /chos don 'dod pa rnams la cho ga bzhin bsnyen mdzod/ /'di na sde tshan gsum po chags las rnam bzlog nas/ /'di dang gzhan du phyin nas lhung ba kun nas 'thob/ /gang zhig don dang chos la gnod nas 'dod pa dang / /chos dang 'dod pa
<p>38a.4</p>yongs su brnyas nas don dang ni/ /'dod dang don dag nye bar zhi bas chos de ni/ /don byas gal te mtha' dag 'dod na don yin no/ /de phyir sde tshan gsum la nges par bsnyen pa yis/ /khyod kyis gzugs 'di 'bras bu bcas pa nyid du mdzod/ /chos dang don dang 'dod pa dman min thob pa la/ /
<p>38a.5</p>mi rnams dag gis dman min skyes bu'i don du smra/ /de phyir gzhu ni rnam par 'gengs 'os rgyas pa'i phyag /'di dag 'bras bu med par byed par 'os min te/ /nga las nu bzhin 'dis ni 'jig rten gsum rnams kyang / /pham par 'os pa yin na sa 'dir smos ci dgos/ /brtse bas nges par de ni
<p>38a.6</p>bdag gis smra ba ste/ /ya mtshan gyis min dbang phyug nyid kyi chags pas min/ /khyod kyis dge slong nyid kyi cha lugs 'di mthong nas/ /rjes su brtse ba skyes nas mchi ma rang byung ngo / /de phyir rang rigs rab mtshungs khyod kyi gzugs ji srid/ /rga bas zil gyis mnan nas slar yang ma 'ongs par/ /
<p>38a.7</p>slong mo'i gnas 'dod 'dod pa rnams la longs spyod la/ /dus su chos la dga' ba chos ni gyis mdzod cig /'khogs pas nges par chos ni 'thob par nus pa ste/ /'dod pa nye bar spyod la rgas pa'i 'gro ba med/ /de phyir dar la bab pa'i 'dod pa rnams smra ste/ /bar ma'i nor yin rgan po rnams
<p>38b</p>
<p>38b.1</p>kyi chos yin no/ /gson pa'i 'jig rten dag na chos dang don dag ni/ /rnam par 'gal bar gyur pa yin phyir lang tsho rnams/ /yang dag srung ba yin yang thub par dka' ba ste/ /gang phyir 'dod pas lam de las ni 'phrog par byed/ /na tshod 'khogs pa rnams ni rnam spyod ldan pa ste/ /shin tu
<p>38b.2</p>brtan pa'i gnas skabs mchog tu song ba rnams/ /ngo tsha ba nyid phyir dang song ba ma yin phyir/ /'bad pa nyung ngus zhi ba'i bdag nyid gyur pa'o/ /de nyid phyir na g.yo zhing yul ni gtso bo dang / /rab myos bzod pa ma yin ring por mthong min la/ /'brog dgon dag la des par thar nas dbugs
<p>38b.3</p>phyung bzhin/ /g.yo sgyu mang bo'i lang tsho shin tu 'das nas so/ /de phyir mi brtan g.yo la bag med ldan pa yi/ /na tshod gsar pa 'di ni re zhig rnam par 'ong / /'dod pa'i lha yi sngon du na tshod dben yin la/ /dbang po rnams las bsrung bar nus pa ma yin no/ /ci ste khyod kyi chos nyid
<p>38b.4</p>mdzad par 'dod pa ni/ /mchod sbyin gyis lha mchod mdzod 'di ni rigs kyi chos/ /mchod sbyin rnams kyis mtho ris logs ni byin brlabs nas/ /lha dbang nyid kyang mtho ris logs su gshegs par 'gyur/ /gser gyi dpung rgyan rnam par bcings pa'i phyag rnams dang / /nor bu'i sgron mas 'bar
<p>38b.5</p>ba'i dpung rgyan sna tshogs can/ /mi skyod drang srong rnams dang drang srong chen po rnams/ /ngal bas gar gshegs 'gros der mchod sbyin rnams kyis gshegs/ /de ltar ma ga d+hA yi bdag pos tshig smras pa/ /gang zhig dbang po'i bzhin du smra ba yang dag mdzes/ /sna tshogs du ma'i sa
<p>38b.6</p>phyogs ti se'i gangs ri ltar/ /rgyal po'i sras des de thos gyur nas rnam ma g.yos/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ bzo sbyangs sngon du song ba'i le'u ste bcu pa'o// //de nas bshes kyi sgo nas phan pa min pa'i don/ /de ltar ma ga d+hA yi
<p>38b.7</p>bdag pos smas pa yis/ /rang gnas rnam par 'gyur min rigs gtsang gtsang pa po/ /zas gtsang rgyal po'i sras kyis tshig 'di smras pa'o/ /seng ges mtshan pa'i yangs pa'i rigs su rab skyes pa/ /khyed kyi cho ga de ni ngo mtshar che ma yin/ /gang phyir bshes gnyen phyogs su
<p>39a</p>
<p>39a.1</p>gshegs 'dod khyod kyi ni/ /yongs su dag pa'i spyod pas spyod pa de yin no/ /rang rigs rjes su spyod pas dam pa min la byams/ /dbang po ma tshang ba la dpal bzhin gnas min la/ /snga mas byas pa'i dga' ba rim rnams kyis/ /de ni dam pa rnams
<p>39a.2</p>kyis rnam par 'phel bar byed/ /don ni dka' ba rnams su mi rnams gang zhig gis/ /mdza' bo rnams kyis mnyam pa'i don gyur 'jig rten na/ /bshes gnyen de rnams blo yis yongs su shes bgyi ste/ /rang gnas dag ni 'phel bar gang gi phyir ma yin/ /de ltar gang gis rdzas dag thob nas
<p>39a.3</p>'jig rten na/ /bshes rnams dang ni chos la nges par sbyor byed pa/ /de rnams kyis ni nor gyi snying po thob pa ste/ /mthar ni nyams las gdung ba skyed par byed ma yin/ /rgyal po mdza' bo nyid dang 'phags pa nyid kyis kyang / /khyod kyi nges pa gang zhig bdag la dmigs pa 'di/ /
<p>39a.4</p>mdza' bo nyid kyis 'dir ni rjes su bsnyad bgyi ste/ /rgol ba gzhan min 'dir ni bdag gis smra bar bgyi/ /bdag gis rga dang 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa rnam rig nas/ /thar pa 'dod pas chos 'di rab tu thob pa ste/ /gnyen 'dun dga' ba mchi ma'i gdong ldan rnams spangs nas/ /mi dge'i rgyur
<p>39a.5</p>gyur 'dod pa rnams ni sngon nyid do/ /bdag ni yul rnams dag la ji ltar 'jigs pa nyid/ /de ltar sbrul gyi dug rnams la ni mi 'jigs shing / /nam mkha' dag las 'phos pa'i thog rnams las min la/ /rlung dang bcas pa'i me rnams dag las ma yin no/ /mi rtag 'dod pa rnams kyis
<p>39a.6</p>dge ba'i nor rku zhing / /stong pa rmi lam sgyu ma dang mtshungs 'jig rten na/ /yid la smos pa yis kyang rmongs par byed pa ste/ /mi yi sems ni bdag nyid gnas pa smos ci 'tshal/ /kye ma 'dod pas zil gyis non na mtho ris su/ /bde ba thob min 'chi ba'i 'jig rten na smos ci/ /rlung grogs
<p>39a.7</p>ldan pa'i me yis bud shing gis ji ltar/ /sred dang bcas pa'i 'dod pa rnams kyis tshim pa med/ /'gro na 'dod pa rnams dang mnyam pa'i don med med/ /rmongs las de rnams kho nar skye bo rab tu chags/ /de nyid shes nas de ltar don med 'jigs pa ste/ /shes ldan su zhig rang gis don
<p>39b</p>
<p>39b.1</p>med mngon par 'dod/ /rgya mtsho'i gos can sa ni kun nas thob nas kyang / /rgya mtsho chen po'i pha rol rgal bar 'dod pa ste/ /rgya mtsho'i chu bo rnams dang chu bran rnams kyis ltar/ /'jig rten pa yi 'dod pa rnams kyis ngoms pa med/ /lha yis gser gyi char pa dag kyang phab gyur la/ /
<p>39b.2</p>gling rnams bzhi po mtha' dag la yang longs spyad de/ /brgya byin gyi yang gdan phyed dag kyang rab thob nas/ /nga las nu ni yul rnams dag la ngoms pa med/ /lha na lha rnams kyi yang rgyal srid longs spyad nas/ /mchod sbyin brgya pa lha min 'jigs las rab nyams tshe/ /rgyags
<p>39b.3</p>las drang srong chen po rnams la'ang khur bcom nas/ /'dod pa rnams la ngoms med sgra med lhung bar 'gyur/ /e la'i rgyal pos mtho ris rnams ni rnam dkrugs te/ /brla mdzes lha mo de nyid dbang du blangs nas kyang / /sred phyir drang srong rnams las gser dag phrogs pa ste/ /yul
<p>39b.4</p>rnams la ni ngoms med nyams par song bar gyur/ /lha min las ni dbang chen dbang chen las dgra med/ /dgra med las slar dbang chen gang du nyer song ste/ /mtho ris dang ni sa 'am yul ni de rnams su/ /bskal ba'i tshogs 'khrugs rnams la su zhig blo gtad byed/ /shing shun gos can
<p>39b.5</p>rtsa ba 'bras bu chu za zhing / /lag 'gro'i sbrul ltar ring ba'i ral ba'i khur rnams kyang / /gang gis don gzhan ma yin thub pa yang nyams te/ /'dod pa zhes bya'i dgra bo rnams ni sa yis tshol/ /rno ba'i mtshon cha dang ni rno 'dzin mtshon cha yang / /gang gi don du 'jigs sde las ni 'chi thob la/ /
<p>39b.6</p>de dag rnams kyi dge min sems kyang spyod rnams kyis/ /'joms phyir de phyir brtul zhugs rnams kyis smos ci dgos/ /yul rnams su ni mya ngan nyung ngur shes gyur nas/ /kun nas sbyor zhing mchog tu ngoms pa med pa nyid/ /dam pa rnams kyis smod cing nges par sdig pa ste/ /'dod
<p>39b.7</p>pa'i mig can dug ni su yis len par byed/ /zhing gi las la sogs pa rnams kyis nyam thag cing / /'dod pa rnams la mi tshar rnams kyi rang gnas dang / /'dod pa'i bdag nyid rnams kyi rang gnas thob nas ni/ /'dod pa rnams ni spong bar sems ldan rnams kyis nus/ /grub 'gyur
<p>40a</p>
<p>40a.1</p>'dod pa rnams su rgyags pa nyer 'thob phyir/ /'dod pa can la 'dod 'byor rgud pa shes bya ste/ /rgyags las bya ba min byed bya ba ma yin la/ /gang gis zad cing ngan 'gror nye bar 'gro bar 'gyur/ /gang la 'bad pas thob cing yongs su bskyangs pa rnams/ /
<p>40a.2</p>rnam par bslus nas slar yang so sor 'gro ba ste/ /bdag nyid ldan pas g.yar po dang mtshungs de rnams su/ /'dod pa rnams la 'di na mkhas pa su zhig dga'/ /btsal nas dang ni blangs nas skom pa skyes pa yin/ /gang rnams mi 'dod sdug bsngal bar ni yongs 'gro la/ /'jig
<p>40a.3</p>rten dag na rtswa sgron dang mtshungs de rnams su/ /'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su mi dga' ba yin/ /dga' ldan min pa'i snying la gang gis rnam rmugs te/ /rnam par nyams par 'gro 'gyur bde bar 'gro min zhing / /kun nas khros pa'i sbrul dang rab mtshungs de rnams su/ /'dod pa
<p>40a.4</p>rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin/ /ltogs pas nyam thag khyi bzhin rus pa zos nas kyang / /gang rnams la ni ngoms par 'gyur ba ma yin nyid/ /'khogs pa'i nus pa'i keng rus dang mnyam de rnams su/ /'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin/ /
<p>40a.5</p>gang gi rgyal po rkun po chu dang me rnams las/ /thun mong gyur pa nyid phyir sdug bsngal sred byed de/ /rab tu gtor ba'i sha dang mtshungs pa de rnams su/ /'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin/ /dgra bo dang ni gnyen 'dun 'brel pa rnams las kyang / /gang la
<p>40a.6</p>gnas pa rnams ni skyen par rgud pa ste/ /skye mched dang mtshungs nye bar 'tshe ba de rnams su/ /'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin/ /ri dang nags dang chu dang rgya mtsho rnams su yang / /gang la rnam par 'phyo ba rnams ni lhung 'gyur te/ /ljon shing rtse mo'i 'bras bu dang
<p>40a.7</p>mtshungs de rnams su/ /'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin/ /rnam pa sna tshogs 'bad pa drag bo 'thob pa rnams/ /gang gis skad cig gis 'dir nyams par 'gyur ba ste/ /rmi lam nye bar longs spyod dang mtshungs de rnams su/ /'dod pa rnams la sems
<p>40b</p>
<p>40b.1</p>ldan su yi dga' ba yin/ /gang rnams bsgrubs nas dang ni rnam par spel nas dang / /yongs su bskyangs nas dang ni bde bar 'gro min la/ /lci ba'i me ma mur dang rab mtshungs de rnams su/ /'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin/ /gtum po long byed
<p>40b.2</p>bcom brlag pa dang daN Da ka /gang gi don du sgra ngan rnams ni nyams gyur la/ /ro bsregs shing dang rab tu mtshungs pa de rnams su/ /'dod pa rnams la bdag ldan su yi dga' ba yin/ /lha min mdzes sbyin dang ni nye ba'i mdzes sbyin bdag /gang gi don du phan tshun dgrar
<p>40b.3</p>song nyams gyur la/ /mdza' bshes gyur cing rnam par 'bral ba de rnams su/ /'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin/ /gang dag rnams kyi don du chu dang me la dang / /sha za rnams la bdag nyid 'dir ni 'dor ba ste/ /dge ba ma yin dgra bor gyur pa de rnams su/ /
<p>40b.4</p>'dod pa rnams la sems ldan su yi dga' ba yin/ /bshes med 'dod pa'i don du bkren por byed pa ste/ /gsod dang 'ching ba la sogs sdug bsngal rab thob la/ /'dod pa'i don du sems ni bkren pa'i dka' thub can/ /gson pa'i 'jig rten 'ching ba dang ni ngal bar 'gro/ /ri dgas rnams
<p>40b.5</p>ni gsod phyir glu yis 'phrog byed la/ /gzugs kyi don du phye ma leb rnams mer mchong zhing / /sha dag don gnyer nya yis lcags ni za ba ste/ /de phyir yul rnams don med nyid du 'bras bu smin/ /'dod pa'i longs spyod yin zhes gang gi blo yin la/ /kha cig longs spyod rnams ni
<p>40b.6</p>yongs su spyod pa ste/ /gos sogs rdzas kyi yon tan yin phyir 'jig rten na/ /sdug bsngal zhi bar byed ces rab tu gzung bar bya/ /skom pa rab tu zhi phyir chu dag 'dod pa ste/ /bkres pa rnam par nyams phyir bza' ba de bzhin du/ /rlung dang gdung ba sgrib pa'i ched du khang pa ste/ /
<p>40b.7</p>mdoms dang grang ba sgrib pa'i phyir ni bgo ba'o/ /de bzhin nyid ni rnam par 'joms phyir gnas yin la/ /de bzhin lam la ngal ba nyams phyir theg pa ste/ /de bzhin gnas ni rnam par sbyong phyir stan yin la/ /gtsang dang nad med stobs la brten phyir khrus yin no/ /sdug bsngal rab tu zhi
<p>41a</p>
<p>41a.1</p>ba'i ched du gyur pa ste/ /de bzhin skye dgu rnams kyi yul nas longs spyod min/ /rab tu zhi ba'i cho gar rab zhugs shes rab can/ /longs spyod rnams ni bza' zhes su yis khas len byed/ /gang zhig 'gro ba'i gdung bas rnam par gdungs pa ni/ /
<p>41a.2</p>longs spyod yin zhes grang ba'i bya bar nan tan byed/ /sdug bsngal zhi ba'i bdag nyid la ni rab 'jug cing / /des ni 'dod pa rnams la longs spyod 'du shes byed/ /gang phyir 'dod pa rnams la mtha' gcig gyur min te/ /de phyir bdag gis de la longs spyod 'du shes med/ /
<p>41a.3</p>dngos po gang nyid kyis ni bde ba ster byed pa/ /de nyid kyis ni slar yang sdug bsngal 'dren par byed/ /bgo ba lci mo dang ni lci ba ma yin nyid/ /grang dang dro ba'i tshe na bde dang bde min la/ /zla 'od rnams dang tsan+dan nyid kyang dro ba na/ /bde ba'i phyir dang sdug bsngal phyir yin grang
<p>41a.4</p>ba na'o/ /gang phyir rnyed dang ma rnyed la sogs 'jig rten na/ /kun gyi gnyis su 'dzin pa rnams ni rab zhugs te/ /de phyir mtha' gcig bde ba yod pa ma yin zhing / /sa na skyes bu kha cig mtha' gcig sdug bsngal min/ /bde dang sdug bsngal nyid ni rnam par
<p>41a.5</p>'dres mthong nas/ /rgyal srid dang ni bran nyid mnyam pa bdag gi lugs/ /rgyal bo nyid ni rtag par rgod pa ma yin zhing / /bran ni kun nas gdung ba nyid kyang ma yin no/ /gang phyir mi skyong nyid du bka' lung lhag par gyur/ /de phyir rgyal po'i sdug bsngal dag ni chen po
<p>41a.6</p>nyid/ /kun nas brten pa'i shing dang rab mtshungs rgyal po ni/ /srid pa'i rgyu las yongs su ngal bar 'gro ba nyid/ /rgyal srid 'dor ldan bshes min mang por mi skyong gis/ /gal te blo gtad 'cha' bar gyur na rgud pa ste/ /ci ste yang na blo gtad nye bar byed min na/ /'dir
