<p>41a.7</p>ni 'jigs ldan rgyal bo'i bde ba zhes bya ci/ /gang tshe sa ni mtha' dag rgyal bar gyur nas kyang / /gnas pa'i ched du grong khyer gcig pu nyid mthong zhing / /de nyid la yang pho brang gcig pu bsnyen bya ste/ /rgyal por gyur pa pha rol don du ngal lam ci/ /rgyal po sdod pa'i gnas kyang
<p>41b</p>
<p>41b.1</p>gnya' shing gcig nyid do/ /de bzhin bkres pa 'gegs phyir bza' ba tsam yin la/ /de bzhin nyal lam gcig dang stan ni gcig nyid de/ /lhag dang lhag min mi skyong gis ni rgyags phyir ro/ /gal te tshim pa'i don du 'bras bu de 'dod na/ /rgyal srid rnams dang bral yang bdag ni
<p>41b.2</p>tshim pa yod/ /tshim pa yod par gyur na skyes bu'i 'jig rten na/ /khyad par med pa ma yin thams cad khyad par ro/ /de phyir dge dang zhi ba'i lam ni rab thob pa/ /kho bo 'dod pa rnams la slu bya ma yin la/ /mdza' bshes nyid du dran par byas nas yang dang yang / /dam bca'
<p>41b.3</p>nges par skyongs zhes bdag la smras pa'o/ /bdag ni nags su zhugs pa mi bzod pas min la/ /dgra bo'i mda' rnams kyis ni mgo bo 'dar ba min/ /'bras bu lhag pa rnams las re ba byas min te/ /de phyir khyed kyi tshig de bzung ba ma yin no/ /gang zhig yang yang shin tu sos
<p>41b.4</p>'debs khros pa'i sbrul/ /spangs nas slar yang len pa la ni nan tan byed/ /yang na sreg pa'i rang bzhin 'bar ba'i rtswa yi me/ /spangs nas 'dod pa rnams ni slar yang de yis brten/ /gang zhig ma long long ba'i phyir ni 'dod pa ste/ /grol ba 'ching ba'i phyir dang phyug po nor med phyir/ /
<p>41b.5</p>rang bzhin gnas pa'i sems ni bsnyon pa'i sems phyir la/ /yul gyi bdag nyid phyir ni 'dod par de yis byed/ /gang zhig 'dir ni mchog tu zhi ba'i bde ba dang / /gzhan du sdug bsngal rnams ni kun nas sgrib pa ste/ /byed ldan rga dang 'chi ba'i 'jigs las sgrol 'dod pa/ /slong mo nye
<p>41b.6</p>bar rgyu zhes rjes su brtse bya min/ /gang zhig 'dir ni zhi ba'i bde ba 'thob min la/ /gzhan du sdug bsngal rnams kyis rab tu 'dzin byed cing / /phun tshogs chen po'i bdag nyid la yang rnam gnas pa'i/ /sred pas zil gyis gnon la rjes su brtse bar byas/ /sems pa yi dang spyod pa yi
<p>41b.7</p>dang rigs nyid kyi/ khyod kyis brjod pa la ni rjes su mthun pa ste/ /sems pa yi dang spyod pa yi dang rigs nyid kyi/ /kho bo yi yang dam bca' 'dren par mtshungs pa'o/ /bdag kyang 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho'i mda' yis rnam phug pa/ /zhi ba thob par 'dod pas rnam par nges 'byung ste/ /nad med mtho ris na
<p>42a</p>
<p>42a.1</p>yang rgyal srid 'thob pa ru/ /'dod pa med na kye ma mi rnams su smos ci/ /mi skyong gang yang sde gsum mtha' dag brten pa ni/ /rab mchog mi yi don zhes khyed kyis bdag la smras/ /de ltar don med ces ni bdag gi bstan pa 'dir/ /mdzad ldan sde tshan gsum
<p>42a.2</p>ni tshim byed kyang ma yin/ /gang du dga' bar 'gro min 'jigs min nad ma yin/ /skyod min nye bar 'da' min sems kyi nad rnams min/ /gang na yang dang yang du bya ba yod min pa/ /de nyid skyes bu'i don ni mchog tu shes pa'o/ /ji srid na tshod so ma rnam par 'gyur bar 'gro/ /de srid dga' ba
<p>42a.3</p>yongs su skyongs mdzod zhes smras pa/ /'di ni nges pa ma yin g.yo bar mthong ba ste/ /rga ba brtan pa min dang lang tsho brtan ldan mthong / /rang gi las mkhan mthar byed gang gi 'gro ba ni/ /na tshod kun la dbang med rnam par 'gugs pa ste/ /rnam gzhag ma yin rnam par nyams tshe gang ltar
<p>42a.4</p>ni/ /zhi 'dod mkhas pa dag gis dga' ba rtogs par byed/ /gang tshe dga' ba'i gzhu dang nad rnams bkram pa'i mda'/ /mthar byed dge ba ma yin rngon pa bzhin gnas pas/ /skye dgu'i ri dwags bskal pa'i nags brten rnams gtor te/ /na tshod rab mchog la dmigs yid la re ba yi/ /
<p>42a.5</p>de phyir gzhon nam rgan dang yang na byis pa ni/ /rab tu 'jug par 'dod dam rnam par ldog pa nyid/ /chos ldan bdag nyid byas pa ji lta bar gyur pa/ /de ltar myur ba ldan pas 'dir ni bya bar 'os/ /yang na 'dod pa'i 'bras bu rigs su 'os pa rnams/ /chos phyir mchod sbyin bya ba
<p>42a.6</p>gyis zhes gang smras pa/ /gang zhig gzhan gyi sdug bsngal bya bas 'dod pa ste/ /mchod sbyin rnams la phyag 'tshal bde ba 'dod pa med/ /'bras bu 'dod pas dbang med pha rol gsod pa la/ /snying rje'i bdag nyid dam pa rnams kyi rigs tshul min/ /gang yang mchod sbyin dag gi 'bras
<p>42a.7</p>bu rtag gyur pa/ /snying rje'i bdag nyid gang gis de ltar byas nas ci/ /sems ni zhi ba yis sam tshul khrims brtul zhugs kyis/ /gal te chos tshul gzhan gyi cho ga ma yin la/ /de lta na yang mchod sbyin bsnyen par 'os min te/ /gang du gzhan la 'tshes nas 'bras bur brjod pa'o/ /'di
<p>42b</p>
<p>42b.1</p>nyid du yang re zhig skyes bu gnas pa yi/ /bde ba gang zhig pha rol 'tshe bas rab zhugs pa/ /de yang brtse bcas blo dang ldan pa'i 'dod min te/ /gang zhig sred pa'i mtha' mar mi mthong kye ma ci/ /rgyal po 'khor bar bdag gi yid ni dga' med cing / /'bras bur rab tu 'jug phyir bdag
<p>42b.2</p>ni bslu bya min/ /chu 'dzin char gyis brgyab pa'i ljon shing bzhin du ni/ /kun du song ba'i rab tu 'jug pa rnams ni g.yo/ /rnam par thar pa smra ldan rtsibs phur thub pa ni/ /blta bar 'dod pas bdag ni 'dir yongs de yi phyir/ /mi skyong khong la dge bar gyur cig de ni 'gro/ /
<p>42b.3</p>bdag gi de nyid ltos med dag ni bzod par mdzod/ /lha na dbang po bzhin srungs rtag par nyi bzhin srungs/ /yon tan gyis srungs sa srungs 'dir ni dge legs srungs/ /tshe srungs 'phags pa yis srungs dam pa'i bu rnams dang / /dpal srungs rgyal po'i bdag nyid kyis ni
<p>42b.4</p>chos srungs shig /kha ba'i dgra yi rdeg las skyes pa las skyes nas/ /ji ltar gnyis skyes gang zhig lus ni rnam thar 'gro/ /kha ba'i dgra yi dgra yis khyim gyi dgra 'joms nang / /nang du de ltar gang zhig yid ni rnam par thar gshegs mdzod/ /thal mo dang bcas re thob mi skyong gis smras pa/ /
<p>42b.5</p>khyed kyis ji ltar 'dod pa bgegs med thob par shog /bya ba byas pa kun nas thob pa dus su 'dir/ /kho bo yi yang rjes su 'dzin pa khyed kyis mdzad pa'o/ /de ltar gyur zhes brtan pa'i dam bca' mdzad nas sa skyong la/ /de nas de ni thams cad sgrol gyi dka' thub gnas su gshegs/ /yongs
<p>42b.6</p>su gshegs pa de mthong nas kyang ya mtshan gyur pa yi/ /mi skyong nyid kyang ri yi tshogs kyi grong khyer nyid du song / /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ 'dod pa la rnam par smod pa'i le'u ste bcu gcig pa'o// //de nas lus kyis gang ba bzhin/ /
<p>42b.7</p>bu ram shing ba'i zla ba yis/ /zhi bar gnas pa'i thub pa yis/ /rtsibs 'phur gyis ni gnas su bsnyen/ /sgyu rtsal shes kyi rigs de yis/ /rgyang nas gzigs nas mthon po yis/ /legs par 'ongs zhes smras pa ste/ /drung du nye bar gshegs pa'o/ /de gnyis phan tshun rigs par ni/ /
<p>43a</p>
<p>43a.1</p>khams ni snyoms par dris nas su/ /shing gtsang brtul zhugs gdan dag la/ /sa phyogs gtsang bar bzhugs pa'o/ /bkur mang rnam par yangs pa yis/ /lta byed dag gis 'thung ba bzhin/ /mi skyong sras po bzhugs de la/ /thub pa mchog des smras pa'o/ /
<p>43a.2</p>zhi ba bdag gi shes pa ltar/ /khyim nas nges par 'byung bar 'gyur/ /gnyis 'thung rgyags pas zhags pa ltar/ /brtse ba'i zhags pa bcad nas 'ongs/ /khyod kyi yid ni shes rab dang / /kun nas brtan pa ldan pa nyid/ /dug gi ljon pa'i 'bras bu bzhin/ /gang khyod dpal dor nas
<p>43a.3</p>'ongs so/ /longs spyad lhag ma'i phreng ba bzhin/ /bu rnams dag la dpal byin nas/ /sa skyong 'khogs pa'i na tshod rnams/ /gang zhig nags 'ongs ngo mtshar min/ /bdag gi lugs ni ngo mtshar te/ /so ma'i na tshod la khyod kyis/ /yul gyi spyod yul la gnas pa/ /dpal
<p>43a.4</p>nyid longs ma spyad nas 'ongs/ /de phyir chos 'di shes pa la/ /khyod ni dam pa'i snod yin la/ /ye shes gru bo byin brlabs nas/ /skyen par sdug bsngal rgya mtsho sgrol/ /gang yang slob mar shes pa na/ /dus kyis bstan bcos la 'jug ste/ /zab pa las dang nan tan las/ /bdag gi yongs
<p>43a.5</p>rtog khyod ma yin/ /de ltar rtsibs 'phur nyid kyi tshig /mi yi drang srong des gsan nas/ /mchog tu dga' bar gyur pa yis/ /lan gnyis rab tu smras pa'o/ /don ma byas kyang 'di yi ni/ /don byas bzhin du da lta nyid/ /chags dang bral ba gang 'di ni/ /dam pa khyed kyi mngon du gyur/ /blta
<p>43a.6</p>bar 'dod pas 'od bzhin dang / /sgrol bar 'dod pas gru bzhin dang / /'gro bar 'dod pas lam mkhan bzhin/ /khyed mthong ba la bdag gis shes/ /rga dang 'chi ba'i 'jigs rnams las/ /gal te gsung byar dgongs nas ni/ /de phyir gsung bar 'os pa'o/ /de ltar rtsibs 'phur gyis gzhon
<p>43a.7</p>nu'i/ /bdag nyid che las bskul ba nyid/ /rang nyid kyi ni bstan bcos kyi/ /nges par mdor bsdus gsungs pa'o/ /ji ltar 'khor ba yin pa la/ /ji ltar nges par ldog pa nyid/ /nyan pa rnams kyi mchog grub mtha'/ /kho bo'i 'di ni gson mdzod cig /rang bzhin dang ni rnam 'gyur dang / /
<p>43b</p>
<p>43b.1</p>skye dang 'chi dang rga ba ste/ /re zhig sems pa zhes brjod pa/ /brtan pa'i sems pa de shes mdzod/ /de la rang bzhin shes bya ba/ /rang bzhin shes pa shes par mdzod/ /'byung ba lnga yi bdag nyid dang / /blo dang mi gsal ba nyid do/ /rnam 'gyur zhes bya mkhyen par mdzod/ /yul
<p>43b.2</p>rnams dang ni dbang po rnams/ /lag pa rkang pa dag dang ni/ /'phongs dang mdoms dang de bzhin yid/ /'di yi zhing ni shes pa la/ /zhing shes pa zhes bya ba ste/ /zhing shes pa zhes bdag nyid du/ /bdag tu bsam byed rnams kyis smras/ /slob ma dang bcas ser skya yis/ /'di ni
<p>43b.3</p>rab tu rtogs zhes dran/ /bu dang bcas pa'i rtogs pa yang / /skye dgu'i bdag por 'di brjod do/ /skye ba nyid dang rga ba dang / /na ba dang ni 'chi ba dang / /de ni gsal zhes rtogs bya ste/ /bzlog las mi gsal ba yang ngo / /mi shes pa dang las dang srid/ /'khor ba'i rgyu rnams
<p>43b.4</p>shes bya ste/ /gsum po 'dir gnas 'gro ba ni/ /snying stobs de ni 'da' ba med/ /log pa las dang ngar 'dzin las/ /the tshom las dang mngon 'phyo las/ /khyad par med las thabs min las/ /chags pa las dang mngon lhung las/ /de la log pa zhes bya ba/ /phyin ci log tu 'jug
<p>43b.5</p>pa ste/ /bsam par bya ba gzhan sems shing / /bya ba gzhan ni byed pa'o/ /smra ba dang rig pa dang / /'gro ba nga dang gnas pa nga / /de ltar 'di ni ngar 'dzin pa/ /ngar 'dzin med kyi 'jug pa'o/ /gang zhig the tshom med dngos rnams/ /gcig tu gyur pas mthong ba ste/ /the tshom med
<p>43b.6</p>pas 'jim gong ltar/ /de 'dir the tshom du brjod do/ /gang zhig nga nyid de nyid 'di/ /yin dang blo dang las yin la/ /gang zhig drangs te de nyid nga / /zhes gang de ni mngon par 'phyo/ /rab rgyas rab rgyas ma yin pa'i/ /khyad par med pa'i khyad shes kyi/ /rang bzhin rnams kyis gang shes
<p>43b.7</p>pa/ /de ni khyad par med ces dran/ /phyag 'tshal ba dang gzhi mi 'grib/ /bsang gtor dang ni mngon 'thor sogs/ /thabs min zhes ni shes ldan gyis/ /rab tu rtogs bya thabs shes kyi/ /chags pa mi skye yul rnams la/ /yid ngag blo dang las rnams kyis/ /blo ngan gang gis
<p>44a</p>
<p>44a.1</p>chags byed pa/ /de ni mngon par chags zhes dran/ /bdag gi 'di dang 'di bdag ces/ /gang zhig sdug bsngal mngon snyam ste/ /gang zhig 'khor bar lhung shes bya/ /de ltar mkhas skye ma rig pa/ /gnas skabs lnga ni rab thob ste/ /mun pa rmongs pa
<p>44a.2</p>rmongs pa che/ /mun las gyur pa gnyis nyid do/ /de la mun pa le lor dang / /rmongs pa skye 'chir rtogs par mdzod/ /rmongs pa chen po 'dod pa zhes/ /kun nas rmongs med mkhyen par mdzod/ /gang phyir 'di na 'byung rnams kyis/ /chen por yang ni rab rmongs byed/ /de phyir phyag chen
<p>44a.3</p>'di dag ni/ /rmongs pa chen po zhes dran no/ /mun las gyur pa khro nyid du/ /lhag par byed pa'o khro med kyis/ /mi shes mun las gyur pa ni/ /skyo bar rab bshad skyo med kye/ /ma rig pa 'dis byis pa 'di/ /gnas skabs lnga dang ldan pa ste/ /'khor bar sdug bsngal gyur pa yi/ /skye ba
<p>44a.4</p>rnams su 'bab par byed/ /lta bo nyan po shes pa po/ /bya ba dang ni rgyu nyid dag /da zhes de ltar 'ongs nas ni/ /'khor bar yongs su 'khor bar byed/ /blo ldan rgyu 'di rnams kyis 'di/ /skye ba'i rgyun la rab tu 'jug /rgyu med pa las 'bras bu med/ /de ltar rnam par shes par
<p>44a.5</p>'os/ /de la rgyun rab rab rgyas mig /gsal ba dang ni mi gsal nyid/ /thar pa 'dod pa bzhin rnams te/ /yang dag 'gro ba rigs par mdzod/ /bzhi po de dag ji lta bzhin/ /'gyur med go 'phang 'thob par byed/ /de phyir 'jig rten na tshangs pa/ /mchog tu tshangs par smra
<p>44a.6</p>ba rnams/ /tshangs pa'i spyod pa spyod byed 'dir/ /tshangs pa rnams kyis gnas par byed/ /mi skyod sras kyis thub pa de'i/ /tshig 'di de ltar gsan nas ni/ /mthar thug go 'phang nyid dang ni/ /thabs mngon pa dag dran pa'o/ /ji ltar ji srid gang du ni/ /tshangs pa'i spyod pa 'di
<p>44a.7</p>spyad cing / /chos 'di yis ni mthar thug pa/ /khyod kyis rnam par bshad par 'os/ /de ltar thub pas bstan bcos ltar/ /rnam gsal don ni mdor bsdus pas/ /cho ga'i rtog pa gzhan nyid kyis/ /chos de de la smras pa'o/ /'dis ni dang por khyim spangs nas/ /slong mo'i
<p>44b</p>
<p>44b.1</p>rtags ni bsten pa ste/ /phrin las rnam par rgyas pa yi/ /tshul khrims blangs nas 'jug par byed/ /byed ldan rtsod med bstan bcos rig /mchog tu tshim pa la gnas nas/ /gang dang de yis gang dang der/ /rnam dben gnas ni bsten pa'o/ /de nas chags las 'jigs
<p>44b.2</p>mthong nas/ /chags pa med las mchog zhi yang / /dbang po'i grong ni nges bzung ste/ /yid la zhi ni 'bad pa byed/ /de nas 'dod pa rnams las dang / /gnod sems sogs las rnam dben nyid/ /bsam gtan dang po rnam dpyod ldan/ /rnam par dben pa las skyes thob/ /
<p>44b.3</p>bsam gtan bde ba de thob nas/ /de dang de nyid rnam dpyod cing / /sngar med bde ba thob pa yis/ /byis pa'i skye bo 'phrog par byed/ /'dod dang sdang ba rnam smad pa'i/ /zhi ba'i cho ga de 'dra 'dis/ /tshangs pa'i 'jig rten thob pa ste/ /yongs su tshim pas gnas pa'o/ /rnam dpyod
<p>44b.4</p>yid ni skyong byed rnams/ /mkhas par rnam par shes nas kyang / /de las rnam par grol ba ni/ /bsam gtan dga' ba'i bde ldan thob/ /gang zhig khyad par ma mthong zhing / /dga' ba de yis phrogs pa de/ /'od gsal ba yi lha rnams su/ /'od gsal ba yi gnas 'thob bo/ /gang
<p>44b.5</p>yang dga' ba'i bde de las/ /yid ni rnam par dben byed pa/ /dga' ba'i bde ba dang bral ba/ /bsam gtan gsum pa thob par byed/ /de 'dra'i bde ba 'dir thob nas/ /gang zhig chags min btang snyoms shing / /bde dang sdug bsngal rnam spangs pa'i/ /bsam gtan bzhi pa thob par
<p>44b.6</p>byed/ /bde dang sdug bsngal zhi phyir dang / /sems kyi bya ba med pa'i phyir/ /thar zhes mngon pa'i nga rgyal gyis/ /der yang kha cig 'bad pa byed/ /bsam gtan de yi 'bras bu ni/ /'bras bu che bas lhas mnyam par/ /longs spyod shes rab che rnams kyis/ /chen po'i dus su smra ba'o/ /
<p>44b.7</p>ting 'dzin de las rnam langs shing / /lus skyes skyon rnams mthong nas ni/ /lus las rnam par ldog pa'i phyir/ /shes ldan bsam gtan la 'jog go/ /de nas bsam gtan de bor nas/ /khyad par la ni nges byas pa'i/ /shes rab ldan de 'dod las bzhin/ /gzugs rnams las
<p>45a</p>
<p>45a.1</p>kyang chags pa med/ /lus 'di la ni kha gang du/ /de la yongs su rtog pa ste/ /de nas rdzas sdug rnams la yang / /nam mkhar lhag par mos par byed/ /nam mkhar song ba'i bdag nyid du/ /bsdus nas gzhan du blo ldan gyis/ /de nyid mtha' med par mthong
<p>45a.2</p>zhing / /khyad par 'phags pa lhag par 'thob/ /nang na mkhas pa gzhan dag ni/ /bdag nyid bdag nyid kyis bzlog nas/ /ci yang med ces mthong ba ni/ /ci yang med pa zhes dran no/ /de nas gur nas bya bzhin dang / /gong bu dag nas srin bal bzhin/ /zhing shes lus las 'thon pa las/ /
<p>45a.3</p>thar pa zhes ni mngon par brjod/ /de nyid shes pa'i mkhas pa yis/ /gang zhig thar pa zhes brjod pa/ /'di de tshangs pa dam pa ste/ /rtags med rtag cing 'gyur ba med/ /de ltar thabs dang thar pa dag /bdag gis khyod la bstan pa ste/ /gal te shes shing gal te sred/ /ji lta ba
<p>45a.4</p>bzhin rtogs par mdzod/ /rgyal 'dod bu dang skyed byed dang / /gzhan mi 'bral ba rgan po dang / /thar pa 'dod pa gzhan rnams kyang / /lam 'di thob nas grol bar 'gyur/ /de yi dam pa'i tshig 'di dang / /rnam par dpyod pa yang bzung nas/ /sngon du rgyu yi stobs thob pas/ /lan ni smras par
<p>45a.5</p>gyur pa'o/ /gong nas gong du zhi ba yi/ /ye shes phra mo 'di thos shing / /zhing shes yongs su ma btang phyir/ /de ni mthar thug min par go/ /rnam gyur dang ni rang bzhin las/ /zhing shes grol bar kho bo yis/ /rab tu skye ba'i chos su dang / /sa bon chos su snyam pa'o/ /gang yang rnam dag
<p>45a.6</p>bdag nyid ni/ /nges par thar zhes rtog pa ste/ /slar yang rkyen dag yod pa las/ /de ni grol bar mi 'gyur ro/ /ji ltar dus sbyor sa dang chu/ /me las sa bon skye ma yin/ /de bzhin rkyen ni de rnams kyis/ /skye ba de yang bdag gi lugs/ /gang zhig mi shes las sred rnams/ /spangs las
<p>45a.7</p>thar pa rtogs byed pa/ /de ni mchog tu yongs spong ba/ /bdag yod gyur na yod ma yin/ /spangs nas spangs nas gsum po 'di/ /khyad par du yang nyer 'thob cing / /gang du bdag ni gnas gyur pa/ /der ni gsum po 'di phra'o/ /skyon rnams phra ba nyid las dang / /sems kyi bya ba med las
<p>45b</p>
<p>45b.1</p>dang / /tshe ni ring ba nyid las kyang / /thar par kyang ni yongs su rtog /ngar 'dzin par ni yongs spong bar/ /gang de yongs su rtog byed la/ /bdag spyod gyur nas ngar 'dzin pa/ /yongs su spong ba yod ma yin/ /drang srong rnams kyis ma spangs pa/ /'di ni yon tan med ma yin/ /de phyir yon tan
<p>45b.2</p>med gyur na/ /'di yi thar par mi brjod do/ /yon tan can gyis yon tan gyi/ /ldog pa yod pa ma yin te/ /gzugs dang 'gro ba dang bral ba'i/ /me ni nye bar 'thob ma yin/ /lus las sngon du lus can dang / /yon tan las sngar yon tan can/ /ma yin de phyir dang por grol/ /lus bzhin slar
<p>45b.3</p>yang 'ching bar byed/ /zhing shes lus dang ma bral ba/ /shes pa yin nam shes min nyid/ /gal te shes 'di shes bya yod/ /shes bya yod na mi grol lo/ /ci ste khyod la shes mi 'grub/ /bdag tu rtog pas ci zhig bya/ /bdag dang bral yang shes pa ni/ /rab grub shing dang rtsig pa bzhin/ /gang
<p>45b.4</p>phyir gong nas gong du ni/ /de ltar rtsibs 'phur gyi ni chos/ /mkhyen nas de ni ma tshim zhing / /mtha' dag min zhes shes nas su/ /de nas so sor gshegs pa'o/ /de nas khyad par chos 'dod pa/ /lhag spyod kyi ni gnas su gshegs/ /de yi bdag tu 'dzin las kyang / /des ni lta bar sred
<p>45b.5</p>ma gyur/ /'du shes 'du shes med pa'i skyon/ /thub pa lhag spyod kyis shes nas/ /'du shes 'du shes med bdag min/ /cung zad med las gzhan 'gro thob/ /gang phyir dmigs pa phra mo ni/ /'du shes 'du shes med las gzhan/ /'du shes med min 'du shes min/ /de phyir der ni re
<p>45b.6</p>'dod min/ /gang phyir der ni blo gnas shing / /gzhan du rab tu rgyu pa med/ /phra zhing rno ldan de phyir der/ /'du shes med min 'du shes med/ /de phyir de yang rab thob nas/ /slar yang 'gro ba 'khor ba ste/ /byang chub sems dpa' mchog 'dod pas/ /de phyir lhag spyod dor ba'o/ /de nas de yi
<p>45b.7</p>gnas thob nas/ /dge legs don gnyer nges byas nas/ /gang yang rgyal ba'i drang srong gis/ /grong khyer zhes bya'i gnas bsnyen no/ /de nas nai rany+dza na'i 'gram/ /gtsang mar gtsang zhing pha rol gnon/ /dben pa'i gnas ni mngon 'dod ba'i/ /thub pa yis ni gnas mdzad do/ /de nas de ni sngar brten
<p>46a</p>
<p>46a.1</p>zhing / /dbang po lnga yi dbang las khengs/ /mun pas bsnyen pa'i brtul zhugs can/ /dge slong lnga rnams des gzigs so/ /bsod nams kyis bsgrubs nor nad med/ /dbang don rnams kyis dbang phyug bzhin/ /dge slong de rnams kyis kyang 'dir/ /de mthong gyur
<p>46a.2</p>nas nye bar gnas/ /de'i dbang gis gnas slob ma rnams/ /dbang po g.yos pas yid bzhin du/ /rab tu de rnams kyis mchod cing / /rnam par dul las rjes su 'jug /'chi dang skye ba mthar byed la/ /de nas thabs ni 'di yis zhes/ /bza' ba med par shes pa yis/ /dka' thub
<p>46a.3</p>gdung ba rnams brtsams so/ /basmyung gnas cho ga du ma rnams/ /mi yis spyod dka' rnams mdzad cing / /las ni thob bzhed lo drug tu/ /bdag gi sku lus rig par mdzad/ /pha mtha' med pa'i 'khor ba yi/ /pha rol thob par 'dod pa nges/ /bza' ba'i dus su til dang 'bru/ /
<p>46a.4</p>rab sha rnams ni re re gsol/ /dka' thub gdung ba des de yi/ /sku las bri bar byas pa gang / /slar yang de yi gzi brjid kyis/ /sku lus nye bar 'phel byas gyur/ /ston ka'i dkar phyogs dang po yi/ /zla bas ku mu ta rnams bzhin/ /ring kyang dpal grags ring min zhing / /gzhan gyis
<p>46a.5</p>mig rnams tshim par mdzad/ /rus lpags lhag ma lhag med par/ /tshil dang sha dang khrag rnams kyis/ /zad kyang zab mo ma zad par/ /rgya mtsho bzhin du de mdzes so/ /de nas sangs rgyas nyid 'dod pas/ /ngal dub gdung bas don med bsal/ /nyon mongs lus can thub pa
<p>46a.6</p>ni/ /srid las 'jigs pa blo mdzad do/ /chos 'di chags bral phyir min zhing / /rtogs phyir ma yin thar phyin min/ /de tshe 'dzam bu'i rtsa bar gang / /bdag gis thos te nges pa yin/ /'di ni stobs chung gis thob par/ /nus pa min phyir gus 'ongs shing / /sku yi stobs ni 'phel don
<p>46a.7</p>du/ /slar yang 'di ni rjes su bsams/ /bkres dang skom pas yongs gtser zhing / /ngal las rang gnas med pa'i sems/ /yid kyis thob bya'i 'bras bu ni/ /ldog pa med pa gang zhig 'thob/ /rtag par dbang po tshim pa las/ /yang dag gnas pa 'thob pa ste/ /dbang po yang
<p>46b</p>
<p>46b.1</p>dag tshim nyid kyis/ /yid ni rang bzhin gnas pa 'thob/ /dang zhing rab dang yid kyis ni/ /ting 'dzin nye bar skye ba ste/ /ting 'dzin gyis sbyar sems kyi ni/ /bsam gtan sbyor ba rab tu 'jug /bsam gtan rab tu zhugs pa las/ /rnyed dka' zhi zhing dga' med mchog /'chi med go 'phang de
<p>46b.2</p>chos rnams/ /gang gis thob pa rab thob po/ /de phyir bza' ba rtsa ba ste/ /'di ni thabs zhes nges pa yin/ /bza' ba byed la brtan pa ni/ /dpag med blo yis blo mdzad nas/ /khrus byas nai rany+dza 'gram nas/ /lag byin 'gram gyi ljon shing ni/ /gus pa yis dud yal ga'i rtses/ /sku lus rid
<p>46b.3</p>pa dal bus drangs/ /de nas lha rnams kyis bskul ba'i/ /ba lang skyong bdag bu mo ni/ /snying la dga' skyes 'gyur ba yi/ /dga' stobs ma ni der 'ongs so/ /dung dkar gyis 'bar lag pa can/ /la ba sngon po gon pa mo/ /dbu ba dang bcas chu sngon phreng / /chu mchog ya mu na bzhin no/ /
<p>46b.4</p>spyan mig ut+pal rab rgyas shing / /dad pas 'phel ba'i dga' ma des/ /de la mgo yis rab btud nas/ /'o ma drangs par gyur pa'o/ /des de gsol nas de la ni/ /skye ba'i 'bras bu thob byas nas/ /yang dag dbang po drug tshim ste/ /byang chub 'thob par nus par gyur/ /phul
<p>46b.5</p>byung rgyas pa'i sku mnga' zhing / /rang gi grags bcas thub pa ni/ /nus gyur rgya mtsho gnyis dag gis/ /mdzes dang bstan pa gcig pus bzung / /bdag ni nges par grol ba la/ /blo ldan khams lnga rnams kyis ltar/ /kun nas 'jug ces rnam shes nas/ /dge slong lnga rnams kyis de dor/ /
<p>46b.6</p>de nas 'bad rtsol gnyis pa ni/ /byang chub ched du nges mdzad de/ /rtswa 'jam bkram pa'i sa gzhi la/ /a shwad tha yi rtsa bar gshegs/ /de tshe glang po'i 'gros mnga' ba'i/ /dpe med zhabs kyi sgra yis sad par byas pa ni/ /thub pa chen po'i byang chub des par rtogs pa yi/ /grub mchog nag po zhes
<p>46b.7</p>byas bstod pa smras par gyur/ /ji ltar thub pa khyod kyis zhabs kyis brdzis pa ni/ /yang nas yang du sa ni sgra skad sgrogs pa 'dra/ /ji ltar khyod kyi 'od ni nyi mar snang ba ste/ /khyod kyis nges par 'dod pa'i go 'phang mkhyen pa nyid/ /ji ltar mkha' la khug rta'i phreng ba rnams bskor zhing / /pad+ma'i
<p>47a</p>
<p>47a.1</p>spyan mnga' khyed la skor ba byed pa nyid/ /ji ltar mkha' la rlung rnams zhi bar 'gro ba ste/ /khyod kyis nges par de ring sangs rgyas 'gyur ba nyid/ /de nas glu mchog gis ni yang dag bstod pa ni/ /lco ga las ni gtsang ma'i rtswa rnams nyer blangs nas/ /byang chub shing
<p>47a.2</p>chen rtsa ba dge la rab brtan cing / /byang chub ched du dam bca' mdzad cing bzhugs pa'o/ /de nas gnyid log lto 'phye'i gdengs kas bsdus pa la/ /des ni rdo rje'i skyil krung g.yo med mchog bcings te/ /ji srid bya ba byas pa nyid ni ma thob par/ /de srid sa las gdan de 'byed par mi
<p>47a.3</p>bgyi'o/ /de nas nges pa'i bdag nyid bcom ldan gdan mdzad tshe/ /lha na gnas rnams mnyam med dga' ba thob gyur la/ /ri dgas tshogs rnams gnas par ma gyur bya rnams dang / /rlung gis bsnun pa'i nags kyi ljon shing sgra med gyur/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i
<p>47a.4</p>snyan dngags chen po las/ ring 'phur dang lhag spyod kyi drung du gshegs pa'i le'u ste bcu gnyis pa'o// //der ni rnam par thar phyir dam bca' mdzad pa na/ /rgyal po'i rigs las rab 'khrungs drang srong chen po ni/ /der ni nye bar zhugs tshe 'jig rten rab
<p>47a.5</p>dga' zhing / /der ni bdud kyang dam pa'i chos kyi dgrar gyur to/ /gang la 'dod pa'i lhar ni 'jig rten na smra ba/ /sna tshogs mtshon cha me tog mda' can de bzhin du/ /'dod pa rab tu spyod pa'i bdag po de nyid la/ /thar ba'i dgra bo bdud du dpe rjod byed pa'o/ /de yi bu ni rol pa dga' ba
<p>47a.6</p>rgyags pa dang / /bu mo dga' ma dges ma sred ma gsum rnams kyis/ /de la sems kyi rnam par 'gyur ba dris pa ste/ /des ni de rnams la tshig mngon par smras/ /thub pa 'dis ni nges pa'i go cha rnam bzung zhing / /sems pa'i mtshon cha blo yi mda' ni bsdogs byas nas/ /bdag cag
<p>47a.7</p>yul rnams la ni rgyal 'dod bsdad pa ste/ /gang phyir 'dis ni bdag gi yid ni rnam par 'gyur/ /gal te 'dis bdag zil gyis mnan nas 'gro ba ste/ /'jigs pa la yang thar ba'i lam dag 'chad byed cing / /lus 'phags jo bo spyod las lhung ba'i bzhin du ni/ /de phyir 'di
<p>47b</p>
<p>47b.1</p>yis bdag gi yul ni de ring stongs/ /de phyir ji srid 'dis ni spyan mig ma thob cing / /ji srid bdag gi spyod yul dag na gnas pa nyid/ /chu bo shin tu 'phel ba'i shugs kyis zam pa bzhin/ /de srid 'di yi brtul zhugs 'joms su 'gro ba'o/ /de nas me tog las byas gzhu
<p>47b.2</p>ni bzung nas dang / /kun du rmongs par byed pa'i mda' lnga rnams bzung nas/ /skye dgu rnams kyi yid kyi rang gnas mi byed pa/ /de ni bur bcas a shwad tha yi rtsa bar song / /de nas srid pa 'khor ba'i pha rol rgal 'dod pa'i/ /thub pa rab tu zhi bar gdan la bzhugs pa la/ /lag pa
<p>47b.3</p>g.yas pa mtshon cha'i rtse mor bdungs nas ni/ /mda' yis rol zhing bdud kyis 'di ni smras pa'o/ /kye ho rgyal rigs 'chi bas 'jigs pa longs mdzod cig /thar pa'i chos ni spongs la 'jig rten mdzod/ /mda' dang mchod sbyin rnams kyis 'jig rten pham byas nas/ /'jig
<p>47b.4</p>rten dag nas dbang po'i go 'phang 'thob par mdzod/ /gang zhig mi dbang snga ma rnams kyis 'drims pa ste/ /nges par 'byung la 'di ni grags pa'i lam yin zhing / /rgyal po'i drang srong rnams kyang rigs su skyes pa yis/ /slong mo rab thob la ni 'di ni bsngags ma yin/ /ji srid nges
<p>47b.5</p>pa'i bdag nyid de ring mi ldang ba/ /dam bca' rnam par ma dor brtan par gyur cig dang / /gang zhig nya dgra sU rwa ka la rnam spangs pa'i/ /de nyid bdag gis mda' 'di 'bar bar byas pa'o/ /'dis ni cung zhig reg pa tsam gyis e la de/ /zla ba'i tsha bo yin yang sems med gyur pa
<p>47b.6</p>ste/ /zhi ba'i lus zhes bya ba de yang der 'gyur nas/ /zad pa'i dus su kye ma mi gzhan smos ci dgos/ /de phyir skyen par longs la 'du shes thob gyis dang / /yang yang shin tu ro myang mda' ni mnan pa ste/ /dga' ma'i byar 'os dga' zhing dges pa rnams la ni/ /gang zhig ngang pa
<p>47b.7</p>rnams la bzhin du mi 'phen no/ /gang tshe de skad brjod kyang chags pa dang bral ba'i/ /shAkya thub pas gdan ni bshig pa ma yin nyid/ /de nas 'di la bdud kyis mda' ni 'phangs pa ste/ /bu mo rnams dang bu rnams bdun nas byas nas so/ /der ni de yis mda' ni rab tu 'phangs na yang / /
<p>48a</p>
<p>48a.1</p>chags par byas pa med cing brtan las g.yos pa med/ /de ltar de mthong gyur nas bdud ni yi mug cing / /bsam mno yongs su ldan pa dal bus smras par 'gyur/ /ri dbang bu mo la dmigs gang gis phug pa yi/ /bde 'byung lha yang yongs su g.yos par gyur
<p>48a.2</p>pa ste/ /'dis ni mda' de nyid la sems bar mi byed pa/ /sems med yin nam mda' 'di de ma yin nam ci/ /de phyir me tog mda' 'di 'os pa ma yin zhing / /dga' ba ma yin dga' bar sbyor ba 'os ma yin/ /'di ni zhi ba ma yin 'byung bo'i tshogs rnams kyis/ /'jigs dang
<p>48a.3</p>bsdigs dang rdeg pa rnams ni 'os pa'o/ /de nas bdud kyis rang gi sde ni dran pa ste/ /shAkya thub pa'i bgegs ni mnyam por byed 'dod pa/ /ral gri be con shing rtse ljon shing rtse gsum mdung lag rnams/ /sna tshogs bsam pa dang ldan rjes su 'brangs rnams 'ongs/ /phag
<p>48a.4</p>dang nya dang bong bu rnga mo'i gdong can rnams/ /stag dang dom dang seng ge gnyis 'thung gdong can rnams/ /mig gcig kha ni du ma mgo bo gsum ldan rnams/ /gsus pa 'phyang ba rnams dang gsus pa che ba rnams/ /brla rnams pus mo'i bar du bum pa'i bus mo rnams/ /mche
<p>48a.5</p>ba'i mtshon cha rnams dang sen mo'i mtshon cha rnams/ /keng rus gdong can rnams dang gzugs ni mang po rnams/ /gdong phyed gzhom pa rnams dang gdong ni chen po rnams/ /thal skya rnams dang thig le dmar po sna tshogs rnams/ /kha T+wAM ga rnams dang ni spre'u ltar ngud sgra rnams/ /
<p>48a.6</p>'phongs 'phyang rnams dang glang bo'i rna ba'i rna ba rnams/ /pags pa'i gos can rnams dang gos dang bral ba rnams/ /gdong phyed dkar po rnams dang lus phyed ljang gu rnams/ /zangs mdog dung mdog rnams dang ljang gu dkar po rnams/ /sbrul gyi sham thabs rnams dang de bzhin
<p>48a.7</p>lag pa rnams/ /rab tu sgra sgrogs dril bu 'khrugs pa'i ske rags rnams/ /ta la'i tshad mnyam rnams dang mdung rnams bzung ba rnams/ /byis pa'i tshad mnyam rnams dang mche ba gtsigs pa rnams/ /lug gi gdong can rnams dang bya yi mig can rnams/ /byi la'i gdong can
<p>48b</p>
<p>48b.1</p>rnams dang mi yi lus can rnams/ /skra bkram rnams dang ral pa can dang byi bo rnams/ /gos dmar rnams dang rnam par 'khrugs pas dkris pa rnams/ /rab dga'i gdong can rnams dang gnyer ma'i gdong can rnams/ /gzi brjid 'phrog pa rnams dang yid ni 'phrog pa rnams/ /kha cig
<p>48b.2</p>dag ni 'pho zhing drag tu phan tshun du/ /mchan khung 'khyud cing de bzhin gzhan rnams mchongs/ /mkha' la 'gro ba rnams ni kha cig rtse ba ste/ /kha cig shing gi rtse mo rnams la zhon pa'o/ /kha cig rtse gsum bskor zhing gar ni byed pa ste/ /kha cig dbyug pa gdengs shing thog sgra sgrogs pa'o/ /kha
<p>48b.3</p>cig dga' bas khyu mchog bzhin du skad 'don zhing / /kha cig lus 'phos rnams las rab tu 'bar bar gyur/ /'dzin par 'dod pa rnams dang 'joms par 'dod pa rnams/ /jo bo'i bka' ni rab tu skyong bar byed pa ste/ /rnam pa de ltar 'byung po'i tshogs rnams kun nas ni/ /byang chub sems
<p>48b.4</p>dpa' de la yongs su bskor nas gnas/ /mtshan mo snga ma la ni shAkya'i khyu mchog dang / /bdud kyi 'thab mo dus de rab tu mthong nas ni/ /nam mkha' gsal ba ma yin sa ni g.yos gyur la/ /phyogs rnams sgra dang bcas pa rab tu 'bar bar gyur/ /drag po'i shugs can rlung ni kun du
<p>48b.5</p>g.yos gyur la/ /skar ma rnams ni mi snang zla ba gsal ma gyur/ /slar yang mtshan mor mun pa rnam par rgyas gyur la/ /rgya mtsho rnams ni thams cad kun du g.yos par gyur/ /sa gzhi 'dzin cing chos dag 'dzin pa'i klu rnams ni/ /thub pa chen po'i bgegs la bzod pa ma yin zhing / /bdud
<p>48b.6</p>las khros pas rnam par log pa'i mig can rnams/ /rngam pa bton zhing lus ni rnam par 'gyur ba'o/ /gtsang mar lhag par gnas pa'i lha yi drang srong ni/ /dam chos bsgrub pa'i don du mngon par zhugs pa rnams/ /bdud las yid kyis rjes su brtse ba byas pa ste/ /chags dang bral ba
<p>48b.7</p>las kyang khros bar ma gyur to/ /'tshe ba'i bdag nyid bdud kyi dpung ni de yis ni/ /byang chub rtsa ba de ni khyab pa mthong nas ni/ /chos kyi bdag nyid 'jig rten thar pa 'dod rnams kyis/ /nam mkha' dag la hA hA'i sgra dag byas par gyur/ /chos kyi cho ga de ni nye bar nyams byed pa/ /bdud dpung
<p>49a</p>
<p>49a.1</p>gnas pa drang srong chen pos gzigs nas ni/ /ba lang rnams kyi dbus su seng ge gnas pa bzhin/ /g.yo 'gul med cing rnam par 'gyur bar yang ma gyur/ /de nas de yi 'jigs pa'i ched du bdud kyis ni/ /'byung po'i sde ni drag po rnams la bka' stsal zhing / /
<p>49a.2</p>de nas 'di yi sde des rang rang mthu rnams kyis/ /de yi bstan pa dbye phyir blo gros byas pa'o/ /kha cig lce rnams g.yo zhing du mar rnam 'phyang zhing / /mche ba'i rtse mo rnams rno mig rnams ljang ser zlum/ /kha rnams gdangs shing phur bu'i rna ba rnams bstan zhing / /kun nas skrag par byed
<p>49a.3</p>pa snyam du gnas zhes grag /des ni gzugs dang bsam pa dag gis mi bzad pa/ /rnam pa de dag nyid du gnas pa de rnams las/ /rtsed mo byed pa'i byis pa rgyags pa rnams las ni/ /drang srong chen po zug med skyo bar ma gyur to/ /de nas kha cig khros pas lta byed rnam 'gyur zhing / /'di
<p>49a.4</p>la dbyug pa rdeg par 'bad pa bya ba ste/ /sngon tshe grong khyer 'joms pa'i rdo rje dang bcas ltar/ /de nas 'di yi dbyug pa dang bcas lag pa rengs/ /kha cig rdo dang shing rnams gyen du 'phyar ba ni/ /thub pa la ni rnam par 'phen par ma nus te/ /'bigs byed ri brags rnams ni rdo rjes bcom pa
<p>49a.5</p>bzhin/ /shing rnams dang bcas rdo rnams bcas pa de bzhin lhung / /kha cig mkha' la gyen du 'phur bas rdo rnams dang / /dgra sta rnams dang shing rnams rnam par 'phangs pa rnams/ /kha dog gcig min mtshams sprin rkang pa rnams bzhin du/ /mngon par lhung ba ma yin nam mkhar gnas par
<p>49a.6</p>gyur/ /gzhan ni de yi steng du 'bar ba'i khyu mchog gis/ /glang bu ri bo tsam pa'i rwa can 'phangs pa ste/ /de ni 'phangs pa tsam du nam mkhar gnas pa nyid/ /de yi mthu las rnam pa brgyar ni gas par gyur/ /'jig rten 'jig tshe lhun po rab tu 'bar ba yis/ /gser gyi bya skyibs
<p>49a.7</p>rnams kyi phye ma rnam bzhin du/ /kha cig nyi ma shar ba bzhin du 'bar ba yi/ /me mdag char pa chen po mkha' las phab par gyur/ /byang chub shing gi rtsa bar rab tu rnam 'phangs pa'i/ /me stag 'phro ba dang bcas me mdag char pa de/ /drang srong dam pa mchog gis byams pa'i gnas pa las/ /
<p>49b</p>
<p>49b.1</p>ut+pal dmar po'i 'dab ma'i char par gyur pa'o/ /lus dang sems la rnam par gnod par bya ba'i phyir/ /rnam pa de ltar phab pa de dang de rnams kyis/ /rang gi nges pa'i gnyen 'dun nye bar 'khyud nas bzhin/ /shAkya thub pa gdan las g.yos par ma gyur to/ /de nas gzhan
<p>49b.2</p>rnams 'khogs pa'i ljon shing rnams nas ltar/ /kha rnams las ni sbrul rnams rnam par skyugs pa ste/ /sngags kyis bcings bzhin de rnams de yi drung du ni/ /song ba ma yin dbugs min g.yos par ma gyur to/ /gzhan rnams glog dang bcas shing thog dang bcas pa yis/ /chu 'dzin chen
<p>49b.3</p>bo gtum pa'i dbyangs ldan rnams gyur nas/ /ljon shing de la rdo ba'i char pa phab pa ste/ /de ni me tog char pa mdzes par gyur pa'o/ /dbang phyug ma yin sron par dkar ba'i mi yi ni/ /snying la yongs su g.yos pa'i khro ba bzhin du ni/ /de nas gzhan gyis gzhu la mda' dag bkang ba ni/ /de nyid
<p>49b.4</p>du ni 'bar zhing lhung bar ma gyur to/ /yul la rab tu 'jug la 'khor ba la 'jigs pa/ /yongs su rtog pa po yi dbang po lnga rnams bzhin/ /gzhan rnams dag gis mda' lnga rab tu 'phangs pa rnams/ /nam mkhar gnas bzhin thub pa la ni ma lhung ngo / /gzhan ni brdeg par 'dod pas khros
<p>49b.5</p>shing rab bskor zhing / /dbyug pa bzung nas drang srong chen po'i mngon du phyogs/ /don med byed pa'i nyes pa rnams la 'jig rten bzhin/ /des ni 'dod pa ma thob dbang med 'gyel bar gyur/ /bud med sprin pa nag mo lag na thod pa can/ /drang srong chen po'i thugs ni rmongs par byed ces grag /g.yo
<p>49b.6</p>ba'i bdag nyid can gyi blo ni lung la bzhin/ /der ni nges pa med par bskor zhing gnas ma yin/ /kha cig mig ni rab tu 'bar bar byas nas ni/ /mig gi me yis sbrul gyi dug bzhin bsreg 'dod pas/ /'dod pa'i bdag nyid can gyis nyer gnas dpal bzhin du/ /der ni drang srong bzhugs
<p>49b.7</p>pa mthong bar ma gyur to/ /ye shes ting 'dzin dag gis 'gro bya nyes legs chos/ /lus kyi ngal ba rnams kyis 'thob par 'dod pa bzhin/ /de bzhin gzhan ni rdo ba lci mo bteg pa ni/ /rab tu 'bad pa rnam bcom don med ngal bar gyur/ /de bzhin gzhan rnams dred dang seng ge'i rnam pa yis/ /
<p>50a</p>
<p>50a.1</p>chen po'i sgra rnams mthon po rab tu sgrogs pa ste/ /rdo rjes bsnun pa'i nam mkha' 'gas pa zhes snyam nas/ /sems can rnams ni gang gis kun nas 'khums par gyur/ /ri dgas glang po rnams ni nyam thag skad 'don zhing / /rnam par 'bros shing thim pa nyid
<p>50a.2</p>du gyur pa ste/ /de yi mtshan mor phyogs rnams las ni nyin mo bzhin/ /nyam thag bya rnams skad 'don yongs su babs par gyur/ /rnam pa de ltar de rnams kyi sgra de rnams kyis/ /'byung po thams cad rnams su g.yos pa yin na yang / /khab rnams dag gi sgra rnams dag gis mkha'
<p>50a.3</p>lding ltar/ /thub pa 'jigs pa ma yin 'khums par ma gyur to/ /'jigs pa 'dron pa yongs su bskor ba'i tshogs rnams las/ /ji lta ji ltar thub pa'i 'jigs pa ma yin pa/ /de lta de ltar chos 'dzin rnams kyi dgra bo yi/ /bdud rnams mya ngan las dang khros nas byer ba'o/ /de
<p>50a.4</p>nas 'byung po cung zhig gzugs ni mtho ba ma yin zhing / /khyad par 'phags par gyur pa nam mkhar gnas nyid kyis/ /drang srong la gnod dgra ma yin la khros mthong nas/ /bdud lha chen po'i dbyangs kyis smras par gyur pa'o/ /don med ngal bar byed par 'os pa ma yin bdud/ /
<p>50a.5</p>'tshe ba'i bdag nyid spongs la bde bar song mdzod dang / /ri bo chen po lhun po rnams kyi sa bzhin du/ /khyod kyis bskyod cing bsgul bar nus pa ma yin no/ /sa yi brtan pa nyid dang chu yi gsher ba nyid/ /me yi dro ba nyid ni rab tu 'dor ba yang / /bskal pa du mar bsgrub pa'i bsod nams las
<p>50a.6</p>mnga' ba/ /'dis ni nan tan nges par 'dor ba ma yin no/ /'dis ni nges pa gang dang pha rol gnon pa dang / /gzi brjid gang dang brtse ba skye dgu rnams la brten/ /'od zer stong gis mun rnams ma bcom gnas bzhin du/ /'di ni de nyid ma thob nas ni ldang ma yin/ /shing la bsrubs nas me ni
<p>50a.7</p>rnyed par 'gyur ba ste/ /sa la brkos na chu yang 'thob par 'gyur ba nyid/ /rigs pa dang ni ldan pa'i thams cad byas pa ste/ /brtson 'grus ldan pa'i bsgrub bya ma yin ci yang med/ /de phyir chags sogs nad rnams dag la gnas pa yi/ /'jig rten nyam thag pa la thugs rje mnga' ba ni/ /
<p>50b</p>
<p>50b.1</p>ye shes dman gyi don du yongs su ngal ba po/ /sman pa chen po 'di la bgegs 'os ma yin no/ /lam ngan mang po rnams kyis 'jig rten stor ba la/ /gang zhig zhi bas dam pa'i lam ni rjes tshol ba/ /chud zos pa la legs par ston byed ded dpon bzhin/ /ston mdzad de ni bskyod par
<p>50b.2</p>rigs pa ma yin no/ /mun pa chen po sems can chud zos rnams la ni/ /ye shes sgron ma rab tu gsal bar mdzad pa 'di/ /mun pa la ni rab tu 'bar ba'i sgron ma yin/ /'phags pa'i mya ngan 'da' bar byed par 'os ma yin/ /'khor ba'i rnam 'gyur chu bo chen por 'gro ba ni/ /pha rol
<p>50b.3</p>ma thob par ni bying bar gzigs nas ni/ /gang gis de ni sgrol bar byed la rab zhugs te/ /de la sdig pa 'phags pa su yis sems par byed/ /bzod pa'i chu rgyus bstan pa'i rtsa ba brtan pa ste/ /spyod pa'i me tog blo dang dran pa'i yal ga can/ /ye shes ljon shing chos kyi 'bras bu ster ba
<p>50b.4</p>po/ /'phel bzhin pa ni zlog par 'os pa ma yin no/ /gang gi snying la rmongs pa'i zhags pa sra rnams kyis/ /bcings pa'i skye dgu rnams kyi grol phyir blo mnga' zhing / /'gro ba bcings pa thar pa'i ched du 'o brgyal ba/ /de la brdegs pa khyod kyis 'thad pa ma yin no/ /byang chub ched du
<p>50b.5</p>las gang dag na mdzad pa rnams/ /de rnams kyis ni nges par de ring dus yin la/ /ji ltar thub pa snga ma rnams ni de bzhin du/ /gnas der de bzhin 'di ni nye bar bzhugs pa'o/ /dbyig 'dzin sa gzhi yi ni lte ba 'di yin zhing / /snying po dam pa mtha' dag dang ni ldan pa nyid/ /gang zhig 'di yis
<p>50b.6</p>ting nge 'dzin gyi shugs bzod pa'i/ /sa yi phyogs de 'di las gzhan pa yod ma yin/ /de phyir khro bar ma byed zhi bar nyer song la/ /bdud ni khyod kyi drags pas nga rgyal ma gyur cig /dpal ni mi brtan blo gtad par ni nus min zhing / /go 'phang g.yo lnga rgyags par mngon par nyer 'gro
<p>50b.7</p>zhing / /de nas de yi tshig de yang dag thos nas dang / /thub pa chen po'i g.yo ba med pa nyid mthong nas/ /gang gis mda' yis 'gro ba'i snying la rdeg byed pa'i/ /bdud ni 'bad pa bcom zhing yid mi bde bar song / /dga' ba med cing 'bras med ngal ba byas pa rnams/ /pha bong rnams ni khyu
<p>51a</p>
<p>51a.1</p>mchog ljon shing rnams gtor te/ /dgrar gyur dgra bo'i dpung ni gtso bo bsad pa ltar/ /de nas 'di yi dpung ni phyogs phyogs bros pa'o/ /me tog tog can 'khor dang bcas pa bros shing nges par 'pham pa ni/ /drang srong chen po mun pa 'pham zhing rdul dang
<p>51a.2</p>bral ba rgyal ba na/ /rgod pa dang bcas lang tsho ma bzhin zla ba dang bcas mkha' gsal zhing / /chu yi snying po can gyi dri zhim me tog char pa bab par gyur pa'o/ /de ltar sdig pa can ni nges par pham pa ni/ /de tshe phyogs ni rab snang mtshan mor byed pa mdzes/ /mkha' las me tog char
<p>51a.3</p>rnams sa la bab pa ste/ /lang tsho ma bzhin ngal ba med par mtshan mo gsal/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ bdud las rnam par rgyal ba'i le'u ste bcu gsum pa'o// //de nas brtan dang zhi ba yis/ /bdud kyi stobs ni pham mdzad nas/ /
<p>51a.4</p>don dam rnam par mkhyen bzhed pa/ /bsam gtan mkhas de bsam gtan mdzad/ /bsam gtan cho ga thams cad la/ /dbang phyug dam pa rab brnyes nas/ /sngon gyi skye ba rim pa ni/ /dang po'i thun la dran pa'o/ /che ge mo bdag ming 'di ni/ /de nas 'phos te 'dir 'ongs pa'o/ /zhes
<p>51a.5</p>ni skye ba stong phrag rnams/ /rjes su myong ba bzhin du dran/ /'thad pa de dang de rnams su/ /skye bar 'chi ba dran nas ni/ /de nas sems can la thugs rjes/ /thugs rje'i bdag nyid can gyis mdzad/ /rang gi skye bo bor nas ni/ /slar yang gzhan du bya ba rnams/ /nges par 'jig rten
<p>51a.6</p>mgon med 'di/ /'khor lo bzhin du yongs su 'khor/ /de ltar nges pa'i bdag nyid ni/ /de yi dran par gyur pa ste/ /chu shing snying po snying po med/ /'khor ba de ltar nges par ro/ /thun ni gnyis pa byung ba na/ /gnyis med pha rol gnon pa de/ /mig dang ldan pa kun gyi mchog /lha
<p>51a.7</p>yi spyan ni thob par gyur/ /de nas des ni lha yi spyan/ /yongs su dag pa de yis ni/ /me long dri ma med pa ltar/ /'jig rten mtha' dag la gzigs so/ /mchog dang mchog min las rnams kyis/ /sems can rnams kyi 'chi 'pho dang / /skye ba gzigs pa de yis ni/ /thugs rje'i bdag
<p>51b</p>
<p>51b.1</p>nyid 'phel bar gyur/ /'di rnams sdig pa'i las can rnams/ /srog chags rnams ni ngan 'gror 'gro/ /'di gzhan dge ba'i las can rnams/ /mtho ris su ni rab gnas so/ /shin tu mi bzad dmyal ba ru/ /rab tu 'jigs par gyur pa rnams/ /'di rnams sdug bsngal sna tshogs
<p>51b.2</p>kyis/ /kye ma bkren pas gtser par byed/ /kha cig me yi kha dog gi /lcags khu khol ma 'thung bar byed/ /lcags kyi ka ba tshan mo la/ /gzhan rnams cho nges 'debs shing 'dzeg /lcags zangs rnams su khas bub rnams/ /kha cig thug pa bzhin du 'tshed/ /me mdag phung po
<p>51b.3</p>'bar rnams su/ /kha cig snying rje bar sreg go/ /kha cig lcags kyi mche rno can/ /mi bzad khyi rnams kyis za zhing / /kha cig ma rungs lcags mchu can/ /lcags 'dra'i bya rog rnams kyis za/ /kha cig gdung bas yongs ngal rnams/ /bsil ba'i grib ma mngon 'dod pas/ /ral gri'i
<p>51b.4</p>lo ma'i nags sngon por/ /'di rnams bcings pa bzhin du zhugs/ /kha cig sta re rnams kyis ni/ /lag pa bteg rnams shing ltar 'gems/ /las rnams kyis bzung srog rnams ni/ /sdug bsngal na yang rnam mi smin/ /sdug bsngal zlog pa'i don ched du/ /bde ba yin
<p>51b.5</p>zhes las gang byas/ /de yi 'bras de dbang med kyis/ /sdug bsngal kho na nyer longs spyod/ /bde don mi dge ba byas nas/ /gang de shin tu sdug bsngal rnams/ /de dag rnams kyi ro myang des/ /bde ba phra mo yang byed dam/ /sdig pa'i bdag nyid rgod rnams kyis/ /sdig pa'i
<p>51b.6</p>las ni byas pa gang / /de ni mngon du gyur pa'i tshe/ /cho nge rnams kyis rjes su myong / /gal te de ltar sdig las can/ /las kyi 'bras bu mthong ba ste/ /dmigs su mngon par bsnun pa bzhin/ /skyen par khrag ni skyugs pa nyid/ /lus kyi sdug bsngal rnams las dang / /
<p>51b.7</p>dmyal ba'i rnams las sems ldan gyi/ /'phags min rnams dang ldan cig 'grogs/ /ngal ba mchog ni bdag gi lugs/ /gzhan 'di sems kyis rnam g.yo las/ /byung ba'i las rnams sna tshogs kyis/ /byol song skye gnas sna tshogs su/ /nye bar skyes rnams gdung ba
<p>52a</p>
<p>52a.1</p>can/ /sha lpags spu dang so yi phyir/ /chags pa las sam rgyags pa las/ /gnyen 'dun rnams kyis mthong na yang / /gang du snying rje bar gsod do/ /nus med ldan yang dbang med rnams/ /bkres skom ngal bas gtser ba rnams/ /lcags
<p>52a.2</p>kyis bsnun pa'i dbyig can rnams/ /rta dang ba lang gyur rnams 'khol/ /stobs can rnams kyang stobs chung gi /glang por gyur pa rnams 'khol te/ /lcags kyus nyon mongs mgo bo rnams/ /rkang pa'i rting pa rnams kyis btags/ /phan tshun rnam par rtsod las dang / /
<p>52a.3</p>gzhan gyi dbang du gyur nyid kyis/ /sdug bsngal gzhan rnams la yod kyang / /gang la sdug bsngal khyad par ldan/ /phan tshun du ni rab phrad nas/ /ma gnas skam gnas rnams kyis dang / /chur gnas chur gnas rnams kyis dang / /mkhar gnas mkhar gnas rnams kyis
<p>52a.4</p>'joms/ /ser snas non pa'i sems ldan rnams/ /yi dgas 'jig rten snang med du/ /skyes pa 'di rnams de bzhin du/ /bkres pa 'bras bu la longs spyod/ /khab mig lta bu'i kha rnams dang / /ri bo lta bu'i lto ba rnams/ /bkres skom gyis bskyed sdug bsngal gyis/ /
<p>52a.5</p>sdug bsngal skal can rnams gtser to/ /ser sna'i 'bras bu 'di 'dra ba/ /skyes bu gal te shes na ni/ /lus kyi cha shas rnams kyang ni/ /zhi ba bzhin du kun nas gtong / /rang gi las rnams kyis bzung zhing / /sred pas shin tu non pa rnams/ /bor ba'i mi gtsang ba rnams
<p>52a.6</p>kyang / /longs spyod par ni 'dis mi rnyed/ /'di gzhan dmyal ba dang mtshungs pa'i/ /mngal phyin mi gtsang khu ba ru/ /nye bar skyes rnams mi rnams su/ /'gro ba rnams ni sdug bsngal 'thob/ /de sngon skye ba tsam na yang / /lag pa rnon pos bzung ba rnams/ /ral gri rnams
<p>52a.7</p>kyis gshegs pa ltar/ /gang du snying rje bar ni ngu / /byams dang bsrung dang skyong rnams kyi/ /gnyen 'dun rnams kyis 'bad nas sos/ /sdug bsngal las slar sdug bsngal drag /rang rang las kyis nyon mongs so/ /bya ba 'di dang bya ba 'di/ /zhes ni gang du lhag par la/ /
<p>52b</p>
<p>52b.1</p>sred dang yongs ldan byis rnams kyis/ /rgyun chad med par rjes su myong / /'di gzhan bsod nams las rnams kyis/ /mtho ris su ni skyes pa rnams/ /'dod chags me yis drag tu ni/ /me ltar rab tu sreg par byed/ /yul rnams kyis ni ngoms med rnams/ /gang
<p>52b.2</p>las 'di rnams gzi bcom ste/ /phreng ba yongs rnyings zhags pa rnams/ /gyen du mig phyogs rnams lhung ngo / /gang du lha mo rnams kyis ni/ /sdug pa dbang med lhung ba la/ /snying la brtse ba ltos rnams kyis/ /lag pa rnams kyis gos rnams 'dzin/ /gang zhig sa
<p>52b.3</p>la lhung ba bzhin/ /lus 'dud do shal g.yo rnams kyis/ /sdug rnams gzhal med khang rnams nas/ /snying rje dang bcas ltung ba lta/ /rnam pa sna tshogs rgyan phreng can/ /gzhan 'dis sdug bsngal lhung rnams la/ /gdung rnams brtse dang g.yo ba yi/ /lta byed rnams kyi rjes
<p>52b.4</p>su 'gro/ /'dod pa can rnams lhung ba la/ /lag pa rnams kyis brang brdung zhing / /'khrugs chen gyi ltar nyam thag pa/ /lha mo'i tshogs rnams kyis bstan to/ /kyi hud shing rta sna tshogs rdzing / /kyi hud sdug pa gang na zhes/ /nyam thag pa rnams rnam zlos shing / /lha la
<p>52b.5</p>gnas rnams sa la lhung / /las mang rnams kyis thob pa yis/ /mtho ris mi brtan g.yo ba la/ /'bral bas byas pa'i sdug bsngal ni/ /gang du 'di 'dra thob par 'gyur/ /kye ma ded las khyad par du/ /'jig rten mdzad pa'i chos nyid de/ /'dod chags bral ba thob nas
<p>52b.6</p>kyang / /gzhan rnams lha nas nges par lhung / /'di ni rtag par gnas pa ste/ /zhes ni nges pa'i sems ldan rnams/ /'jig rten 'di yi rang bzhin ni/ /'di lta bur ni mthong ma yin/ /dmyal ba rnams su sdug bsngal drag /dud 'gro rnams su phan tshun za/ /bkres
<p>52b.7</p>skom sdug bsngal yi dgas su/ /mi la tshol ba'i sdug bsngal lo/ /lha na sdug pa dang bral bas/ /skyed pa'i sdug bsngal phul byung ste/ /bskor ba gson pa'i 'jig rten gyis/ /gang na zhi ba nges par byed/ /'khor ba'i chu bo rten med du/ /'di ni 'chi bas bskor ba
<p>53a</p>
<p>53a.1</p>ste/ /tsam tsom du ni bskor ba yi/ /'gro bas gnas ni thob ma yin/ /de ltar des ni 'gro ba lnga/ /lha yi spyan gyis gzigs pa ste/ /chu shing gshags pa bzhin du ni/ /srid par snying po rnyed ma yin/ /de nas de yi mtshan mo'i thun/ /gsum
<p>53a.2</p>pa nye bar gnas pa na/ /'jig rten 'di yi rang bzhin ni/ /bsam gtan rig pa mchog gis bsgoms/ /kye ma 'jig rten ngal thob gang / /yang dang yang du skye ba dang / /'khogs pa dang ni 'chi ba dang / /'pho ba dang ni skye ba nyid/ /yang na sdug bsngal che 'di
<p>53a.3</p>las/ /chags las long min gyis bsgribs pa/ /skyes long shin tu dog sa nas/ /phyi rol 'gro ba shes ma yin/ /de ltar bsams pa de yis ni/ /thugs kyis rnam dpyod gyur pa ste/ /gang du gyur na nges sam zhes/ /rga bas 'chi ba mngon par song / /skye gnas nas
<p>53a.4</p>de nyid bsgoms pa/ /de yis mngon par rtogs par gyur/ /rga dang 'chi ba dag gis ni/ /skye ba yod na rdzogs pa'o/ /mgo bo yod na mgo bo yi/ /nad 'di 'byung ba mthong ba ste/ /shing gi skye ba yod gyur na/ /'gyel ba 'byung bar 'gyur ba'o/ /de nas de yi slar gyur pa/ /
<p>53a.5</p>skye ba 'di slar gang la zhes/ /de nas las srid las skye bar/ /skye ba yang dag mkhyen pa'o/ /des ni lha yi spyan gyis ni/ /las las 'jug par mkhyen pa ste/ /dbang phyug las min rang bzhin min/ /bdag las ma yin rgyu med min/ /ji ltar rig pa las gling bu/ /dang po'i tshigs
<p>53a.6</p>ni bcad pa na/ /cho ga bzhin du kun myur 'gro/ /de ltar ye shes go rims so/ /de nas srid pa'i skye ba ni/ /mkhyen phyir thub pas blo gros mdzad/ /de nas srid pa'i skye ba des/ /nye bar len las byung bar mkhyen/ /tshul khrims brtul zhugs mchog 'dzin dang / /'dod blo
<p>53a.7</p>bdag tu lta rnams kyis/ /bud shing rnams kyis me bzhin du/ /'di yis las ni nye bar len/ /gang gi rgyu las len pa zhes/ /de nas de yi gyur pa ste/ /de nas nye bar len pa'i rkyen/ /sred par des ni mkhyen pa'o/ /chung ngu'i me yis nags kyi me/ /rlung gis bud de bskyed pa
<p>53b</p>
<p>53b.1</p>bzhin/ /'dod sogs nyon mongs rgya chen rnams/ /sred pa yis ni skyed par byed/ /de nas de yis bsams pa ni/ /sred pa gang las byung zhes so/ /tshor ba'i rkyen gyis sred pa zhes/ /de nas rnam par nges pa mdzad/ /tshor bas mngon bcom skye dgu rnams/ /gnyen por byed la
<p>53b.2</p>sred pa ste/ /skom pa med na chu la ni/ /kha cig mngon par dga' ba yin/ /de nas slar yang tshor ba yi/ /skye ba'i gnas ni gang zhes bsams/ /tshor ba tshor ba mthar byed kyis/ /reg pa'i rgyu can nyid du mkhyen/ /yul dang dbang po blo rnams kyis/ /'dus pa reg par brjod
<p>53b.3</p>bya ste/ /gtsub shing las ni me bzhin du/ /gang las tshor ba skye ba'o/ /de nas reg pa rgyu yin zhes/ /de yis bsams par gyur pa'o/ /de nas skye mched drug gi ni/ /rgyu can nyid du des mkhyen to/ /long bas gzugs ni mi rig cing / /mig ni blo yis mi sbyor phyir/ /mig yod
<p>53b.4</p>gyur na des sbyor te/ /de phyir dbang po yod na reg /de nas skye mched drug gis ni/ /skye ba mkhyen phyir blo gros mdzad/ /de nas de'i rgyu mid dang gzugs/ /rgyu la mkhas pas mkhyen pa'o/ /ji ltar myu gu yod pa las/ /lo ma sdong bu 'byung bar dran/ /de ltar ming dang gzugs
<p>53b.5</p>yod na/ /skye mched drug ni 'byung ba'o/ /ming dang gzugs ni rgyu gang zhes/ /de yi de nas gyur de nas/ /de yi skye ba rnam shes su/ /ye shes pha rol son pas mkhyen/ /rnam par shes pa 'das pa na/ /ming dang gzugs ni rab gnas te/ /sa bon bskrun pa rdzogs pa na/ /myu gu
<p>53b.6</p>rnam par 'dzin pa'o/ /de nas rnam par shes pa ni/ /gang las yin zhes bsams par gyur/ /ming dang gzugs la brten nas de/ /de nas de yi skye ba mkhyen/ /de nas rgyu yi go rims ni/ /mkhyen nas de yi blor gyur te/ /sems ni lugs 'byung bskor ba ste/ /gzhan du lugs
<p>53b.7</p>las zlog par min/ /rnam par shes pa'i rkyen las ni/ /ming dang gzugs la brten nas ni/ /slar yang rnam par shes pa skye/ /ji ltar gru yis mi 'dren zhing / /de bzhin rnam par shes pa dang / /ming gzugs phan tshun gyi rgyu'o/ /ji ltar lcags ni 'bar ba yis/ /rtswa rnams
<p>54a</p>
<p>54a.1</p>'bar bar byed na yang / /'bar ba de yis de gdung ste/ /de bzhin phan tshun rgyu nyid do/ /de ltar rnam par shes pa las/ /ming gzugs 'byung ba mkhyen gyur pa/ /de nas dbang po 'byung 'gyur zhing / /dbang po las byung reg pa'o/ /reg pa las skyes
<p>54a.2</p>tshor ba mkhyen/ /tshor ba las skyes sred pa'o/ /sred pa las skyes len pa'o/ /len pa las ni de bzhin srid/ /srid pa las ni skye ba dag /skye bas rga shi 'byung bar mkhyen/ /'gro ba dag ni rkyen rnams las/ /skyes zhes yang dag mkhyen pa'o/ /de nas 'di yi
<p>54a.3</p>blo gros nges par song ba ni/ /skye ba zad las 'chi dang rga ba 'gags pa ste/ /srid pa nyams pa las kyang skye ba nyams pa nyid/ /len pa 'gags pa las ni srid pa rnam ldog cing / /de nas srid 'gags pa las de ni 'gag pa ste/ /tshor ba yod pa min na sred pa yod ma yin/ /
<p>54a.4</p>reg las chud zos gyur na tshor ba yod min zhing / /skye mched 'jug pa med las reg pa zad pa'o/ /de bzhin ming dang gzugs ni yang dag 'gags pa las/ /skye mched drug po thams cad rnam par nyams par byed/ /rnam par shes pa 'gags las de dag 'gags
<p>54a.5</p>pa ste/ /'du byed 'gags pa las kyang de ni 'gag pa'o/ /ma rig pa ni mtha' dag med las de bzhin du/ /'du byed 'gag par drang srong chen pos mkhyen pa ste/ /'di las mkhyen bya 'di ni yang dag mkhyen mdzad nas/ /sangs rgyas zhes ni 'jig rten na rab
<p>54a.6</p>gnas par gyur/ /yan lag brgyad dang ldan pa rab tu shar ba yi/ /rtse mor myur 'gro dam pa'i lta ba'i lam gyis ni/ /srid rtse'i bar las mchog gyur bdag med rnam gzigs nas/ /bud shing tshig pa'i me bzhin zhi bar gshegs par gyur/ /de nas bdag nyid mdzad pa de yi
<p>54a.7</p>gyur pa ni/ /mchog gi drang srong mchog dang mchog min mkhyen pa'i tshogs/ /gna' ma rnams kyis don dam rgyu las gshegs pa yi/ /snying po'i lam 'di bdag gis lhag par thob par gyur/ /thun ni bzhi pa'i skya rengs shar ba'i yud tsam na/ /rgyu dang mi rgyu'i 'byung po rnams ni zhi
<p>54b</p>
<p>54b.1</p>ba na/ /drang srong mchog gis 'gyur ba med pa'i go 'phang dang / /kun gyi mgon gyis thams cad mkhyen pa nyid brnyes so/ /de nyid 'di ni sangs rgyas nyid kyis mkhyen pa na/ /bud med chang gis myos bzhin sa ni g.yos gyur la/ /grub pa rnams kyis mngon gang phyogs ni rab
<p>54b.2</p>snang ste/ /mkha' la rnga bo che rnams rab tu grag par gyur/ /dge ba'i rlung rnams rab tu zhi bar g.yos gyur zhing / /sprin med 'o ma rnams ni lha yis char phab ste/ /ljon shing rnams la dus min me tog 'bras bu rnams/ /mchod pa rab tu sbyor ba'i ched bzhin brul bar
<p>54b.3</p>gyur/ /man dA ra ba'i me tog rnams dang pad+ma dang / /gser dang bai DUr+ya yi rang bzhin pad+ma ni/ /mkha' las bab pa rnams kyis shAkya thub pa'i sa/ /de tshe mtho ris bzhin du kun nas bkram par gyur/ /yud tsam de ni kha cig khro ba med gyur la/ /nad med gyur zhing mi
<p>54b.4</p>dga' bar yang ma song ste/ /sdig pa bsnyen pa ma yin rgyags par ma byas shing / /grub pa brnyes pa bzhin du 'jig rten zhi bar gyur/ /thar pa 'dod pa'i lha yi tshogs rnams dga' ba ste/ /sems can 'og tu song ba rnams kyang dga' bar gyur/ /yon tan phyogs kyis
<p>54b.5</p>'phel bas chos ni rgyas pa ste/ /rdul dang mun pa dag las 'gro ba gyen du byung / /de yi las kyis ya mtshan dga' bas gang ba yi/ /bu ram shing pa'i rigs kyi mi skyong drang srong rnams/ /rgyal po'i drang srong rnams dang drang srong che rnams kyis/ /yang dag mchod rnams
<p>54b.6</p>mkha' la gzhal med rnams su gnas/ /mthong min 'byung po'i tshogs kyis drang srong chen po yi/ /ston pa rnams ni mthon por 'thon zhing sgrogs pa ste/ /gson pa'i 'jig rten 'phel ba bzhin du dga' gyur zhing / /ltung ba mchog la bzhin du bdud ni yi mug cing / /de nas
<p>54b.7</p>nad mi mnga' ba zhag bdun bdag nyid kyis/ /sems la gzigs shing spyan mi 'dzums par bzhugs pa ste/ /kho bos 'dir ni rnam par thar pa brnyes so zhes/ /thub pas yid la re ba yongs su rdzogs par gyur/ /de nas rkyen nyid thob pa 'di ni thub pa nyid/ /bdag med
<p>55a</p>
<p>55a.1</p>cho gar rnam par gzhag pas gsan nas ni/ /zhi phyir 'jig rten dag la mchog tu brtse bas so/ /sangs rgyas spyan gyis rnam par gzigs par gyur pa'o/ /lta ba ngan pas chud zos 'bad la 'khrugs pa yi/ /'gro ba rdul ni rgya chen dang ldan
<p>55a.2</p>gzigs nas dang / /rnam thar chos ni mchog tu phra pa nyid gzigs nas/ /g.yo ba med pa nyid phyir thugs ni mdzad par gyur/ /de nas sngon gyi dam bca' yang dag mkhyen gyur nas/ /zhi ba'i gdams pa la ni so sor nges par gshegs/ /de nas chen po'i rdul dang
<p>55a.3</p>chung ngu'i rdul nyid dang / /ldan pa'i skye bor yid ni rnam par dpyad pa'o/ /de nas zhi ba'i don du gdams pa'i ched du nges par ni/ /gzung ba'i bde bar gshegs pa'i thugs ni shes gyur nas/ /mngon par snang zhing 'gro la phan par 'dod pa can/ /mtho ris
<p>55a.4</p>gnas pa'i gtso bo nyid ni nye bar 'ongs/ /sdig pa spangs shing don mdzad gdan la bzhugs pa po/ /mchog gi chos ni gzigs pa de la mchog gnyis so/ /mchog tu zhi bas rab tu bstod nas de gnyis kyis/ /'jig rten phan pa'i don du tshig 'di gsol ba'o/ /e
<p>55a.5</p>ma 'gro ba 'di gang nor 'os 'di lta bu/ /skye dgu rnams la rjes su brtse mdzad khyed kyi thugs/ /'jig rten na yod skye bo rnam par bsre ma'i rgyu/ /chen po'i rdul dang nyung ngu'i rdul nyid ldan pa'o/ /thub pa srid pa'i mtsho las rang nyid rab rgal nas/ /'gro ba sdug bsngal
<p>55a.6</p>bying ba rab tu drongs mdzod cig /legs pa'i dbang phyug gis ni phun sum tshogs pa thob nas bzhin/ /gzhan rnams la yang rang gi yon tan gyis sbyor mdzod/ /don mkhyen 'di na'i don dang pha rol du 'am gang / /skye bo kha cig 'di na bdag gi phan pa byed/ /gang
<p>55a.7</p>zhig 'jig rten dge ba'i ched du rab zhugs de/ /mi yi 'jig rten dang ni mtho ris su rnyed dka'/ /de ltar drang srong che la tshig 'di gsol nas ni/ /lha na gnas pa de gnyis ji ltar 'ongs par gshegs/ /thub pa yis kyang de yi tshig de rab mnod nas/ /'gro ba rnam par thar
<p>55b</p>
<p>55b.1</p>phyir nges par rgyas par mdzad/ /de nas bsod snyoms dus su phyogs bzhir drang srong la/ /lha na gnas pas lhung bzed rnams ni phul ba ste/ /gau ta mas bzhi po de rnams rab bzhes nas/ /de yi chos kyi ched du gcig nyid mdzad pa'o/ /de nas de tshe don bcas rab song
<p>55b.2</p>tshong dpon gnyis/ /mdza' bshes nyid kyis lha yis rab tu bskul ba dag /rgya chen thugs mnga' drang srong che la thog ma ru/ /dga' ba dang ldan phyag byas nas ni bsod snyoms phul/ /rtsibs 'phur dang ni rangs byed bu ste de gnyis ni/ /chos 'dzin nus pa'i blo gros
<p>55b.3</p>thub pas gzigs pa ste/ /de gnyis lha na gshegs par thugs kyis mngon gzigs nas/ /dge slong lnga po rnams la thugs kyis gshegs pa'o/ /de nas zhi ba'i gdams pa las ni gau ta mas/ /nyi ma shar bas mun bzhin mun pa rnam 'joms phyir/ /bA rA Na sIs
<p>55b.4</p>brgyan pa'i sna tshogs nags tshal can/ /'jigs byed shing rtas bsnyen pa'i grong khyer dge bar gshegs/ /de nas khyu mchog 'dra ba'i spyan mnga' glang chen myos pa'i 'gros ldan pa/ /'gro ba mngon par rnam par 'dus phyir kA shi sa la gshegs bzhed pa/ /glang chen bzhin du
<p>55b.5</p>rang gi sku lus ma lus phyir la rab log nas/ /thub pas spyan mig mi 'dzums par ni byang chub shing gi rtsa bar gzigs/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i le'u ste bcu bzhi pa'o// //zhi
<p>55b.6</p>zhing mdangs ldan mdzad pa kun nas brnyes pa de/ /gcig pur rab gshegs mang po dang ni thabs cig bzhin/ /lam na dge slong chos ldan kha cig gis mthong nas/ /ya mtshan dang bcas thal mor bcas pas 'di skad gsol/ /dbang po'i rta ni g.yo bar dbang po'i rta thul zhing / /
<p>55b.7</p>sems can chags rnams ji ltar chags ma gyur/ /shin tu ro ldan gsar pa'i shes rab ro yis ni/ /ri bong gis mtshon dang mtshungs tshim par gyur pa rnams/ /brtan pa khyod kyi zhal ni ji ltar rab rgyas shing / /'dir ni dbang po rnams kyi dbang phyug mdzad pa ste/ /khyu mchog chen
<p>56a</p>
<p>56a.1</p>po'i spyan mnga' nges par don mdzad cing / /khyod kyi bla ma su lags gang las grub pa gsungs/ /de rnams la des smras pa bdag la ston pa med/ /bdag la mchod bya med cing smad bya su yang med/ /mya ngan 'das pa thob cing gzhan rnams dang mi
<p>56a.2</p>mnyam/ /bdag ni chos la rang byung du ni shes par mdzod/ /gang phyir gzhan rnams kyis ma rtogs pa'i rtogs bya ni/ /bdag gis mtha' dag rtogs pa de phyir sangs rgyas te/ /gang phyir bdag gi nyon mongs rnams ni dgra bzhin 'pham/ /de phyir zhi ba dag ni kun nas
<p>56a.3</p>shes bar mdzod/ /sdug bsngal rnams kyis nyam thag grogs la phan don du/ /zhi ba kho bo 'di yang bA rA Na sIr 'gro/ /der ni 'chi med chos kyi rnga dag rdung ba ste/ /snyan grags bde ba'i phyir min nga rgyal phyir ma yin/ /rgal bas 'gro ba rnams ni rgal bar 'gyur bgyi zhing / /
<p>56a.4</p>grol bas sems can rnams ni yongs su thar bar bgyi/ /de ltar gson pa'i 'jig rten nyam thag par mthong nas/ /sngon du bdag gi dam bca' 'di ni gyur pa'o/ /'di na kha cig nor ni thob nas bdag nyid ni/ /gcig tu nyid kyang 'dzin par byed pa ngo mtshar cing / /skye bo chen po ma
<p>56a.5</p>btsums mig la gang gis kyang / /khyad 'phags thob nas rnam par 'dzin pa de don yin/ /gang zhig skam la gnas pas mi ni chus khyer ba/ /'dren par 'dod min de ni legs pa'i gzugs ma yin/ /gang zhig gter ni thob nas skye bo dbul po la/ /nor gyi sbyor
<p>56a.6</p>ba med pa de ni spyang po min/ /rang bzhin gnas pas nad kyis mngon par bcom pa la/ /lag tu song ba'i sman gyis gso bar rigs pa ste/ /de ltar lam ngan song ba'i ched du lam dag ni/ /nges par byad ba'i lam gyis bshad par 'thad pa yin/ /ji ltar sgron ma rab tu gsal
<p>56a.7</p>bar byed pa ste/ /de yi rgyu can dmar por 'gro ba ma yin nyid/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas nyid kyis ye shes rab gsal bar/ /mdzad de de phyir chags par 'gro ba ma yin no/ /ji ltar shing rnams la ni me dag nges pa dang / /mkha' la rlung dang sa la chu ni nges pa ste/ /de bzhin
<p>56b</p>
<p>56b.1</p>gang yang rnams su thub pa rnams kyis ni/ /byang chub nges shing kA shi rnams dang chos smra des/ /de nas nye bar 'ongs nas a la la zhes pa/ /rnam par brjod nas ji ltar 'dod bzhin rab spangs nas/ /yang dang yang du ya mtshan mig ni g.yo ba yis/ /re 'dod skyes shing
<p>56b.2</p>sangs rgyas la ni lta bzhin song / /de nas thub pas rim gyis kA si'i grong khyer ni/ /nor gnas snying po dang ni rab mtshungs gzigs pa ste/ /grogs mo bzhin du 'khyud nas yang dag 'dus pa ni/ /skal ldan shing rta dang ni bA rA Na sI nyid/ /mthu dang gzi brjid dag gis mngon par
<p>56b.3</p>mdzes pa des/ /khu byug rnams kyis sgra sgrogs shing gi tshogs ldan zhing / /drang srong chen pos bsnyen pa'i ri dgas nags nyid du/ /rnam par mdzes pas nyi ma bzhin du rab 'thob po/ /kauN+Di n+ya'i rigs dang de nas ming chen dang / /rlangs pa dang ni rta thul de bzhin bzang rgyal te/ /dge
<p>56b.4</p>slong lnga yis de ni rgyang ring nas gzigs nas/ /phan tshun du ni tshig 'di smras par gyur pa'o/ /bde ba'i bdag nyid dge slong gau ta ma 'di/ /dka' thub de las phyir log mngon par 'ongs pa ste/ /mngon du 'gro bya ma yin nges par phyag 'os min/ /dam bca' bcom pa mchod par
<p>56b.5</p>'os pa ma yin no/ /de ni brgya la gal te sdod par 'dod gyur na/ /de nyid la ni gtam 'di rab tu gsol mdzod dang / /'gron po nye bar 'ongs pa gang dang su la ni/ /'phags pa rnams kyis mi byed par ni 'os ma yin/ /de ltar bya ba byas nas dge slong de rnams ni/ /nye bar
<p>56b.6</p>gnas pa'i nye bar sangs rgyas gshegs pa ste/ /ji lta ji ltar de rnams la ni nye bar gshegs/ /de lta de ltar de rnams dam bca' nyams par gyur/ /de nas kha cig 'di yi na bza' blangs pa ste/ /de bzhin gzhan ni phyag 'tshal nas ni lhung bzed bzung / /kha cig 'di la 'os
<p>56b.7</p>pa'i gdan ni phul ba ste/ /de bzhin gzhan gnyis zhabs bsil nye bar phul bu'o/ /de ltar rab byed mchod pa mang po ldan pa rnams/ /'di la thams cad kyis ni bla mar spyod pa byas/ /rigs su mngon brjod de rnams kyis kyang ma spangs shing / /de rnams la rjes brtse bcas
<p>57a</p>
<p>57a.1</p>bcom ldan gyis smras pa/ /mchod 'os dgra bcom la ni gus pa ma yin pas/ /sngar gyi spyod pas dge slong rnams kye ma smra shig /bstod dang smad pa nges par bdag gis mnyam pa ste/ /khyed rnams bsod nams min las rnam par bzlog par bgyi/ /sangs
<p>57a.2</p>rgyas 'jig rten phan pa'i ched du sangs rgyas shing / /'byung po kun la phan pas rab tu zhugs pa la/ /bla ma nye bar 'joms las ming gis gang smras de/ /ma rungs pa yi pha ma bzhin du chos 'chad do/ /de ltar drang srong chen po'i thugs rje'i bdag nyid can/ /smra ba rnams kyi mchog gis
<p>57a.3</p>de skad gsungs pa ste/ /rmongs las snying po med pas chud zos de rnams kyis/ /gdong ni cung zad bzhad pa dang ldan rgol ba smras pa'o/ /gau ta ma re zhig dka' thub mchog dang ni/ /dam pa de yis de nyid rtogs pa ma yin te/ /don ni dga' bas bsgrub bya bde bas gnas pa'o/ /
<p>57a.4</p>khyed kyis mthong zhes bya ba 'dir ni gtan tshigs gang / /gang tshe de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i de nyid la/ /de nas dge slong de rnams dad par gyur min te/ /byang chub pa yi lam ni de las gzhan du shes/ /de nas lam mkhyen pa yis lam ni bka' stsal pa/ /byis pa'i skye bo
<p>57a.5</p>bdag nyid ngal bar ldan pa dang / /dbang po'i spyod yul rnams la de bzhin chags pa ste/ /'chi ba med pa'i lung gis lam ma yin pa'i phyogs/ /skyon dang ldan pa gnyis po de la ltos mdzod cig /gdung bar mngon par brjod pa'i lus kyi ngal rnams kyis/ /yongs su
<p>57a.6</p>'khrugs shing rnam par gnod pa'i sems la ni/ /'jig rten tha snyad kyang ni brgya la shes min na/ /dbang po las 'das de nyid lam ni kye ma ci/ /ji ltar sgron mas mtshan mo'i mun pa nyams pa ru/ /'dir ni mngon par nyer 'gro chu rnams gtor bas min/ /de bzhin ye
<p>57a.7</p>shes mi yis mi shes mun pa ni/ /nyams par sngon 'gro lus kyi ngal ba rnams kyis min/ /ji ltar me ni 'dod pas shing la 'bigs pa dang / /rnam par 'gems pas me ni thob pa ma yin la/ /de nyid mngon pa'i thabs las bsrubs pas thob pa ste/ /de bzhin sbyor las 'chi
<p>57b</p>
<p>57b.1</p>ba med thob ngal bas min/ /de ltar don med 'dod pa rnams la chags pa ni/ /rdul dang mun pa dag gis zil non sems ldan rnams/ /bstan bcos don la nus kyang grub pa thob min na/ /chags bral 'gog pa'i cho ga la ni sngon nyid do/ /ji ltar nad kyis mngon par bcom pa'i
<p>57b.2</p>srog chags kyis/ /mi phan bza' ba za ba'i gso ba 'dir yod min/ /de bzhin mi shes nad kyis mngon par bcom pa yi/ /'dod pa rnams la chags pa'i zhi ba gang las so/ /ji ltar skam pa'i rten la gnas pa'i rlung gis ni/ /bus pa'i me yi zhi ba yod pa ma yin no/ /
<p>57b.3</p>de bzhin 'dod pa'i rten la gnas pa'i chags pa yis/ /rjes su song ba'i sems kyi zhi ba yod ma yin/ /mtha' 'di gnyis po dag kyang rnam par dor byas nas/ /bdag gis lam gzhan dbu mas lhag par rtogs pa ste/ /shin tu sdug bsngal nye bar zhi ba'i 'dren pa po/ /bde
<p>57b.4</p>ba dang ni dge ba nyid dang bral ba'o/ /yang dag lta ba'i nyi mas rab tu gsal byas shing / /rnam dag yang dag rtogs pa'i shing rtas drangs pa ste/ /yang dag brjod pa'i yang dag dag ni gtsug lag khang / /dge ba'i bya ba'i skyed tshal brgya phrag mngon par dga'/ /smad pa med pa'i
<p>57b.5</p>'tsho ba lo legs chen po ste/ /yang dag rtsol bas stobs rab rjes su 'gro ba can/ /kun du yang dag dran pa'i sbas pas sbas pa ste/ /ting 'dzin gzims mal dang ni gdan dang khyab pa yis/ /de ltar mchog gi yan lag brgyad 'dir 'di lam ste/ /'chi dang rga dang na ba
<p>57b.6</p>rnams las 'dren pa po/ /gang la drangs nas bya ba thams cad byas pa ste/ /'di dang che ge mor ni slan chad 'gro ba med/ /'di ni sdug bsngal mtha' dag 'di ni mtshan ma ste/ /'di ni 'gog pa 'di yi lam ni 'di yin te/ /de ltar ma thos chos kyi cho ga sngar med pa'i/ /rnam par mthar phyin
<p>57b.7</p>bdag gi spyan mig skye ba'o/ /skye dang rga dang na dang de nas rgud pa dang / /sdug pa dang bral mi sdug pa la sbyor ba dang / /'dod pa'i don ni rab tu 'thob pa med pa ste/ /rnam pa sna tshogs sdug bsngal 'di ni yongs su 'thob/ /'dod pa'i bdag can gyi 'am bdag rgyal can gyi 'am/ /lus
<p>58a</p>
<p>58a.1</p>can gyi 'am yang na lus can ma yin pa'i/ /gang zhig yon tan med pa gang la rab zhugs kyang / /mdor bsdus nas de sdug bsngal du ni shes par mdzod/ /de ltar 'bar ba zhi ba'i me ni chung na yang / /lhan cig skyes pa dro ba'i ngo bo spong min nyid/ /de bzhin bdag tu
<p>58a.2</p>'du shes zhi sogs kyis phra yang / /sdug bsngal bdag nyid can zhes bdag gi shin tu nges/ /ji ltar sa chu sa bon dus rnams myu gu'i bzhin/ /'dod chags la sogs rnam pa sna tshogs skyon rnams dang / /skyon las rab tu skyes pa'i las rnams nyid dag ni/ /sdug bsngal dag gi rgyur ni
<p>58a.3</p>nges par shes par mdzod/ /mtho ris su 'am 'og tu srid pa'i rgyun las ni/ /'dod chags la sogs skyon gyi tshogs rnams rgyu yin zhing / /dman dang 'bring dang mchog ste sna tshogs nyid kyi ni/ /de dang der ni las rnams dag ni rtsa ba'o/ /nyes pa zad las 'khor ba'i rgyun ni yod min te/ /las
<p>58a.4</p>zad pa las sdug bsngal de ni yod ma yin/ /gang phyir don gang yong pa las ni kun 'byung ste/ /de phyir med pa las te slar yang 'byung ba med/ /gang du skye ba med cing rga med 'chi ba med/ /me med sa med chu med mkha' med rlung med la/ /thog ma bar dang mtha' med 'phags pa dbrog bya min/ /
<p>58a.5</p>dge zhing 'gyur med 'gog pa de ni shes par mdzod/ /yan lag brgyad ldan gang zhig mngon brjod de lam ste/ /lhag par rtogs phyir 'di yi thabs de'i gzhan ma yin/ /lam 'di yin na ma mthong ba las 'jig rten rnams/ /de nyid dang ni nye du rnams ni yongs su 'khor/ /sdug bsngal
<p>58a.6</p>yongs su shes par bya zhing rgyu 'di ni/ /spang bya 'gog pa yang ni dbang du bya ba'o/ /de bzhin lam 'di yang ni bsgom par bya ba ste/ /de ltar 'di ni bdag gi blo gros rab zhugs so/ /sdug bsngal 'di ni yongs shes rgyu ni spangs pa ste/ /de bzhin du ni 'gog pa mngon du byas pa'o/ /de bzhin du
<p>58a.7</p>ni 'di yi lam 'di bsgoms pa ste/ /de ltar 'dir ni bdag gi spyan mig rab zhugs so/ /ji srid du ni yang dag 'phags pa'i bden pa ni/ /bzhi ba'i rkang pa 'di rnams mthong ba ma yin pa/ /de srid bdag 'dir grol ba med pa zhes brjod cing / /bdag nyid la ni don byas nyid du yang ma
<p>58b</p>
<p>58b.1</p>mthong / /gang tshe 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams ni rtogs pa ste/ /rtogs byas kyang ni dor byar 'os pa byas pa'o/ /de tshe bdag 'dir rnam par grol zhes brjod pa ste/ /bdag nyid la ni don byas nyid du yang mthong ngo / /de ltar drang srong chen po thugs rje mnga' ba yis/ /'dir
<p>58b.2</p>ni chos dag de skad mngon par gsungs pa na/ /kauN+Di n+ya'i rigs dang lha ni brgya phrag rnams/ /gtsang zhing rdul dang bral ba'i mig ni thob par gyur/ /bya ba thams cad nges par byas shing zhi ba de la ni/ /thams cad mkhyen pas khyu mchog bzhin du mthon po'i dbyangs kyis gsungs/ /
<p>58b.3</p>khyod kyis shes shes bdag nyid chen po des ni tshig gsol pa/ /legs so khyod kyi blo gros mchog ni bdag gis shes pa'o/ /legs so bdag gis shes shes de nas des ni 'jig rten ni/ /kauN+Di n+yas de yi go 'phang rigs ni bzung ba ste/ /bla ma dam pa de bzhin gshegs
<p>58b.4</p>pa'i slob ma rnams kyis ni/ /gtso bo nyid du chos la yang dag lhag par gshegs pa'o/ /sgra de sa la rgyu ba'i gnod sbyin rnams kyis thos nas ni/ /rnam par rgyas pa'i dbyangs 'di rab tu gsol bar gyur pa ste/ /'byung po rnams kyi 'chi med zhi ba'i ched du nges par ni/ /
<p>58b.5</p>dam pa gzigs pas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba de legs so/ /tshul khrims rtsibs dang zhi dang dul ba'i mu khyud blo rnams yangs/ /dran pas blo gros brtan pa brtson 'grus lta ba ngo tsha'i gzer/ /zab pa'i phyir dang brdzun med phyir dang legs par bstan nyid phyir/ /
<p>58b.6</p>'jig rten gsum na brtan zhing bstan bcos gzhan rnams kyis mi ldog /sa 'dzin gnod sbyin rnams las sgra ni nye bar thob byas nas/ /mkha' la lha yi tshogs rnams kyis ni dbyangs byas shing / /de ltar thos nas mtho ris rim dang rim rnams kyis mthon por/ /tshangs
<p>58b.7</p>pa'i 'jig rten bar du sgra yis nye bar 'dzegs pa'o/ /mtho ris dag na gnas pa'i bdag nyid ldan pa kha cig gis/ /drang srong che las 'jig rten gsum ni g.yo zhes thos nas ni/ /sna tshogs yul rnams la ni chags par gshegs pa ma yin zhing / /yang dag skyo las
<p>59a</p>
<p>59a.1</p>srid pa gsum na zhi ba nyid du gshegs/ /de ltar 'jig rten rnams kyi mchog tu zhi ba'i ched du ni/ /mtho ris dang ni sa na chos kyi 'khor lo bskor tsam na/ /sprin bral mkha' las me tog dang bcas chu yi char bab cing / /srid gsum gnas pa
<p>59a.2</p>rnams kyis rnga bo che rnams mngon par brdungs/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i le'u ste bco lnga pa'o// //de nas thams cad mkhyen pa yis/ /rta thul la sogs dge slong rnams/ /
<p>59a.3</p>rab snyoms sems ldan de rnams kun/ /thar pa'i chos la bkod pa'o/ /nyi ma dang ldan skar ma lngas/ /nam mkhar zla ba ldan pa bzhin/ /lnga sde pham pa'i lnga sde yis/ /kun nas bskor ba de mdzes so/ /de nas de tshe kha cig ni/ /mo rnams glos phab nyal mthong
<p>59a.4</p>nas/ /grags pa zhes bya chen po'i bu/ /yang dag skyo bar nye bar song / /'di kun nye bar mdzes pa ste/ /zhes ni tshig dang brjod bzhin du/ /dpal ldan mchog gi rgyan ldan pa/ /sangs rgyas ga la ba der song / /sems dang nyon mongs mkhyen pas de/ /gzigs
<p>59a.5</p>nas de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs/ /mya ngan 'das la nyer 'tshe med/ /tshur shog dge ba thob par gyis/ /de ltar rnam rgyas grags pa'i gsung / /'di ni thos nas tsha ba yis/ /nyam thag chu la 'dzul nas dang / /mchog tu tshim pa nye bar 'ong / /sngon gyi
<p>59a.6</p>rgyu yi stobs brten nas/ /de nas lus de nyid bzung ste/ /lus kyis dang ni sems kyis ni/ /dgra bcom nyid ni nye bar thob/ /ston ka'i chu yis bkrus pa yi/ /gos la tshon ni bkod pa bzhin/ /dkar po'i blo yis dam pa'i chos/ /thos nas rab tu rtogs pa
<p>59a.7</p>nyid/ /cha lugs de yis ngo tsha bzhin/ /gnas pa de ni gzigs gyur na/ /don mdzad dam pa'i don mkhyen pa/ /smra ba rnams kyi mchog gis smras/ /rtags ni chos kyi rgyu min zhing / /'byung po rnams la snyoms pa ste/ /zhi zhing dul la dbang po dul/ /brgyan pa yin
<p>59b</p>
<p>59b.1</p>yang chos la spyod/ /gang zhig lus ni 'thon pa ste/ /sems kyis 'thon pa ma yin pa/ /nags na gnas kyang chags pa can/ /khyim na gnas shes de shes bya/ /gang zhig sems ni 'thon pa ste/ /lus kyis 'thon pa ma yin pa/ /khyim na gnas kyang nga med
<p>59b.2</p>pa/ /nags na gnas shes de shes bya/ /khyim na gnas par gyur pa'i lam/ /rab tu byung bar gyur pa'i yang / /gang gis bsgrub pa yod na ni/ /de yi thar pa mngon par brjod/ /ji ltar rgyal 'dod dgra sde la/ /rgyal phyir go cha 'dzin pa ste/ /de bzhin nyon mongs dgra
<p>59b.3</p>de la/ /rgyal phyir rtags ni 'dren pa'o/ /de nas dge slong tshur shog ces/ /de bzhin gshegs pas de la gsungs/ /des ni dge slong rtags bzung ste/ /skad cig de nyid kyis grol to/ /de nas de yi rjes chags pas/ /de yi 'khor ni lnga bcu dang / /gsum rnams
<p>59b.4</p>nyid dang gcig nyid dang / /chos de rab tu thob par gyur/ /'dag chal gyis bsgos gos rnams ni/ /chu yis yang dag reg pa bzhin/ /sngon tshe bsgoms pa'i las can rnams/ /de rnams myur du dag par gyur/ /de nas de tshe dgra bcom slob ma yi/ /dang po don byas
<p>59b.5</p>drug cu thams cad la/ /dgra bcom rnams kyis mngon mchod dgra bcom pas/ /ji ltar 'os par yang dag bka' stsal to/ /dge slong rnams kyis sdug bsngal rgal/ /rang gi bya ba legs chen byas/ /pha rol sdug bsngal rnams la yang / /rjes su 'dzin par byed pa'i
<p>59b.6</p>rigs/ /de phyir re re thams cad kyis/ /sa 'dir yongs su gshegs mdzod la/ /nyam thag 'jig rten ched du chos/ /rjes su brtse bas bstan par bya/ /grub phyir rdzu 'phrul ldan pa'i sbun/ /'od srungs drang srong rnams 'dul phyir/ /rgyal po'i drang srong gis bsnyen pa'i/ /ga
<p>59b.7</p>yar kho bo 'di yang 'gro/ /de nas de nyid mthong de rnams/ /de yi bka' las phyogs su song / /rtsod bral bde bar gshegs pa ni/ /drang srong che yang ga yar gshegs/ /de nas dus su der gshegs nas/ /chos kyi dgon par nye bar gshegs/ /dka' thub dngos su gnas
<p>60a</p>
<p>60a.1</p>pa bzhin/ /der ni 'od srungs gzigs pa'o/ /ri rnams dang ni nags rnams su/ /gnas rnams yod pa na yang de/ /rnam par 'dul bzhed stobs bcu bas/ /rab tu brten nas bslangs pa'o/ /de nas grub pa nyams tshad phyir/ /me khang lto 'phye ches
<p>60a.2</p>bsnyen par/ /ma rungs gnas des 'di la byin/ /der gzims mtshan mor rang gnas shing / /ltos bral thub ba chen po la/ /mthong ba'i dug can khros pa yi/ /sprul des mthong nas dbugs phyung ngo / /de yi khro bas 'bar ba yi/ /me yi khang par gyur pa des/ /drang srong
<p>60a.3</p>chen po'i sku lus la/ /'jigs pa bzhin du mes ma reg /dus mtha'i me nyer zhi ba na/ /tshangs pa bzhugs pa mdzes pa ltar/ /me yi khang par bsregs na yang / /gau ta ma rnam 'gyur med/ /gang tshe sangs rgyas der bzhugs tshe/ /gnod med g.yo ba med pa ste/ /de tshe
<p>60a.4</p>klu de ya mtshan zhing / /drang srong mchog la phyag 'tshal lo/ /ri dgas nags der skye bo yis/ /thub pa der bzhugs shes gyur nas/ /srugs pa 'o brgyal 'di 'dra ba'i/ /dge slong tshig ces rjes su brtse/ /de nas mtshan mo 'das pa na/ /rnam par 'dren pas 'od srungs la/ /sbrul
<p>60a.5</p>ni zhi bas lhung bzed kyis/ /blangs nas de la bstan pa'o/ /de nas sangs rgyas che bdag nyid/ /thos nas de ni ya mtshan gyur/ /de lta na yang bdag nyid kyis/ /che zhing gong na med pa snyam/ /de nas dus su rab sbyar ba'i/ /sna tshogs rdzu 'phrul gzugs rnams kyis/ /de yi sems de
<p>60a.6</p>mkhyen nyid las/ /zhi ldan thub pas thugs dgongs mdzad/ /ji ltar bdag las rdzu 'phrul gyis/ /sangs rgyas khyad par 'phags pa snyam/ /de yi chos ni rab sgrub phyir/ /de tshe nges ni nges par byas/ /kun nas slar log gnas pa yis/ /lteng rgyas 'od srungs mthong nas ni/ /slob ma rnams
<p>60a.7</p>kyi tshogs rnams kyang / /lnga brgyas de yi chos la bsnyen/ /der ni spun zla slob mar bcas/ /mthar phyin shun lpags spangs pa na/ /ga ya chu klung zhes byas kyang / /der song lam la bsnyen pa'o/ /de nas thub pas slob mar bcas/ /'od srungs gsum po de rnams la/ /sa 'dzin ga ya'i rtse mor
<p>60b</p>
<p>60b.1</p>ni/ /nges par mthar phyin gtam mdzad do/ /rnam par rtog pa'i skye gnas dang / /gti mug rnam bkram du ba can/ /chags sdang me yis 'gro ba ni/ /thams cad dbang med par bsreg go/ /de ltar nyon mongs mes tshig cing / /rab tu ma zhi mgon med can/ /rga na 'chi ba'i me rnams
<p>60b.2</p>kyis/ /slar yang rgyun mi chad par sreg /rnam pa sna tshogs mes tshig pa'i/ /'gro ba skyabs med 'di mthong nas/ /yid bcas dbang po dang bcas pa'i/ /gzugs la blo ldan skyo ba ste/ /skyo ba las ni chags bral ro/ /chags bral las ni rnam grol zhing / /rnam grol de nas thams cad
<p>60b.3</p>na/ /rnam par grol zhes shes pa'o/ /skye ba'i rgyun ni yongs 'dzad cing / /tshangs pa'i spyod pa 'dir gnas la/ /byed pa thams cad byas pa ste/ /sred pa gzhan ni yod ma yin/ /bcom ldan gyi gsung 'di thos nas/ /dge slong stong phrag dag gi sems/ /len pa med nas zag pa las/ /
<p>60b.4</p>de ma thag tu rnam par grol/ /sbyin pa tshul khrims dul rnams kyis/ /chos ni yongs su yongs bskor bzhin/ /de nas shes rab rgya che ba'i/ /'od srungs gsum gyis sangs rgyas mdzes/ /chos don 'dod pa dang bral ba'i/ /sems can ngan pa'i srog bzhin du/ /bgres mchog de rnams kyis
<p>60b.5</p>bor ba'i/ /dka' thub nags de mdzes ma gyur/ /de nas de rnams kyis yongs bskor/ /thub pa rgyal po'i khab tu gshegs/ /ma ga d+hA yi mi dbang phyir/ /sngon gyi dam bca' dran pa'o/ /de nas 'od ma'i tshal yul ni/ /de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu thob/ /blon po rnams ni rjes 'gro bas/ /
<p>60b.6</p>thos nas rgyas po sngon du song / /de nas rang gi skal mtshungs pa'i/ /rkang pa bzhon pas skye bo ni/ /ya mtshan gyis ni rnam yangs mig /ri yi lam nas phyi rol byung / /ma ga d+hA yi mi dbang gis/ /thub mchog rgyang ma nas mthong nas/ /skyen pa dang bcas mchod pa'i phyir/ /shing rta
<p>60b.7</p>las ni sa la babs/ /des ni rnga yab rlung yab dang / /rjes su 'brang ba rnam spangs nas/ /tshangs pa la ni dbang pos bzhin/ /thub pa rgyal po sngon du song / /cod pan rab g.yo mgo bo yis/ /drang srong mchog la phyag 'tshal nas/ /sa yi logs la rtswa 'jam la/ /mngon par rjes gnang
<p>61a</p>
<p>61a.1</p>bsdad pa'o/ /der mi rnams kyis bsams par gyur/ /e ma shAkya thub pa'i stobs/ /'od srungs bcom ldan drang srong ni/ /'di yi slob ma nyid du song / /de nas de'i sems sangs rgyas kyis/ /mkhyen nas 'od srungs la smras pa/ /'od srungs yon tan gang mthong nas/ /
<p>61a.2</p>khyed kyis me ni spangs pa'o/ /chu sbyin chen po'i dbyangs kyis ni/ /bla mas de ltar de bskul te/ /mthon pos skye bo kun khyab par/ /thal mo sbyar zhing rnam par gsol/ /gang phyir mchod dang sbyin sreg gi/ /'bras bu yongs su 'khor ba ste/ /sems nad sna tshogs dang ldan te/ /de phyir me rnams bdag
<p>61a.3</p>gis spangs/ /gang phyir yul la skom pa yis/ /bzlas dang sbyin sreg la sogs 'jug /yul rnams dag gis skom pa med/ /de phyir me rnams bdag gis spangs/ /gang phyir bzlas nas bsregs nas kyang / /skye ba la ni thar min zhing / /skye ba yi ni sdug bsngal che/ /de phyir me rnams bdag gis
<p>61a.4</p>spangs/ /gang phyir mchod sbyin dka' thub kyis/ /dge legs yin zhes yid gyur pa/ /de ni brdzun pa nyid yin te/ /de phyir me rnams bdag gis spangs/ /gang phyir skye 'chi las grol ba/ /'gyur med go 'phang dge bar ni/ /brjod pa bdag gis shes pa ste/ /de phyir me rnams bdag gis spangs/ /de
<p>61a.5</p>ltar de'i tshig dang skyed cing / /don dang ldan pas gsan gyur nas/ /'dul ba'i slob dpon gau ta mas/ /dul ba'i 'od srungs la gsungs so/ /skal chen khyod ni legs par 'ongs/ /'di ni legs byas byas min min/ /gang khyod tha dad chos rnams su/ /dge legs gang de nye bar thob/ /de phyir
<p>61a.6</p>re zhig 'khor rnams ni/ /rnam rgyas yang dag 'phel ba bzhin/ /sna tshogs sdug bsngal ston bzhin du/ /yid ni yang dag skyo bar gyis/ /de nas mchog ces smras nas ni/ /bdag la bdag ni yongs bsdus nas/ /mkha' 'gro'i bya ltar 'od srungs ni/ /rlung gi lam la 'phur ba'o/ /de mkhar sdong
<p>61a.7</p>dum bzhin gnas shing / /sa la bzhin du rnam par rgyu/ /khri la bzhin du bzhugs pa dang / /rdzu 'phrul mkhas pa gzims pa'o/ /slar yang me bzhin 'bar ba dang / /slar yang sprin bzhin char 'bab ste/ /slar yang cig car shin tu ni/ /'bar ba dang ni 'bab pa'o/ /glog gi snang ba'i 'od ldan pa'i/ /
<p>61b</p>
<p>61b.1</p>rab 'bab chu gter sprin bzhin du/ /'bar ba dang ni 'bab pa yis/ /rgya cher rnam par gnon te mdzes/ /der ni mig rnams chags byas nas/ /ya mtshan gyen phyogs skye bo rnams/ /mchod mang po las phyag 'tshal zhing / /seng ge'i sgra ni sgrogs pa'o/ /de nas rdzu 'phrul bsdus nas des/ /bya ba
