<p>61b.2</p>byas pa'i slob ma ni/ /bdag gi ston pa bcom ldan zhes/ /thub la mgo bos phyag 'tshal lo/ /drang srong mchog la de bzhin du/ /phyag 'tshal 'od srungs rab mthong nas/ /bde bar gshegs la kun mkhyen zhes/ /ma ga d+hA pa rnam nges so/ /de nas zhing byas mkhyen nas ni/ /dge phyir dge
<p>61b.3</p>legs la gnas pas/ /chos thos par ni 'dod pa yi/ /bzo sbyangs la ni bka' stsal ba/ /gzi chen ldan pa yid bcas shing / /dbang po thul ba dbang por bcas/ /sa yi bdag po gzugs nyid ni/ /skye ba dang ni rnam par nyams/ /yon tan 'phel phyir 'di yi ni/ /skye dang 'gag pa shes bya
<p>61b.4</p>ste/ /shes nas de gnyis yang dag par/ /lus ni yang dag rig par mdzod/ /skye dang 'gag pa'i chos can du/ /dbang po dang bcas lus shes nas/ /bdag ldan bdag ces cung zhig ni/ /nye bar len min nyer 'gro min/ /lus dang dbang po blo rnams las/ /gzhan ni dmigs pa ma yin te/ /
<p>61b.5</p>sdug bsngal 'di ni skye ba ste/ /sdug bsngal nyid ni 'gag pa'o/ /gang tshe 'di kun mngon par 'gro/ /bdag med bdag gi ba yang med/ /de tshe mchog tu mi g.yo ba'i/ /mya ngan 'das pa thob pa'o/ /ngar 'dzin la sogs nyon mongs kyis/ /bdag tu 'dzin las 'ching ba ste/ /'jig rten bdag med
<p>61b.6</p>par mthong na/ /chags pa rnams las rnam par grol/ /mi bden par mthong 'ching ba ste/ /bden par mthong ba rnam par grol/ /bdag yod ces ni 'jig rten 'dir/ /rab tu 'jug 'di bden min 'dzin/ /gal te bdag yod gyur na de/ /rtag gam yang na mi rtag nyid/ /phyogs ni
<p>61b.7</p>gnyis po 'di dag la/ /nyes pa chen po rab tu chags/ /gal te re zhig mi rtag gyur/ /las kyi 'bras bu med par 'gyur/ /yang srid yod pa ma yin zhing / /thar pa 'bad pa med par 'gyur/ /ci ste rtag cing khyab bdag 'gyur/ /skye ba med dang skye ba min/ /nam mkha' khyab cing rtag pa
<p>62a</p>
<p>62a.1</p>ni/ /'god pa med cing skye ba med/ /gal te bdag 'di khyab bdag 'gyur/ /gang du mi gnas pa ma yin/ /'di dang song nas dang thar par/ /thams cad du ni cig car 'gyur/ /khyab bdag nyid phyir bya med 'di'i/ /las kyi bya ba med par 'gyur/ /las rnams ma
<p>62a.2</p>byas pa las ni/ /'bras bur sbyor bar gang gis 'gyur/ /gal te 'di yi byed par 'gyur/ /bdag gi sdug bsngal byed ma yin/ /rang dbang gyur na sdug bsngal ni/ /bdag gis bdag gi byed pa su/ /bdag ni rtag pa nyid las ni/ /rnam par 'gyur ba skye min zhing / /bde dang sdug bsngal
<p>62a.3</p>thob pa las/ /de yis rnam par 'gyur ba mthong / /ye shes thob pas dang nyon mongs/ /spangs las thar pa yod pa ste/ /bya ba med khyab bdag 'di yin/ /de phyir thar pa yod ma yin/ /yod min gyur las de nyid kyis/ /bdag ste 'di ni brjod min la/ /rgyur gyur pas kyang ma yin zhing / /
<p>62a.4</p>'di ni cung zad byed ma yin/ /bya ba las kyang gsal min zhing / /gang rnams kyis 'di byas min la/ /rnam pa de ltar gyur min smra/ /de phyir bdag gi yod ma yin/ /byed pa po med 'dir ni rig pa po yang med/ /bdag po med pa'i lus po 'di ni 'dren par byed/ /ji ltar 'khor ba'i chu
<p>62a.5</p>bo rab tu bskor ba ste/ /smra ba de ni nyon mdzod nyan pa rnams kyi mchog /dbang po drug dang dbang po'i spyod yul drug rnams la/ /brten nas rnam par shes pa rnam drug 'char ba ste/ /gsum po so sor rig pa'i cho ga rab bskor zhing / /gang las dran dang blo dang las kyi 'jug par yin/ /nor bu bud
<p>62a.6</p>shing nyi ma yang dag phrad pa las/ /ji ltar me ni sbyar ba'i dbang gis skye ba ste/ /de bzhin blo dang dbang don dbang po la brten nas/ /skyes bu la brten bya ba rnams ni thams cad 'gyur/ /ji ltar sa bon las ni myu gu skye ba ste/ /myu gu des na sa bon de ni shes min zhing / /gzhan las gzhan du ma yin de
<p>62a.7</p>las de ma yin/ /de bzhin lus dang dbang po blo yi rim pa'o/ /de ltar thub pa mchog gi gsung ni mchog tu dge /dam pa'i don du bsngags pa yang dag thos nas ni/ /dri ma med pa'i rdul med gzhal du med pa'o/ /ma ga d+hA yi bdag po chos mig skyes par gyur/ /'khor der ma ga d+hA yi grong na
<p>62b</p>
<p>62b.1</p>gnas pa yi/ /mi ni du ma rnams dang lha na gnas pa rnams/ /thub pa'i gsung thob pa las rnam dag bsam ldan rnams/ /'gyur med 'chi ba med pa'i go 'phang thob par gyur/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ slob ma mang po dang ldan pa'i le'u ste
<p>62b.2</p>bcu drug pa'o// //de nas rgyal po des ni thub la rnam gnas phyir/ /dpal ldan nags tshal 'od ma'i tshal ni rab phul nas/ /de nyid khong du chud phyir kun nas dmigs pa ni/ /mngon par rjes gnang byas pa grong khyer la zhugs so/ /de nas gtsug lag khang der
<p>62b.3</p>'gro la phan pa'i phyir/ /ye shes las gyur dge ba'i sgron ma bsnams pa ste/ /tshangs dang lha dang de bzhin 'phags pa rnams kyi ni/ /gnas pa de dang de yis sangs rgyas rnam par gnas/ /de nas rta thul dbang po'i rta ni kun bsdams shing / /bsod snyoms 'dod pas rgyal po'i khab
<p>62b.4</p>ni rab thob ste/ /gzugs kyis dang ni zhi ba yis dang rnam 'gyur gyis/ /skye bo chen po rnams kyi mig rnams phrogs par gyur/ /ser skya'i rigs kyi dge slong slob ma du ma can/ /sha ra dwa ti'i bu zhes rab tu grags pa yis/ /dbang po zhi bar 'ongs pa de ni mthong ba ste/ /lam na rjes su gnas
<p>62b.5</p>nas tshig ni mngon par smras/ /khyod kyi gsar pa'i rtags mtshan dang ni zhi ba nyid/ /mthong nas kho bo'i blo gros ya mtshan mchog gyur te/ /de phyir re zhig gal te de nyid rig pa dang / /khyod kyi ston pa'i mtshan ci smra ba gang yin smros/ /de ltar mchod mang sngon 'gro bram ze de yis ni/ /de skad
<p>62b.6</p>brjod cing rta thul gyis kyang smras pa ste/ /bu ram shing pa'i rigs su rab 'khrungs thams cad mkhyen/ /bdag gi ston pa bla na med pa shes par mdzod/ /byis pa gsar bu chos las skyes par gyur pa yis/ /khyod la ston pa brjod par nus pa ma yin te/ /smras pa mkhyen pa'i mchog gyur thub pa
<p>62b.7</p>chen po'i gsung / /nyung ngu cung zad tsam zhig nges par rtogs par mdzod/ /gang zhig chos rnams mtshan ma las ni byung ba ste/ /de dag rnams kyi mtshan ma bcom ldan gyis gsungs shing / /gang zhig de dag rnams kyis nges par 'gog pa dang / /yang dag 'gog pa de yi thabs gang gsungs
<p>63a</p>
<p>63a.1</p>pa'o/ /de ltar rta thul gyi ni tshig 'di thos nas ni/ /gnyis skyes nyer rgyal zhes bya'i ming can de yi ni/ /skyen par chos la mig ni rdul dang bral ba ni/ /dge zhing rnam par dag par nges par gyur pa'o/ /rgyu med pa dang bya ba med dang dbang phyug ste/ /zhing shes pa ni
<p>63a.2</p>nges par de yis sngon rig cing / /rgyu las 'di rnams rab tu 'jug par thos nas ni/ /bdag med gyur pa mthong nas dam pa'i bden pa gzigs/ /sbom po'i nyon mongs tshogs kyis rnam par nyams pa ni/ /grangs can lus las cha shas dang bcas mthong ba ste/ /sbom po dang ni phra mo de yis nyams
<p>63a.3</p>pa ni/ /sangs rgyas pa yi bstan las 'gyur zhes snyam par gyur/ /bdag tu 'du shes skyes pa nye bar mkhyud nas ni/ /ngar 'dzin spong ba ma yin de nas nga yi nyid/ /sgron ma dang ni nyin mor byed pa yod pa na/ /'od kyi rnam par nyams par gtan tshigs shes bya ci/ /ji ltar pad+ma'i chu ba che bar gyur pa
<p>63a.4</p>yi/ /snal ma phra mo nyid ni bzhin dang 'brel pa ste/ /thar pa'i cho ga mthar thug min par de snyam zhing / /sangs rgyas pa yis rdo ba phye dang mnyam par rtogs/ /de nas bram zes rta thul de la mngon mchod nas/ /tshim zhing rang nyid kyi ni khang par rnam song zhing / /bsod snyoms rim bzhin rta thul gyis kyang
<p>63a.5</p>rab thob nas/ /rang bzhin gnas shing mkhas pa 'od ma'i tshal du song / /de bzhin rab tu dang bas mchog dang ldan pa yi/ /nye rgyal kyang ni mngon du zhugs pa mthong nas ni/ /thos pa dang ni bsam pas bya ba mnyam pa yi/ /maud gal rigs su rab tu skyes pas smras pa'o/ /dge slong de nyid gang
<p>63a.6</p>gis gzhan bzhin gyur pa ste/ /brtan pa yin yang yang dag dga' bzhin nye bar song / /khyed kyis 'chi med ci zhig de ring thob pa ste/ /bzhin ni rab tu dang 'di gtan tshigs med ma yin/ /de nas 'di ltar bgyi zhes 'di la nges bden smras/ /de nas des ni bdag la smos pa shes des smras/ /de
<p>63a.7</p>nas tshig de nyid ni de yis smras pa ste/ /thos nas nyid kyi yang dag mig ni skyes par gyur/ /las dang bsam pa rnam dag blo ldan de gnyis ni/ /lag nas sgron ma bzhin du de nyid mthong ba ste/ /shes pas ston la rnam par g.yo min bsam ldan dag /de ni lta ba'i don du da lta nyid du gshegs/ /slob
<p>63b</p>
<p>63b.1</p>ma'i sder bcas de gnyis rgyang ma nas gzigs nas/ /bcom ldan drang srong chen pos dge slong rnams la gsungs/ /shes rab can dang rdzu 'phrul ldan ba rnams kyi gtso/ /kho bo'i mchog gi slob ma 'di gnyis 'dir 'ongs so/ /de nas zab dang brtan pa'i gsung ni zhi ba yis/ /thub pas de
<p>63b.2</p>gnyis la ni gtam dag mdzad pa ste/ /dge slong 'dir ni mngon par nyer 'ongs rab zhi'i phyir/ /chos 'di ji lta ba bzhin yang dag thob par gyis/ /dbyu gu gsum lag gtsug phud dang ldan gnyis skyes te/ /gnyis la de bzhin gshegs pas 'di skad ces gsungs te/ /sangs rgyas mthu
<p>63b.3</p>yis ngur smrig gos dang ldan pa yi/ /dge slong nyid du skad cig gis ni gyur pa'o/ /slob ma'i sder bcas cha lugs de yis de gnyis kyis/ /mgo bo dag gis thams cad mkhyen la mchod pa ste/ /de nas sangs rgyas kyis chos de gnyis la gsungs shing / /dus kyis de gnyis kyis ni nges
<p>63b.4</p>legs thob par gyur/ /de nas 'od srungs rigs kyi sgron ma gnyis skyes kyis/ /kha dog dang ni gzugs dang nor dang nyer ldan las/ /rdzu 'phrul dang ni bdag ldan bzang mo rnams spangs nas/ /thar pa'i ched du ngur smrig bzung zhing gshegs pa'o/ /mdog bzangs gser gyi mchod sdong dang
<p>63b.5</p>mtshungs 'bar ba ni/ /bu mangs ming bcas mchod rten du ni nges mthong nas/ /dngos po thams cad spangs shing ya mtshan dang bcas pas/ /thams cad mkhyen la thal mo rab sbyar mngon par song / /thub pa la ni rgyang nas mgo bos phyag 'tshal zhing / /phyag 'tshal nas ni ji lta ba bzhin mthon
<p>63b.6</p>por gsol/ /bdag ni slob ma bcom ldan bdag gi ston pa lags/ /mun pa rnams su bstan pa bdag gi sgron mar gyur/ /gnyis skyes skom pa skyes shing nye bar 'ongs par ni/ /mkhyen nas bsam pa rnam dag thar 'dod de la ni/ /sems la gsung gi chab kyis rab tu tshim mdzad pa/ /de bzhin
<p>63b.7</p>gshegs pas legs par 'ongs zhes bka' stsal to/ /gsung 'di yis ni ngal ba rnam par sos bzhin te/ /nges par legs par rtogs pa'i ched du gnas pa ste/ /de nas dag pa'i bdag nyid 'di la thugs rje can/ /thub pas chos ni mdor bsdus pa yis gsungs pa'o/ /gang phyir thub
<p>64a</p>
<p>64a.1</p>pas chos ni phra mor gsungs tsam na/ /de yis don ni mtha' dag yang dag thob gyur te/ /de phyir yang dag rig dang na tshod che gnyis las/ /dgra bcom 'od srungs chen po nyid du mtshan gyur to/ /gang gis lus las gzhan dang yang na lus su ni/ /bdag dang bdag gi
<p>64a.2</p>ba zhes bdag tu rtogs pa ste/ /de yis bdag tu lta ba de ni nges spangs shing / /nyi tshe ba min sdug bsngal 'di ni mthong bar gyur/ /tshul khrims brtul zhugs dag gis dag par byed ces gang / /rgyu med pa dang rgyu las de yis rtogs pa ste/ /sdug bsngal nyid dang lam ni yang dag thob nas te/ /tshul
<p>64a.3</p>khrims dang ni brtul zhugs mchog tu ma bzung ngo / /phyin ci log tu gyur par song ba gang gis ni/ /mngon du bskor zhing mchog ni rab tu thob ma yin/ /bden pa bzhi po'i go 'phang rnams ni mthong gyur nas/ /the tshom som nyir gyur te yang dag mchod par gyur/ /'dod pa gang rnams su ni yang dag
<p>64a.4</p>rgyar nyid dang / /brgyal bar gyur dang brgyal bar 'gyur nyid 'jig rten pa/ /mi gtsang bden pa ma yin de rnams des shes nas/ /'dod chags shes bya'i yul de spangs par gyur pa'o/ /de bzhin du ni byams par gyur ba'i sems kyis des/ /bshes dang bshes min rnams su khyad par med pa ste/ /
<p>64a.5</p>'byung po kun la rjes su brtse ba byas pa yis/ /nad du song ba'i gnod sems spangs par gyur pa'o/ /gzugs la brten pa rnams dang grong khyer brten pa rnams/ /sna tshogs nyid dang ldan pa'i 'du shes rnams spangs nas/ /des ni gzugs kyi khams su chags pa rnam bcom ste/ /gzugs la
<p>64a.6</p>'jug pa'i nyes pa rnams ni rtogs nas so/ /rmongs las snyoms 'jug rnams su thar pa'i 'du shes dang / /gzugs med lha rnams mdzad pa can du rtogs nas ni/ /zhi zhing mtshan ma med pa'i sems ni gzung nas su/ /gzugs med sred pa las ni chags dang bral bar song / /chu bo sin d+hu'i shugs
<p>64a.7</p>chen rab tu 'jug pa bzhin/ /sems kyis g.yo zhing skyod par byed pa shes nas ni/ /brtan pa'i brten las rgod pa rnam par spangs pa ste/ /zhi zhing rdzing bu gang ba bzhin du gnas par gyur/ /snying po med pa'i phyir dang 'god ba'i chos nyid phyir/ /bdag med nyid phyir dngos rnams yang dag rab mthong nas/ /
<p>64b</p>
<p>64b.1</p>khyad 'phags nyid dang mnyam dang mchog nyid mthong ba ste/ /nga rgyal rnam par spangs nas yod ma yin zhes rtogs/ /ye shes me yis mi shes mun pa rnams bcom nas/ /zad pa can dang zad pa med par sna tshogs mthong / /rnal 'byor gyis ni rig pa nyid ni yongs bsgoms nas/ /ma rig pa ni
<p>64b.2</p>mtha' dag ji lta ba bzhin spangs/ /mthong dang bsgom pa dag gis kun du sbyor ba ni/ /bcu po 'di dag mtha' dag rnams kyis rnam par grol gyur cing / /thal mo sbyar byas sangs rgyas nyid la lta bzhin du/ /bya ba kun byas rang bzhin gnas te gnas par gyur/ /skar ma gsum gyis gnas skabs
<p>64b.3</p>gsum skyong rjes skyes lha dang ni/ /ldan pa'i lnga gsum tshes kyi dus su skar ma'i rgyal po bzhin/ /gsum ni chud zos gyur cing gsum ni lhag par thob pa yi/ /gsum rig slob ma gsum gyis bde bar gshegs pa rnam par mdzes/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ 
<p>64b.4</p>nyan thos chen po rab tu gshegs par mdzad pa'i le'u ste bcu bdun pa'o// //de nas 'ga' zhig tshe na nor ldan khyim bdag ni/ /skal ba med pa rnams la nor ni rab sbyin pa/ /bzang sbyin zhes ni rab tu grags pa'i ming ldan pa/ /byang phyogs yul ko sa la rnams nas der song
<p>64b.5</p>gyur/ /de yis der ni thub pa bzhugs pa thos pa ste/ /thos nas blta bar 'dod pas mtshan mo rab tu song / /rnam dag sems pa des ni rab sleb rab mkhyen nas/ /rab tu phyag byas pa la bde bar gshegs pas bstan/ /gang phyir chos la bsgoms pas nyid ni rnam spangs nas/ /blo ldan
<p>64b.6</p>mtshan mor bdag la lta 'dod rab sleb ste/ /da lta nyid du 'ongs pa de yi de ma thag /nges par legs pa'i mgron 'di rab tu long mdzod cig /gang zhig khyod kyis lhag bsam gang zhig bstan pa dang / /bdag gis grags pa nyid las gang zhig dang ba dang / /gang zhig sngon gyi rgyu las blo gros rab
<p>64b.7</p>zhugs te/ /des ni yon tan chen po rnams kyi snod yin no/ /de phyir 'jig rten dag na grags dang gzhan du ni/ /'bras bu sbyin pa mchog las byung bar rig nas ni/ /bkur sti byas nas dus su snyoms pa'i bdag nyid kyis/ /chos las thob pa'i nor ni sbyin par bya ba'o/ /tshul khrims yang dag
<p>65a</p>
<p>65a.1</p>blangs nas spyad par bya ba ste/ /tshul khrims nyid ni bsrung ba dang ni rgyan yin zhing / /'og tu song ba rnams kyi rnam par ldog byed do/ /nam mkha'i steng gi nges par rdzogs pa po nyid yin/ /'dod pa rnams su gcig min zhes pas rjes bcings pa'i/ /yongs su tshol ba la
<p>65a.2</p>sogs skyon rnams thos nas ni/ /nges par 'byung ba'i cho gar yon tan rnam shes nas/ /rnam dben las skyes shi ba'i bden pa bsnyen par mdzod/ /'chi bas nye bar gzir zhing rga bas zil non pa'i/ /'jig rten rab tu bskor ba yang dag yongs shes nas/ /zhi ba skye ba med phyir 'bad pa mdzod cig dang / /
<p>65a.3</p>skye ba bden pa med na rga med 'chi ba med/ /ji ltar mi rnams la ni mi rtag bdag nyid kyis/ /rab chags sdug bsngal mngon sum du ni rig mdzod la/ /de bzhin lha rnams la yang sdug bsngal rig mdzod dang / /'jug pa rtag pa nyid ni su yang yod ma yin/ /gang du mi rtag pa nyid der ni sdug bsngal zhing / /
<p>65a.4</p>gang du rang nyid med pa der yang sdug bsngal te/ /gang du bdag ces pa dang bdag gi ba zhes pa/ /de tshe mi rtag sdug bsngal bdag med gang la yin/ /de phyir sdug bsngal las ni sdug bsngal 'di dang ni/ /mtshan ma las ni 'di yi mtshan ma ltos mdzod la/ /rnam par nye bar zhi las sdug bsngal zhi ba
<p>65a.5</p>dang / /lam las khyod kyi lam ni dge ba shes par gyis/ /'gro ba g.yo ba sdug bsngal 'di ni shes nas su/ /me dang rab mtshungs dus kyi me yis 'jig rten 'di/ /mtha' dag rab tu tshig par yongs su rtogs bzhin du/ /srid dang srid min rnams su smon pa med par gyis/ /stong pa nyid dang bdag
<p>65a.6</p>med bdag gi ba med pa/ /sgyu ma dang mtshungs 'jig rten 'di ni shes byas nas/ /'du byed tsam zhig rab tu yongs su rtogs bzhin du/ /lus 'di la ni khams kyi 'du shes nyid du gyis/ /sems ni srid pa g.yos las yang dag g.yos nas dang / /'khor ba'i 'gro ba rnam pa sna tshogs mthong nas
<p>65a.7</p>ni/ /rtog pa med cing zhi la bden zhing chags med par/ /sems ni snyoms shing \u0f37mtshan ma med pa bsnyen par gyis/ /de nas drang srong chen po'i chos de thos pa las/ /chos kyi cho ga'i sngon gyi 'bras bu thob gyur zhing / /gang zhig thob nas 'di yi sdug bsngal las lhag ma/ /rgya mtsho chen po las ni thigs pa
<p>65b</p>
<p>65b.1</p>gcig bzhin gyur/ /chags bral rnams kyi dgon par yang dag gnas kyang ngam/ /lus med rnams kyis srid rtser yang dag gnas na yang / /nags sam lha na de nyid mthong min ma yin la/ /khyim na gnas pa yin yang lta bas dge legs gyur/ /rnam pa sna tshogs lta ba'i dra ba rnams kyis
<p>65b.2</p>dang / /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal rnams kyis de rnams rnam mi 'grol/ /de phyir rab tu nyams shing de nyid ma mthong bar/ /chags pa rnam par bsal nas khyad par 'phags par gshegs/ /lta ba legs skyes des ni lta ba ngan de rnams/ /ston ka'i sprin gyis rdo yi char bzhin spangs pa ste/ /dbang phyug la
<p>65b.3</p>sogs mi mthun rgyu las ma yin zhing / /des ni 'jig rten rgyu med par min zhes rtogs so/ /de phyir mi mnyam rgyur ni 'thad pa ma yin zhing / /rgyu med par ni 'gal ba chen po yod pa nyid/ /'dir yang rigs pa shes pas so sor mthong ba ste/ /the tshom med pas de nyid mthong ba kye ma ci/ /gal
<p>65b.4</p>te dbang phyug gis ni 'gro ba skyed gyur na/ /'gro ba rim gyis rab tu 'jug pa ma yin la/ /skye dgu rnams kyi 'khor ba'i 'khor lo ma yin zhing / /gang du gang zhig bskyed nas de dang de nyid 'gyur/ /lus can rnams kyis mi 'dod thob pa ma yin zhing / /de yi bdag nyid rnams kyis 'dod pa'i spyod pa
<p>65b.5</p>med/ /gang zhig lus can rnams kyi dge dang mi dger gyur/ /de ni dbang phyug nyid phyir dbang phyug la yin no/ /de yi dbang phyug nyid la the tshom 'gyur min zhing / /der ni mi rnams dag gis byams pa pha bzhin 'gyur/ /de la nyam thag pas ni smod pa smra min zhing / /lha rnams de dang de la 'jig rten mchod ma yin/ /
<p>65b.6</p>gal te 'di mi bskyed la dgongs par gyur na ni/ /bya ldan nyid phyir deng 'dir dbang phyug ma yin zhing / /gal te 'di yis 'jug la 'dod par gyur na ni/ /de nyid dbang phyug yod pa nyid la byed par 'gyur/ /ci ste 'di yi skye la nus pa cung zhig med/ /byis pa bzhin du 'di yis spyod rnams rgyu med do/ /gal
<p>65b.7</p>te dbang phyug gi ni bdag la mnga' nyid med/ /'jig rten bskyed la 'di yi stobs de ci zhig yod/ /ji ltar 'dod la gal te bde sdug la bsnyen na/ /'byung po rnams ni 'jig rten na des byas pa nyid/ /gang phyir 'dod la chags pa khong khro la 'jug ste/ /de phyir de yi dbang nyid yod pa ma yin no/ /
<p>66a</p>
<p>66a.1</p>de'i rten nyid la sems med rnams kyis gnas bya ste/ /skyes bu'i 'bad rtsol tshad mar gyur pa nyid yin no/ /las 'bras med par 'gyur zhing lung ni byas min la/ /las kyi sbyor ba rnams ni de yi rten yin na/ /gal te dbang phyug rang gi las kyis 'gyur na ni/ /thun mong gyur pa'i las
<p>66a.2</p>la dbang phyug gyur ma yin/ /ci ste de yi khyab bdag rgyu med gyur na ni/ /'gro ba kun gyi dbang phyug nyid ni rab tu grub/ /ci ste de yi dbang phyug nyid gzhan las yin zhing / /de nyid kyi yang byed po'i dbang phyug gzhan yin la/ /de yis gzhan zhes de ltar 'dir ni rnam gzhag med/ /de phyir 'gro ba skyed pa yod
<p>66a.3</p>pa ma yin nyid/ /dbang phyug skyed por gyur na rigs pas tha dad du/ /rnam par 'gal ba rnam pa du ma mthong ba ste/ /de yi phyir yang rang bzhin la ni nyes pa de/ /slar yang rab tu chags par 'gyur ba nyid yin no/ /rgyu shes rnams kyi rten ni cung zad rnam log pa'o/ /rgyu ni bya ba'i cho gar smra ba ma yin zhing / /bya
<p>66a.4</p>ba'i cho gar sa bon la sogs de dang de/ /ltos pa yin te de phyir rang bzhin rgyu ma yin/ /'bras mi rdzogs par byed pa po ni gcig pa nyid/ /'ga' zhig gi yang rgyu ni cung zad yod ma yin/ /gcig gi bdag nyid can gyi rang bzhin rab bstan te/ /de phyir rab tu 'jug la rang bzhin rgyu ma yin/ /gang gi rang
<p>66a.5</p>bzhin gyis ni khyab pa nyid 'dod pa/ /de yi bya ba med pa nyid kyang rab chags shing / /bya ba ma gtogs 'bras bu'i cho ga mthong min te/ /de yi phyir yang bskyed la rang bzhin rgyu ma yin/ /de yi khyab pa po nyid la ni rgyu nyid phyir/ /thams cad las ni thams cad rgyun mi 'chad par 'gyur/ /'bras bu'i rab tu
<p>66a.6</p>'jug la nges pa mthong ba ste/ /de phyir skyed pa la ni rang bzhin rgyu ma yin/ /ji ltar 'di yi yon tan med nyid grub pa ste/ /de ltar 'bras bu la ni yon tan med nyid 'gyur/ /rnam 'gyur yon tan can rnams 'jig rten na mthong ste/ /de phyir rab tu 'jug la rang bzhin rgyu ma yin/ /rtag pa'i rgyu las
<p>66a.7</p>khyad par 'gyur ba ma yin phyir/ /rnam 'gyur la ni tha dad yon tan nyid ma yin/ /rnam 'gyur la ni tha dad yon tan zhugs pa ste/ /de phyir rang bzhin las ni skyed pa rigs ma yin/ /rang bzhin gyis ni bskyed pa'i bdag nyid can nyid la/ /'bras bu rnams su nyams pa'i rgyu ni grub ma yin/ /gang
<p>66b</p>
<p>66b.1</p>phyir rnam 'gyur gyi ni nyams pa mthong ba ste/ /de phyir rtogs par bya ba rgyu ni gzhan nyid do/ /nus par gyur pa'i sbyor la shin tu mthar thug pa'i/ /thar pa 'dod pa'i sdom brtson rnams kyi ma yin zhing / /skye dgu rnams kyi rang bzhin rab tu 'jug pa'i phyir/ /gang las thar pa'i ched dang pha rol gnon
<p>66b.2</p>par gyur/ /skyed pa'i bdag nyid rang bzhin gyis ni nges nyid phyir/ /de yi bdag nyid rnam 'gyur la ni nges nyid yin/ /'jig rten dag na rnam 'gyur la ni brtan nyid med/ /de phyir rang bzhin gyis ni skyed par rigs ma yin/ /sems kyi spyod pa mi gsal rang bzhin zhes bya zhing / /rnam 'gyur
<p>66b.3</p>gsal ba 'di ni de nas grags pa ste/ /de phyir rab tu 'jug la rang bzhin rgyu min zhing / /gsal ba'i rgyu la 'dir ni 'bras bu grub pa nyid/ /sems med rang bzhin las ni sems dang bcas pa yi/ /rta glang bong bu la sogs 'bras bu rigs pa ma yin zhing / /sems dang rnam par bral ba'i rgyu
<p>66b.4</p>rnams dag las ni/ /sems dang ldan pa cung zad zhig ni 'jug ma yin/ /gal te 'gro ba skyed phyir dus ni nges pa ste/ /de phyir yongs su rtog byed rnams kyis thar pa med/ /gang phyir skye dgu rnams kyi mtha' ni byas min te/ /de phyir 'jig rten rgyun chad med par skye bar 'gyur/ /gang zhig
<p>66b.5</p>yon tan rnams kyi gcig dang du mas byas/ /rjes rnams su ni rang nyid nges pa mthong ba ste/ /gal te rgyu gcig nyid du gnas par gyur pa na/ /de yang tha dad khyad par gyur pa ma yin no/ /gang zhig smin pa las skyes rdzas kyi cho gar sar/ /yon tan shes pas yon tan tha dad nyid du mthong / /gang
<p>66b.6</p>phyir rgyu ni khyad par min pa 'dod pa ste/ /stong pa'i rdzas rnams su yang nges par gyur pa nyid/ /gang gi mi gsal ba las rdzas ni 'char ba ste/ /de yi rjes su dpag pa nges par grub ma yin/ /'bras bu gsal ba yi ni yang dag rab 'jug pa/ /mi gsal ba las gang gis mngon du mthong ma
<p>66b.7</p>yin/ /gsal ba gnyis pa dag las rab tu 'jug pa bzhin/ /mi gsal ba las gang gi 'bras bu dang por gyur/ /de yi 'dod pa las 'dir mi 'dod chen po'o/ /rang bzhin nyid kyis nyes pa gnyis ni rab tu chags/ /ji ltar gser gyi phreng ba khyad par 'phags pa ste/ /de ltar rang bzhin
<p>67a</p>
<p>67a.1</p>gyi ni rnam 'gyur khyad par 'phags/ /'bras bu khyad par yin zhing rgyu yi ma yin te/ /de phyir skyed la rang bzhin rigs pa ma yin no/ /gal te bya bar skyes bu de ni rgyu yin na/ /gang gis nges par gang 'dod des de 'thob par 'gyur/ /'dod kyang kha cig don ni
<p>67a.2</p>'thob pa ma yin la/ /mi 'dod na yang dbang med 'dir ni 'thob par 'gyur/ /gang zhig ba glang rta bong rnga mo'i skye gnas 'gro/ /mnga' bdag nyid du gyur na de ni bsnyen min zhing / /de ru 'gro ba'i sdig pa'i las ni byed pa dang / sdug bsngal mi 'dod su yis sdug bsngal byed par 'gyur/ /gal te 'jig rten
<p>67a.3</p>dag na skyes bu byed par gyur/ /sdug bsngal byed pa ma yin bde ba kho na byed/ /'dod pa byed par 'dod kyang mi 'dod byed pa ste/ /dbang phyug chen por 'gyur na mi 'dod su yis spyod/ /gang tshe mi ni chos min pa las rnam 'jigs shing / /'bad pas chos ni rab tu son par byed pa nyid/ /sna tshogs
<p>67a.4</p>nyon mongs rnams kyis dbang med 'phrog pa ste/ /de phyir 'di na mi ni pha rol rgyud du gyur/ /grang dang dro dang char dang thog dang glog sogs kyi/ /bya ba rnams ni mi la bzlog nas mthong ba ste/ /gang phyir rang dbang ma yin mi ni gzhan ldan te/ /de phyir bya ba rnams su skyes bu dbang phyug min/ /gang tshe
<p>67a.5</p>sa bon las dang sa chu'i rten las ni/ /dus sbyor rab tu 'jug la lo thog phun tshogs shing / /mar me dag las rab gsal shing las me yin te/ /rgyu med las yin zhes pa rgyu med ma yin no/ /rgyu med pa las gal te 'gro ba'i rab 'jug na/ /mi yi byed pa yis ni med par 'gyur ba ste/ /
<p>67a.6</p>thams cad kyis ni thams cad nges par 'thob byed cing / /rtag na 'di ni thams cad du ni song bar grub/ /bde dang sdug bsngal gal te rgyu med las yin na/ /gang char kun gyi bde dang sdug bsngal skal min zhing / /rgyu med las kyang bde dang sdug bsngal rtogs min te/ /de phyir rgyu med las
<p>67a.7</p>shes 'di ni rgyu ma yin/ /de skad ces pa la sogs mi mnyam rgyu rnams des/ /'jig rten rab tu 'jug la rgyu rnams shes ma yin/ /rgyu med par ni 'jig rten mthong ba ma yin zhing / /nyes pa 'di rnams rgyu med las ni yang dag rtogs/ /brtan pa dang ni g.yo ba'i 'byung po rnams su yang / /
<p>67b</p>
<p>67b.1</p>de dang de la brten nas de dang de 'byung ste/ /'jig rten dag na rgyu med ci yang yod min zhing / /kun gyi rgyu ni 'jig rten pa yis shes ma yin/ /de nas sbyin pa bzang por byin pa'i bzang byin des/ /rgya che'i chos kyis dam pa'i chos ni rnam shes nas/ /g.yo ba med pa'i blo gros nges par rab
<p>67b.2</p>dang bas/ /drang srong chen po la ni tshig 'di gsal ba'o/ /mnyan yod rta ljang rta rid kyis bsnyen grong khyer ni/ /bdag gi gnas kyi sa ni bsod nams grags pa can/ /der ni bdag gis khyed kyi gnas ni byed 'dod de/ /sdig med gnas mchog dam pa de ni bsnyen par mdzod/ /gang lta na yang
<p>67b.3</p>thub pa khyed kyi gnas su snyoms pa ni/ /gzhal yas khang gi logs sam rnam dben nags su ste/ /bdag la rjes su brtse phyir gnas kyi ched du ni/ /dgra bcom rab tu gzhes par mdzad par 'os pa lags/ /de nas gtong bar lhag par mos pa 'di yis ni/ /rnam par grol ba'i sems ni
<p>67b.4</p>rnam par mkhyen nas ni/ /chags pa med pa'i blo mnga' blo gros mkhyen pa yis/ /mchog tu zhi bas blo gros yang dag bka' stsal to/ /sems dpa' brtan kye gang zhig rdzas glog g.yo rnams su/ /khyod kyi sems dpa' gtong la lhag par mos pa ste/ /rang bzhin gyis ni sbyin la dga' zhing chos
<p>67b.5</p>la dgyes/ /de nyid mthong ba khyed la de ni ngo mtshar min/ /gang zhig khyim ni tshig las phyi rol 'thon byed pa/ /de yi don de 'tshig par byed pa ma yin te/ /de bzhin dus kyi me yis 'gro ba tshig pa na/ /gang gis gang zhig sbyin pa de yis de nyer 'thob/ /de phyir rnam spangs sems dpa'
<p>67b.6</p>rnams kyis sbyin par dang / /yul rnams yang dag longs spyod par ni shes pa nyid/ /bkren pa 'jig rten dag na zad pa'i skyon mthong bas/ /nye bar longs spyod ma yin 'jigs las sbyin ma yin/ /dus su smod la don ni rnam par gtong ba dang / /dpal dang nga rgyal las ni de bzhin g.yul
<p>67b.7</p>'gyed par/ /sems dpa' lhag pa nyid kyis shes te gzhan gyis min/ /sems dpa' yis ni sbyin pa nyid dang g.yul 'gyed do/ /sbyin byed dga' ba nyid du 'gro la 'gro ba ste/ /snyan pa dang ni dam par grags pa rab tu 'thob/ /sbyin pa po yod gang zhes dam pa rnams sbyin nas/ /yang
<p>68a</p>
<p>68a.1</p>dag bkur ba dang ni mngon du 'gro bar byed/ /de bzhin 'jig rten dag na blo gtad nyid 'gyur zhing / /mi bzad pa rnams las kyang nyes pa 'thob ma yin/ /bsod nams rnams ni bdag gis byas zhes tshim pa ste/ /'chi ba'i dus su skrag par mngon par 'gro ma yin/ /
<p>68a.2</p>sbyin pa'i 'bras bu 'dir ni me tog tsam zhig ste/ /sbyin pa po yi 'bras bu gzhan nyid rab tu 'thob/ /'khor ba'i 'khor lo la ni 'khor ba'i skye bo yi/ /gtong ba dang mnyam gnyen ni yod pa ma yin no/ /mi yi 'jig rten na dang lha na skyes pa rnams/ /gtong ba las dang mnyam pa rnams las lhag
<p>68a.3</p>par 'gyur/ /rta dang glang po'i skye gnas su yang gnas pa rnams/ /'bras bu de ni gtso bo thob par 'gyur ba'o/ /sbyin pas longs spyod rnams kyis yongs su 'dzin pa ste/ /tshul khrims kyis bsrungs mtho ris su ni 'gro bar 'gyur/ /ye shes sngon du 'gro ba can gyi zhi ba yis kyang ni/ /
<p>68a.4</p>rten dang bral ba gang na grangs su 'gro ba 'gro ma yin/ /'chi med bdud rtsi de yis 'thob pa'i ched du yang / /sdom par gyur pa rab tu sbyin pa yin pa nyid/ /sbyin pa dran nas rab tu dga' bar gyur pa ste/ /yid ni rab tu dga' las nges par ting 'dzin yin/ /mnyam par gzhag na yang
<p>68a.5</p>dag mtho ba 'di ru ni/ /skye dang 'god pa shes par rim gyis 'gyur ba ste/ /gzhan la sbyin pa sbyin pa'i sbyin pa po yis ni/ /snying la gnas pa'i nyon mongs rnams ni bsrabs par 'gyur/ /gang zhig sbyin pa byin byed de yi don rnams su/ /chags par grags pa de ni dang por chod pa
<p>68a.6</p>nyid/ /gang la rab tu byams pa'i sems kyis sbyin pa ste/ /de phyir zhe sdang dang ni nga rgyal spangs par gyur/ /rab tu len pa po ni bde ldan rnams mthong nas/ /gang zhig 'ga' ste des na ser sna yod ma yin/ /sbyin pa pos ni sbyin pa'i 'bras bu mngon rtogs nas/ /med pa nyid dang
<p>68a.7</p>mi shes mun pa 'joms pa po/ /de phyir zhi ba 'phags min gyis bsnyen ser sna dang / /sred pa gang las sbyin pa byed pas bcom pa ste/ /de nas thar pa'i yan lag gyur pa sbyin pa ni/ /yin zhing nyes pa rab tu thob phyir thar pa'o/ /ji ltar gzhan rnams grib ma'i don du shing 'dod
<p>68b</p>
<p>68b.1</p>cing / /kha cig 'bras bu'i don du gzhan rnams me tog phyir/ /de ltar sbyin pa yongs su sbyin par byed pa ste/ /kha cig zhi ba'i don du gzhan rnams nor gyi phyir/ /de phyir khyad par du ni khyim na gnas rnams kyis/ /sbyin pa ji ltar nus pa mchog ni gter yin zhing / /sbyin pa snying po med pa'i nor
<p>68b.2</p>gyi snying po ste/ /dam pa rnams kyi rjes su song ba lam 'di yin/ /bza' ba rab tu sbyin par stobs ni rab ster zhing / /bgo ba sbyin byed la yang lus ni ster ba'o/ /gang gis dam pa rnams la gnas ni sbyin byed pa/ /des kyang 'jig rten dag na thams cad byin pa yin/ /theg pa sbyin byed
<p>68b.3</p>la yang bde ba byin pa ste/ /mar me sbyin byed la ni spyan mig sbyin pa nyid/ /de nas dbrog bya ma yin 'chi med rab sbyin zhing / /gang gis mthar thug gyur pa'i chos kyis ston pa nyid/ /kha cig 'dod pa'i ched du sbyin pa gtong ba ste/ /gzhan ni don gyi don du gcig ni grags pa'i phyir/ /
<p>68b.4</p>kha cig mtho ris don du gzhan ni brtse ba'i phyir/ /khyod kyi sbyin pa 'di ni chags pa med pa yin/ /de phyir legs so khyod ni sred pa de ltar gyur/ /gang zhig yang dag bsgrubs mdzod 'dod pa tshim par shog /rdul bcas mun pa dang ldan gang khyed 'ongs nas ni/ /ye shes rnam dag blo ni rab
<p>68b.5</p>tu 'gro bar 'gyur/ /de nyid de bzhin gshegs pas lam gyi yang dag par/ /dga' ba byas pa dang yang gzhug pa byas pa ni/ /gtsug lag khang de snying la rnam par byas nas ni/ /nye rgyal dang ni lhan cig dus su song bar gyur/ /song nas de na kau shAm rgyal po'i khab dang ni/ /gtsug
<p>68b.6</p>lag khang gi sa la so sor yang dag rgyus/ /dpal ldan mnyam zhing mdzes la yid 'ong shing ldan pa/ /der ni de yis rgyal byed kyi ni tshal mthong ngo / /de nas de yi don du rgyal byed la zhus te/ /de yis chags pa las ni de la ma byin no/ /khyod kyis gal te don gyis kun nas bkram na yang / /
<p>68b.7</p>sa ni bdag gis sbyin pa ma yin zhes smras so/ /de nas der ni bzang sbyin gyis de la smras pa/ /tshal de la ni rin byas shes ni mngon 'dod do/ /de nas des ni nor gyis sa ni yongs g.yogs nas/ /chos kyi tha snyad mthong zhing nyos par gyur pa'o/ /de yi gtong ba de ni mthong nas rgyal byed kyis/ /
<p>69a</p>
<p>69a.1</p>sangs rgyas la ni mchog tu rab tu dang ba byas/ /nags tshal de yi lhag ma dag ni kun nas ni/ /de bzhin gshegs pa la ni phul bar gyur pa'o/ /de nas mgon med zas sbyin gyis ni drang srong chen po yis/ /nye rgyal gyis ni nges par gzigs par bya ba'i don
<p>69a.2</p>ldan par/ /myur ba'i blo gros dang ldan ma chags grol ba'i sems kyis ni/ /mdzes shing dge ba mchog gis gtsug lag khang ni byed du bcug /nor gyi dbang phyug nyid kyi gnas ni 'phos pa lta bu dang / /byang phyogs ko sha la yi khang pa'i bde ba lta bu dang / /de bzhin gshegs pa
<p>69a.3</p>nyid kyi gzhi ni mtshungs pa lta bu dang / /rang gi nor dang stobs kyi dang ni lta ba yi yang ngo / /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ mgon med zas sbyin la rjes su ston pa'i le'u ste bco brgyad pa'o// //de nas thub pa sna tshogs tha dad blo can
<p>69a.4</p>gyi/ /ston pas thams cad ye shes kyis ni zil mnan nas/ /bcu phyed phrag ri nas dang grong khyer nas rim gyis/ /rgyal po bum pas bsnyen pa'i grong khyer du gshegs so/ /de nas slob ma stong phrag tsam ni dul ba na/ /gshegs so des ni yab kyi yul ni rab tu thob/ /de
<p>69a.5</p>nas de la rjes su 'dzin pa mdzad bzhed pa/ /rang gi grong gi gnas la mtha' ru bsnyen pa'o/ /de nas mdun na 'don dang blon po blo gros can/ /dga' ba'i gtam la dam pa rgyu ba de rnams kyis/ /yongs su rdzogs pa'i rab brnyes 'phags pa ste/ /sa skyong rgyal po de la zhus shing
<p>69a.6</p>gsol ba'o/ /de nas de ni 'ongs pa thos nas sa skyong ni/ /dga' ba yongs ldan sems kyis blta bar 'dod pa yis/ /grong khyer ba ni kun gyis rjes su 'gro byas pa/ /myur bas brtan pa spangs shing bsu ba la gshegs so/ /drang srong dbus su tshangs pa bzhugs pa bzhin du
<p>69a.7</p>ni/ /slob mas bskor ba de ni rgyang ring nas gzigs nas/ /drang srong chen po'i chos la rjes su 'gro bas ni/ /shing rta spangs nas rkang pa rnams kyis nye bar gshegs/ /myur bar de yi nye logs su ni yongs phyin nas/ /thub pa mthong ba nyid de des ni ma smras so/ /de la bu zhes smra bar
<p>69b</p>
<p>69b.1</p>nus pa ma yin zhing / /de bzhin dge slong zhes ni nus pa ma yin no/ /de nas de yi dge slong cha lugs de mthong zhing / /bdag tu song ba'i sna tshogs dpal la brtags nas ni/ /dbugs ring brgyus nas mchi ma rnam par bton pa de/ /drag tu mun par gyur cing rnam par zlos pa nyid/ /
<p>69b.2</p>lam 'gro skom par gyur pa mngon par song ba yis/ /rgyang ring dag nas rdzing bu skam po mthong nas ltar/ /rang gnas rnam pa dang bral nye bar nyer bzhugs pa/ /mthong nas bdag gi nyam thag stobs ldan mchog tu gyur/ /'jig rten mtha' ru gnas pa'i sems gyur thim pa na/ /sdug pa'i
<p>69b.3</p>rnam 'gyur ri mor song ba ji lta bar/ /gzugs de nyid ni mthong ba na ni bdag la ni/ /dga' ba yod pa ma yin 'di la dga' ba thal/ /gang gis mtha' dag ri yis zlums pas sa gzhi ni/ /dang po'i dus su nga las nu ni gnas pa bzhin/ /gang zhig dbang po la yang slong bar 'os min pa/ /
<p>69b.4</p>bdag gi de ni pha rol rnams la slong mos 'tsho/ /gangs 'di snying po lhun po las ni khyad 'phags shing / /gsal bas nyi ma la dang mdzes pas zla ba la/ /'gros kyis glang po che la dbyangs kyis khyu mchog la/ /des ni slong mo za zhing sa ni rdzogs la min/ /de nas bu yi 'du shes kyis ni 'phyo
<p>69b.5</p>ba nyid/ /rgyal po'i bsam pa 'di ni rnam par mkhyen nas dang / /'jig rten lhag ma la yang rdzas su brtse ba ste/ /de yi don du sangs rgyas mkha' la 'phur bar gyur/ /nyi ma'i shing rta phyag gis reg par mdzad nas ni/ /rlung gis bsnyen pa'i lam la zhabs dag gis gshegs shing / /sku la
<p>69b.6</p>gcig tu gyur zhing du mar gyur pa dang / /mang po nyid du gyur nas gcig tu gyur pa'o/ /sa la chu bzhin du yang zhugs shing thogs med la/ /chu yi logs la sa la bzhin du spyod pa dang / /ra ba dang ni ri la thad kar mdzad pa dang / /thogs pa med cing mkha' la bzhin du rab tu zhugs/ /lus kyi
<p>69b.7</p>phyed kyis chu yi char pa 'bebs pa dang / /phyed kyis me bzhin du ni 'bar bar gyur pa ste/ /ri bos 'bar ba'i sman dang rab tu 'bar ba bzhin/ /mkha' la gang zhig 'bar dang 'bar bas mdzes par gyur/ /dbang phyug mngon par 'dod pa'i skye bo de yi ni/ /sems kyi rab tu dga' ba de ltar skyed
<p>70a</p>
<p>70a.1</p>nas ni/ /nyi ma gnyis pa bzhin du mkha' la bzhugs nas su/ /mi skyong la ni chos dag bgro bar mdzad pa'o/ /mi skyong khyed kyis bdag la gang zhig ltos pa dang / /mya ngan rjes su zhugs pa snying rje'i bdag nyid shes/ /bu la dga' ba de ni chod mdzod zhi bar gshegs/ /
<p>70a.2</p>bdag las bu yi 'bras bu gsar pa snoms mdzod cig /gang zhig sngon chad bu yis pha la ma byin zhing / /sngon ni pha yis bu las rab tu ma thob pa/ /rgyal srid las khyad 'phags shing mtho ris las khyad 'phags/ /rgyal po mchog gi bdud rtsi de ni bzhes mdzod cig /sa skyong las kyis bdag nyid las
<p>70a.3</p>kyi skye gnas dang / /las kyi rten dang las kyi rnam smin skal ba dang / /las kyi dbang gis gnas par 'gro ba shes nas ni/ /phan pa'i ched du las gang gyur pa de bsnyen mdzod/ /'jig rten de nyid rtogs nas dang ni btsal nas su/ /dam pa'i las ni mi yi bshes min gzhan ma yin/ /
<p>70a.4</p>thams cad bor nas las dang lhan cig khyod kyi ni/ /rten dang bral zhing gcig pur 'gro bar bya ba'o/ /lha 'am dmyal ba dud 'gro mi yi 'jig rten du/ /las kyi rten las son pa'i 'jig rten 'gro ba ste/ /srid pa'i rgyu ni rnam pa gsum dang skye gnas gsum/ /sna tshogs las ni 'jig rten pa
<p>70a.5</p>yis rab tu byed/ /de phyir sde tshan gnyis ni yang dag 'jug par yang / /lus dang ngag gi las 'di rnam par dag pa dang / /yid kyis rab tu zhi la 'bad par bya ba ste/ /de ni bdag gi don yin gzhan don ma yin no/ /'gro ba chu yi dba' rlabs g.yo bar shes nas ni/ /brtags nas khyod kyis
<p>70a.6</p>srid pa rnams su dga' mi bya/ /las ni yongs su zad phyir dam pa'i las gang de/ /mchog tu bde ba'i don du gang gyur bsnyen par bya/ /rgyu skar 'khor lo mkha' la bzhin du rtag par ni/ /'jig rten yongs su 'khor bar shes par byas nas ni/ /rtse mo 'das nas lha nas lha yang lhung ba
<p>70a.7</p>ste/ /kye ma mir gyur smos ci blo gtad byed pa su/ /bde ba rnams las mchog tu thar pa'i bde ba dang / /dga' ba rnams las bdag tu dga' ba gtsor shes nas/ /lag 'gro rnams kyis brang la bzhin du bdag ldan ni/ /su zhig 'jigs pa du ma'i dpal gyis bde la dga'/ /de phyir
<p>70b</p>
<p>70b.1</p>brten pa khyim la mes bzhin 'jig rten ni/ /'jigs pa chen po dang ni yongs ldan mthong nas ni/ /gang zhig skye 'chi ngal ba mya ngan dang bral ba/ /zhi zhing brtan pa'i go 'phang de ni slongs mdzod cig /don gyis ma yin g.yul gyis ma yin mtshon gyis min/ /gang la rta dang glang pos don ni yod
<p>70b.2</p>ma yin/ /skyon ni dgra bo rnams kyi sde de choms mdzod dang / /de las rgyal na rnam par rgyal ba gzhal du med/ /sdug bsngal dang ni sdug bsngal gyi rgyu zhi ba dang / /zhi ba yi yang mngon pa'i thabs ni shes par mdzod/ /bzhi po 'di yi kun nas khong du chud pa las/ /'jigs pa chen po dang
<p>70b.3</p>ni ngan 'gro rnams 'gog go/ /de nas bde bar gshegs pas rdzu 'phrul gyi sngon du/ /zhing du byas pa'i sems la dga' ba skyes pa ste/ /thos nas mi skyong de yis chos ni rab thob cing / /dga' bzhin thal mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces gsol to/ /blo ldan dang bcas 'bras bu dang bcas khyed
<p>70b.4</p>dgyes shing / /sdug bsngal chen po las ni rnam grol khyed dgyes so/ /mya ngan ched du don med sa sbyin bdag dga' la/ /bu yi 'bras bu dang ldan bdag ni dga' bar gyur/ /phun tshogs spangs nas gshegs pa khyed ni gnas su gyur/ /ngal ba chen pos dub las khyed ni gnas su gyur/ /
<p>70b.5</p>dga' ba'i gnyen 'dun dga' ba khyod kyis bor ba rnams/ /bdag cag rnams ni snying rje bar du gnas su gyur/ /lha yi drang srong rnams sam rgyal po'i drang srong rnams/ /de rnams sngon dus na yang gang la ma gshegs pa/ /nyam thag 'jig rten dag gi dge ba'i ched du lam/ /nges par
<p>70b.6</p>legs pa 'di dang khyed kyis lhag par thob/ /khyod ni 'khor los sgyur bar gal te gyur na ni/ /bdag gi dga' ba de ltar 'gyur ba ma yin zhing / /rnam pa de ltar rdzu 'phrul 'di dang khyod kyi chos/ /mthong nas ji ltar bdag gi bstan pa dga' bar 'gyur/ /'dir ni yang srid nyid du sbyor
<p>70b.7</p>ba'i chos la ni/ /'khor los sgyur bas skye dgu rnams ni skyong ba ste/ /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal chen po rnams ni 'joms pa la/ /'jig rten ched du chos kyang thub pa khyod kyis gsungs/ /gang gi rdzu 'phrul 'di dang rnam rgyas blo gros dang / /'khor ba'i 'jigs pa mtha' dag nges par
<p>71a</p>
<p>71a.1</p>log pa ni/ /dpal dang bral yang 'jig rten na khyod dbang phyug ste/ /dpal ni 'phel yang dbang med sred bcas ma yin no/ /brtse ba'i chos kyis bstan pa'i 'os gyur pa/ /shAkya'i rgyal pos mang po de dag smras nas ni/ /rgyal po nyid dang yab nyid du ni gnas na yang / /
<p>71a.2</p>sras la de nyid khong du chud phyir phyag byas so/ /thub pa'i mthu ni lhag par thob pa mthong nas dang / /de nyid rab tu 'bigs pa'i bstan bcos mthong nas dang / /bla ma rgyal pos sbyar ba'i mchod pa mthong nas ni/ /du ma rnams kyis rab tu 'byung phyir re 'dod byas/ /de nas gzhon nu mang po 'bras bu la gnas rnams/ /chos kyi
<p>71a.3</p>cho ga de nyid rab tu thob gyur te/ /sngags dang 'dod pa chen po rnams la ltos med nas/ /byams pa'i gnyen 'dun du ba rnams ni spangs nas so/ /kun dga' mdzes dga' kra mi la dang ma 'gags pa/ /dga' bo nye dga' dag dang de nas 'khyil pa 'dzin/ /slob ma'i lkog tu ston pa yis ni lha sbyin te/ /thub pas rjes su
<p>71a.4</p>bslabs pa de rnams byung bar gyur/ /de nas mdun na 'don gyi bu ni bdag nyid che/ /'char kas lam de nyid la rab tu song ba ste/ /de yis nges pa rab tu mthong nas de bzhin du/ /nye ba 'khor dang rgyun shes bu yi blo byas so/ /rgyal po yis kyang sras kyi mthu ni mthong nas dang / /mchog gi bdud rtsi rgyun ni
<p>71a.5</p>rab tu thob byas nas/ /chags pa med par rgyal srid spun zla la byin zhing / /rgyal po'i drang srong spyod pas khyim rnams la bsnyen to/ /de skad ces pa la sogs legs pa'i gnyen rnams dang / /'khor dang gnyen rnams rjes su brtul nas sangs rgyas ni/ /mchi ma dang bcas grong khyer pa yis mngon
<p>71a.6</p>dga' ba/ /rang gnas grong khyer la ni dus su rab zhugs pa/ /don kun grub pa zhes pa rgyal po'i sras po ni/ /don mdzad grub pa grong khyer du ni rab zhugs pa/ /zhes ni don thos khang pa rnams su mi mo rnams/ /sgo rnams dang ni skar khung rnams la mnyam par brten/ /mtshams kyi sprin gyis phyed
<p>71a.7</p>bkag 'od zer ldan pa bzhin/ /ngur smrig bsnams shing mdzes pa de ni rab mthong nas/ /bud med de rnams mig nas mchi ma phyung ba ste/ /pad+ma dang mtshungs thal mo rnams kyis phyag 'tshal lo/ /chos kyis dang ni gzugs kyis gsal bar gyur pa ni/ /'og tu zhal gzigs gshegs pa
<p>71b</p>
<p>71b.1</p>de ni mthong gyur nas/ /brtse ba dang ni gus pa rnam par ston pa ste/ /mchi mas rnyogs pa'i mig can rab myos ma rnams zlos/ /legs skyes dbu ni bzhar bar rnam par mdzad nas dang / /na bza' rnying pa yongs su gsol nas dang / /sku la gser gyi kha dog rab tu g.yogs nas
<p>71b.2</p>dang / /des ni spyan mig rab tu bkod nas gshegs/ /gang zhig gdung ba skyob pa'i gdugs dkar bsnyen phyir dang / /sras po rnam par dul ba blta ba'i phyir 'ongs shing / /kun nas gnas phyir 'os shing rgyal ba'i phyir 'os pa/ /des ni lhung bzed yang dag yongs su bzung nas gshegs/ /
<p>71b.3</p>'gram par ta ma la yi lo ma rnam bkod pa'i/ /mdzes ma'i gdong dang gdung ba skyob pa'i gdugs dkar ni/ /gang gis bsnyen par 'os shing mgyogs 'gro 'os pa ste/ /des ni lhung bzed yongs su bzung nas rkang pas gshegs/ /sa skyong bdag skyes rnams kyi dgra rnams zad par dang / /dga'
<p>71b.4</p>ba rnams kyi chags dang 'gro ba'i rjes chags par/ /blta bar 'os shing sna tshogs dbu rgyan bsnams pa gang / /des ni sa yi gnya' shing gang tsam gzigs shing gshegs/ /'di yi blta ba ci zhig mtshan nyid de ni ci/ /don gnyer ci zhig rol pas dgra bor gyur pa ci/ /gang 'di brtul zhugs
<p>71b.5</p>dang ni lhan cig rol ba ste/ /bu byis rnams dang mo btsun mdzangs ma rnams dang ni/ /rgyal po'i mna' ma nges par mya ngan 'dzin ma'o/ /grags 'dzin ma de shin tu dka' thub byed pa ste/ /gang gis jo bo'i rab tu spyod pa 'di thos shing / /thos nas kyang ni gnas shing nyams par 'gro ba med/ /'di
<p>71b.6</p>yi gzugs ni nges par rjes su mthun pa dang / /kha dog ngan pa'i gzugs 'di snang ba mthong nas ni/ /sras 'dod mi dbang rgyal po ji lta bur gyur zhing / /'tshe ba'i dgra bo la yang ji lta bur byed dam/ /mchi mas gang ba'i sras po sgra gcan 'dzin mthong nas/ /gal te de lta nyid du 'di ni
<p>71b.7</p>chags ma yin/ /byams pa'i gnyen rnams las kyang gzhan du kha bltas pa/ /'di 'dra nges pa'i brtul zhugs la ni dge legs shog /gzi mdangs dang ni lus kyi dbyibs dang 'gros sam ste/ /bde ba'i rab tu 'jug la nges par tshad ma yin/ /yon tan de rnams dag gis
<p>72a</p>
<p>72a.1</p>'di ni mdzes pa ste/ /zhi bas ldan zhing yul rnams kyis ni rnam par bral/ /sna tshogs ston ni rang mtshungs bsam pa yang dag yongs bzung nas/ /de skad ces sogs rab myos ma rnams mang po rnam par labs/ /sangs rgyas ma chags thugs kyang rang gi grong khyer
<p>72a.2</p>la gshegs nas/ /bsod snyoms brnyes shing n+ya gro d+ha yi mtshan ma'i nags su gshegs/ /nyung ngu nyung ngu'i bsod snyoms sbyin pa rnams kyis nor rdzas phra zhing dge ba ma byas skye bo sgrol bar mdzad bzhed pa/ /spyod pa 'di yis yang dag tshim pa ma yin dge sbyong skye bo bsam pa ma thul ba la
<p>72a.3</p>brten par mdzad bzhed la/ /'jig rten dag na skyid de ba zhes rgol ba nub par mdzad bzhed de bzhin yongs su bris nyid ston par mdzad bzhed pa/ /brtag par snyam la bsod snyoms phyir ni yab kyi grong khyer la ni sred med thugs mnga' de bzhin gshegs pa zhugs par gyur/ /sangs rgyas kyi
<p>72a.4</p>spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ yab dang sras mjal ba'i le'u ste bcu dgu pa'o// //nga rgyal nyid kyis skye bo dam pa ma smod cig /bshes gnyen 'du shes dka' thub rnams ni ma 'joms shig /nyon mongs dbang gis dam pa'i brtul zhugs ma byed cig /
<p>72a.5</p>dam pa min pa'i lta ba cung zad ma bsnyen cig /mtshar la ma 'gro mi dge'i lam la ma gnas shig /rgyags par ma 'gro dga' min mi bzod ma nyan cig /snyan grags mi bzad brdzun la blo gros ma 'dzin cig /bstan bcos mthong las lhag par gtor ma ma 'phrog cig /blo ni mnyam
<p>72a.6</p>par zhog cing chos ni gyis mdzod cig /dam pa rnams dang sbrel mdzod ri mo khod mdzod cig /ji ltar phul byung 'di ni thob nas slar yang ni/ /rgya cher mngon par 'gro ba de ltar gyis mdzod cig /brtson 'grus brtsams nas dang ni bstan pa yongs bzung nas/ /rigs pa rnams ni bskyed
<p>72a.7</p>nas skyon rnams zil mnan nas/ /'chi ba yang dag dran nas 'phags pa'i bya ba gyis/ /che ba'i bdag nyid thob nas zhi lam thob par gyis/ /gang gi 'bras bu 'di ni zhi ba skyong ba ni/ /las de nyid ni slar yang byed par 'os pa ste/ /yid gzhungs ldan pa 'di dang byed pa byas pa nyid/ /'bras bu
<p>72b</p>
<p>72b.1</p>gang zhig mthong bas sa bon bskrun par byed/ /'di na mchog gyur gang zhig sdig pa byed pa ste/ /snang ba de ni mun par gnas pa bdag gi lugs/ /chos ni gtso bo skyes bu gtso bo ma yin pa/ /mun pa snang ba la ni gnas pa bdag gi lugs/ /khyad 'phags gang zhig chos kyi cho gar 'jug pa ste/ /
<p>72b.2</p>dkar po dkar por mchog tu 'gro ba bdag gi lugs/ /dman pa gang zhig sdig pa'i las ni byed pa ste/ /de yang mun pa mun pa'i mtha' ru 'gro ba lugs/ /de phyir phung po bzhi po de rnams shes byas nas/ /rgyal po 'bad pa gyis shig de ltar ji ltar 'dir/ /bde nas bde bar gal te 'gro bar
<p>72b.3</p>'dod na ni/ /phyogs ni gsum pa bsnyen zhing snga ma ma yin no/ /gzhan gyis gzhan la dge ba byed pa ma yin zhing / /ci ste byed na de la rjes su 'gro ma yin/ /byis pa'i nyams pa yod min rang la 'thob pa ste/ /ma byas pa yi 'ong ba 'grub pa yod ma yin/ /ma byas pa yang brgya
<p>72b.4</p>la byed pa ma yin zhing / /ma byas pa ni gzhan du dge legs 'gyur ma yin/ /der ni 'gro ba la yang nor ni yod min te/ /de phyir dge ba'i las kyi cho gar 'bad pa bgyis/ /gang zhig sdig pa lhag par spyod pa legs min zhing / /gson pa'i 'jig rten na de'i bdag la dga' ma yin/ /bdag
<p>72b.5</p>gi ched du bdag gis sdig pa byas nas ni/ /gzhan du 'bras bu bdag nyid kho nas longs spyod do/ /rgyal po chen po ri bo chen po bzhi rnams ni/ /'ongs pa rnams su 'gro ba kun nas srub pa ste/ /chos kyi bya ba rnam pa sna tshogs bsten las ni/ /ji ltar 'thad pas gzhan na bya ba ci zhig
<p>72b.6</p>yod/ /rga dang rgud pa nad dang de nas 'chi ba ste/ /bzhi po 'di rnams de bzhin du ni 'ongs pa ste/ /ri bo rnams kyis kun nas bskor ba bzhin du ni/ /'jig rten mtha' dag dbang med 'khol bar byed pa'o/ /de nas 'ongs pa rnams su dbang med sdug bsngal te/ /rten ni yod min mngon du
<p>72b.7</p>'thab min srung ba med/ /der ni byed pa'i ched du nor med chad pa med/ /chos las ma gtogs sman gzhan yod min na/ /de ltar mi rtag gyur na gson pa'i 'jig rten na/ /glog ni g.yo ba'i yul la rab tu zhugs pa na/ /'chi ba'i lag pa'i rtse la yongs su gnas pa ste/ /chos ma yin pas
<p>73a</p>
<p>73a.1</p>'bras bu longs spyod par 'os min/ /dbang chen dang mtshungs mi dbang de dang de rnams ni/ /g.yul du lha yi mngon par 'thab la phyin nas kyang / /rab tu rgyas pa rnams dang nges par zum pa rnams/ /dus kyi dus su bde dang sdug bsngal skal ba'o/ /'byung po 'dzin
<p>73a.2</p>pa'i sa yang zad par 'gro ba ste/ /'jig pa'i mes ni lhun po de bzhin sreg par byed/ /rgya mtsho chen po yongs su bskams par 'gro ba ste/ /dbu ba dang mtshungs mi yi 'jig rten kye ma ci/ /shugs byas nas kyang rlung ni zhi bar 'gro ba ste/ /'jig rten gdungs nas kyang ni nyi ma
<p>73a.3</p>nub par 'gro/ /bsregs nas kyang ni me nyid 'da' bar nyer 'gro ste/ /gang de de ltar gnas par 'gyur ba yin snyam mam/ /lus po 'di ni yun rings dus su bsrungs kyang ngam/ /sna tshogs longs spyod rnams kyis nye bar bskyangs kyang ni/ /de yis 'dir ni nyin zhag 'ga' zhig bzhugs
<p>73a.4</p>nas su/ /skye bo chen po'i rjes su brtse ba mdzad nas ni/ /bde bar 'pham byed kyis ni phyag gis mngon bsrungs pa'i/ /grong khyer la ni chen po'i tshogs kyis rab tu dpags/ /me tog rab rgyas mya ngan med pas gsal byas shing / /yan lag dmar por gyur cing khu byug skad sgrogs
<p>73a.5</p>pa/ /ti se'i gangs ltar mtho ba'i lding khang phreng ba can/ /dpal ldan rgyal byed tshal ni de nas rab tu thob/ /des ni gtsang ma'i chus gang phreng ba dkar po can/ /gser gyi bum pa dang bcas bum pa blangs nas ni/ /de nas dus su rgyal byed tshal ni bzang sbyin gyis/ /de bzhin gshegs pa la
<p>73a.6</p>ni rab tu phul bar gyur/ /de nas shAkya thub pa lta 'dod rgyal po ni/ /sde rab 'pham byed rgyal byed tshal du song ba ste/ /song nas de nas bkur sti byas te thub pa la/ /rab tu btud cing gdan byas tshig 'di gsol ba'o/ /thub pa grong khyer 'dir ni khyed kyi gnas bzhed pa/ /nges par rang ni ko
<p>73a.7</p>sa la rnams kyi dge ba'o/ /de nyid gzigs pa 'di 'dra brten pa med pa ni/ /nye bar 'tshe byas yul ni skal ba med pa'am/ /khyed mthong ba 'am yang na mngon par phyag 'tshal ba/ /yang dag thob po bdag cag rnams kyi rjes bzung phyir/ /dam pa rnams kyi 'dus pa thob nas 'jig rten na/ /tshim
<p>73b</p>
<p>73b.1</p>pa med kyang ji ltar tshim pa nyid yin no/ /gang gis rten can rlung ni rab tu g.yos pa ste/ /de yi bdag nyid las ni nye ba las 'gro ste/ /mkha' 'gro'i bya rnams lhun po'i 'dus pa nyer thob nas/ /rang bzhin rnam par spangs nas gser du 'gyur ba'o/ /de phyir 'di dang che ge mor ni mgon gyur
<p>73b.2</p>zhing / /skye bo legs pa'i rten las gzhan min bdag gi nags/ /ga d+ha'i sras po thub pa chen po rab thob nas/ /phur bu gsum pa'i khyim ltar lta na mdzes par gyur/ /'jig rten dag na rnyed pa rab rnyed sna tshogs pa/ /tshad dang ldan pa dag ni mdzad pa can yin la/ /khyod kyi nye ba las ni don gang
<p>73b.3</p>yin pa rnams/ /de dag rnams kyi grangs med nyams pa yod ma yin/ /legs pa khyod kyi nges pa'i lta ba'i lta ba las/ /'di las gzhan du rnyed pa shes pa ma yin zhing / /khyab bdag bdag ni gnod pa rnyed bla sdug bsngal ba/ /chags pa dang ldan rgyal po'i chos la spyod par 'gyur/ /de ltar dbang
<p>73b.4</p>po dang mtshungs rgyal po de yis ni/ /rnam pa de ltar mngon du gyur te gsan nas ni/ /don dang 'dod pa dag gi chags pa mkhyen nas su/ /de yi bsam pa yang dag bskul ba thub pas gsungs/ /mi dbang khyod kyi tshig 'di ngo mtshar che ma yin/ /khyod kyi spyod pa 'di ni legs pa rnams la min/ /'og
<p>73b.5</p>nas 'phos pa 'gro bar 'dod pa rnams kyis ni/ /phan pa 'dod pa'i dam pa'i skyes bu rnams la sdang / /gang phyir sa skyong khyed kyi dgongs ba de nyid ni/ /des na khyod la 'dir ni cung zad smra 'dod de/ /de ni shes par gyis shig bdag gi lta ba ni/ /'bras bcas ji ltar gyur pa khyed kyi de ltar gyis/ /mi skyong
<p>73b.6</p>rgyal bo'i dus kyis bcings nas bkug pa na/ /mdza' bshes ma yin gnyen min phun tshogs rjes 'gro min/ /thams cad kyis ni dman zhing dbang med 'gro ba ni/ /grib ma bzhin du las gcig rjes su 'gro ba nyid/ /de phyir mtho ris dang ni grags pa dam pa ni/ /mngon par 'dod bzhin chos kyi rgyal
<p>73b.7</p>srid rjes su skyongs/ /rmongs pa las ni chos la 'khrul pa'i rgyal po yi/ /rgyal srid de nyid mtho ris na yang ma yin no/ /'dir ni rgyal srid yang dag yongs su bskyangs nas ni/ /chos las ring min rta rid mtho ris rab 'thob nas/ /'dir ni rmongs las mi yi bdag po ni kum+b+ha/ /chos las
<p>74a</p>
<p>74a.1</p>'phos shing ka shi rnams su sa la zhugs/ /'phags pa yi dang sdig pa yi ni las kyi ni/ /khyod la dper bstan zhi ba bdag gis de smras te/ /rang gi skye dgu rnams ni rtag tu legs bsrungs shing / /dpyad nas de phyir brtan pa dge la 'bad pa gyis/ /ji ltar srog chags
<p>74a.2</p>rnams ni gtse bar ma byed cig /rtag par dbang po rnams ni rol par ma byed cig /'phags min gyis bsnyen khro ba 'dzin par ma byed cig /phyogs min bya bar sems ni g.yo bar ma byed cig /nga rgyal dang ni rgyags pa khur nas dus su ni/ /rab tu 'thor zhing shin tu gyur pa gnyid log gyur/ /
<p>74a.3</p>rnam pa de ltar 'jig rten 'gro ba shes nas su/ /de la ma nyal dge ba la ni gnyid ma log /'khor ba'i phyogs ni g.yo bar 'dzegs nas su/ /nges par ltung na sa gzhi bag med 'gyur ba'o/ /gang zhig bde ba 'brel min de ni bsnyen bya min/ /gang gis 'bras bu legs min gang de bya
<p>74a.4</p>ba min/ /gang zhig dge la sbyor min de ni bshes ma yin/ /sdug bsngal rnam par 'joms min gang de ye shes min/ /gal te ye shes min na yang srid ma yin zhing / /srid par gyur na lus med nyid la yin pa ste/ /lus su gyur na yul las thar pa ma yin zhing / /nyi tshe ma yin 'dod
<p>74a.5</p>pa'i srid pa don med do/ /gang phyir lha na gnas rnams dus kyi dbang gis ni/ /gzugs med rnams kyang mdzad pa can phyir mi rtag ste/ /de bzhin 'jug pa min la blo gros zhugs bya zhing / /gal te 'jug pa med na sdug bsngal yod ma yin/ /gang phyir lus ni 'gro dang gnas pa la sogs pa'i/ /
<p>74a.6</p>sna tshogs rten gyi sdug bsngal dag gi rtsa ba ste/ /de phyir lus med du ni ye shes nus pa gang / /de yod lus kyi bu lon yod pa ma yin no/ /gang las 'gro bas 'dod pa'i ched du bskyed pa yis/ /sdug bsngal chen po du ma rnams la nyer 'gro ste/ /'di las 'dod pa'i srid las rnam par
<p>74a.7</p>dben nus shing / /sdug bsngal rnams las chags med nyam thag yod ma yin/ /de phyir gzugs dang bral ba'i lha rnams na yang ngam/ /'dod pa rnams dang ldan pa'i gzugs ldan rnams na yang / /skor ba nyid phyir 'jug pa zhi ba ma yin na/ /'dod pa spyod pa drug po rnams su sngon nyid do/ /
<p>74b</p>
<p>74b.1</p>rnam pa de ltar mi rtag sdug bsngal de med cing / /rtag par 'bar ba'i 'jig rten gsum po nyid mthong nas/ /bya tshang shing la sgong skyes rnams kyis gdung ba ltar/ /gang du 'jug la smon lam rigs pa ma yin no/ /mchog de rig par bya zhing gzhan ni rig bya min/ /mchog
<p>74b.2</p>de blo gros yin zhing gzhan ni blo gros min/ /mchog de bya ba yin zhing gzhan ni grub pa min/ /chos 'di khyim dang ldan pa'i skye bo rnams kyis te/ /yod pa min zhes de ltar nges par rig bya min/ /nags sam khyim na gnas pa dag gi zhi ba ni/ /gang gis sgrub pa yod pa de yis
<p>74b.3</p>yod pa'o/ /tshad pas mngon par gdungs pa chu la rnam zhugs te/ /spyi las thams cad tshim pa nye bar 'gro ba nyid/ /sgron ma dang ldan mun pa ru ni mthong ba ste/ /rnal 'byor tshad ma'o na tshod ma yin rigs ma yin/ /kha cig nags na gnas kyang na tshod la mi sbyor/ /brtul zhugs zad
<p>74b.4</p>cing ngan 'gro la ni bsnyen pa nyid/ /kha cig khyim na gnas kyang rnam dag las can ni/ /bag dang ldan pa nges legs la ni bsnyen pa'o/ /mun pa'i rgya mtsho la ni lta ngan dba' rlabs can/ /sred pa'i chu la srog chags rnam par 'phyo rnams su/ /shes rab gru bo dran dang brtson 'grus skya ba
<p>74b.5</p>ni/ /gang gis yod pa de ni de la sgrol ba yod/ /de ltar yul la mchog tu song ba'i rgyal po de yis ni/ /thams cad mkhyen las chos kyi de nyid 'di ni nyer thob nas/ /rgyal srid ngan pa mi rtag g.yo zhes nyer skyes blo can ni/ /myos pa dang bral gnyis 'thung bzhin du mnyan yod nyid du zhugs/ /
<p>74b.6</p>sa dbang btud pa de ni shes nas mu stegs can gzhan rnams/ /der ni stobs bcu pa la rdzu 'phrul gyis ni 'gran btsugs gyur/ /sa skyong las ni rnam par gsol nas de nas bdag 'pham pa'i/ /drang srong gis ni rdzu 'phrul ched du sdug pas gnas pa byas/ /de nas gsal zhing 'od zer 'phro
<p>74b.7</p>ba dang bcas dkyil 'khor can/ /skar ma rnams ni 'bar bar gyur pa'i nyi ma shar ba bzhin/ /yang dag dga' zhing rnam pa sna tshogs blo can ston pa rnams/ /der ni thub pas rdzu 'phrul rnam pa mang pos pham par mdzad/ /de nas mnyan yod kyi ni de las skyes pa'i grags pa dang / /bkur
<p>75a</p>
<p>75a.1</p>sti nges pa mchog gi dpal gyis yongs su spangs par gyur/ /de nyid kyis ni srid pa gsum las gyen du 'dzegs pa ste/ /de'i phyir chos dag gsung bar bzhed cing yul la phan phyir ro/ /de nas thub pa mtho ris gnas pa'i yul ni ye shes kyis/ /rnam par btul nas
<p>75a.2</p>mtho ris gshegs pa lo ni rnam phul des/ /mkha' la lha yi rgyal po'i bsod snyoms cho ga bzhin bzhes nas/ /lha yi 'jig rten dag nas sAm ka par ni yang dag babs/ /de la gzhal med gnam sa'i logs la babs pa yi/ /zhi ba thob cing ltos pa dang bcas lha rnams rjes su 'ongs/ /sar gnas nam
<p>75a.3</p>mkha'i logs la gyen du gdong phyogs rgyal po ni/ /de dang de rnams mgo bo rnams kyis btud cing rab tu bzung / /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ rgyal byed kyi tshal rab tu bzhes pa'i le'u ste nyi shu pa'o// //thar 'dod lha na gnas rnams dang / /skyed ma
<p>75a.4</p>mtho ris su btul nas/ /thub pas gdul bya rnams 'dul zhing / /de nas de ni 'jig rten rgyus/ /ri lnga'i dbus kyi grong khyer du/ /'od ldan 'tsho byed dbang po dang / /gro bzhin skyes dang yan lag sbyin/ /rnam par 'dren pas de nas btul/ /rgyal po'i bu ni 'jigs med dang / /dpal
<p>75a.5</p>sbas dang ni nye ba 'khor/ /n+ya gro d+ha sogs mthar ldan rnams/ /snga ma'i lta ba las zlog go/ /chos kyi thos pa nyid las ni/ /mi skyong dpal ni yangs pa can/ /spos 'dzin gyi ni dbang phyug 'dir/ /pad+ma zhes bya rnam par btul/ /de nas gnod sbyin gangs ldan dang / /rtse mo brgya pa de nas ni/ /rnam
<p>75a.6</p>rgyas pha rol gnon pa yis/ /rnam rgyas ri bor btul ba'o/ /yon tan gzigs pas mi skyong ni/ /lta byed btsun mo'i 'khor bcas la/ /'tsho byed a mra'i nags tshal du/ /mtshan mo dad pas sbyar bar mdzad/ /de nas pha rol 'gro ba can/ /bram ze zhi bar 'gro rnams des/ /rdo ba'i
<p>75a.7</p>ri bor phra mo yi/ /tshigs bcad don rnams klog tu bcug /de nas dam pa dran mdzad pas/ /dngos su nor sbyin mthong ba mo/ /dga' ba'i skyed ma legs ldan ma/ /'od ma'i tsher ma can du btul/ /de nas brtan ldan grong khyer du/ /brtsegs sbyin gnyis skyes dam pa ni/ /mchod
<p>75b</p>
<p>75b.1</p>sbyin rnam pa sna tshogs kyis/ /mchod 'dod thar pa'i chos la btsud/ /de nas lus 'phags ri bo ru/ /btsud phyed rtse mo nyid dang ni/ /lha min skyes ma dang lha rnams/ /nges par 'dzin du btsud par gyur/ /de nas ang+ga'i grong khyer du/ /gnod sbyin gang ba bzang po dang / /mchog dang dbyug pa
<p>75b.2</p>dkar dmar dang / /gtum po lto 'phyo che rnams btul/ /a pa Na yi grong khyer du/ /bram ze ke bya she la dag /dka' thub thob pa thar par sbyar/ /'tsho byed sor mo'i phreng ba can/ /bran bzangs dang mtshungs gnyis skyes ni/ /bcom ldan rdzu 'phrul phun tshogs kyis/ /phra mo rnams su
<p>75b.3</p>btul ba mdzad/ /gang ba bzang po dang mtshungs rdzas/ /lug ces bya ba bzang pos 'tsho/ /nor sbyin bzang dang bzang po'i bu/ /bzang por yang dag rtogs par mdzad/ /de nas tshangs pa'i tshe ldan ming / /rnam rgyas tshangs pa'i tshe ldan pa/ /gang gi smra ba smra mchog gis/ /lus 'phags po
<p>75b.4</p>yi grong du pham/ /yangs pa can gyi rdzing bu ru/ /srin bu sha za dang seng ge /la sogs lits+tsha bI rnams dang / /mchog dang bden byed nyid btul to/ /de nas las bzang pos gnod sbyin/ /bzang po bzang po'i sems ldan pa/ /rgyan byed dang mtshungs grong khyer du/ /chos kyi lam la btsud
<p>75b.5</p>pa'o/ /de nas blo dang ldan pa yis/ /shin tu mi bzad 'brog tu ni/ /gnod sbyin 'brog gnas zhes bya dang / /gzhon nu legs 'ongs la ston to/ /de nas gnod sbyin sdig med la/ /gnod sbyin bdag pos phyag byas pas/ /bde dga'i grong du thar pa ni/ /thar pa gzigs pas gdams pa
<p>75b.6</p>mdzad/ /thub pa grags pa yangs rnams dang / /gnod sbyin drag po'i las can dang / /kha spu ldan pa gnyis la ni/ /ga yar drang srong gis bstan to/ /de nas drang srong dkar min gyi/ /tsha bo kA t+yA ya na ni/ /bA rA Na sI'i grong du sngon/ /gnyis skyes stobs bcu ldan pas btul/ /mtsho 'obs
<p>75b.7</p>bde bar pha rol 'gro'i/ /grong la rdzu 'phrul gyis gshegs nas/ /dus su tshangs pa rna bstod la/ /de nas des ni rjes su bstan/ /rjes su bstan de rab dang bas/ /drang srong mchog gi gtsug lag khang / /rtag par dri ldan kha la reg /tsan+dan rang bzhin byed du bcug /de nas gang du
<p>76a</p>
<p>76a.1</p>thub pa'i zhabs/ /rdo las 'khor lo'i mtshan mthong bas/ /ser skya dka' thub ldan pa ni/ /'od zer ldan pa des btul lo/ /de nas gnod sbyin glang po la/ /glang po ldan par bstan pa ste/ /de bzhin dgra po bong bu ni/ /bcom brlag tu ni btul ba'o/ /
<p>76a.2</p>yul 'khor skyong dang rdzas mnyam pa/ /yul 'khor skyong zhes dran pa ni/ /grong rdal rags pa'i mdzod ldan du/ /ston pas de nas rnam par btul/ /tshangs pa dang 'dra skye bo mchog /dgra can du ni btul ba ste/ /mkhas pa rgya chen skyes bu can/ /nyon mongs dul bar de
<p>76a.3</p>bzhin no/ /'jigs bcas kyi dang mtshams bzangs kyi/ /bu'i bu mos 'jug bu dag dang / /mu stegs gzhan rnams kyi mun pa/ /mnyan yod nyid du thub pas bcom/ /'dir ni bram ze mchod sbyin can/ /dge sogs rnams dang rigs gtsang dang / /ko sa la yi dbang phyug ni/ /
<p>76a.4</p>sangs rgyas nyid kyis dad pas sbyar/ /de nas bram ze mkhas pa ni/ /bram ze su ka sA ri dang / /she ta bi ka'i 'brog zhi bar/ /bstan pa mchog gis bstan pa'o/ /de nas 'thab pa'i grong khyer du/ /grong khyer gtso dang dus byed dang / /'jigs pa'i las can chu srin klu/ /rab
<p>76a.5</p>tu ma zhi zhi bar mdzad/ /de nas b+har ga rnams su des/ /gnod sbyin 'jigs byed btul mdzad cing / /rigs med kyi ni bla ma gnyis/ /rgan po de bzhin rjes su bzung / /nor ldan gyi mchog dbyangs ldan dang / /bud med sgur mchog sogs rnams dang / /skyes chen de rnams de rnams
<p>76a.6</p>ni/ /kau shAm bIr ni rjes su bzung / /de nas spos 'dzin yul nyid dang / /klu chen sog ma med pa ni/ /dul ba'i bdag nyid dul ba la/ /nang gi pha rol son par gshegs/ /'bar zhing 'jigs pa'i las can ni/ /mthar byed bzhin du sreg 'dod pa/ /rnam par btul nas mkhas
<p>76a.7</p>pa des/ /dus su de nas gdams ngag bstan/ /de la sogs pa'i 'byung po rnams/ /sa pa rnams dang mkha' 'gro rnams/ /btul nas tshigs su rgya mtsho bzhin/ /sangs rgyas grags pa 'phel bar gyur/ /che ba'i bdag nyid de mthong nas/ /lha sbyin rlom sems byas pa ste/ /bsam
<p>76b</p>
<p>76b.1</p>gtan rnams las 'khrul thob cing / /'dra ba min pa mang po byas/ /nye bar bcom pa'i sems ldan des/ /thub pa dge 'dun dben byas shing / /'phye las 'dod pa ma byas te/ /de la gnod pa'i phyir brtsams so/ /de nas bya rgod phung po'i rir/ /rdo ba'i 'khrul 'khor byas pa ste/ /
<p>76b.2</p>thub pa'i steng du gang 'phangs pa/ /ltung ba ma yin gnyis su gyur/ /'jig rten dus su chu 'dzin sngon po sgra sgrogs pa/ /zla ba 'gog pa la ni mkha' la rlung bzhin du/ /de bzhin gshegs pa la ni mngon du gdong phyogs par/ /glang po'i dbang po rgyal po'i lam la gtad pa'o/ /lus kyis snun
<p>76b.3</p>pas yan lag mchog ni nyer blangs shing / /mche bas phug pas rgyu ma'i dra ba rab bkram pa'i/ /lus po rnams kyis rgyal po'i khab kyi lam rnams ni/ /rgyu bar dka' bar byed la mngon par rab tu zhugs/ /sha ni 'dod pas mi yi brla la rmugs pa ste/ /mche ba'i rtse mos reg cing g.yo
<p>76b.4</p>ba'i rgyu ma'i phreng / /khrag gis gsher ba'i mgo bo sna ljags drag po yis/ /'phen pa'i don du rdo rnams bzhin du gyen du 'phen/ /gsum du rab dga'i chang gis 'thor ma'i dri ldan zhing / /rul ba'i khrag dang zhag gi dri yis bsgos rnams kyis/ /de tshe bskor zhing mtha' med khro
<p>76b.5</p>ba dang ldan pa/ /grong khyer skye bo de la skyo bas 'jigs par byed/ /gnyis 'thung myos pa dus kyi dbyug pa 'jigs 'dra ba/ /khengs las gdong ni bcos shing sgra skad 'thon pa ste/ /khros pas rnam par log pa'i mig can de mthong nas/ /hA hA byed pa rgyal po'i khab nas byung bar
<p>76b.6</p>gyur/ /kha cig yid mi bde bas phyogs su bros pa ste/ /gzhan ni mtho ba min pa'i yul rnams la thim zhing / /de bzhin 'jigs pa las gzhan 'jigs pa ma bzung nas/ /gzhan rnams gzhan rnams dag gi khyim rnams la zhugs so/ /kha cig rnam par 'dug pa'i seng ge'i
<p>76b.7</p>sgra rnams ni/ /rang gi srog la the tshom yang dag ma bsams shing / /sangs rgyas la ni mngon par 'tshe ba ma byed ces/ /rab tu bzung nas gnyis 'thung de la rgyab nas 'bod/ /de bzhin gzhan rnams glang po skyong la 'bod pa ste/ /gzhan rnams 'di la thal mo dag gis phyag 'tshal lo/ /de nas
<p>77a</p>
<p>77a.1</p>de la gzhan rnams bsdigs par byed pa ste/ /kha cig nor gyis sred cing 'dod par byed pa'o/ /rlung 'gro skar khung dag nas rnam par lta bzhin du/ /lang tsho ma rnams lag pa g.yo zhing ngu ba ste/ /'jigs ma gzhan rnams gser gyi gdu bu dag dang ldan pa yis/ /
<p>77a.2</p>zangs mdog lag pa rnams kyis mig rnams 'gebs pa'o/ /yongs su ro myang glang pos 'joms par 'dod pa na/ /gyen du lag bteg skye bo ngu bar gyur na yang / /gshegs pa 'byed pa med cing gnod pa mi mnga' bar/ /bde bar gshegs pa rang gnas rnam 'gyur med par gshegs/ /
<p>77a.3</p>byams pas 'byung po rnams la rjes su brtse ba ni/ /gus pas lha rnams kyis ni rjes su 'gro ba ste/ /de la dbang po'i glang po ches kyang reg pa ru/ /nus pa ma yin gang phyir thub pa brtan par gshegs/ /gang phyir sangs rgyas la ni rjes 'gro dge slong ste/ /des ni rgyang nas glang chen mthong nas
<p>77a.4</p>bros pa ste/ /sna tshogs bdag nyid 'jig rten rang bzhin gyis bzhin du/ /kun dga' bo gcig sangs rgyas la ni rjes su song / /de nas glang chen khros pa de ni nyer 'ongs nas/ /thub pa'i mthu las 'du shes nye bar thob pa ste/ /mig sman ri bo rdo rjes phye mar bcom pa bzhin/ /lus po
<p>77a.5</p>rab tu zegs shing spyi bos 'gyel bar gyur/ /de la shin tu mdzes shing 'dam skyes 'jam po yis/ /legs skyes sor mo'i dra ba'i phyag gis mgo bo la/ /zla ba chu 'dzin la ni 'od zer gyis bzhin du/ /gnyis 'thung dbang bo la ni thub pas reg par gyur/ /chu yi shin tu khur las
<p>77a.6</p>dus kyi sprin bzhin du/ /zhabs kyi rtsa bar gnyis 'thung de ni bsdad pa ste/ /thub pas rna ba'i ta la g.yo med la gzigs shing / /de la sems can ma 'os zhi bas bstan pa'o/ /sdig med dang bcas rnam par 'joms pa sdug bsngal te/ /sdig med nyid la glang chen gnod pa
<p>77a.7</p>ma byed cig /srid pa srid par sdig med bcom pa'i srog chags kyis/ /bde 'gro brgyad la glang chen 'gyur ba ma yin no/ /'dod chags dang ni zhe sdang de bzhin gti mug ste/ /glang chen gsum bo bzod par dka' ba'i chang yin la/ /chang gsum rnams dang thub pa rnams ni bral ba ste/ /
<p>77b</p>
<p>77b.1</p>rims nad med cing mya ngan 'das pa mngon par brnyes/ /de phyir mun par 'dod pa 'di ni spongs 'dod pa/ /chang ni spangs la rang bzhin 'du shes thob par gyis/ /'khor ba'i rgya mtsho'i 'dam ni rgyas par chags pa ste/ /slar yang de ltar gnyis 'thung dbang po ma ltung cig /de nas
<p>77b.2</p>glang po des ni gsung 'di thos nas su/ /chang ni spangs shing yang dag rig par song ba ste/ /bdud rtsi 'thungs nas nad rnams dag las grol ba bzhin/ /nang du song ba'i bde ba dam pa thob par gyur/ /slob ma bzhin du thub la rab btud de ma thag /chang ni yongs
<p>77b.3</p>spangs glang po'i dbang po de mthong nas/ /kha cig chos rnams bskor zhing g.yug par gyur pa ste/ /gzhan rnams lag pa rnams ni rdebs shing skad 'don to/ /gzhan rnams kyis ni mgo bos thub la phyag 'tshal zhing / /de nas de la gzhan rnams bskor ba byas pa ste/ /gzhan
<p>77b.4</p>rnams 'phags pa nyid las glang chen la bstod cing / /ya mtshan dang bcas gzhan rnams reg par gyur pa'o/ /lding khang la gnas bud med gzhan rnams de la ni/ /gtsang zhing rin thang chen po'i gos rnams kyis mchod cing / /gzhan rnams gsar ba'i phreng ba
<p>77b.5</p>yon tan yid 'ong dang / /rgyan ni de dang de dag rnams kyis mngon par 'thor/ /dus dang mtshungs pa'i glang po dul bar gnas pa na/ /skye bo dad pa med pa dbus nas song ba ste/ /dbus gnas khyad par las ni dang bar rab song zhing / /dad pa rnams kyang gang de bstan par nye bar
<p>77b.6</p>song / /dad pa la gnas ma skyes dgra ni thub pa yis/ /glang chen dbang po de ni brtul ba mthong nas ni/ /ya mtshan gyur zhing de nas dga' ba skyes pa ste/ /sangs rgyas la ni mchog tu dad pa byas pa'o/ /nyon mongs rtsod ldan dus ni nges par log pa na/ /rdzogs ldan
<p>77b.7</p>dus ni 'ongs nas slar yang chos don bzhin/ /de ltar rdzu 'phrul dang ldan snyan grags mchog rnams kyis/ /rab tu gnas pa'i dka' ldan thub pa mchog 'phel to/ /mi dge ba dang yongs su ldan pa'i lha sbyin no/ /nyon mongs sdig pa'i las ni mang po byas nas ni/ /mi skyong
<p>78a</p>
<p>78a.1</p>ste na rgu ba gnyis skyes drang srong gi /dmod pa las bzhin sa yi 'og tu bying bar gyur/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ las kyi rgyun gyi le'u ste nyi shu rtsa gcig pa'o// //de nas 'jig rten rjes bzung nas/ /
<p>78a.2</p>dus kyi smra ba rnams kyi mchog /chos kyis sa ni khyab mdzad nas/ /mya ngan 'da' ba dang mtshungs dgongs/ /de nas dus su rgyal khab na/ /pa TA li yi grong du gshegs/ /mchod rten pa TA li mtshon pa/ /der ni 'phags pa de bzhugs so/ /dus ni de tshe grong khyer gyi/ /lits+tsha
<p>78a.3</p>bI ni zhi ba'i phyir/ /ma ga d+hA yi rgyal po yi/ /blon po char dbyibs kyis byas so/ /lha rnams kyis der rang gi nor/ /nye bar len pa rab gzigs nas/ /grong de 'gro na phul byung du/ /de bzhin gshegs pas rnam par gsungs/ /de tshe char pa'i rnam pa yis/ /bkur
<p>78a.4</p>byas byed pa rnams kyi mchog /rgya mtsho'i chung ma gtso bo la/ /mngon phyogs slob ma dang bcas gshegs/ /gang+gA'i 'gram du de gshegs nas/ /ji ltar rnyed gru de dang des/ /skye bo rnams ni sgrol ba gzigs/ /de rnams gzigs nas thugs mdzad do/ /'bad pas chu bo sgrol
<p>78a.5</p>ba la/ /bdag gi de ltar 'dra ba yin/ /de phyir rdzu 'phrul mthu yis ni/ /bdag gi gru med rab tu 'gro/ /de ltar der ni slob mar bcas/ /lha mi rnams la mi snang zhing / /rlung gis 'gros kyang phan mdzad nas/ /skad cig gis ni pha rol gyur/ /sdug bsngal mtsho yi pha rol
<p>78a.6</p>sngon/ /ye shes gru bos de mkhyen nas/ /slar yang gru 'di ma dmigs nas/ /thub pas gang+gA bsgral ba'o/ /bcom ldan nyi ma mdzes pa ni/ /gang gi sgo las nges 'byung ba/ /de ni de tshe gau tam sgor/ /de la mchod don nyid du byas/ /'gram gang dag las rnam 'dren pa/ /gang+gA'i
<p>78a.7</p>pha rol du gshegs pa/ /de ni stegs su 'gro la grags/ /de yi rigs kyis mngon par brjod/ /de nas sgrol 'dod mi rnams dang / /rgal ba rnams dang sgrol ba rnams/ /ya mtshan rnam rgyas gdong rnams kyi/ /mig rnams de la btung bar gyur/ /de nas gang+gA'i 'gram nas ni/ /
<p>78b</p>
<p>78b.1</p>sangs rgyas ku Da'i grong du gshegs/ /der ni chos ldan gtam mdzad nas/ /nA dA'i kar ni mngon par gshegs/ /dus ni de tshe de na ni/ /skye bo chen po rgud pa ste/ /gang gis gang du gang 'gro ba/ /de rnams la der thub pas gsungs/ /der ni mtshan mo gcig phul nas/ /yangs pa
<p>78b.2</p>can gyi grong du gshegs/ /de nas a mra skyong ba'i sa/ /dpal ldan tshal du dpal stug gshegs/ /a mra skyong ma res ma'i gtso/ /rnam par 'dren pa der thos nas/ /rnam dul theg pa la gnas nas/ /mchog tu dga' bas rab tu song / /phra ba'i gos dkar 'dzin
<p>78b.3</p>pa mo/ /phreng ba med cing dbyug bral ma/ /lha yi bya ba'i dus su ni/ /legs ma rigs kyi mna' ma 'dra/ /rang gi gzugs kyis khengs pa yi/ /dam pa lits+tsha bI rnams kyi/ /sems rnams dang ni nor rnams dang / /yon tan mtha' dag rnams kyis phrogs/ /dpal
<p>78b.4</p>dang mdzes pa brtan pa yis/ /nags kyi lha mo'i gzugs 'dra ba/ /de ni theg pa la babs nas/ /skyen par nags der rab tu zhugs/ /rigs kyi mo btsun gdung ba mo/ /mig rab g.yo ba de gzigs nas/ /bde bar gshegs pas rnga dbyangs kyis/ /dge slong rnams la
<p>78b.5</p>bka' stsal pa/ /stobs chung rnams kyi yid kyi rim/ /a mra skyong ma 'di mngon 'ongs/ /dran ldan bdud rtsi'i sems ldan rnams/ /ye shes kyis ni khyed rnams gnas/ /nye sar sbrul ni mchog yin zhing / /ral gyi gdengs pa'i dgra bo mchog /dran dang ye shes rnams
<p>78b.6</p>bral ba'i/ /nye sar bud med rnams ma yin/ /bsdad pa'am ni nyal ba'am/ /'gro 'am yang na gnas pa 'am/ /bud med ri mor bris pas kyang / /mi rnams kyi ni yid 'phrog go/ /'di rnams zhen pas nyam thag gam/ /gyen du lag bteg du na yang / /skra bkram rnams
<p>78b.7</p>kyis bsreg pa ru/ /nus na mo btsun rnams sngon nyid/ /pha rol po 'brel rnam mang po'i/ /dbrog bya yon tan gyis bslus rnams/ /de yi rang bzhin ma mthong ste/ /bud med rnams la byis rnams rmongs/ /mi rtag sdug bsngal bdag med dang / /mi dge ba zhes mthong nas ni/ /
<p>79a</p>
<p>79a.1</p>lta zhing sgom pa po rnams kyi/ /sems ni zil gyis non ma yin/ /gnas de rnams su legs goms blo/ /spyod yul rnams su ba lang bzhin/ /lha yi yul rnams kyis 'joms par/ /nus min mi rnams kyis ci smros/ /de phyir shes rab mda'
<p>79a.2</p>'dzin zhing / /brtson 'grus gzhu ni lag pa na/ /dran pa'i go cha yongs bgos shing / /yul gyi 'du shes can du mnos/ /lcags kyi thur ma tsha mo yis/ /mig la reg pa mchog yin zhing / /g.yo ba'i mig can bud med la/ /ma rungs dran pas lta phyir min/ /gal
<p>79a.3</p>te dus ni de yi tshe/ /chags pa'i sems kyis dus byed na/ /dud 'gro 'am ni 'og nyid du/ /dbang med bcings nas khrid par byed/ /de phyir 'jigs pa 'di shes nas/ /mtshan mar spros pa mi bya zhing / /lus po la ni gzugs tsam du/ /gang gis mthong ba de mthong ngo / /
<p>79a.4</p>dbang pos 'jig rten na yul rnams/ /'chi min dbang po rnams des min/ /gang zhig de rnams la chags gyur/ /de ni de rnams las 'ching ngo / /ba lang gnyis kyi sbyor ba'i phyir/ /sbyor ba la gcig ji ltar gyur/ /yul dang dbang po de dag ni/ /chags pa
<p>79a.5</p>phan tshun de ltar min/ /mig gis gzugs ni 'dzin pa ste/ /sems kyis rnam par rtog par byed/ /rnam par rtog las der skye zhing / /chags dang chags bral nyid kyang ngo / /rnam par ma brtags dbang po'i don/ /gal te don med ched gyur na/ /dbang po'i
<p>79a.6</p>spyod yul la spyod pa/ /thams cad don med kyis sbyor to/ /de phyir ma dor dran pas dang / /bag yod mchog tu 'gro bas dang / /rang don rjes su mthong bas dang / /gdung med sems kyis bsgom par bya/ /de ltar don mthar ma gyur pa'i/ /dge slong rnams la de rjes
<p>79a.7</p>bstan/ /ltos byas a mra skyong ma ni/ /thal mo sbyar byas nye bar 'ongs/ /des ni thugs zhi drang srong ma/ /shing drung gnas pa mthong nas ni/ /nags kyi yongs su longs spyod kyis/ /mchog tu rjes su 'dzin pa snyam/ /de nas bkur sti mang po las/ /g.yo yang lta
<p>79b</p>
<p>79b.1</p>byed rab bkod nas/ /me tog tsam pa ka rgyas ltar/ /mgo bos thub pa la phyag 'tshal/ /kun mkhyen gyis kyang rjes gnang ma/ /de nas sa la bsdad pa ste/ /de yis blo la bzod gsung gis/ /thub pas de la bka' stsal to/ /bsam pa 'di ni yon tan ldan/ /
<p>79b.2</p>rnam dag sems dpa' nyid bstan to/ /bud med byis pa phul gnas pa/ /chos la 'dod pa rnyed par dka'/ /gal te chos kyi bdag nyid gyur/ /zhen pas bcom pa'i sems ldan pa'i/ /na rab mi mo rnams kyis dang / /blo ldan mi rnams kyis mtshar cing / /rang bzhin
<p>79b.3</p>gyis ni blo chung zhing / /g.yo ba'i sems ldan lang tsho ma/ /yul gcig ro yis 'jig rten na/ /chos shes shes pa ya mtshan no/ /khyod kyi chos la yid gyur pa/ /de ni khyod kyis bdag nyid don/ /mi rtag gson pa'i 'jig rten na/ /chos las gzhan na nor yod min/ /nad kyis
<p>79b.4</p>nad med 'joms pa ste/ /rga bas lang tsho gcod pa nyid/ /'chi bas srog ni len pa ste/ /chos kyis rgud pa yod ma yin/ /gang phyir dga' ba rnams dang bral/ /mi dga' ba rnams dang sbyor zhing / /mngon par 'dod pa thob pa na/ /de phyir chos ni mchog tu 'gro/ /gzhan dbang
<p>79b.5</p>sdug bsngal chen po ste/ /rang dbang mchog tu bde ba nyid/ /ma nu'i rigs su skyes na yang / /bud med thams cad gzhan dbang ngo / /gang phyir gzhan dbang nyid phyir dang / /de bzhin phru gu 'dzin pa'i phyir/ /bud med rnams kyi sdug bsngal lhag /de phyir yang dag nges par 'os/ /de
<p>79b.6</p>ltar thub pa chen po'i gsung / /rang bzhin gyis dang mkhas las dang / /brtan las byis kyang byis min bzhin/ /thos shing mngon par dga' ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi smra ba yis/ /'dod pa'i bdag nyid can gyis sems la brabs pa ni/ /bud med nyid ni smad
<p>79b.7</p>cing yul las log pa ste/ /gang gi skye bo'i rten la btsog par byas pa'o/ /de nas me tog khur las tsu ta'i mchod sdong bzhin/ /yang dag kun nas dud pa'i lus kyi mchod sdong can/ /thub pa chen po la ni gus pas mig zhugs shing / /yang yang chos ni rnam par dag pa'i lta bas
<p>80a</p>
<p>80a.1</p>gnas/ /rang bzhin gyis ni ngo tsha dang ldan bud med de/ /chos ni mngon par 'dod pas yang yang bskul ba ni/ /'dam skyes mdzod dang 'dra bas thal mo sbyar nas ni/ /dal bus smra ba'i skad kyi gdangs kyis gsol ba'o/ /bcom ldan don mdzad bdag la
<p>80a.2</p>gsung don du/ /nang par bsod snyoms dus su dge slong sder bcas pa/ /sdug bsngal nye bar zhi ba'i mdzad po 'jig rten na/ /'bras bur gyur pa'i bdag la 'bras bur mdzad du gsol/ /de nas de yi gus pa de ltar gzigs nas dang / /sems can rnams ni bza' ba'i dbang
<p>80a.3</p>nyid mkhyen nas ni/ /gsung ma phye nas bde bar gshegs pas de ltar zhes/ /de la nges par rnam 'gyur brda yis mdzad pa'o/ /skad cig mdzad pa dang ldan spyan yangs mchog gi chos mnga' zhing / /chos kyi snod la des ni dga' zhing mgu la rungs pa ste/ /gus pas rnyed pa
<p>80a.4</p>mchog ni rnam par nges shing bstod par gyur/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ a mra skyong ma'i nags gzigs pa'i le'u ste nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa'o// //de nas thub pa'i thugs rig nas/ /phyag 'tshal nas kyang grong du song / /de
<p>80a.5</p>ni lits+tsha bIs thos nas/ /lta 'dod sangs rgyas la song ngo / /dkar po'i rta dang shing rta gdugs/ /phreng ba rgyan dang bgo ba rnams/ /kha cig kha cig de rnams dang / /dmar ser rnams dang de bzhin gzhan/ /kha cig bai DUr+ya ljang dang / /gzhan rnams rma bya'i mjug ma ste/ /de ltar cha
<p>80a.6</p>lugs rgya chen po/ /bdag gis dga' byed rnams dang song / /ri bo rnam rgyas ro stod can/ /gser gyi gnya' shing lag pa rnams/ /dpal ldan bong ring dngos su ni/ /de rnams mtho ris bzhin du mdzes/ /mtshams sprin rkang la sna tshogs rnams/ /glog ni rab tu
<p>80a.7</p>snang ba bzhin/ /shing rta rnams las babs 'dod pas/ /de rnams gnas pa rnam par mdzes/ /dbu rgyan rnam g.yo rnam btud pa'i/ /brtan rnams thub la phyag 'tshal nas/ /nga rgyal ldan rnams rgyags med bzhin/ /chos la dga' bas de rnams gnas/ /nyi ma sprin
<p>80b</p>
<p>80b.1</p>dang bral ba yi/ /logs su khyer 'jigs gzhu bzhin du/ /thub pa'i drung der de rnams kyi/ /chags bral dkyil 'khor mdzes pa'o/ /sa la seng ge gnas pa rnams/ /gser gyis spras pa'i seng ge'i gdan/ /seng ge la sogs de rnams la/ /mi yi seng ges de
<p>80b.2</p>nas gsungs/ /gzugs dang dpal dang stobs la sogs/ /bkur mang rnams dang ldan pa ni/ /khyed kyi chos la gus 'di gang / /de las lhag par mdzes pa nyid/ /tshul khrims la sogs yon tan gyis/ /ji ltar 'jig rten mdzes de ltar/ /lus ni sna tshogs gos
<p>80b.3</p>sam rgyan/ /phreng ba rnams kyis ma yin no/ /gang du khyed cag bdag po rnams/ /chos shes 'dul ba 'dod pa rnams/ /spong byed pa rnams rjes bzung zhing / /skal ba bcas rnams bdag gi lugs/ /'phags skyes rnyed par dka' dus su/ /chos la gnas rnams srung
<p>80b.4</p>byed gyur/ /phyis 'byung ma yin yul rnams kyi/ /skal bas dman pa rnams kyis min/ /dpal ldan skal ba chen po rnams/ /chos shes srung bar byed rnams kyis/ /bsrung ba nyid kyis yul 'di ni/ /chos kyis kyang ni rjes su 'dzin/ /rlung rnams rgal 'dod pa la rnams/ /
<p>80b.5</p>khyu mchog rgal ba rnams kyi bzhin/ /rgyal po rnams kyis gang bzung ba'i/ /yul la de nas skye dgu 'gro/ /khyed cag rnams la tshul khrims de/ /rtag par 'gyur bar 'os pa ste/ /bdag gi don ni 'dod rnams kyi/ /'dir dang song nas dbrog bya min/ /yid ni tshim zhing
<p>80b.6</p>bkur mang dang / /rnyed dang grags dang yid ches nyid/ /dga' ba nyid dang song nas bde/ /tshul khrims kyi ni 'bras bu che/ /'byung po rgyu dang mi rgyu yi/ /rten ni ji ltar sa yin pa/ /de ltar yon tan thams cad kyi/ /rten ni tshul khrims dam pa'o/ /'phur 'dod gshogs
<p>80b.7</p>pa med pa dang / /rgal 'dod gru med ji lta bar/ /mi ni tshul khrims rnam spangs par/ /dge legs 'dod pa de ltar shes/ /me tog 'bras bus khyab pa'i shing / /tsher ma can gyur ji lta bar/ /thos dang gzugs don phun tshogs pa/ /tshul khrims 'chal pa de ltar ro/ /
<p>81a</p>
<p>81a.1</p>sna tshogs gos dang rgyan ldan zhing / /khang bzangs rnams su gnas na yang / /tshul khrims dang ldan skye bo gang / /de yi drang srong dang mnyam 'gros/ /ngur smrig shing shun zur phud dang / /gtsug phud spyi bo ral pa rnams/ /tshul khrims nyams pa kun rnams
<p>81a.2</p>kyi/ /bcos ma nyid du shes par bya/ /stegs las dus gsum khrus byas nas/ /me la lan gnyis bsregs nas dang / /gdung ba drag por gdungs nas kyang / /tshul khrims med na bdag ma yin/ /sha za rnams la lus byin nas/ /ri yi logs nas bor nas sam/ /me 'am
<p>81a.3</p>chur ni bdag mchongs na/ /tshul khrims med na bdag ma yin/ /'bras bu rtsa ba chu za zhing / /ri dgas bzhin du rtswa za'am/ /rlung gi bza' ba 'dod pa yang / /tshul khrims med na bdag mi 'gyur/ /mi gang tshul khrims kyis dman pa/ /de ni bya dang ri dwags mtshungs/ /rdol
