<p>81a.4</p>ba'i snod ni chu yis bzhin/ /de ni chos kyi snod ma yin/ /'jigs pa dang ni gtam ngan dang / /yid mi ches dang mi dga' nyid/ /mngon sum 'dir ni thob pa ste/ /song nas don med za bar 'gyur/ /de phyir tshul khrims gzhom mi bya/ /'brog dgon dag na lam mkhan bzhin/ /rang
<p>81a.5</p>dbang dag ni rnyed dka' ba'i/ /tshul khrims mtho ris dag na gru/ /skyon rnams kyis bcom sems kyis ni/ /thams cad bcom nas 'jug pa ste/ /tshul khrims rab tu gnas byas nas/ /nyon mongs 'joms la 'bad pa gyis/ /de phyir dang por nga snyam pa/ /brgyan par 'dod
<p>81a.6</p>pas spang bar bya/ /bsreg bya za ba'i du ba bzhin/ /yon tan rnams kyis nga snyam nyid/ /skar ma nyi ma zla ba rnams/ /sprin gyi dra ba chen pos bzhin/ /nga rgyal gyis bcom yon tan rnams/ /yod par gyur kyang mdzes ma yin/ /dregs pa ngo tsha 'joms pa ste/ /mya ngan gyis
<p>81a.7</p>gtan dga' bas lus/ /yon tan rnams kyi rtsa ba nas/ /'joms phyir nga'o snyam pa skye/ /'gran pa dang ldan nga rgyal las/ /lha min lha rnams kyis bcom zhing / /mi skyong ta la'i byin pa dang / /dong gsum pa rnams zad par gyur/ /gang zhig mi rtag dngos rnams su/ /mchog
<p>81b</p>
<p>81b.1</p>ni nga yin snyam pa dang / /mi dman pa ni nga zhes snyam/ /de ni mkhas pa min par rtogs/ /gzugs ni brtan pa ma yin zhing / /'jig pa'i chos can g.yo ba yis/ /nga zhes gang zhig nga rgyal te/ /yongs su rtog pa min gzhan ci/ /'dod pa'i 'dod chags stobs ldan
<p>81b.2</p>pa/ /rab gab lhan skyes dgra bo ste/ /bshes min nang na spyod pa bzhin/ /gang zhig bshes kyi sgo nas 'joms/ /'dod chags me dang me nyid ni/ /sreg pa'i bdag nyid kyis mnyam ste/ /'dod chags me ni 'bar ba na/ /mtshan mo de nyid ring bar 'gyur/ /'dod chags me'i
<p>81b.3</p>stobs ji 'dra ba/ /me yi stobs ni de 'drar smin/ /me ni chu rnams kyis shes te/ /'dod chags me ni mtshos kyang min/ /dus su nags su mes tshig rnams/ /nags kyi shing rnams skye ba ste/ /'dod chags mes tshig blo med rnams/ /chos la skye ba ma yin no/ /chags las
<p>81b.4</p>bde ba tshol ba ste/ /bde phyir mi dge ba byed cing / /mi dge ba las dmyal bar 'gro/ /chags pa dang mnyam dgra bo med/ /chags las sred pa skye ba ste/ /sred las 'dod pa rnams la chags/ /'dod pa rnams las sdug bsngal 'thob/ /chags pa dang mnyam yul med do/ /chags pa zhes bya'i
<p>81b.5</p>nad chen po/ /de ni byis pas rtogs ma yin/ /mi rtag nyid las mi gtsang las/ /sdug bsngal nyid las bdag med las/ /gal te mthong na mi chags te/ /log pa'i blo yis chags pa'o/ /de phyir dngos po la chags pa/ /gang du nye bar skye ba na/ /der ni ji ltar 'gyur brtag
<p>81b.6</p>ste/ /gyur pa mthong ba zhes brjod do/ /yon tan yongs su rtogs pa na/ /ji ltar chags par nye bar 'gro/ /yon tan med na yongs rtogs na/ /de bzhin khro ba 'gugs par byed/ /de phyir khro ba spong 'dod pas/ /zhe sdang yongs su brtag mi bya/ /dkar min 'gros
<p>81b.7</p>las ngu ba bzhin/ /khro ba las ni zhe sdang 'dzag /khro ba gzugs ldan rnams kyi dga'/ /mig ldan rnams kyi mun pa yang / /chos don 'dod pa rnams kyi gshed/ /mos pa'i mi mthun pa nyid do/ /khro ba blo yi mun pa mchog /mdza' bshes gyur pa'i dgra bo mchog /
<p>82a</p>
<p>82a.1</p>bkur sti mang po'i gcod pa po/ /zil gyis non pa'i byed pa po/ /de bzhin khro ba mi bya zhing / /byas nas kyang ni dor bar bya/ /dmug pa'i rang bzhin lto 'phye bzhin/ /khro ba'i rjes su 'jug mi bya/ /skor ba'i shing rta bzhin gang gis/ /khro ba brtan pas thag
<p>82a.2</p>pas bzung / /de bdag kha lo sgyur snyam ste/ /cig shos skye bo thag pa 'dzin/ /gang zhig khro ba 'dod pa ste/ /skye ba 'gog pa 'dod ma yin/ /phyis de khro ba med pa na/ /me la reg pa bzhin du bsreg /khro ba skyes pas sngon rol du/ /bdag nyid kyis ni sems bsreg ste/ /rnam par
<p>82a.3</p>'phel zhing phyin pa ni/ /gzhan ni sreg gam mi sreg gam/ /nad sogs nye bar 'tshe rnams kyi/ /gang tshe 'jig rten brtse ba rnams/ /lus can bshes ma yin rnams la/ /gnod sems byas nas yon tan ci/ /de phyir 'jig rten sdug bsngal ba/ /shes nas khro ba zlog
<p>82a.4</p>pa'i phyir/ /'byung po kun la byams pa dang / /snying rje nyid ni bsgom par bya/ /de ltar nyon mongs lhag pa gang / /de yi de tshe gzigs pa ste/ /de la brtse bas sangs rgyas kyis/ /de rnams la gsungs smad pa'o/ /sems can nyam thag rnams la ni/ /ji ltar rang bzhin gyis
<p>82a.5</p>mkhas pa'i/ /sman pas sman ni gsungs pa ste/ /nad rnams nye par zhi phyir ro/ /de bzhin chags dang rga sogs kyi/ /nad kyis 'byung po nyam thag la/ /thub pas bsam pa mkhyen nas ni/ /de nyid shes pa'i sman byin to/ /de ltar thub pa'i gsung la ni/ /lits+tsha bI rnams
<p>82a.6</p>mngon dga' ste/ /rab 'phyang gtsug gi nor bu can/ /mgo bo rnams kyis phyag 'tshal lo/ /de nas thal mo rnam sbyar nas/ /cung zhig dud pa'i lus rnams kyis/ /phur bu la ni lha rnams bzhin/ /sangs rgyas la ni byon par zhus/ /dang po a mra skyong ma'i rigs/ /thub pas
<p>82a.7</p>de rnams la gsungs shing / /dam pa rnams kyis thog mar ni/ /snyan mnan 'dor bya min par gsungs/ /de rnams bud med de yis ni/ /bdag la bslus par shes pa ste/ /de bzhin gshegs la mchod mang po/ /nyis 'gyur nyid du byas pa'o/ /legs brjod drang srong sngags
<p>82b</p>
<p>82b.1</p>rnams kyis/ /sbrul rnams kyi ni dug bzhin du/ /kun mkhyen gyis bstan de rnams ni/ /rab tu zhi ba'i yid rnams song / /de yi mtshan mo 'das nas ni/ /a mra skyong mas bkur byas te/ /'od ma ldan pa'i grong du ni/ /dbyar rnams rnam par 'das pa na/ /yangs pa can nyid
<p>82b.2</p>du gshegs shing / /spre'u rdzing gi 'gram du ni/ /thub pa chen po bzhugs pa'o/ /shing gi rtsa bar de bzhugs so/ /de bzhin du ni 'bar ba la/ /nags tshal de ni snang byas shing / /nye bar 'ongs nas bdud kyis smras/ /nai rany+dza na'i 'gram du sngon/ /thub pa khyod la bdag gis
<p>82b.3</p>smras/ /bya ba byas pa mya ngan zlos/ /zhes 'dir khyod kyis lan smras so/ /nyam thag pa rnams 'jigs med cing / /nyan thos rnams ni don byas par/ /bdag gi ji srid ma gyur pa/ /de srid mya ngan mi 'da' zhes/ /de 'di mang po rnams grol zhing / /de bzhin grol bar
<p>82b.4</p>'dod rnams dang / /grol bar gyur pa rnams nyid de/ /de phyir mya ngan 'da' bar 'os/ /de nas tshig 'di gsan gyur nas/ /zla ba gsum na mya ngan 'da'/ /mi brtan pa ni dor cig ces/ /dgra bcom rnams kyi mchog gis gsungs/ /de nas dam bca' 'di shes nas/ /yid la re
<p>82b.5</p>ba gang ba ste/ /rab tu dga' zhing mgu ba ni/ /de nyid du ni mi snang gyur/ /de nas drang srong chen po'i thugs kyi ting nge 'dzin/ /rnam pa de ltar rnal 'byor stobs las mdzad pa nyid/ /sku tshe ji ltar gyur pa sngon du btang ba ste/ /rdzu 'phrul mthu las mtshungs pa med pa 'tsho bar gyur/ /
<p>82b.6</p>des ni sku tshe btang ba'i yud tsam de la ni/ /bud med myos ma bzhin du sa ni g.yos gyur la/ /ma yis tshos pa'i lhun po'i rdo ba rim bzhin du/ /phyogs rnams dag las sgron ma chen po rnams lhu dang / /de bzhin kun nas dbang po'i rdo rje mi bzad rnams/ /glog dang bcas shing me yi snying po
<p>82b.7</p>can g.yos shing / /bskal pa 'jig che 'jig rten bsreg par 'dod pa bzhin/ /phyogs rnams thams cad rnams su me dag 'bar bar gyur/ /shing rnams kyis ni phung po 'khogs pa rnams bor zhing / /ri rnams kyis ni rtse mo rnams ni dor ba ste/ /rlung gis mngon par gang ba'i rdo ba'i phug
<p>83a</p>
<p>83a.1</p>bzhin du/ /mkha' la rnga rnams kyi ni ma rungs sgra rnams bsgrags/ /de nas de ltar kun du bskyod tshe yud tsam la/ /mi yi 'jig rten na dang lha dang nam mkha' la/ /ting 'dzin chen po de las rnam par bzhengs mdzad nas/ /thub pa chen pos gsung ni 'di nyid
<p>83a.2</p>gsungs pa'o/ /shing rta srog shing rnam par nyams pa dang 'dra ba'i/ /tshe btang lus po nang gi stobs las 'dren bgyi zhing / /sgo nga'i skye gnas pa rnams sgo nga phye nas bzhin/ /srid pa'i 'ching las tshe dang lhan cig 'grol bar bgyi/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags
<p>83a.3</p>chen po las/ sku tshe'i 'du byed byin gyis brlabs pa'i le'u ste nyi shu rtsa gsum pa'o// //de nas bskyod pa de mthong nas/ /kun dga' bo ni spu langs shing / /ci zhig gyur zhes shugs 'ongs te/ /'dar bar gyur cing dga' ma gyur/ /kun mkhyen gtan tshigs
<p>83a.4</p>mkhas pa la/ /des der gtan tshigs dris pa ste/ /de nas de la thub pas ni/ /khyu mchog myos pa'i dbyangs kyis gsungs/ /rgyu mtshan gang gis g.yos pa 'di/ /bdag gi tshe 'di btang ba la/ /zla ba gsum ni yongs bgrangs par/ /byin gyis brlabs nas de ni 'tsho/ /de
<p>83a.5</p>ltar thos nas kun dga' bo/ /tsan+dan ljon pa'i thang chu ni/ /glang po che yis brabs pa bzhin/ /mchi ma phyung zhing g.yos par gyur/ /des gnyen nyid phyir bla ma'i phyir/ /chags bral min phyir sdug bsngal zhing / /snying rje bar ni rnam zlos te/ /yongs su dga' ba med par
<p>83a.6</p>dus/ /mgon gyi nges pa thos gyur nas/ /bdag gi lus ni lhung ba bzhin/ /bdag gi phyogs rnams spobs pa med/ /bdag gis chos rnams thos pa rmongs/ /gangs kyis gtser rnams la me bzhin/ /rga ba rnyings pa'i chos rnams su/ /kyi hud mis bsngags skyen par ni/ /
<p>83a.7</p>de bzhin gshegs pa mya ngan 'da'/ /nyon mongs 'brog dgon chen po ru/ /chud zos lus dang ldan rnams la/ /lam mkhyen shin tu skyen pa ru/ /lam mkhan nges par nyams par 'gyur/ /thag ring lam la rab zhugs pa'i/ /sred pa yongs ldan bdag rnams kyi/ /lam
<p>83b</p>
<p>83b.1</p>na rdzing bu bsil ba'i chu/ /shin tu myur bar bskam par gyur/ /blo ni rdzi ma zhi ba smin/ /'das dang ma 'ongs da ltar gzigs/ /ye shes rnam spangs 'jig rten gyi/ /mig ni nges par zum par 'gyur/ /nges par lo thog skyed rnams su/ /chu ni don gnyer ngal rnams la/ /char
<p>83b.2</p>bab gyur nas skyen pa ru/ /chu sbyin sprin ni nub par 'gyur/ /mi shes mun pas phrogs rnams su/ /sems can lam gol ba rnams la/ /rab tu gsal ba'i sgron ma ni/ /shin tu skyen par zhi bar 'gyur/ /de nas de ltar mya ngan gyis/ /sems gzir kun dga' bo gzigs nas/ /
<p>83b.3</p>zhi byed mgon pos de nyid ni/ /de nyid rig pa'i mchog gis gsungs/ /'gro ba'i rang bzhin shes nas ni/ /mya ngan ma byed kun dga' bo/ /'dus byas ngo bo mi rtag cing / /'gro ba 'di kun 'dzad pa nyid/ /lus can rtsod pa'i skyed tshal du/ /sdug pa kun dang bral ba ste/ /brtse
<p>83b.4</p>ba kun nas thang cig ces/ /sngon du bdag gis smras pa nyid/ /'dus byas g.yo ba skyes pa gang / /rten nas 'byung ba dbang med de/ /bdag gis rtag par gyur cig ces/ /'di ni rnyed par mi nus so/ /sa stengs 'byung po rtag gyur na/ /'jug pa g.yo ba ma yin zhing / /thar
<p>83b.5</p>pas bya ba su yis 'gyur/ /de phyir mthar thug 'dod pa'o/ /ci ste khyod dam skye bo gzhan/ /bdag la khyod kyi sred pa ci/ /gang phyir ngal ba skyes pa 'di/ /khyod kyis bdag dang bral bas byas/ /lam ni mtha' dag khyed cag la/ /bdag gis bstan cing bshad pa ste/ /sangs
<p>83b.6</p>rgyas rnams dang slob dpon gyi/ /dpe mkhyud med ces gzung mdzod cig /bdag gi gnas sam nyer zhi na/ /don ni de tsam nyid yin te/ /de bzhin gshegs rnams chos kyi sku/ /lus kyis khyed cag la don ci/ /de phyir dang ngam bdag 'das tshe/ /skyo ba yis dang bag yod
<p>83b.7</p>dang / /bdag gi sgron mas gsal byas te/ /chos kyi sgron ma rtag par ro/ /der zhugs brtson 'grus brtan pa dang / /rtsod med bdag gi don la mkhas/ /blo ni gzhan dbang ma yin pa/ /bdag gi sgron ma zhes shes bya/ /rig pa dang ldan mkhas pa ni/ /gang gi sgron mas
<p>84a</p>
<p>84a.1</p>mun pa bzhin/ /shes rab sgron mas 'joms pa ste/ /chos kyi sgron mar shes par bya/ /dge legs nye bar thob bya'i phyir/ /de dag rnams kyi spyod yul zhi/ /lus dang tshor ba nyid dang ni/ /sems dang bdag med pa nyid do/ /rus lpags khrag dang rgyus
<p>84a.2</p>pa dang / /sha dang spu sogs rnams kyis dkris/ /mi gtsang lus su mthong bas ni/ /lus la chags pa ma yin no/ /de lta de ltar rkyen rnams kyis/ /'jug pa'i tshor ba rnams su ni/ /sdug bsngal zhes de ltar mthong ba'i/ /bde ba'i shes rab rab tu 'joms/ /skye ba dang ni
<p>84a.3</p>gnas pa dang / /chos kyi 'god pa nyid dag ni/ /zhi ba'i sems kyis mthong ba yin/ /rtag par 'dzin pa ldog pa'o/ /rkyen rnams las ni skyes pa rnams/ /phung po rnams ni mthong ba yi/ /ngar 'dzin gyis ni skyed pa po/ /bdag tu 'dzin pa 'jug ma yin/ /sdug bsngal nye bar
<p>84a.4</p>zhi ba'i phyir/ /bgrod pa gcig pa'i lam 'di ni/ /lam ni bzhi po de rnams su/ /de ltar dran pa nye bar gzhag /de ltar ram ni bdag 'das tshe/ /gang rnams 'di la gnas 'gyur ba/ /de rnams 'god med go 'phang mchog /nges par legs pa thob par 'gyur/ /de ltar kun
<p>84a.5</p>dga' bo la gtam/ /de rnams rnam par 'dren pas mdzad/ /lits+tsha bI rnams kyis thos nas/ /de la gus phyir skyen par song / /thub la brtse dang gus pa'i phyir/ /gdung bas phrog pa'i sems can rnams/ /spyod mthas bkod pa'i don rnams kun/ /myur las rdzu 'phrul don
<p>84a.6</p>rnams so/ /ston pa la ni smra 'dod pa/ /de rnams btud nas nye bar gnas/ /smra bar 'dod rnams ston pa yis/ /mkhyen nas thub pas tshig gsungs so/ /gang 'di bdag la song ba'i sems/ /khyed cag rnams kyis de kun shes/ /de nyid gzhan bzhin mya ngan gyis/ /de ring khyed
<p>84a.7</p>kyis spobs par gyur/ /dpal gyi bde rnams la gnas kyang / /khyed cag rnams kyis thams cad nas/ /mngon par zhugs pa 'di yis ni/ /gsal ba nyid dang chos mkhan nyid/ /gal te ye shes bdag las kyang / /cung zhig thos shing shes pa na/ /bdag gi zhing ba rab dmigs te/ /
<p>84b</p>
<p>84b.1</p>gdung ba ma byed brtan par song / /mi rtag 'dus byas dngos po rnams/ /g.yo zhing yongs su gyur pa can/ /snying po dang bral blo gtad min/ /cung zhig brtan par gnas pa med/ /gnas 'jog rgyun shes la sogs dang / /gang gzhan thig le gzhan rnams dang / /dus kyi dbang
<p>84b.2</p>du song ba ste/ /srid pa 'di ni ma rungs nyid/ /sa 'dzin nga las nu dang ni/ /brgya byin dang mtshungs dbyig nor dang / /skal ba che dang skal med min/ /'byung por mnyes gshin 'byung ba'o/ /'gro mgyogs de nas 'gro byar 'gro/ /skal ldan shing rta shing rta bzang / /sgra ngan gyis smad sgra ngan
<p>84b.3</p>rdzogs/ /rangs byed ri mo rdul ma skyes/ /mi skyong drang srong bdag nyid che/ /de rnams dang gzhan mang po rnams/ /dbang chen dang mtshungs nyams pa ste/ /mi nyams pa ni yod ma yin/ /nyi ma gnas las 'phos pa ste/ /nor lha rnams ni sa la song / /dbang po brgya
<p>84b.4</p>rnams 'das pa ste/ /rtag pa ci yang yod ma yin/ /gang gzhan yang dag sangs rgyas rnams/ /'gro ba'i snang ba mdzad nas su/ /mar me snum zad bzhin du ni/ /de rnams mya ngan 'das par gyur/ /gang gzhan bdag nyid chen po rnams/ /'byung 'gyur de bzhin gshegs rnams
<p>84b.5</p>kyang / /bud shing tshig pa'i me bzhin du/ /de rnams mya ngan 'da' bar 'gyur/ /thar 'dod dka' thub nags su bzhin/ /de phyir bdag kyang 'gro bar bgyi/ /bdag gi don med lus ming ni/ /'gran pa la ni rgyu mtshan med/ /gang du gdul bya 'ga' zhig yod/ /gang phyir 'di nas
<p>84b.6</p>'gro bar blo/ /nyams dga' yangs pa can la ni/ /khyed cag blo gzhan ma gyur cig /de phyir 'jig rten skyabs med cing / /dbang med g.yo bar shes nas su/ /chags bral la ni 'gro bar dang / /skyo ba thob par 'os ba'o/ /de ltar gtam bcad nas dus su/ /ltos med
<p>84b.7</p>de bzhin gshegs pa ni/ /ston gyi zla ba snang byed bzhin/ /lus ngan phyogs su rab tu gshegs/ /de la mchi mas yongs gang mig /lits+tsha bI rnams rjes song zhing / /rgyan bcas lag pa rgyas rnams kyis/ /thal mo sbyar nas rnam par smras/ /kyi hud 'o brgyal gser
<p>85a</p>
<p>85a.1</p>mtshungs shing / /sum cu rtsa gnyis mtshan mnga' ba/ /ston pa'i sku lus dbye 'gyur zhing / /thugs rje mnga' ba mi rtag nyid/ /srid cing 'o ma med pa yi/ /sems ma thob pa'i be'u ni/ /bkren rnams ye shes 'jo ba'i bas/ /kye ma shin tu skyen par 'bor/ /
<p>85a.2</p>'gro na mig ldan mi rnams kyis/ /rmongs pa'i mun pa bcom mdzad nas/ /ye shes 'od zer skyen pa ru/ /thub pa nyi ma nub par 'gyur/ /mi shes rgyun gyis 'jig rten na/ /de las de las khyer ba la/ /rnam yangs chos kyi zam pa ni/ /shin tu myur bar chag par 'gyur/ /brtse ldan
<p>85a.3</p>sman pa chen po ni/ /ye shes mchog gi sman mnga' bas/ /sems nad kyis na 'jig rten ni/ /bor nas nges par gshegs par 'gyur/ /sems kyis gzer bu'i yo byad dang / /shes rab rgyan gyis brgyan pa ste/ /ltad mo la ni skom rnams kyis/ /dbang po'i tog ni 'gyel bar 'gyur/ /
<p>85a.4</p>'gro ba sdug bsngal skal ba can/ /'khor ba'i 'ching bas bcings pa la/ /gal te thar pa'i sgo 'di ni/ /dus kyis sdom par 'gyur ba'o/ /de ltar rnam zlog lits+tsha bI/ /mig rnams mchi mas rnams 'khrugs pa/ /rjes su 'ongs pa de rnams ni/ /thub pas slar la zlog
<p>85a.5</p>par mdzad/ /de nas thub pas bcad shes nas/ /bstan pa rab tu bzung nas su/ /phyir la ldog phyir nges pa ni/ /sdug bsngal sdug bsngal gyis byas so/ /rlung gis bskyod pa'i me tog rnams/ /kar ni ka ra'i ljon shing bzhin/ /gser gyi ri ltar dkar de rnams/ /
<p>85a.6</p>thub pa'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal te/ /de la sems rnams kyis chags shing / /rkang pa rnams kyang 'khyar ba ste/ /gnyen po'i rlung la chu gnyer bzhin/ /'gro ba med par de rnams log /zhe sa yin zhing dga' ma yin/ /dga' ba yin zhing zhe sa min/ /thub pa la ni de dag
<p>85a.7</p>gis/ /dga' dang zhe sa g.yo ba med/ /'brog mtha' nas 'thon khyu mchog che/ /khyu mchog chen po rnams kyis bzhin/ /gnas na gnas kyang de rnams kyis/ /yang yang stobs bcu ldan la lta/ /de bzhin gshegs par sems song ba/ /lus dang ldan yang 'od med
<p>85b</p>
<p>85b.1</p>rnams/ /rkang pas de nas mya ngan 'das/ /log pa'i 'khrus bzhin rjes su 'ongs/ /rnam par ma 'khrugs mnga' gzhu rnams kyi sgra rnams zil mnan nas/ /de rnams nga rgyal ldan yang stobs dang ldan yang 'gugs ldan yang / /'gro na dpal 'dod li ts+tsha bI ni 'dod pa chen po rnams/ /mya ngan
<p>85b.2</p>gyis 'khrugs gdong rnams rang gi khang pa rnams su 'ongs/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ li ts+tsha bI rnams la thugs brtse ba'i le'u ste nyi shu rtsa bzhi pa'o// //snang byed 'dzin par gyur pa na/ /mun bcas kyis 'khrugs nam mkha' bzhin/ /
<p>85b.3</p>thub pa 'da' phyir gshegs pa na/ /de phyir yangs pa can ma mdzes/ /dpal ldan dregs pa mi ldan zhing / /thams cad du ni nyams dga' yang / /bdag po nyams las bud med bzhin/ /kun nas gdungs pas mdzes ma gyur/ /thos pas dman pa'i gzugs bzhin dang / /yon tan
<p>85b.4</p>dang bral rig pa bzhin/ /ngag gis dman pa'i blo bzhin dang / /'du byed dang bral ngag bzhin no/ /spyod pas dman pa'i dpa' bzhin dang / /dang po dang bral byams pa bzhin/ /rnam gnon phun sum tshogs pa bzhin/ /chos kyis dman pa'i bya ba bzhin/ /ston kar char ni log pa na/ /
<p>85b.5</p>sha li bskams pas nor 'dzin bzhin/ /de tshe mya ngan las ma mdzes/ /gang du der ni ma btsos shing / /zos pa ma yin mya ngan des/ /kun du ngu zhing thams cad kyis/ /grags ldan thub pa grags pa byas/ /gzhan ni ma gtams ma byas shing / /sus kyang bsams pa ma yin la/ /mya
<p>85b.6</p>ngan dang ni ngu ba ste/ /grong khyer pa kun bya ba gcig /de nas dga' 'dun gtso bo la/ /brtan kyang mya ngan gyis nyam thag /sde chen bdag po seng ge ni/ /bsams shing rnam par zlos pa'o/ /lam log mu stegs rnams 'pham nas/ /'di 'dra'i lam la gshegs nas su/ /gang
<p>85b.7</p>gis dam pa'i lam bstan te/ /slar mi ldog phyir gshegs pa nyid/ /nyam thag nyams par gyur pa yi/ /snang med 'jig rten bor nas su/ /skye dgu mgon med mdzad nas ni/ /mgon po de ni zhi phyir gshegs/ /rnal 'byor gtso bo bla ma mchog /mthar thug zhi la mngon phyogs nas/ /
<p>86a</p>
<p>86a.1</p>tshe zad pa las gzi mdangs bzhin/ /bdag gi brtan pa nyams par 'gyur/ /mi skyong sgra ngan mtho ris las/ /rdzu 'phrul dang ldan lhung pa bzhin/ /de dang bral ba rtse byar gyur/ /sa la mi shes bya ba ci/ /tsha bas dub pa chur bzhin dang / /grang bas nyam thag me
<p>86a.2</p>la bzhin/ /the tshom gcod la skye bo rnams/ /da ni su la brten par 'gyur/ /me ni 'phel phyir sbud pa bzhin/ /gang gis sbud ba dge legs phyir/ /'jig rten slob dpon thub pa der/ /nyams tshe chos ni nyams par 'gyur/ /tshul med tshul ngan gyis bcings pa'i/ /rga shi dbang bdag
<p>86a.3</p>rnams kyi ni/ /sdug bsngal 'khrul 'khor chen po yi/ /bshig byed de 'dra su zhig yod/ /sin d+hur shing ni skams pa rnams/ /dpyid mthar chu gter gyis bzhin du/ /chags skyes rgod pa'i mi rnams ni/ /gsung gis tshim mdzad su zhig lags/ /gang du bla ma lhun po'i snying / /kun mkhyen
<p>86a.4</p>nyid kyang rgud 'gyur na/ /blo gros ldan pa 'jig rten na/ /blo gtad la 'gro 'os pa su/ /ji ltar gsang bya bskyangs byas nas/ /'chi ba'i ched du 'khrid par byed/ /de bzhin gson pa'i 'jig rten sdug /'ching ba'i ched du skye bar byed/ /ji ltar shing ni rno ba yi/ /sog le yis ni
<p>86a.5</p>gshegs par byed/ /de bzhin 'gro 'di nyams pa yi/ /sog le yis ni gshegs par byed/ /nyon mongs mtha' dag bsregs nas kyang / /ye shes kyi ni stobs ldan kyang / /'gro ba'i mchog gi slob dpon ni/ /rab tu nyams phyir gshegs par gyur/ /lta ngan srog chags ngan pa
<p>86a.6</p>chu/ /srid pa'i dba' rlabs rdul ni nya/ /ye shes gru bo chen po yis/ /gang gi srid pa'i mtsho las rgal/ /rga ba'i yal ga nad me tog /'chi ba'i rtsa ba srid myu gu/ /ye shes mtshon cha chen po yis/ /gang gis srid pa'i ljon shing bcad/ /ma rig gtsub shing las skyes shing / /
<p>86a.7</p>'dod chags me lce yul bud shing / /gang gis ye shes bsil ba'i chus/ /skyon gyi me ni zhi bar mdzad/ /gang gis zhi ba'i lam la gshegs/ /gang gis mun pa chen po spangs/ /gang gis dge legs mchog mkhyen zhing / /mkhyen nas byams pa yis bstan to/ /nges kyang nyon mongs kun
<p>86b</p>
<p>86b.1</p>mthar phyir/ /kun du zhi ba gzigs pa ste/ /kun mkhyen kun la phan pa mdzad/ /kun spangs ched du gshegs pa nyid/ /mnyen zhing rnam yangs dbyangs mnga' ba'i/ /phyag ring thub pa chen po de'i/ /gal te mtha' na su yi mtha'/ /'byung 'gyur ma yin 'byung 'gyur min/ /'brog
<p>86b.2</p>dgon dag na chu mthong nas/ /lam 'gro don bcas 'khrul ba bzhin/ /myur ba dang ldan mkhas pas ni/ /de phyir chos la bsnyen par 'os/ /nyams phyir khyad par med pa yi/ /sdig pa mi rtag nyid shes nas/ /gang zhig chos la gnyid ma log /de ni nyal yang gnyid ma
<p>86b.3</p>log /de nas mi yi seng ge yi/ /ye shes za phod seng ge des/ /skye ba'i nyes pa rnams smad cing / /srid pa zad pa'i bstod pa nyid/ /srid pa'i rtsa ba 'dor 'dod cing / /brtul zhugs dam pa len 'dod la/ /g.yo ba'i sems ni thul 'dod de/ /dge ba'i lam la gnas par
<p>86b.4</p>'dod/ /zhi ba'i lam la 'gro 'dod cing / /srid pa'i mtsho las rgal 'dod la/ /rtag par sbyin pa gtong 'dod de/ /yang srid gcod par 'dod pa'o/ /sbyin pa byin zhing nga rgyal spangs/ /chos ni bsams shing zhi bar song / /thub pa mya ngan 'da' bzhed tshe/ /de yis sa ni stong par
<p>86b.5</p>go/ /de nas sku lus thams cad kyis/ /gnyis 'thung rgyal po bzhin bzlog nas/ /grong khyer la ni gzigs bzhin du/ /thub pas 'di skad bka' stsal to/ /yangs pa can gyi bdag gi 'di/ /khyod la lta ba'i phyi ma yin/ /gyad gnas kyi tshe tshong dus su/ /mya ngan
<p>86b.6</p>'da' phyir 'gro par gyis/ /de nas gus ldan chos 'dod pa/ /nye bar 'ongs pa rnams gzigs nas/ /de yi rab spyod las rnams la/ /thub pas mngon par rjes gnang mdzad/ /de nas rim gyis rnam 'dren pa/ /longs spyod grong la bsnyen pa ste/ /der bzhugs
<p>86b.7</p>thams cad mkhyen pa yis/ /dge slong rnams la mngon par gsungs/ /da ltar ram ni bdag 'das nas/ /chos la mchog tu gzhol bar bya/ /de ni khyod kyi don mchog ste/ /gang gzhan de ni ngal bar 'gyur/ /gang zhig mdo sder ma zhugs shing / /'dul ba na yang mi snang
<p>87a</p>
<p>87a.1</p>la/ /rigs par so sor gnod pa ste/ /de ni cis kyang gzung mi bya/ /de ni chos min 'dul ba min/ /de ni bdag gi tshig ma yin/ /mang po rnams kyi tshig yin kyang / /nag po'i gdams pa de dor bya/ /dag pa'i gdams pa gzung bya zhing / /gang
<p>87a.2</p>la yod min zlog pa ste/ /de ni chos yin 'dul ba ste/ /de ni bdag gi tshig yin no/ /de phyir bdag gis mdor bsdus nas/ /tshad ma 'di rnams bshad pa ste/ /gang zhig byed de tshad ma yin/ /'di las gzhan du tshad ma min/ /bdag gi dgongs pa phra mo de/ /rnam par ma
<p>87a.3</p>bzhag ma shes nas/ /rmongs las chos ma yin pa la/ /chos kyi blo rnams 'byung bar 'gyur/ /mun pa dang bcas lta bas sam/ /khyad par rnams ni shes min las/ /gser dang rab tu mtshungs pa yi/ /ji ltar zangs kyis slu bar byed/ /shes rab khyab pa med pas sam/ /
<p>87a.4</p>de nyid 'dzin pa ma yin pas/ /dam pa'i chos kyi gzugs brnyan gyi/ /de ltar chos ma yin pas slu/ /brdar las gcad las bsregs pa las/ /mkhas pa rnams kyis gser bzhin du/ /'dul ba mdo las rigs pa las/ /de phyir yongs su rtog par rigs/ /bstan
<p>87a.5</p>bcos rnam par mi shes pas/ /mkhas pa rnams ni ma yin zhing / /tshul min la tshul blo gros dang / /tshul la tshul min mthong ba nyid/ /de phyir don dang tshig gis ni/ /yang dag thos pas gzung bya ste/ /bstan bcos log par gzung ba yis/ /mtshon cha bzhin du rnam par 'joms/ /
<p>87a.6</p>sngar med ldan pas 'khyog mang po'i/ /mtshan mo'i 'od byed khyim la bzhin/ /tshig ni log par brjod pa yi/ /don la sdug bsngal gyis 'jug go/ /don nyams pa las chos nyams shing / /chos nyams pa las nus pa ste/ /de phyir ma log don la ni/ /gang gi blo de blo ldan no/ /dge
<p>87a.7</p>mang de skad gsungs nas ni/ /dus su sdig pa'i grong la gshegs/ /der ni 'di la mkhyen rnams kyis/ /bsnyen bkur dam pa byas pa'o/ /de nas der ni gus ldan pa/ /skul byed legs pa'i khyim nyid du/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis zas mdzad de/ /de yi phyir yin rgyas phyir
<p>87b</p>
<p>87b.1</p>min/ /de nas nyan thos tshogs bcas te/ /de bzhin gshegs pas zas mdzad nas/ /skul byed la ni chos gsungs te/ /ku sha ldan pa'i grong du gshegs/ /de bzhin nor ldan zhes pa'i klung / /skul byed bcas pa de rgal nas/ /grong khyer der ni zhi ba yi/ /pad ma'i nags
<p>87b.2</p>bcas nags su bsnyen/ /gser dang 'dra ba'i 'od mnga' des/ /gser ldan la ni khrus mdzad nas/ /kun dga' bo ni dga' med la/ /'jig rten dga' bas bka' stsal to/ /kun dga' gshin rje'i ra ba yi/ /dbus su bdag gi khri shoms shig /de ring nam gyi cha smad la/ /
<p>87b.3</p>de bzhin gshegs pa mya ngan 'da'/ /zhes gsungs kun dga' bos thos nas/ /mchi mas zhag ngan mig ldan pas/ /thub pa'i gzims mal bshams pa ste/ /bshams nas bstod cing kyi hud do/ /de nas gzims mal bstabs pa la/ /rkang gnyis rnams kyi mchog byon te/ /
<p>87b.4</p>yang yang sad pa med phyir dang / /sdug bsngal thams cad zad phyir ro/ /de ni rtsib logs g.yas kyi ni/ /phyag la dbu ni rnam gzhag nas/ /zhabs la zhabs ni bkod nas su/ /slob mas mdun bdar gzims pa'o/ /de nas yud tsam de na der/ /bya rnams skad ni mi sgrogs te/ /
<p>87b.5</p>zags shing snyoms pa'i lus rnams kyis/ /bsam gtan la ni gzhol bzhin gnas/ /de tshe 'dab ma g.yo rnams las/ /rlung rnams kyis kyang ma g.yos pa'i/ /ljon shing rnams kyi mchi ma bzhin/ /mdog ngan me tog rnams gtor to/ /nub ri'i rtse la nyin mor byed/ /gnas la
<p>87b.6</p>lam 'gro rnam pa bzhin/ /khri la thub pa lta bzhin du/ /don dam mthong rnams skyen par gyur/ /de nas mthar thug gzims mal la/ /thams cad mkhyen pa gzims pa yis/ /mchi mas rnam 'khrug kun dga' la/ /rjes su brtse bas bka' stsal to/ /bdag ni mya ngan 'da' ba'i
<p>87b.7</p>dus/ /gyad rnams la smros kun dga' bo/ /mya ngan 'da' ba ma mthong na/ /phyis nas bdag la gdung bar 'gyur/ /de nas gsung ni rab bzung nas/ /mchi mas brgyal ba'i kun dga' bos/ /thub pa'i gzims mal mthar thug pa/ /gyad rnams la ni smras pa'o/ /de nas de'i tshe kun
<p>88a</p>
<p>88a.1</p>dga' bo yi tshig thos nas/ /mig nas chu yi char ldan de rnams ngu bzhin du/ /seng ge'i 'jigs las sa 'dzin dag nas khyu mchog ltar/ /brtan min rnam par gnon rnams grong khyer nas 'thon to/ /zhen pa med pas gos rnams g.yengs shing rnam bkram
<p>88a.2</p>ste/ /'gros kyis kun nas bskyod pas cod pan g.yo ba rnams/ /lha na gnas rnams bsod nams yongs su zad las bzhin/ /de na nyam thag 'ongs pa rnams ni nags der song / /de ltar 'ongs pa rnams kyis thub pa mthong ba ste/ /mthong nas mchi ma'i gdod ldan rnams
<p>88a.3</p>kyis phyag 'tshal zhing / /phyag 'tshal nas ni yongs gdung sems rnams gnas pa ste/ /gnas pa de rnams la ni thub pas bka' stsal to/ /dga' ba'i dus su mya ngan byed par rigs min zhing / /yid mi bde bas don med bstan pa bsnyen par gyis/ /bskal pa du ma rnams su
<p>88a.4</p>bdag gi 'dod pa gang / /shin tu rnyed dka'i don de bdag la nye bar gnas/ /sa dang chu dang me dang rlung dang mkha' med pa'i/ /dge zhing 'gyur med dbang po'i dbang don las 'das pa/ /zhi zhing dbrog bya ma yin mchog de gang thob nas/ /skye ba med cing 'pho ba med la mya ngan med/ /
<p>88a.5</p>ga ya rnams su byang chub tshe na bdag gis sngon/ /dge min srid pa'i rgyu rnams sbrul bzhin dor ba ste/ /sngon tshe bsags pa'i lus kyis rnam par gnas pa 'di/ /lus 'di nyid ni de ring nye bar 'gro bar 'gyur/ /sdug bsngal gyi ni gter chen phung po song ba na/ /'jigs pa chen po
<p>88a.6</p>yang srid nye bar zhi ba na/ /gang tshe sdug bsngal chen po las ni byung ba ste/ /gang gis ngu ba bdag la mya ngan 'os ci yod/ /rab tu zhi ba'i dus yin na yang 'brug gi dbyangs/ /shAkya thub pa'i gsung ni de rnams kyis thos nas/ /de nas kha rnams bye zhing smra 'dod gyur pa ste/ /de dag
<p>88a.7</p>rnams kyi tshig de gnas brtan gyis gsol to/ /gang gis ngu ba khyod kyi mya ngan 'os ci yod/ /me ni khang pa 'bar las rnam par 'thon pa ltar/ /de ltar thub pa de ni lha gtso rnams kyis kyang / /nges par bsnyen bya yin na mi rnams kyis smros ci/ /khyab bdag skye bo gang 'di de bzhin
<p>88b</p>
<p>88b.1</p>gshegs pa ni/ /mya ngan 'das 'di mthon min des na mya ngan byed/ /'brog dgon dag na song ba'i lam mkhan bzang po ni/ /rnam par nyams tshe kun nas 'khrul bar cis ma 'gyur/ /bla ma drang srong chen po thams cad gzigs pa ni/ /dngos su mthong nas gal te khyad par ma thob na/ /
<p>88b.2</p>gser gyi 'byung gnas dag nas dbul po song rnams bzhin/ /de tshe 'di na bzhad gad nyid du 'gro ba nyid/ /de ltar don ldan mang po de de smra ba rnams/ /bu rnams la bzhin gus ldan thal mo sbyar ba rnams/ /dge zhing zhi la dam pa'i don ni bsngags pa yis/ /gyad rnams dag la
<p>88b.3</p>mchog bdag rnams kyi mchog gis gsungs/ /de ltar nges pa de ni kho bo mthong ba las/ /rnal 'byor cho gar 'bad rtsol med par grol min te/ /bdag gi chos 'di gang zhig rjes su rtog byed pa/ /sdug bsngal dra ba las de ma mthong na yang grol/ /ji ltar sman ni bsnyen par mi byed
<p>88b.4</p>skyes bu yis/ /sman pa mthong ba las kyang nad ni 'joms min te/ /de bzhin bdag gis ye shes 'di ni ma bsgoms na/ /bdag ni mthong ba las kyang sdug bsngal 'joms ma yin/ /'di ni bdag ldan gang zhig bdag gi chos mthong ba/ /rgyang ring dag na gnas kyang des ni bdag
<p>88b.5</p>mthong ste/ /gang zhig dge legs la ni gzhol zhing mi 'jug pa/ /bdag gi nye bar gnas kyang de ni rgyang ring nyid/ /de phyir brtson 'grus ma spangs bsdams pa'i sems rnams kyis/ /dge ba'i las rnams la ni bag dang ldan par gyis/ /sdug bsngal du ma nye bar 'dus shing g.yo ba
<p>88b.6</p>ste/ /srog ni tho rangs mar me dang ni mtshungs pa nyid/ /de ltar thub pa'i skyes mchog gis bstan de rnams ni/ /mig nas chu ni rnam byung nyam thag yid rnams kyis/ /chu bo'i gzhung ni so sor sgrol bar byed pa bzhin/ /ku sha zhes bya'i grong la dal bus dbang med zhugs/ /sangs rgyas
<p>88b.7</p>kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ mya ngan las 'da' bar gshegs pa'i le'u ste nyi shu rtsa lnga pa'o// //de nas bzang pos yang dag nyer ldan legs bzang ni/ /dbyu gu gsum 'dzin 'byung po'i tshogs su mi mchod pa/ /bde bar gshegs pa lta 'dod
<p>89a</p>
<p>89a.1</p>dge slong thar 'dod pas/ /kun dga' byed pa'i kun dga' bo la smras pa'o/ /thub pa mya ngan 'da' ba'i dus ni bdag gis thos/ /gang gi ched du bdag gis lta 'dod skyes pa ste/ /'jig rten dag na mchog gi chos kyi rtogs pa po/ /zla ba gnam stong la bzhin mthong
<p>89a.2</p>bar zla ba min/ /sdug bsngal mtha' dag rnams kyi tha mar gshegs bzhed pa/ /khyod kyi 'dren pa de ni lta bar 'dod pa ste/ /sprin gyis mngon par bkag pa'i mkha' la nyi ma bzhin/ /bdag gis ma mthong bar de nub par 'gro ma yin/ /de nas yongs su 'gro ba po ni 'ongs pa ste/ /smra
<p>89a.3</p>bar 'dod cing chos 'dod pa ni des shes nas/ /ngal ba dang ni ldan pa'i sems ldan kun dga' bos/ /dus ma yin zhes mchi ma'i gdong gis smras pa'o/ /de ni zla ba'i 'od mnga' bsam pa mkhyen pa po/ /'dab ma rgyas pa'i spyan yangs rnam par mkhyen nas su/ /gang phyir kho bo 'jig
<p>89a.4</p>rten phan phyir skyes pa ste/ /kun dga' bo kye gnyis skyes ma 'gogs zhes gsungs so/ /de las legs bzang mchog tu dga' zhing yid ches shing / /dpal stug dge legs mdzod la mngon du song ba ste/ /de nas dus kyi rjes su mthun pas zhi ba yi/ /gsung ni mngon par gsungs
<p>89a.5</p>nas slar yang de gsol to/ /kho bo lta ba'i yongs su rtog pa po rnams las/ /thar pa'i lam gzhan lhag par khyed kyis lhag par thob ces grag /de phyir bdag la gsung mdzod bdag la 'dzin 'dod yod/ /bdag gis lta 'dod rtse bar 'dod pa'i phyir ma yin/ /de nas gnyis
<p>89a.6</p>skyes mngon par 'ongs pa de la ni/ /yan lag brgyad kyi lam ni sangs rgyas kyis gsungs shing / /rab tu chud zos lam ni yang dag dran pa bzhin/ /thos nas gang ni gang gis yang dag rtogs/ /des ni sngon du mthong bar gyur pa'i lam gzhan la/ /des ni mthar thug dam pa nye bar ma thob
<p>89a.7</p>ste/ /sngon du ma mthong lam ni lhag par thob nas su/ /snying la mun pa dang bcas lam de dor bar gyur/ /rdul dang lhan cig mun pa rab tu 'phel ba ste/ /de dag rnams kyi mi dge'i las ni sogs zhes grags/ /snying stobs dang bcas rdul ni rab tu 'phel ba ste/ /de dag rnams
<p>89b</p>
<p>89b.1</p>kyi dge ba'i las ni rgyas zhes grags/ /thos dang blo dang 'bad pas snying stobs 'phel ba na/ /rdul dang mun pa nag ni rnam pa med pa'i phyir/ /las nyams pa las las ni zad par 'gro ba ste/ /de dag rnams kyi las de 'thad pa yin zhes grags/ /yid ni rmongs par byed
<p>89b.2</p>pa rdul dang mun pa dag /rang bzhin par ni 'jig rten dag na smra ba ste/ /de phyir de gnyis zad pa yod min brtan nyid phyir/ /rang bzhin par ni brtan pa nyid du rab tu grub/ /snying stobs sbyor las de dag bde skye bar gyur na yang / /dus kyi dbang gis slar yang 'byung bar 'gyur ba
<p>89b.3</p>ste/ /bsil ba'i chu ni tshan mo bzhin du rim gyis ni/ /dus kyi rim las rang bzhin du ni 'gro bar 'gyur/ /rtag pa'i bdag nyid snying stobs de ltar 'phel ba ru/ /thos pa blo dang 'bad pa rnams kyis mi nus te/ /de ma 'phel na de dag nyams pa yod min zhing / /de dag ma
<p>89b.4</p>nyams pa las zhi ba yod ma yin/ /sngon du des ni rang bzhin las ni skyes snyam ste/ /des kyang der ni thar pa mthong ba ma yin zhing / /me yi 'bar ba'i 'od kyi nyams pa ji lta bar/ /rang bzhin la ni gnas na mthar thug gang las yin/ /sangs rgyas pa yi lam gyis de nyid mthong ba
<p>89b.5</p>ste/ /srid pa la ni brten nas 'jig rten des rtogs shing / /de yi rnam par nyams pas zhi ba rigs pa ste/ /rgyu ni rab tu nyams phyir 'bras bu nyams pa'o/ /gsal ba 'di yin rnam par 'gyur ba med pa'i bdag /lus las gzhan ni de yis sngon du rtogs pa ste/ /thub pa'i
<p>89b.6</p>gsung ni yongs su thob nas 'jig rten ni/ /bdag med pa dang bdag tu bya ba med par shes/ /chos ni du ma so sor brten nas skyes pa ste/ /rang nyid dbang med yongs su shes nas ni/ /des ni rab tu 'jug pa sdug bsngal nyid du dang / /nges par ldog ste sdug bsngal nyid du kye ma mthong / /
<p>89b.7</p>ji ltar 'jig rten dag ni skye ba rtogs nas su/ /des ni chad pa'i lta ba rnam par spangs pa ste/ /'jig rten dag gi nub par 'gro ba shes nas su/ /rtag pa'i lta ba brtan po skyen par spangs pa'o/ /drang srong chen po'i gsung ni thos nas bzung ba ste/ /de ltar 'di na des ni sngon gyi lta ba dang / 
<p>90a</p>
<p>90a.1</p>de yis sngon du yongs su las ni byas pas te/ /gang gis skyen par dam pa'i chos la rjes su song / /yid ni rab tu dang bas mchog dang ldan pa des/ /zhi zhing 'gyur med go 'phang de ni rab thob nas/ /thub pa gzims pa la ni bsngags pa byas pa ste/ /lta bzhin 'di
<p>90a.2</p>las blo 'di rnams ni byas pa'o/ /mchod 'os dam pa mya ngan 'da' bar 'os pa yi/ /mgon po mthong nas bdag ni gnas par 'os ma yin/ /ston pa thugs rje ldan pa mya ngan 'da' ba yi/ /sngon du re zhig bdag ni mthar thug la 'gro'o/ /de nas des ni thub pa la ni phyag 'tshal nas/ /
<p>90a.3</p>sbrul bzhin g.yo ba med pa'i gdan ni bcings nas su/ /sprin rlung gis ni phra mo'i phra mor byed pa bzhin/ /de ma thag tu zhi ba mya ngan 'da' bar gshegs/ /de nas de phyir gdung gi 'du byed cho ga ni/ /cho ga mkhyen pa'i thub pas rnam par bka' stsal pa/ /mthar gyur de ni skye
<p>90a.4</p>ba mthar mdzad drang srong che/ /rgya chen slob ma mnga' ba'i slob mar gyur pa'o/ /de nas nam gyi thun ni 'das pa na/ /zla bas skar ma rnams kyi 'od ni phrogs pa na/ /nags rnams nyal ba bzhin du sgra med gyur pa na/ /dge slong rnams la thugs rje chen po mnga' bas bstan/ /slob dpon
<p>90a.5</p>bzhin du sgron ma bzhin du don bzhin du/ /bdag 'das tshe na so sor thar pa bstan bya ste/ /khyed kyi ston pa de yin de'i dbang gis 'gyur bya/ /kho bo gnas pa na yang de tsam nyid smra'o/ /lus dang ngag gi las ni rnam par dag 'dod pas/ /de bzhin 'jig rten tha snyad thams cad 'dor
<p>90a.6</p>ba dang / /sa dang srog chags sa bon rdzas la sogs rnams kyis/ /rab tu 'dzin pa las ni me bzhin ldog pa'o/ /sa la skye ba gcod dang 'byed pa dag las dang / /sa yi logs la rko dang rmo ba dag las dang / /gso ba dang ni skar rtsis mtshan nyid rnams las ni/ /nges par
<p>90a.7</p>ldog pa bza' ba'i cho ga dus yin no/ /pho nya'i rigs pa sman dang sngags ni bsnyen rnams la/ /sbyor min nyid dang 'chab pa nyid ni med pa nyid/ /chos las ma bkag pa yi sgrub pa rnams la ni/ /tshod shes nyid dang tshim dang sogs pa ma yin no/ /rnam pa de ltar tshul khrims
<p>90b</p>
<p>90b.1</p>yang dag bsdus pa 'di/ /thar pa'i rtsa ba zhes pa so sor thar pa ste/ /'di las ting nge 'dzin rnams rab tu skye ba ste/ /ye shes thams cad rnams dang mthar thug rnam 'da'o/ /de phyir ma ral ma nyams dbrog bya ma yin pa'i/ /gang gis tshul khrims gtsang ma yod pa de yi
<p>90b.2</p>chos/ /de med gal te 'di yi thams cad med pa ste/ /tshul khrims yon tan dam pa rnams kyi rten yin no/ /tshul khrims ma nyams rnam par dag pa gnas pa na/ /dbang po spyod yul rnams la 'jug pa ma yin zhing / /dbyug pas ba lang tshogs rnams lo thog la
<p>90b.3</p>bzhin du/ /brtan las dbang po drug rnams bsgrib par bya ba'o/ /dbang po'i rta rnams yul rnams la grol gang zhig gzhan/ /len zhing de rnams las ni de tsam nyid ma yin/ /g.yo ba'i rta rnams kyis phrogs lam ngan la bzhin du/ /des ni de yi ched du don med thob par
<p>90b.4</p>'gyur/ /dgra bo chen po rnams kyi dbang du song ba rnams/ /'di na kha cig sdug bsngal 'thob par 'gyur ba ste/ /rmongs pas yul rnams dag gi dbang du song nas ni/ /song nas deng 'dir dbang med rnams ni sdug bsngal 'os/ /de phyir dgra bo ma rungs dbang po rnams kyi
<p>90b.5</p>bzhin/ /dbang po rnams kyi 'gro ba 'gro bya ma yin zhing / /dbang po rnams kyi dga' bo 'jig rten na byas nas/ /dbang po rnams kyi gshed ma 'jig rten na mthong ngo / /rang gi g.yo ba'i sems las 'jigs pa ji lta bar/ /stag rnams las dang sbrul dang 'bar ba'i me
<p>90b.6</p>las dang / /dgra bo las ni de ltar 'jigs par mi bya ste/ /gang gis sbrang rtsi dang ni yang dag rtog pa med/ /lcags kyu med pa'i gnyis 'thung myos pa lta bu dang / /yal ga'i ri dgas shing la rab tu ma zhi ltar/ /sems ni ji ltar 'dod bzhin phyogs su skor ba ste/ /g.yo zhing
<p>90b.7</p>bskyod pa de la go skabs sbyin mi bya/ /de ni rang dbang yin na zhi ba yod min zhing / /de yi gnas pa yin na byed pa byas pa nyid/ /de phyir sems 'di ji ltar rnam par mi g.yo ba/ /de ltar rab tu 'bad pa yis ni gyis mdzod cig /bza' ba tsam ni sman bzhin nges par bsten
<p>91a</p>
<p>91a.1</p>bya ste/ /'dir ni khong khro bya ba ma yin chags pa min/ /ji srid bkres pa nyid ni ldog pa'i ched du dang / /lus kyi 'khrul 'khor gyis 'dzin pa yi ched du'o/ /ji ltar nags su bung ba rnams kyis me tog ro/ /'thung ste me tog rnams ni nyams par byed
<p>91a.2</p>ma yin/ /de bzhin dus kyi dbang las bsod snyoms rgyu ba ste/ /pha rol dad pa rnams ni nyams par byed ma yin/ /drang pos rtag par khur bar byed ces khur bya dang / /skye bo sbyin pa po yang yod pa ma yin te/ /'di na sbyor ba min las khur ba ltung ba ste/ /ji ltar khur bu de
<p>91a.3</p>ltar sbyin pa po yin no/ /rnal 'byor rim las nyin mo mtha' dag phul nas dang / /mtshan mo'i dang po'i thun dang cig shos dag kyang ste/ /dran pa dang bcas snga ma'i cig shos la nyol la/ /gnyid kyi tshe ni don med byed pa ma yin no/ /dus kyi me yis 'di na 'gro ba sreg pa na/ /
<p>91a.4</p>mtshan mo mtha' dag la ni gnyid par 'os pa su/ /nyon mongs dgra po dang mtshungs 'joms pa po rnams ni/ /snying la gnas pa yin na su yi gnyid log 'gyur/ /de phyir khyim na nag po'i sbrul rnams nyal ba ltar/ /yid la nyes skyon sbrul rnams rab tu nyal ba rnams/ /rigs pa dang ni
<p>91a.5</p>rkang pa sman gyis ston nas su/ /gnyid log par 'os 'di las gzhan du ngo tsha'o/ /ngo tsha rgyan nyid dang ni mchog gi gos yin zhing / /ngo tsha lam las 'khyog pa rnams kyi lcags kyus te/ /ngo tsha ldan pas de ltar gyur na 'jug bya zhing / /ngo tshas rnam par spangs ba'i yon tan
<p>91a.6</p>rnams kyis spangs/ /ji srid pa la skyes bu ngo tsha dang bcas pa/ /de srid de yi mi yi ngo tsha nyid yin te/ /don dang don min rnams la rnam dpyod med pa ni/ /ngo tshas rnam par dman pa phyugs dang mnyam pa'o/ /gang yang yan lag nying lag rnams ni ral gris gcod/ /der yang
<p>91a.7</p>yid kyis nyes pa bya ba ma yin zhing / /zhi ba ma yin dag ni brjod par mi bya ste/ /bdag gi de yis khyed cag rnams kyi bar chod yin/ /bzod pa dang mnyam dka' thub yod pa ma yin zhing / /gang gi bzod pa de yis stobs dang brtan pa ste/ /gang rnams pha rol rnams las
<p>91b</p>
<p>91b.1</p>rtsub mo mi bzod pa/ /de rnams chos byed rnams kyi lugs min grol ba min/ /chos kyi 'byed pa po dang grags pa'i 'joms pa po/ /gzugs kyi dgra bo dang ni snying gi me yin te/ /khro ba de yis go skabs rab 'byam mi sbyin zhing / /yon tan rnams kyi dgra bo de 'dra gzhan ma yin/ /
<p>91b.2</p>yongs su bsil ba'i chu las glog gi me bzhin du/ /ji ltar rab byung las ni khro ba 'gal ba ste/ /de ltar khyim pa rnams kyi skyes pa mi 'gal te/ /chags ldan de rnams de la dam bca' ma yin no/ /mdzes pa'i skra ni rgyang ring mgo la reg nas dang / /rnam par 'gyur ba'i gos dang
<p>91b.3</p>lhung bzed mthong nas dang / /gzhan las mthar gyur spyod pa rnam par bsams nas su/ /snying la skyes pa'i nga rgyal rab tu spang bar bya/ /khyim la brten pa khengs pa ldan pa rnams kyi yang / /nga rgyal rnam par 'phel ba 'joms pa'i phyir yin na/ /slong mo za bas bdag nyid
<p>91b.4</p>yongs su rtog pa po/ /thar pa la dmigs skra bzhar rnams kyi sngon nyid do/ /ngan g.yo dang ni chos kyi mtshams sbyor yod min te/ /gang phyir 'di las 'khyog po nyid ni bsnyen mi bya/ /ngan g.yo nyid dang sgyu ni slu ba'i don du ste/ /chos kyi bdag nyid rnams kyi bslu bya yod ma yin/ /
<p>91b.5</p>gang zhig rgya chen rnams las sdug bsngal 'ongs pa ste/ /nyung ngu 'dod la 'ong ba ma yin de dang bral/ /de yi phyir yang nyung ngu 'dod nyid bsnyen bya ste/ /gang zhig yon tan rnams kyis rdzogs byed kye ma ci/ /de ni bkren pa'i lta ba rnams la mi 'jigs shing / /dbang po
<p>91b.6</p>rnams las gang zhig cung zad 'jigs min la/ /gang zhig thos nas med ces mya ngan med pa ste/ /gang gis nyung ngu 'dod de de yi thar pa min/ /gal te grol bar 'dod na tshim pa bsnyen mdzod dang / /tshim pa na ni 'dir bde de 'di chos yin zhing / /tshim pa rnams ni sar yang bde bar
<p>91b.7</p>gnyid log ste/ /tshim med rnams ni mtho ris na yang rnam par sreg /phyug kyang tshim pa med pa rtag tu dbul po ste/ /dbul yang tshim pa dang ldan rtag tu phyug po nyid/ /tshim pa med pa sdug pa'i yul rnams dang 'bye zhing / /tshim pas 'gro ba ngal ba ldan la mya ngan byed/ /zhi
<p>92a</p>
<p>92a.1</p>ba'i bde ba dam pa thob par 'dod rnams kyis/ /de ltar tshogs la dga' ba rnams su 'gyur mi bya/ /zhi ba'i bdag nyid gcig tu rgyu phyir 'jig rten na/ /brgya byin la sogs lha rnams kyis kyang re 'dod byed/ /chags po sdug bsngal gyi ni gnas pa'i shing yin
<p>92a.2</p>te/ /rang gi skye bo la 'am skye la chags pa spangs/ /chags pa rnam rgyas sdug bsngal la ni 'jig rten na/ /gnyis 'thung 'khogs pa 'dam la bzhin du chags par 'gyur/ /rtag par rab zhugs chu yi rgyun ni mnyen na yang / /rdo yi logs la dus su rnam par 'bigs pa ste/ /brtson
<p>92a.3</p>'grus kyis ni rnyed par dka' ba ci yang med/ /de phyir khur rnams mi 'bor bar ni bzod bgyis dang / /gang zhig yang yang ngal bso nas ni srub byed pa/ /de yi shing la me ni rnyed par sla min zhing / /brtson 'grus brtsams pas rnyed par sla bar 'gyur ba ste/ /de phyir sbyor ba yod na bya ba
<p>92a.4</p>'grub pa nyid/ /dran pa yod na skyon rnams 'jug pa ma yin te/ /dran pa dang mnyam mdza' bo med cing bsrung ba med/ /dran pa nyams las des par thams cad nyams pa ste/ /de phyir lus la song ba'i dran pa spang mi bya/ /ji ltar dpa' bo rnams ni go cha bzung nas su/ /dgra bo'i
<p>92a.5</p>sde la 'jigs pa med rnams 'jug pa ste/ /de bzhin lus la dran pa'i go cha bgos nas su/ /brtan pa rnams ni yul gyi g.yul rnams la spyod do/ /mnyam par gzhag pa'i blo dang sems ni yongs bsdams shing / /'jig rten dag gi skye dang 'god pa shes pa ste/ /de phyir ting nge
<p>92a.6</p>'dzin la yongs su 'jug bya ste/ /ting 'dzin rab tu thob pa'i sems nad yod ma yin/ /rnam par 'thor ba'i chu ni rnam par 'dzin don du/ /ji ltar 'bad pas dong dang 'obs ni byed pa ste/ /ye shes chu ni gnas pa'i don du ting nge 'dzin/ /de ltar dong dang 'obs dang mtshungs par rab
<p>92a.7</p>tu bstan/ /shes rab ldan pa yongs su 'dzin pa btang ba yi/ /chos 'di nang la mchog tu gzhol ba dag gis te/ /de ltar gnas pa'i grol ba yod cing 'di yi ni/ /phyin ci log ni khyim pa ma yin dge slong min/ /shes rab dga' dang 'chi ba'i mtsho chen dag la gru/ /rmongs
<p>92b</p>
<p>92b.1</p>pa'i mun pa rnams la ji ltar sgron ma ste/ /nad rnams thams cad 'joms pa dag gi sman yin zhing / /nyon mongs ljon shing 'joms byed mtshon cha rnon po yin/ /de phyir thos pa bsam pa bsgom pa rnams kyi ni/ /shes rab rnam par 'phel la rab tu 'jug par bya/ /gang gi shes
<p>92b.2</p>rab rang bzhin lta byed mig yod pa/ /de ni mig dang bral yang mig dang ldan pa nyid/ /sems la rgyu ba'i spros pa de dang de rnams kyis/ /khyim na gnas pa spangs nas kyang ni grol min nyid/ /mchog tu zhi ba thob par 'dod pa rnams kyis 'di/ /shes nas spros pa med pa rnams su
<p>92b.3</p>'gyur bar bya/ /de phyir bag yod bla ma bzhin du bsnyen mdzod la/ /bag med dgra bo bzhin du rnam par spongs mdzod dang / /bag yod pa las brgya byin gyi na dpal thob cing / /bag med pa las lha min khengs rnams rnam par nyams/ /phan pa dang ldan rjes su brtse ba mnga' ba yi/ /
<p>92b.4</p>ston pa thugs rje mnga' bas mdzad bya gang yin pa/ /de ni bdag gis byas shing dang ni rab bsdams pa/ /khyed cag rnams kyi sems ni zhi bas byas pa'o/ /ci ste ri rnams dang ni khang pa stong pa dang / /dgon pa de rnams gang dang der ni yod pa na/ /rab tu sbyor la rtag tu 'bad pa bya ba ste/ /
<p>92b.5</p>phyi nas yongs su gdung ba ldan par ma gyur cig /sman pa rang bzhin yang dag legs par shes nas ni/ /nad pa rnams la dam pa'i sman ni brjod bya ste/ /de yi dus kyis sbyar bar nges par bsten pa la/ /nad pa gang de bdag po yin te sman pa min/ /dpal ldan drang zhing mnyam la 'jigs
<p>92b.6</p>pa med pa yi/ /lam ni lam mkhan gyis ni rnam par bstan pa na/ /thos nas gang zhig mi 'gro de yi nyams pa ste/ /bstan pas 'dren pa po ni bu lon yod ma yin/ /sdug bsngal la sogs bden pa bzhi po kho bo yis/ /bstan pa rnams la 'di ni gang gi 'dod pa yod/ /de ni myur zhing
<p>92b.7</p>spobs par bdag la smros shig dang / /the tshom shin tu rnam par dpyad bya bcad par bgyi/ /de ltar mthon por gsungs pa'i drang srong chen po la/ /the tshom med pa de rnams ci yang ma gsol to/ /sems kyis de dag rnams kyi sems kyi gting dpags nas/ /byed ldan ma 'gags pas
<p>93a</p>
<p>93a.1</p>kyang tshig 'di smras pa'o/ /rlung ni g.yo ba ma yin nyi ma bsil ba dang / /ri bong mtshan ma can ni dro ba nyid na yang / /'jig rten dag na rkang pa bzhi po de rnams ni/ /bden pa min par byed par nus pa ma yin no/ /gang zhig sdug bsngal brjod pa de ni bde ba min/ /
<p>93a.2</p>'di yi rgyu gang rab tu skye bo de gzhan min/ /rgyu ni 'gags pa las ni nges par thar pa ste/ /gang zhig 'di yi lam ni thabs ma yin pa min/ /de phyir bdag nyid chen po bden pa bzhi rnams la/ /dge slong skye bo nges 'di gtam ci yod ma yin/ /ston pa mya ngan 'da' ba rnyed par 'gyur
<p>93a.3</p>zhes te/ /gang zhig don ni rdzogs pa ma yin sdug bsngal te/ /gang zhig tshogs pa 'di ni brtul zhugs gzhon nyid las/ /sngon du don ni mthong bar gyur pa ma yin pa/ /de yang khyed kyi gsung 'dis da ni de ma thag /glog gi 'od kyis lam bzhin yang dag mthong bar gyur/ /gang
<p>93a.4</p>gi don gyi lhag ma yod pa ma yin zhing / /gang yang srid pa'i mtsho yi pha rol phyin pa ste/ /mgon po shin tu skyen par nges par gshegs thos te/ /de dag gi yang snying la bsams par gyur pa nyid/ /de ltar 'phags pa ma 'gags pa yi tshig de yis/ /don ni rnam par shes kyang
<p>93a.5</p>shes nas slar yang ni/ /gus ldan rnams kyi blo gros brtan po mdzad bzhed pa/ /byams pas slar yang sangs rgyas kyis ni bka' stsal to/ /gang phyir skal bar gnas kyang de ni nyams pa ste/ /phan tshun du ni 'du ba nges par yod ma yin/ /bdag nyid kyi dang gzhan gyi don ni byas nas
<p>93a.6</p>ni/ /kho bo gnas pa la ni dgos pa yod ma yin/ /gang rnams mkhar dang sa na bdag gi gdul bya rnams/ /de rnams thar par byas shing rgyun la bcug pa ste/ /'di las gzhan du slob ma rim dang rim rnams kyis/ /nga yi chos 'di skye dgu rnams la gnas par 'gyur/ /de
<p>93a.7</p>phyir 'gro ba'i rang bzhin rnam par shes byas nas/ /bsam mno ma byed nges par rnam par 'bral ba ste/ /rnam pa de ltar 'gro ba shes nas su/ /ji ltar 'di ltar ma yin de ltar gyis mdzod cig /ye shes sgron mas mun pa rnam par bsal byas nas/ /srid pa rnams la snying po
<p>93b</p>
<p>93b.1</p>med par mthong nas su/ /ji ltar nad ni nye bar zhi ba de ltar ni/ /tshe ni rnam par 'gags na tshim pa nyid yin no/ /dor bar bya zhing rtsod ldan lus zhes bya ba ni/ /srid pa'i mtsho yi rgyun ni rnam par 'gags pa na/ /don med byed pa'i dgra bo'i rnam par nyams las bzhin/ /tshe ni nye bar
<p>93b.2</p>zhi bas tshim pa ma yin su/ /rgyu dang mi rgyu thams cad rnam par 'god pa ste/ /de phyir khyed cag rnams ni legs par bag yod gyis/ /mya ngan 'da' ba'i dus ni yongs su gyur pa ste/ /khyed cag ma smra 'di ni bdag gi phyi ma'i tshig /de nas bsam gtan rig pa rnams kyi mchog
<p>93b.3</p>gis ni/ /yud tsam de la bsam gtan dang po thob mdzad nas/ /de las rnam par bzhengs nas gnyis par gshegs pa ste/ /rim gyis ma tshang med par thams cad la gshegs so/ /de nas rjes su rim pas rab tu byed pa dgu/ /snyoms par 'jug pa'i tshogs ni mtha' dag
<p>93b.4</p>bsam gtan mdzad/ /de nas drang srong chen pos slar yang rim gyis ni/ /bsam gtan dang po de nyid la ni bab pa'o/ /de las rnam par bzhengs nas kyang ni rim gyis ni/ /bsam gtan bzhi pa la ni slar yang 'dzegs pa ste/ /bsam gtan bzhi pa'i cho ga las de rnams
<p>93b.5</p>bzhengs shing / /mngon sum nyid du nye bar zhi ba la gshegs so/ /de nas thub pa mya ngan 'da' bar gshegs pa na/ /char gyis snun pa'i ba lang bzhin du sa g.yos shing / /phyogs kyi glang po rnams kyis sbyangs pa bzhin du ni/ /nam mkha' las kyang sgron ma rnams ni lhung bar gyur/ /
<p>93b.6</p>lha yi nags tshal sna tshogs shing rta sreg 'dod pa'i/ /nags kyi me ni bar snang dag la byung ba bzhin/ /bud shing med cing rlung med du ba med pa'i me/ /phyogs ni sreg par byed pa byung bar gyur pa nyid/ /lha min 'joms par 'dod pa g.yul du 'jug pa na/ /khro ba brgya bas khro ba
<p>93b.7</p>rnam par gtong ba bzhin/ /de bzhin me stag brgya pa'i me ni skyug pa yi/ /dbang po'i rdo rje mi bzad pa rnams lhung bar gyur/ /'jig pa'i rlung rnams dag gis btags pa rnams kyi bzhin/ /'dzin pa 'dzin pa rnams kyi rtse mo rnams lhung zhing / /'khri shing shing rnams dag ni
<p>94a</p>
<p>94a.1</p>zug rngu byed pa yi/ /phyag dar khur ba'i rlung ni drag tu g.yos par gyur/ /'dam gyi chus bsgos sdong du gzhon nu rnams kyis ni/ /lus ni yongs su dkris pa'i ngang pa'i rgyal po bzhin/ /cung zhig 'od zer kha dog ngan pa de rnams kyis/ /'od ni bcom ste zla
<p>94a.2</p>ba mngon par gsal bar gyur/ /sprin dang bral yang mkha' la zla ba gnas na yang / /mun pa mi bzad rnams kyis phyogs rnams rgyas pa ste/ /yud tsam de la mya ngan gyis ni zil non bzhin/ /chu bo rnams ni de ma thag tu chu dron 'bab/ /de nas nye sar skyes pa'i sha la'i shing dag gis/ /
<p>94a.3</p>rang gis me tog mdzes pa 'jug pa dus min la/ /rnam par btud nas drang srong chen po'i sku lus ni/ /gser gyi stegs bu'i gzugs brnyan la ni yang dag gtor/ /mkha' la mgo bo lnga rnams mi g.yo'i klu rnams ni/ /mya ngan gyis slar so sor dmar ba'i mig can rnams/ /rab
<p>94a.4</p>tu gnyid log gdengs ka stod pa'i lus rnams kyis/ /thub pa la ni gus pas lta bzhin gnas par gyur/ /nang du song ba'i kun nas gdung ba rnams/ /de rnams shin tu dron po'i dbugs ni brgyus pa ste/ /'gro ba'i rang bzhin mi rtag pa ni rtogs nas su/ /mya ngan 'ongs pa min rnams
<p>94a.5</p>mya ngan smad par gyur/ /nges par legs pa'i chos kyis cho gar rab zhugs pa/ /rgyal po rnam thos sras kyi 'dus pa dam pa de/ /chos la mngon par chags pas mya ngan ma byas shing / /lha yi rten la mchi ma phyung bar ma gyur to/ /gtsang mar lhag par gnas pa'i byed ldan lha rnams
<p>94a.6</p>kyang / /drang srong chen po'i yang dag shin tu gus ldan rnams/ /rang gnas gyur zhing rnam par 'gyur ba ma song ste/ /'jig rten dag ni rang bzhin rnam par smad pa'o/ /dri za'i rgyal po rnams dang de nas klu yi rgyal po rnams/ /gnod sbyin rnams dang dam chos la dga' lha rnams ni/ /mya
<p>94a.7</p>ngan byed cing mya ngan mchog la gzhol rnams kyis/ /rigs chen po yi nyam thag bzhin du kha la gyur/ /yid la re ba thob pa'i bdud kyi sde rnams ni/ /rab tu dga' bas skad ni 'thon zhing dgod pa ste/ /'phyo zhing glu dbyangs gar byas dga' bar gyur pa rnams/ /rnga bo che dang rdza rnga pa Ta
<p>94b</p>
<p>94b.1</p>ha rnams brdungs/ /de nas rdo rje rtse mo bcom pa'i ri bo bzhin/ /chang dang bral ba'i gnyis 'thung dga' ba med pa bzhin/ /nog gis rnam par dman pa'i dbyibs can khyu mchog bzhin/ /thub pa'i khyu mchog nub ba na ni 'jig rten gyur/ /nyin mor byed pas rab tu dman pa'i nam mkha'
<p>94b.2</p>bzhin/ /ba mos bsregs pa'i pad+ma dang ldan rdzing bu bzhin/ /nor dang bral zhing bya ba med pa'i rigs bzhin du/ /srid pa nyams mdzad rab tu nyams las 'gro bar gyur/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba chen po'i le'u ste nyi
<p>94b.3</p>shu rtsa drug pa'o// //de nas ngang pa stong dang ldan pa'i lha yi ni/ /gzhal med khang nas gdong ni cung zhig rab btud nas/ /yud tsam thams cad mkhyen pa la ni bltas nas su/ /lha na gnas pa chen po gzhan zhig gis smras pa'o/ /kye ma 'gro na dngos po thams cad
<p>94b.4</p>mi rtag cing / /skye ba'i chos can dang ni 'dzad pa'i chos can la/ /skye ba rnams ni sdug bsngal skyed par byed pa ste/ /de dag rnams ni lhag med zhi bas zhi ba nyid/ /skye ba'i bud shing tshad ma min pa bsregs mdzad nas/ /ye shes me lce grags pas rnam khyab du ba can/ /chu yis
<p>94b.5</p>mi bzhin du ni dus kyi chu yis ni/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i me de mya ngan 'da' bar bya/ /de nas mchog gi drang srong dang mtshungs drang srong gzhan/ /mtho ris gnas kyang 'bras bu rnams la ma chags pas/ /rab tu zhi ba'i dgra bcom drang srong mthong nas su/ /ri dbang brtan pas tshig
<p>94b.6</p>ni rnam par smras pa'o/ /'jig rten dag na 'ga' zhig nyams par mi 'gro med/ /de ltar 'gro ba med cing song ba med pa ste/ /mchog dang mchog min mkhyen pa mchog gi don rig pa/ /ston pa mtshungs med gang du rab tu zhi bar gyur/ /shes rab rnam par dag cing mchog gi spyan mnga'
<p>94b.7</p>ba/ /yongs su 'dren pa po nyid 'di yis dman pa ni/ /rmongs pa nges par mig long gson pa'i 'jig rten ni/ /'du shes nyams shing lam ngan la ni gnas par 'gyur/ /de nas 'gro ba'i 'gal ba ma yin ma 'gags pa/ /rjes su chags pa nyams shing skye ba 'gags byas
<p>95a</p>
<p>95a.1</p>pas/ /'jig rten snang bas dman pa mthong nas su/ /thub ba zhi ba na ni zhi ba'i yid kyis smras/ /shes rab ldan pa 'du byed cho ga la gnas pa/ /dus 'dir nges par blo gtad bya ba ma yin zhing / /mi rtag nyid kyi rdo rje nges par btung ba yis/ /gang du thub
<p>95a.2</p>ba ri bo chen po bcom par 'gyur/ /snying po med cing nga med rnam par nyams pa'i chos/ /'jig rten gson pa'i 'jig rten kye ma smod par shog /gang du thub dka' drang srong chen po seng ge yang / /nyes pa'i gnyis 'thung rnams ni nyams par mdzad nas nyams/ /'dod chags bral ba
<p>95a.3</p>min pa'i 'gro ba 'jug pa la/ /da ni 'jigs pa chen po ma yin su yi lags/ /thun mong las ni gang du de bzhin gshegs pa yang / /gser gyi ka ba lta bu kun nas chag par gyur/ /sa bon drug dang myu gu gcig dang lo ma gcig /rtsa ba drug dang 'bras bu lnga dang yal ga gnyis/ /
<p>95a.4</p>phung po gsum dang bdag nyid gcig la nyon mongs kyi/ /sdong po 'di ni bcag nas thub pa gnyis 'thung gzims/ /'gro rgyal mda' bzhin dgra bo rnams ni bcom nas su/ /chu med pa na rma bya bzhin du chags bral zhing / /mgyogs 'gro rta bzhin du ni rnam rgyal lam song ba/ /me bzhin
<p>95a.5</p>thub pa skye ba med cing zhi bar gyur/ /mtho ris dbang phyug rdo rje 'dzin pa mig 'phel na/ /rab tu tshim byed rgyun bzhin gsung rnams btang nas su/ /'od kyis nyam thag ba lang bzhin sar rnam brgyus nas/ /grags pas phyogs ni mngon par bkang nas bla ma gzims/ /snyan grags
<p>95a.6</p>ldan pa nyid dang 'od zer ldan pa ste/ /chu bo sin d+hu bzhin du gser skyug shugs ldan pa/ /rnam thos bu yi rdzu 'phrul mi skyong sder bcas pa/ /lam la bcug nas mi yi nyi ma nub par gyur/ /rmug pa'i do shal gyi ni phyogs rnams dkris pa bzhin/ /rgya chen sprin rnams kyis dkris nyi ma'i 'od
<p>95a.7</p>rnams bzhin/ /mchod sbyin rdzogs tshe mar gyis sman pa'i me bzhin du/ /thub pa zhi tshe de ring 'jig rten gsal ma gyur/ /mdud pa med pa bden pa'i lam ni bsnyen nas su/ /mdud pa med pa zhi ba'i chos 'di brnyes nas ni/ /rdzu 'phrul gyis ni sku lus 'dren par nus na yang / /sdug bsngal
<p>95b</p>
<p>95b.1</p>dag gi gter ni lus yin zhes spangs so/ /mun pa mun pa nyi mas bzhin du zil mnan nas/ /rdul ni rdul ni char pa bzhin du mngon bcom nas/ /slar yang slar yang sdug bsngal 'khrul 'khor mi len te/ /thub pa thub pa skar rgyal bzhin du mngon par gshegs/ /gang zhig skye ba'i
<p>95b.2</p>sdug bsngal 'joms phyir skyes pa ste/ /gang la 'jig rten pas ni zhi ba'i ched du bsnyen/ /gang zhig 'od zer mchog gis rnam par gsal ba dang / /khyad par 'phags pa'i blo yis rnam par gsal bar gyur/ /gang gis skye dgu rnams ni dge legs la bcug ste/ /yon tan rgya chen rnams kyis sa
<p>95b.3</p>la rgyas pa nyid/ /'dod pa'i snyan grags gsal ba rnams kyis 'phel ba ste/ /khyim na gnas pa yin kyang grags pas 'phel ba nyid/ /gang gis mkhyen zhing smod pas 'o dod ma bos shing / /mi ni nyam thag rnams la brtse bas bos pa ste/ /bza' ba ngan pa rab tu 'joms shing ma gsol la/ /bza'
<p>95b.4</p>ba legs pa rjes su 'gro zhing ma gsol to/ /mi gnas dbang po zhi ba gang zhig yul rnams la/ /stobs rab dbang po nyid las yang dag mi gnas shing / /gzhan rnams kyis ma thob pa'i lam bzangs thob pa ste/ /ro mkhyen pas ni nges par 'byung ba'i ro gsol to/ /
<p>95b.5</p>gang gis sngar ma byin pa'i sbyin pa byin pa ste/ /'bras bu 'dod pas cung zad zhig ni mi byin la/ /mnyam nyid rjes mthun phun sum tshogs pa dor ba ste/ /dam pa rnams kyi yid rnams yon tan rnams kyis phrogs/ /brtan pa rnams kyi g.yo ba'i spyan ni bsrungs pa ste/ /
<p>95b.6</p>brtan par gshegs shing sems ni bsrung du bcug gyur la/ /dge legs rnams ni bsrungs shing 'phel bar mdzad pa ste/ /chos skyes pa ni cung zhig 'dod par ma mdzad do/ /brtan pas mi dge ba las mi dge rnam spangs nas/ /dge legs kyi ni dgra bo skyon rnams spangs pa
<p>95b.7</p>ste/ /gang zhig blo yis nyes pa rnams ni kun spangs la/ /de ni 'phags min mi rtag nyid kyis nub par gyur/ /gang la chos ni 'dod pa yang dag rjes song zhing / /dga' bas mchog tu nges pa rnam par bzung ba ste/ /me yis nor ni zos pa ji lta ba bzhin du/ /khyab bdag ye
<p>96a</p>
<p>96a.1</p>shes nor can de yang srog song ngo / /brgyad po rnams la mchog tu sde [(]tshen [,]tshan [)]lnga thul zhing / /gsum gzigs spyod pa gsum ni zad byed spyan gsum pa/ /gcig ni bsrungs nas gcig ni thob nas gcig rtogs nas/ /lci ba bdun rnams spangs nas
<p>96a.2</p>bla ma gzims par gyur/ /gang gi zhi ba'i ched du lam ni gsal mdzad de/ /legs pa'i skye bo zhi bas rab tu dang mdzad cing / /nyon mongs ljon shing rab tu chags pa bcad pa ste/ /srid pa rnams las gus pa ldan pa rnams bsgral to/ /gsung gi bdud rtsis 'jig rten shin tu tshim
<p>96a.3</p>mdzad cing / /bzod pa yis ni khro ba yongs su bzung ba ste/ /slob ma'i sde ni dge legs la ni rol mdzad la/ /dge legs don du gnyer rnams phra mo rtogs su bcug /legs pa rnams la chos kyi sa bon skyed mdzad cing / /rgyu yi bdag nyid 'phags pa'i lam ni thob mdzad la/ /
<p>96a.4</p>'jig rten 'das pas 'phags pa min pa ma brten zhing / /chos las ma gtogs gzhan la sbyar ba ma yin no/ /kA shi gnas su chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba ste/ /blo dang ldan pa nyid kyis 'jig rten tshim mdzad cing / /gdul bya rnams ni chos kyi cho gar spyad mdzad la/ /bdag cag
<p>96a.5</p>rnams la phan pa'i ched du dge bar mdzad/ /gzhan rnams kyis ma mthong ba'i de nyid mthong mdzad cing / /yon tan rnams kyis chos byed rnams la sbyar ba ste/ /gzhan gyi lugs rnams tshar bcad nas ni skul gyur la/ /rtogs par dka' ba'i don ni rnam par shes par mdzad/ /
<p>96a.6</p>thams cad mi rtag pa dang bdag med par gsungs shing / /srid pa rnams su bde ba cung zad ma bsrungs la/ /snyan pa'i ba dan gyen du rnam par bsgrengs pa ste/ /nga rgyal ka ba mthon po rnam par bsgyel ba mdzad/ /smad kyang rang gi thugs ni bskyod pa ma yin zhing / /thams cad
<p>96a.7</p>la ni 'jug pa rnams la sred ma mdzad/ /rang nyid rgal zhing bying ba bsgral bar mdzad pa ste/ /zhi zhing pha rol 'khrul pa zhi bar mdzad gyur la/ /grol zhing pha rol bcings pa grol bar mdzad pa ste/ /rtogs shing pha rol rmongs pas rtogs par mdzad pa'o/ /thub pa thub pas tshul dang
<p>96b</p>
<p>96b.1</p>tshul min mkhyen 'di des/ /sems can rnams ni yang dag gtam gyis rjes bzung nas/ /tshul min la dga' tshul min 'byung po rnams la ni/ /bskal pa 'jig pa'i tshe na chos bzhin rab tu gzims/ /chu ldan sprin bzhin sa 'dzin ri bo nags tshal bzhin/ /'od ldan rgan po
<p>96b.2</p>bzhin du 'od ldan gzhon nu bzhin/ /'jig rten dag gi lta byed bcom nas 'jig rten gyi/ /lta byed nye bar phrogs nas 'gros su 'di gshegs so/ /dbang phyug dam pa gang la ltung bas me reg cing / /gang gis mchog tu zhi ba'i lam ni brnyes pa ste/ /zhi ba brnyes pa de ni gus
<p>96b.3</p>pas mthong nas su/ /de ring 'jig rten gnyen 'dun med cing rgud pa 'dra/ /'joms par 'dod cing stobs ni rab zhugs bdud kyang ni/ /sde dang bcas pas gang ni thub par ma nus pa/ /'joms par 'dod cing stobs zhugs bdud kyis de ring ni/ /de ni dus kyi sbyor las 'joms
<p>96b.4</p>par nus par gyur/ /'byung po rnams ni thams cad rnams ni 'dus pa rnams/ /sdug bsngal rnams kyis zil non lha dang bcas pa rnams/ /'khor ba'i 'jigs pa gang rnams zad pa ma yin zhing / /de ltar mchog tu mya ngan 'das pa thob ma yin/ /skye dgu rnams kyi snang mdzad
<p>96b.5</p>gang gis 'jig rten ni/ /nye bar skye ba me long bzhin du gzigs pa ste/ /rgyang ring du'am nye bar mtho ris su'am mthar/ /lha yi rna bas sgra ni rnam par thos pa'o/ /bar snang dag la skar ma'i khang par 'dzegs pa ste/ /sa la rab tu zhugs kyang theg pa ma yin zhing / /chu la rab
<p>96b.6</p>tu gshegs kyang nub pa ma yin la/ /sku yis rnam par 'gyur ba mang po rnams mdzad do/ /de rnams de rnams gnas rnams lam 'gros lam na bzhin/ /gang gis skye ba du ma rnams kyang dran pa ste/ /yid kyis pha rol rnams kyi yid kyi spyod pa rnams/ /dbang po las 'das sna
<p>96b.7</p>tshogs rnams kyang mkhyen ba'o/ /thams cad mnyam par rab zhugs thams cad mkhyen pa des/ /zag pa thams cad bcad cing bya ba thams cad mdzad/ /ye shes kyis ni nyon mongs thams cad rnam spangs nas/ /ye shes de nyid kun nas brnyes nas gzims par gyur/ /skyes bu
<p>97a</p>
<p>97a.1</p>rnams kyi rno ba'i sems rnams btul ba ste/ /rno ba ma yin blo rnams rim gyis drag par mdzad/ /rigs las chos kyi nyes pa spang bar mdzad pa ste/ /'chi med ched du chos ni su yis ston par 'gyur/ /rten dang bral ba'i 'jig rten nyam thag pa la
<p>97a.2</p>ni/ /zhi ba'i ched du chos kyi 'thor ma su yis ster/ /thugs rje'i bdag nyid ldan la rang gi don mdzad nas/ /gzhan gyi nyon mongs dra ba su yis 'byed par 'gyur/ /'khor ba'i rgya mtshor gzhol ba'i 'jig rten dag gi ni/ /zhi ba'i ched du ye shes dam pa su yis smra/ /shes
<p>97a.3</p>pa med par gzhol ba'i 'jig rten dag gi ni/ /dge ba'i ched du ye shes dam pa su yis smra/ /ji ltar nyin mor byed pa 'od zer med pa dang / /ji ltar chu bo sin d+hu 'bab pa med pa dang / /sa bdag rgyal srid dang ni rnam par bral ba'am/ /de phyir 'jig rten 'jig rten mkhyen
<p>97a.4</p>pas rnam par dman/ /blo yis rig pa bzhin du bde bas dbyangs bzhin du/ /dpal gyis mi skyong bzhin du bzod pas chos bzhin du/ /de bzhin skyes bu mchog gis rnam par dman pa ni/ /'gro ba de ni yod pa dang ni med pa nyid/ /ji ltar kha lo sgyur bas shing rta dor ba
<p>97a.5</p>dang / /skya ba 'dzin pas gru dang tshul gyis sde dang ni/ /tshong dpon gyis ni tshong pa sman pas nad pa ste/ /de bzhin 'jig rten bde bar gshegs pas rnam par sman/ /dbyar tha dang ni ston rar mkha' la sprin med na/ /rlung gis kyang ni mkha' la bsnyen pa med pa na/ /'tsho bar
<p>97a.6</p>'dod pa rnams kyi sdug bsngal ji lta ba/ /de ltar thar 'dod rnams kyi nga ni nyam thag 'di/ /de ltar dam pa'i don mdzad dgra bcom yin na yang / /byed pa shes pa nyid kyis bla ma la zhugs pa/ /de ni chags bral yin kyang srid pa'i skyon rnams dang / /ston pa'i yon tan rnams
<p>97a.7</p>ni mang po rnams smras so/ /de nas chags bral min rnams mchi ma 'thon pa ste/ /brtan pa btang nas dge slong tshogs ni mya ngan dang / /'jig rten 'god pa'i bdag nyid can zhes byar bzung nas/ /bya ba'i 'khor lo rnams ni brtan las ma g.yos so/ /de nas dus kyi dbang gis
<p>97b</p>
<p>97b.1</p>gyad rnams kyis thos nas/ /gus pa'i dbang gis skyen par 'thon zhing song ba ste/ /khra yi stobs kyis zil mnan khrung khrung rnams bzhin du/ /kyi hud 'o brgyal zhes ni nyam thag 'thon pa'o/ /mun pa rab tu rgyas phyir thub pa rab gzims pa/ /nyi ma 'od med bzhin du de
<p>97b.2</p>rnams kyis mthong nas/ /seng ges khyu mchog rmugs tsha ba lang rnams bzhin du/ /gus pas drag tu cho nges btab cing ngus pa'o/ /chos dga' chos kyi bla ma rab tu zhi ba na/ /gus pas ji lta ba dang bsam pa ji lta bar/ /'o dod 'bod cing mchi mas mig bcom de
<p>97b.3</p>rnams kyi/ /dpal ldan dam pa 'ga' zhig 'di ni smras pa'o/ /gang zhig gson pa'i 'jig rten gnyid tshe rab sad pa/ /'di de mthar thug gzims mal la ni gzims pa ste/ /chos ni rnam par 'dzin pa'i rgyal mtshan 'di de ni/ /mchod sbyin mtha' na dbang po'i rgyal
<p>97b.4</p>mtshan bzhin du btul/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i nyi ma nges par blo gsal zhing / /brtson 'grus tshad gdung ye shes 'od zer stong ldan pa/ /nub par gyur tshe mi shes mun pa rnams bcom nas/ /'jig rten dag na slar yang mun pa 'di mdzad do/ /'das dang ma 'ongs
<p>97b.5</p>pa dang da ltar gzigs nas su/ /da ni nges par 'jig rten mig ni sgrib pa ste/ /sdug bsngal rgya mtsho chen po rgod pa'i dba' rlabs las/ /'dren mdzad zam pa 'di ni nges par de ni rgud/ /de ltar 'di na kha cig snying rje bar zlos shing / /gzhan rnams shing rta'i rta rnams dud
<p>97b.6</p>pa bzhin du sems/ /gzhan rnams skad bton gzhan rnams sa la 'gyel ba ste/ /bya ba de rnams de rnams sems can dbang gis byas/ /de nas dus su gser gyis spras shing sna tshogs pa/ /mche ba rin thang chen po longs ma spyad pa'i khyogs/ /gyad rnams ngu bzhin
<p>97b.7</p>drang srong la ni glang chen gyi/ /lag pa dang mtshungs lag pa rnams ni btsugs pa'o/ /de nas dus dang mthun pa'i cho ga byas nas su/ /de la phreng ba yid 'ong rnam pa sna tshogs dang / /dri mchog dam pa rnams kyis de rnams kyis mchod cing / /de nas dga' dang gus pas
<p>98a</p>
<p>98a.1</p>mtha' dag bzung ba'o/ /de nas shing gzhon lus can gzhon nu ma rnams kyis/ /gdu bu rab 'khrol zangs mdog lag pa rnams kyis ni/ /glog gi 'phan rnams dag gis sprin ni dkar po bzhin/ /'di la rin thang mchog gi bla re bzung ba'o/ /de bzhin
<p>98a.2</p>mi rnams kha cig dag gis gdugs rnams ni/ /phreng ba dkar po ldan rnams kun nas bzung ba ste/ /kha cig dag gis gser gyi yo byad dang ldan pa'i/ /rnga yab dkar po rnams ni rnam par g.yabs pa'o/ /de nas khyu mchog rnams kyis bzhin du ngal ba yis/ /mig
<p>98a.3</p>dmar gyad rnams dag gis khyogs ni bzung ba ste/ /sil snyan rnams ni rna ba'i yid du 'ong ba rnams/ /dbyar dus chu gter bzhin du mkha' la rab tu grags/ /phyogs kyi glang po'i dbang po rnams kyi bskul ba yis/ /mdzes pa dang ni rtsub 'gyur shing rnams las bzhin du/ /me tog
<p>98a.4</p>pad+ma la sogs de rnams de rnams ni/ /lha yi me tog rnams ni lha nas lhung bar gyur/ /dbang po'i glang po las skyes glang po che rnams kyis/ /nor gnas snying po'i chu skyes pad+ma rnams dang ni/ /man dA ra yi me tog 'dab bcas chags pa rnams/ /chu thigs zer mas 'thor
<p>98a.5</p>ba rnams kyis mngon bar 'thor/ /de nas dga' ba'i tshal skyes lus mchog ldan pa yi/ /tsan+dan dmar po'i ro ni rnam par dul ba dang / /'bad pas ma bsgrubs bgo ba rnams ni dkar po rnams/ /dri za'i bu mo rnams kyis yang dag 'thor ba'o/ /rab tu g.yo ba'i ba dan rnams ni
<p>98a.6</p>bzung ba ste/ /phreng ba rnam pa sna tshogs rnams kyis bkram pa ste/ /sil snyan rgya chen rnams kyis rjes su 'gro ba ste/ /zhi ba'i ched du zhi ba'i lam las khyogs te drangs/ /gus pa dang ldan gyad rnams kyis de yongs bzung nas/ /thub pa'i mthu las lan brgyar mngon
<p>98a.7</p>par phyag 'tshal zhing / /de yi rnam par nyams las kun nas ngu ba ste/ /grong khyer gyi ni dbus nas yongs su drangs pa'o/ /klu yi sgo nas zhugs te phyi rol byung nas ni/ /chu bo gser ldan zhes pa yang dag rgal nas su/ /cod pan zhes bya'i mchod rten gyi ni rtsa ba ru/ /grags
<p>98b</p>
<p>98b.1</p>pas bsags phyir bsags pa de rnams kyis byas so/ /de nas shun pa 'dab ma dri bzangs a ka ru/ /tsan+dan e la klu rnams kyis bsags bsags pa ru/ /mya ngan las ni sbrul bzhin dbugs rgyu de rnams ni/ /brtan min mig can rnams kyis thub pa'i sku bzhus so/ /
<p>98b.2</p>de nas lan gsum bkod kyang me yi sgron ma yis/ /de tshe drang srong chen po'i bsags pa ma 'bar te/ /bag med ldan pa gzhu ni rnam par 'khrugs pa yis/ /mda' ni rang bzhin sa yi bdag po'i dpal bzhin no/ /lam dag tu ni rnam par 'ong ba'i 'od srungs ni/ /rnam
<p>98b.3</p>par dag pa'i sems kyis sems ni gyur pa ste/ /bcom ldan 'das kyi sku gdung tshang ba lta 'dod de/ /gang gi mthu las me yi 'bar ba ma yin no/ /de nas de tshe bla ma blta ba'i don du ni/ /der ni dge slong skyen par nye bar song ba na/ /thub pa mchog la rab tu btud pa byas pa na/ /
<p>98b.4</p>de ma thag tu me ni rang nyid 'bar bar gyur/ /nyon mongs rnams kyis ma tshig thub pa'i sku gdung la/ /pags pa sha dang spu dang cha shas rnams tshig nas/ /mar dang rlung dang bud shing yongs su rgyas na yang / /me yis rus pa tshig par nus pa ma yin no/ /de nas bdag nyid chen
<p>98b.5</p>po 'das pa'i de rnams ni/ /chu mchog gis ni dang bar byas nas dus su ni/ /mngon par bstod cing gyad rnams dag gis grong khyer du/ /gser gyi bum pa rnams kyis rab tu spyan drangs so/ /'di ni ri bo chen po'i rin chen khams bzhin no/ /dge legs gang ba chen po rnams ni
<p>98b.6</p>'dzin pa ste/ /mtho ris dag na lha yi gtso bo'i khams bzhin du/ /khams ni me yis log par sbyor ba ma yin nyid/ /byams pas yongs su rnam par bsgoms pa 'di rnams ni/ /'dod chags me yis tshig pas rnam par spangs pa ste/ /de yi gus pa'i dbang gis gzung
<p>98b.7</p>ba'i gdung rus rnams/ /bsil ba yin kyang bdag cag rnams kyi yid rnams bsregs/ /sred pa 'joms mdzad gang gi mthu las khyab 'jug gi /mkha' lding gis kyang khur bar nus pa ma yin pa/ /'jig rten dag na mtshungs med de yi rus pa rnams/ /mi rus gyur
<p>99a</p>
<p>99a.1</p>pa kho bo cag gis khur bar gyis/ /e ma 'jig rten chos ni nges par stobs ldan te/ /chos la nus kyang nus pas gang gis ma bzlog cing / /gang zhig snyan pas 'gro ba mtha' dag khyab pa ste/ /de yi sku yi cha shas 'di ni bum par gnas/ /gang zhig bdag gi snang bas nyi ma gzhan snang zhing / /de yi
<p>99a.2</p>sa ni snang bas rnam par mdzad pa ste/ /gser gyi mdog dang ldan pa de yi sku lus ni/ /me rnams kyis ni rus pa lhag mar byas pa'o/ /gang gis nyon mongs ri bo rgyas pa rnams phye ste/ /sdug bsngal thob pa na yang bstan pa ma phye zhing / /sdug bsngal mtha' dag rnams ni bkag par gyur pa ste/ /drang srong de yi sku lus
<p>99a.3</p>me yis bsregs pa'o/ /g.yul du dgra bo rnams kyis mchi ma phyung nas su/ /skyabs 'ongs rnams kyi mchi ma rnam par btul nas su/ /sdug pa na yang mchi ma bstan pas ma bton pa/ /lam du mchi ma 'thon zhing de rnams rnam par zlos/ /de rnams nga rgyal ldan zhing lag pa stobs dang ldan na yang / /de ltar
<p>99a.4</p>mya ngan byed cing nags bzhin grong khyer der zhugs shing / /lam rnams su ni gdung de rnams ni skye bos mchod pa ste/ /mchod pa'i don du gzhal yas khang par mdzes par byas pa'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las/ /mya ngan las 'da' ba bsngags pa'i le'u ste nyi shu rtsa bdun pa'o// //
<p>99a.5</p>ji lta ba bzhin nyin zhag 'ga' zhig de rnams kyis/ /de rnams mchod pa dam pa rnams kyis mchod pa ste/ /chab 'og rgyal phran pho nya bdun rnams rim gyis ni/ /de yi ched du grong khyer der ni nye bar 'ongs/ /de nas de'i tshe gang rnams thos nas dus su ni/ /nga rgyal las dang de yi gus pa'i dbang las ni/ /
<p>99a.6</p>gyad rnams 'thab mo la yang nges par song ba ste/ /sbyin pa la ni yid rnams byas pa ma yin no/ /de nas de dag rnams kyis rnam gzhag 'di rtogs nas/ /rlung bdun bzhin du mi dbang bdun po de rnams ni/ /gyen du zhugs pa'i gang gA'i shugs 'dra stobs tshogs ni/ /shin tu drag po rnams kyis ku sha
<p>99a.7</p>zhes byar 'ongs/ /de nas grong ba'i skye bo nags mtha' nas skyen par/ /mi skyong de dag rnams kyi mgyogs 'gro'i sgra yis ni/ /khros pa las ni mgo bo rnams la bzung ba bzhin/ /'jigs pas rgyas pa'i gdong rnams grong khyer la zhugs so/ /de nas mi skyong de rnams grong khyer de bkag nas/ /glang
<p>99b</p>
<p>99b.1</p>po'i dbang po rnams bcings rtsed mo'i nags rnams su/ /gyad mchog rnams kyis mi mthun spyad du gyur pa rnams/ /rigs kyi rjes mthun cha lugs ldan rnams la gsos so/ /de nas mda' yab mdzes shing ring pa'i smin ma de/ /sgo yi mig ni rnam par btsums shing grong khyer de/ /mi dga' ba dang 'dus pa'i yan
<p>99b.2</p>lag ma bzhin du/ /dpung pa'i khyogs ni bteg pa nyam thag par gyur to/ /rgyal po bdun po rnams ni bya ba gcig pa ste/ /dpal gyis 'bar zhing shugs kyis 'phro ba rnams kyis ni/ /mnyam du dus gcig la ni gza' bdun rnams kyi ni/ /'jigs pa dang bcas nam mkha' bzhin du sa gyur to/ /
<p>99b.3</p>sna rnams gnyis 'thung myos pa'i chang dri rnams kyis dang / /mig rnams dpung gis bsnun pa'i rdul rnams dag gis dang / /rna ba rnams ni rta glang rnga yi dbyangs rnams kyis/ /mi mo'i skye bo yi yang der ni bcom par gyur/ /de nas skyogs rnams nang du khu ba 'bab pa ni/ /mdun du bdar rnams bsdogs byas
<p>99b.4</p>rta pa'i tshogs rnams dang / /glang po rnams kyis yongs bskor sgo ni phyed bkag ste/ /'gegs shing g.yul la phyogs rnams kyis byas so/ /de nas shag ti ral gri mda' lag grong khyer pa/ /skrag pas da ni dpa' bas ngo tsha btang ba rnams/ /khra rnams bzhin du dgra bo rnams la lta bzhin du/ /nye ba'i 'thab ra rnams su kun
<p>99b.5</p>nas gnas pa'o/ /brtan min ldan pa kha cig 'o dod 'bod pa ste/ /de bzhin gzhan rnams tshogs nas dung ni rab tu sgrogs/ /drag tu dregs rnams kha cig rab tu 'phen pa ste/ /de bzhin gzhan rnams ral gri sngon po rnams 'debs so/ /de nas rgyal ba'i ched du gyad rnams 'thab 'dod cing / /gyad rnams bzhin du mtshan rnams sgrogs
<p>99b.6</p>pa mthong nas ni/ /g.yul 'gyed yan lag ma rnams dag gi sems rnams dang / /sman rnams dang mnyam mchod yon rnams ni g.yos par gyur/ /g.yul der thog mar 'gro bar 'dod pa'i bu la ni/ /yul 'gyed yan lag ma rnams der ni yongs 'dar zhing / /go cha bcings nas zhi ba'i shes pa byed pa ste/ /sems khral gdong
<p>99b.7</p>rnams mchi ma bton pa ma yin no/ /sems khral gdong las gzhan rnams ri dwags mo bzhin du/ /khyim thab 'gro bar 'dod pa'i gzhu la 'phyangs pa ste/ /gang gi gdong ni 'thab la dpa' ba de mthong nas/ /bcings pa'i 'phro spong song ba ma yin gnas ma yin/ /bum pa'i nang du yang dag bkag pa'i sbrul rnams bzhin/ /stobs
<p>100a</p>
<p>100a.1</p>kyis de ltar rab tu 'phro ba de rnams ni/ /de ltar rnam par gzhag pa'i gyad rnams mthong nas ni/ /mi dbang rnams kyis g.yul gyi ched du blo bsams so/ /shing rta glang po rta dang rkang thang dregs pa ni/ /g.yul la kun nas nye bar gzhol ba mthong nas ni/ /
<p>100a.2</p>mkhas pa nyid kyis dang ni mdza' bo nyid kyis ni/ /gnyis skyes bre bos tshig ni 'di skad ces smras so/ /g.yul du dgra bo rnams kyi srog dang dregs pa ni/ /khyed cag rnams kyi mda' yis 'joms par nus pa ste/ /rdzod pa tha dad gnas rnams bde bar
<p>100a.3</p>mi nus na/ /pha rol bya ba gcig pa rnams ni smos ci dgos/ /ci ste kun nas bkag pas pha rol 'joms pa la/ /blo ni byas rnams de ni rnam par zlog mdzod dang / /nyes pa med pa'i grong pa'i skye bo 'gegs pa yi/ /gtse bar byed pa de ni chos ni ci zhig yin/ /dong du zhugs
<p>100a.4</p>pa'i nag po'i sbrul rnams bgrod pa ni/ /gcig la gnas pa rnams kyis dus su rmugs pa bzhin/ /bkag nas rgyal ba mtha' gcig yod pa ma yin zhing / /brgya la bkag pa rnams kyis rgyal ba 'thob par 'gyur/ /grong gi nang du bkag pa'i gtad rnams
<p>100a.5</p>zhugs pa rnams/ /yid dang ldan pa nyid las mi rnams kyis thos nas/ /bsreg bya rnams kyis 'thor ba'i chung ngu'i me bzhin du/ /gzi brjid dman kyang legs pa chen por 'gro bar 'gyur/ /chos kyi bdag nyid can rnams grong du bkag na yang / /'joms 'dod
<p>100a.6</p>thob pa rnams ni dka' thub [(]gyis [,]kyis [)]gtor te/ /dpung ni zad par gyur kyang kA sha'i grong khyer du/ /lag pa sgra byed chos kyi stobs las rnam par rgyal/ /snyan grags ched dam yul ni 'thob pa'i ched du sa/ /mtha' dag gang rnams kyis kyang mngon par thob pa ste/ /ba lang
<p>100a.7</p>rnams kyis chu gnas nas chu 'thungs nas bzhin/ /bor nas nor 'dzin bdag po de rnams sa la song / /de phyir chos dang don ni yang dag mthong nas su/ /khyed cag rnams kyis zhi bas 'bad pa mdzod cig dang / /mda' yis 'pham pa rnams ni slar yang 'bar ba ste/ zhi bas
<p>100b</p>
<p>100b.1</p>'pham pa rnams kyi rnam 'gyur yod ma yin/ /'di kun khyed cag rnams kyi tshad ma ma yin te/ /khyed kyi stobs kyi dgra yi stobs las 'gro bar nus/ /shAkya thub pa gang la mchod par blo yod na/ /de nyid kyi ni gsung la bzod pas bsnyen mdzod cig /de skad ces sogs 'dod pa
<p>100b.2</p>rnam par nges pa ni/ /bram ze'i drang pos dang ni rab tu dga' ba yis/ /rgyal po yin yang rjes su bstan nas legs pa des/ /dge legs smras shing de nas de rnams kyis smras so/ /dus dang sbyar te mkhas shing phan la bshes kyis ni/ /tshig gang 'di de khyed kyis rnam par smras pa ste/ /
<p>100b.3</p>chos la dga' ba nyid dang stobs la brten pa las/ /rgyal po rnams kyis bsam pa nges par shes par mdzod/ /'dod pa'i phyir dang khro phyir stobs phyir 'chi ba'i phyir/ /phal che bar ni bya bar song zhing 'gro ba ste/ /mngon pa'i nga rgyal dang bcas kho bo cag rnams kyis/ /sangs rgyas nyid la
<p>100b.4</p>mchod pa la ni gzhu rnams bzung / /nga rgyal don du mchod yon blangs la rtsod pa ni/ /byis pa skyong dang drag po dag gis khyab 'jug byung / /nga rgyal spang phyir mchod pa'i don du nged rnams kyis/ /tshe rnams dag kyang 'dor bar mi bgyi gang las yin/ /bu mo la ni sa skyong dag gi rgyal
<p>100b.5</p>po rnams/ /gtum po long byed rnams ni rtsod par song ba ste/ /'dod pa 'joms phyir mchod pa'i don du nged rnams kyis/ /tshe rnams dag kyang 'dor bar mi bgyid gang las yin/ /rgyal rigs zad phyir drang srong drag tu khros pa ni/ /ngan spong bu yis g.yul du mtshon rnams bzung
<p>100b.6</p>ba ste/ /khro ba 'joms phyir mchod pa'i don du nged rnams kyis/ /tshe rnams dag kyang 'dor bar mi bgyid gang las yin/ /lha mo sI tar mngon brjod 'chi ba yongs bzung nas/ /srin po shin tu dregs pa yang ni nyams pa ste/ /yongs 'dzin spong phyir mchod pa don du nged rnams
<p>100b.7</p>kyis/ /tshe rnams dag kyang 'dor bar mi bgyid gang las yin/ /e Di lam ni pa ka zhes ni dgra 'phel zhing / /rgyal rigs bye ba rnams ni de ltar nyams pa ste/ /rmongs mun gtor phyir mchod pa'i don du nged rnams kyis/ /tshe rnams dag kyang 'dor bar mi bgyid gang las yin/ /
<p>101a</p>
<p>101a.1</p>de skad ces sogs 'jig rten dag na 'thab mo ni/ /skyon las skyes pa mang po rnams ni byung gyur te/ /ston pa bla na med pa'i gus pas mchi ba dang / /bcas pa yin kyang 'thab mo mi bgyid gang las yin/ /de lta na yang bdag cag rnams kyi nges pa 'di/ /
<p>101a.2</p>khyed kyi pho nyar gyur cig skyen par gshegs mdzod la/ /ji ltar don ni 'thab mo min pas 'grub pa cig /de ltar bdag nyid kun gyis 'bad pa gyis mdzod cig /khyed kyis chos ldan tshig rnams kyis ni nged cag rnams/ /'thab par 'dod cing mda' yi mche ba rnon po can/ /
<p>101a.3</p>nang du rab tu 'phel ba'i dug ni 'thungs pa rnams/ /sngags rnams kyis ni sbrul rnams bzhin du bkag pa'o/ /de ltar bgyi zhes rgyal po rnams kyi tshig bzung nas/ /bram ze de ni grong khyer de la rab zhugs shing / /ji ltar rim gyis gyad rnams dag ni mthong ba ste/ /mthong nas
<p>101a.4</p>dus su tshig ni 'di skad ces smras so/ /gzhu rnams lag na gnas pa'i mi dbang 'di rnams ni/ /nyi ltar byi dor go cha 'bar rnams kyis/ /khyed cag rnams kyis grong 'dir nges par ro myang zhing / /seng ge bzhin du rnam par 'gying zhing gnas pa'o/ /de rnams kyi ni shubs su bkod
<p>101a.5</p>pa'i ral gri dang / /gser gyi rgyab ldan gzhu rnams nges par rtogs pa ste/ /grub pa'i chos dran nas ni chos min gyis 'jigs shing / /zhu ba gsol bar byed de g.yul la 'jigs rnams min/ /de rnams mngon par 'ongs rnams sa yi phyir min zhing / /nor phyir ma yin
<p>101a.6</p>rgyags phyir ma yin dgra phyir min/ /thub pa'i gus pas nged cag rnams kyi zhe sa 'di/ /de phyir khyed cag rnams kyi bya bas bkur sti mdzad/ /thub pa de la khyed cag gi dang nged cag gi /bla ma nyid du mnyam ste 'di las ngal ba 'di/ /de phyir spun gyi tshogs ni 'dus nas
