<p>161b.7</p>phyir mjug thogs nas 'byung ba smos te/ sna tshogs dang khyad par byed pa ste 'dod pas na brda sprod pa'o/ /yi ge'i phyi mo klog tu 'jug gi thams cad du brda sprod pa pa yin te/ rgyas par ni mi ston to/ /sdig pa dag las rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir te/ dper na dga' byed la sogs pa'i mdo las
<p>162a</p>
<p>162a.1</p>'byung ba lta bu'o/ /bsod nams 'grub bya'i phyir zhes bya ba ni/ 'phags pa sdong po bkod pa la sogs pa las 'byung ba lta bu'o/ /sngar bshad pa rnams bsod nams bsgrub pa ma yin nam ci zhe na/ sdig ba byed pa rnams ni de las zlog pa'i sgo nas so/ /bsod nams byed
<p>162a.2</p>pa rnams ni bsod nams kho na 'grub par bya ba'i phyir ro/ /gnyis brten pa ni nyan thos la sogs pa'i theg pa pa rnams la'o/ /gnyis mi brten pa ni theg pa chen po pa la'o/ /khu 'phrigs can de dmigs pa can rnams 'jigs pa ste 'jigs par byed pa'o/ /gang la snying po ste 'byung ba'i
<p>162a.3</p>gnas stob pa nyid dang snying rje'i bdag yod pa de la de skad ces bya'o/ /de lta bas na zhe 'gras pa rnams kyis de ltar bsams nas so/ /zhe ma 'gras pa ye shes mtha' yas pa 'dod pa gang dag yin pa de dag gis ni rab tu dang ba'o/ /thob pa ni rnyed pa'am rten pa'o/ /so sor thar pa ni 'dul ba mdor
<p>162a.4</p>bsdus pa de rgyas pa'o/ /'dul ba ni 'dul ba gzhi'o/ /mang du thos pa ni mdo la sogs pa'o/ /don gtan la dbab pa ni de dag nyid kyi'o/ /de dang zhes bya ba ni khro ba dang ngo / /sdig la zhen pa ni chags pa'o/ /khros bas bslad pa ni kun nas dkrugs pa'o/ /khyad bar 'phags pa dag dang
<p>162a.5</p>bdag nyid mnyam par ro/ /khyad 'phags ni mchog ste/ de bas kyang mchog go snyam pa la de skad ces bya'o/ /mchog pas kyang mchog go snyam pa de ji lta bu zhig ce na/ mjug thogs nas 'byung bas smos te/ 'bras kyi thog tu phol mig byung ba bzhin no/ /nye bar len zhes bya ba zag pa dang
<p>162a.6</p>bcas pa'i phung po rnams so/ /dgos pa med pa ni mi nus pa'o/ /tshig 'jam pa ni kha snyan pa'o/ /de sngar smra ba ni je smra ba'am/ gtsor byed pa'o/ /mtshan mas tha snyad 'dogs pa de la gnas pa na gzhogs slong byed pa'o/ /smod byed pa ni skyon brjod pa'o/ /rnyed pas rnyed pa 'dod pa
<p>162a.7</p>rnams zhes bya bar sbyar bar bya'o/ /zlos pa ni nyes pa yang dang yang du brjod pa'o/ /mgu ba ni rangs pa'o/ /de lta bu ma yin pas na de skad ces bya'o/ /slong ba ni sems so/ /yang na sbungs med pa ni 'di lta bu yin te/ chags pa ni zhen pa'o/ /de'i phyir sbungs med pa ni chags can gyi yid de/ /
<p>162b</p>
<p>162b.1</p>brtson 'grus med pa'i zhen pa yin no/ /tha dad pa nyid kyi 'du shes ni bdag dang gzhan no snyam pa ste/ des na thams cad du bdag ces bya ba'i don sgrub pa'o/ /lta ba med pa ni chags pa'am sdang ba'am rmongs pa zhig ces dpyod pa med pa'o/ /bkur sti dang ldan pa'i tshul ni bcom
<p>162b.2</p>ldan 'das kyi tshul yin te/ bcom ldan 'das rnams la bya ba dang 'dra bas so/ /yang na rab tu 'bad pa dang ldan pa'i tshul la de skad ces bya'o/ /lus dang ngag yon tan dang ldan pa ltar ston pa de ni tshul 'chos pa de sgrub pa yin no/ /dam pa rnams mgu ba ni chos shes pa
<p>162b.3</p>ste de nyid dpal yin no/ /rjes rnam rig ni phyis shes par 'dod pa'o/ /'dod pa ni re ba'o/ /brnyogs pa ni sems yongs su nyams pa'o/ /brtson pa med pa ni brtson 'grus med pa'o/ /sgyid lug pa ni bya ba rnams la sgrim pa med pa'o/ /lus 'gyur ba ni mi thub pa'o/ /'dod
<p>162b.4</p>pa ni dga' ba'o/ /de lta bu ma yin pas na mi 'dod pa'o/ /yon tan lnga dag la 'dod pa ni don du gnyer ba gang yin pa'o/ /gnod dogs zhes bya ba ni de sems par byed pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go/ /dgu ni 'dis bdag la zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o/ /rmya ba ni lus dang sems lci ba
<p>162b.5</p>nyid de/ lus las su mi rung ba nyid dang / sems las su mi rung ba nyid do/ /las bral ba ni bya ba med pa'o/ /gnyid ni sems mngon par sdud pa'o/ /'gyod pa ni yid mi bde ba'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ba ni khyim pas so/ /sdom brtson can gyis zhes bya ba ni rab tu
<p>162b.6</p>byung bas so/ /snying rje ro gcig pa ni sdug bsngal dang bral bar ro gcig pa'o/ /mdangs ni mdzes pa nyid do/ /dge bas zhes bya ba ni brtson 'grus kyi mtshan nyid kyis so/ /brjid pa ni sba ba ste zil gyis mi non pa nyid do/ /zhi ba ni nye bar zhi ba'o/ /ci'i phyir 'di kho na las rnam par gzhag ce
<p>162b.7</p>na/ mjug thogs nas 'byung ba smos te/ sa dang po la kun du sbyor ba gsum po rjes su chags pa dang / khong khro ba dang the tshom rnams spangs pa'i phyir ro/ /skyes phyir zhes bya ba ni 'khrungs pa'i phyir ro/ /ngang gis rang bzhin gyis dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam de dag la gnas pa'i phyir ro/ /
<p>163a</p>
<p>163a.1</p>'dod chags dang zhe sdang chen po dang 'bring yongs su zad pa'i phyir ro/ /bzod pa dang brtson 'grus lhag par spyod pa ni bzod pa dang brtson 'grus kyi mchog ces bya ba'i don to/ /dbang chen ni mang po'i dpon po ste lha'i tshogs chen po'i bdag po'o/ /'dod pa ni
<p>163a.2</p>gzugs la sogs pa'o/ /de dag la 'dod chags pa ni 'dod chags pa'o/ /zlog pa ni zlog par byed pa'o/ /gang la 'od 'phro ba yod pa de la ni de skad ces bya'o/ /sa dang po la gnas pa la sogs pa yang de dag sgom par byed pas khyad par du zhes bya ba smos so/ /'jig tshogs la lta ba
<p>163a.3</p>rab tu 'byung ba ni rgyu yin te/ 'di las rab tu 'byung bas na ma rig pa'o/ /de las ni ngar 'dzin pa rab tu 'byung ste/ ma rig pa bsrabs pa'i phyir de spong ngo / /kun nas 'joms pa ni drungs 'byin pa'o/ /chos bdag med pa'am rnam par thar pa la sogs pa gang la dang po 'phags pa'i
<p>163a.4</p>bden pa rnams yod pa ste de rnams shes pa'o/ /de la mkhas pa ni khong gzo ba ste de byung ba'i phyir ro/ /mu stegs byed pa thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa ni lus kyi gdung ba lnga la sogs pa'o/ /'dis thar ro snyam pa'i log par lta ba'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi chos thob par bya ba la mngon du
<p>163a.5</p>phyogs shing mthun pa'i phyir ro/ /zhi gnas ni ting nge 'dzin to/ /lhag mthong ni shes rab po/ /de dag goms pa yis zhes bya ba ni yang dang yang du mngon du byed pas so/ /'gog pa ni snyoms par 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid dam nyon mongs pa'i 'gog pa'o/ /de thob pas rgyas pa'i phyir ram/ 
<p>163a.6</p>yongs su dag pa'i phyir ram/ yongs su rgyas pa'i phyir ram/ gang la sprul pa bzang po yod pa de la de skad ces bya'o/ /mi 'phrogs pa ni zil gyis mi non pa'o/ /nga rgyal lhag pa ni lhag pa'i nga rgyal te/ de gang dag la yod ba de dag la de skad ces bya'o/ /de dag zhi bar byed pa
<p>163a.7</p>ni nye bar zhi bar byed pa'o/ /'di ni grangs kyang yin la ring du song ba yang yin pas na grangs ring du song ba ste/ de dang ldan zhing rjes su 'brel pa'i phyir ro/ /ring du song ba nyid kyi rgyu smos pa/ gang gi phyir sa 'di thob nas skad cig la 'gog pa la snyoms par 'jug pa de'i phyir sa de dus
<p>163b</p>
<p>163b.1</p>dang yon tan gyi grangs kyis ring du song ba'i phyir ro/ /'di skad du bshad pa yin te/ gang la grangs dang yon tan gyi sgo nas ring du song ba yod pa de ni 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa la dbang bar 'gyur gyi gzhan ni ma yin no/ /dbang sgyur ni nyon mongs pa rnams sam 'gog pa la'o/ /
<p>163b.2</p>de nyid kyi phyir 'di'i ming ni de kho na nyid do/ /byang chub sems dpa' mtshan dang rtsol ba'i rnam par rtog pa dag gis mi g.yo bas na mi g.yo ba ste/ de nyid mi g.yo ba zhes bya bas bstan to/ /ji ltar mi g.yo zhe na mi rtog pa'i phyir ro/ /mi g.yo ba ji lta ba de bzhin du lus dang ni zhes bya ba

<p>163b.4</p>pa la gzhon nu zhes bya ba ste/ nyon mongs pa rnams kyis ni byis par 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin du nar son pa la rgyal tshab ces bya ba dang 'dra bar 'dir yang chos kyi nar son pa la rgyal tshab ces bya'o/ /gang la blo gros sa 'og ma pa dag las khyad par du 'phags par bzang ba yod pa de
<p>163b.5</p>ni legs pa'i blo gros so/ /so so yang dag par rig pa ni don la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid gzhi'o/ /sprin zhes bya ba'i sgra ni mang po nyid nye bar mtshon pa'o/ /gang la de bzhin gshegs pa rnams las chos kyi sprin 'thob pa yod pa de la de skad ces bya'o/ /de nyid dam pa'i chos kyi
<p>163b.6</p>char zhes bya ba la sogs pas ston to/ /dbang phyug chen po ni ming ngo / /gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid kyi stobs bcu dang ngo / /stobs la sogs pa sangs rgyas rnams kyis tshad med pa nyid do/ /rgyu tshad med pa de lta bu la 'bras bu sna tshogs tshad

<p>164a</p>
<p>164a.1</p>thams cad yongs su bzung ba nyid ni bsod nams thams cad khas blang zhing yongs su gzung ba ste/ bya ba dang rjes su yi rang ba'i sgo nas bsod nams thams cad yongs su gzung ba yin no/ /gsol ba ni bkur sti dang ldan pas don du gnyer ba'o/ /ma bgyis
<p>164a.2</p>pa ni ma 'ongs pa'o/ /mi khom pa ni log par 'dzin pa la sogs pa brgyad do/ /de dag la 'das pa ni rgal ba'o/ /spyod pa rang dbang yod pa ni bcom ldan 'das rnams dang / de dag gi nyan thos zag pa zad pa rnams te/ nyon mongs pa dag gis ni gzhan dbang du 'gyur ro/ /ldan pa
<p>164a.3</p>ni ldan par 'gyur ba'o/ /skyes mchog ni sangs rgyas nyid de/ sems can thams cad pas mchog tu gyur pa'i phyir ro/ /yang na des ma bsdus pa skyes bu'i mchog gzhan no/ /rig pa ni yang dag pa'i lta ba'o/ /yan lag lhag ma rnams ni rkang pa'o/ /yang na rig pa ni lha'i

<p>164a.6</p>gyi mchog ni gtso bo'o/ /gang la byams pa ste 'jam zhing byams pa'i mtshan nyid yod pa la de skad ces bya'o/ /gang dag la sems rab tu dang ba ste/ dri ma med pa yod pa de dag ni rab dang do/ /de'i phyir 'khrug pa dang bral bas na 'khrug med do/ /rnal ma ni khral khrul med pa'o/ /ji ltar rab tu dang

<p>164b</p>
<p>164b.1</p>skad ces bya'o/ /srog ni gson pa ste de dang 'dra bar ro/ /de ni bcom ldan 'das kyis mdo gzhan dag las gsungs te/ sems yongs su sbyong ba'i phyir dang / bsod nams kyi tshogs bsags pa'i phyir zhes bya ba lhag ma yin no/ /khyim bdag dpas byin gyis zhus pa las ni
<p>164b.2</p>byang chub kyi sems kyi bsod nams yongs su bsgrags pa'i phyir ro/ /de bzhin du ting 'dzin rgyal po'i mdo las ni byams pa'i yon tan bstan pa'i phyir ro/ /'phags pa blo gros mi zad pa'i mdo las ni pha rol tu phyin pa bstan pa'i phyir ro/ /de ni chos kyi byed par 'gyur/ /gang
<p>164b.3</p>gi phyir chos kyis phan par 'gyur ba de'i phyir ji ltar khyod la bdag nyid phangs pa de bzhin du chos la yang gyis shig pa'o/ /ji ltar shes rab las 'dod pa thams cad 'byung ba de bzhin du mkhas ba rnams las kyang de 'byung ngo zhes mjug thogs nas 'byung bas ston to/ /gtsang ba ni dben zhing dri
<p>164b.4</p>ma med pa ste/ chags pa la sogs pa'i mi gtsang ba dang bral ba'i phyir ro/ /byams pa ni byams pa dang ldan pa'o/ /gang zhig de 'dra ba la dogs shing bag tsha ba skyed par byed pa'o/ /chog shes pa ni rnyed pas chog par 'dzin pa'o/ /snying rje ni pha rol sdug bsngal bas sdug bsngal bar
<p>164b.5</p>'gyur ro/ /tshul khrims ni spong ba bdun gyis bdag nyid dam/ sems can gyi don bya ba dang / dge ba chos sdud pa'i mtshan nyid do/ /shes rab ni mnyam par gzhag pa'i gnas skabs de de kho na nyid yongs su dpyod pa'o/ /gang gi phyir chos de dag sgom par byed pa ni rtag tu bag yod pa
<p>164b.6</p>yin pa de'i phyir de dag nyid ston pa'o zhes bya ba ste/ de dag gi rang bzhin mkhyen par bgyis nas rjes su mthun pa'i don sgrub par mdzod cig pa'o/ /'dod pa'i gnas thob par byed pas na lugs te/ rgyas pa dang mdor bsdus te ji skad bshad pa 'dis so/ /grub pa'i mchog ni sems
<p>164b.7</p>can rnams kyi nang na'am/ sems can rnams kyi nang du sangs rgyas nyid do/ /bden pa'i ngang tshul ni 'grogs na bde ba'am bde ba'i rang bzhin te/ bde ba skye ba'i rgyu yin pas na bde ba'o/ /bsnyen dka' ba ni brda phrad par dka' ba ste zab pa'i phyir ro/ /khyad du gsod pa ni gzhan dag
<p>165a</p>
<p>165a.1</p>la brnyas pa'o/ /de'i ched du byas pa'i gzhung gang yin pa de la yang de skad ces bya ste/ tshul dang ldan pa ni tshul shes pa yin gyi gzhan ni ma yin no zhes bya ba yin no/ /rang dbang ni shes rab rno ba'i phyir rang la dbang ba'o/ /la la byams kyang nyes pa smra ba smra
<p>165a.2</p>bas de'i phyir legs par smra ba zhes bya ba smos te/ legs par smra ba brjod pa'o/ /ci rigs par zhes bya ba ni rgyal po'i bya ba ma gtogs pa'o/ /phan par 'dod pas zhes bya ba ni phan par 'dod pa nyid kyis so/ /tshul khrims ni srung ba'am bsten par bya ba'o/ /phrag dog med
<p>165a.3</p>pa ni gzhan gyi phun sum tshogs pa la'o/ /dogs pa med pa ni dge ba dag la 'jigs pa med pa'o/ /gang la gzhan don gyi nor yod pa de la de skad ces bya'o/ /phongs par gyur pa ni nyam thag par gyur pa'o/ /yongs gzung ni kun nas gzung ba'o/ /dor ba ni gtong ba'o/ /
<p>165a.4</p>rin chen phreng ba'i tshig don rnams/ /bdag gis rnam par dbye byas nas/ /bsod nams cung zad gang bsgrubs des/ /'jig rten thams cad mkhyen par shog /rin po che'i phreng ba'i rgya cher bshad pa slob dpon mi pham bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //
<p>165a.5</p>rgya gar gyi mkhan po bid+yA ka ra pra b+hA dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ / @##/ /rgya gar skad du/ swap+na tsin+ta ma Ni pa ri ka thA/ bod skad du/ rmi lam yid bzhin nor bu'i gtam/ dkon
<p>165a.6</p>mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang zhig rtogs pa'i phyir na rmi lam mthar/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams las rigs rnyed de/ /phan phyir sems can dga' ba 'ga' zhig ni/ /skye dgu rnams la 'doms par byed pa yin/ /bdag dang sems can thams cad bde sdug
<p>165a.7</p>mtshungs/ /bde sdug mtshungs pa can ni gnyen yin na/ /bdag gis de dag rab tu spangs nas kyang / /mya ngan 'das par 'jug pa mi rigs so/ /skye bo 'di dag dang ni lhan cig tu/ /ngan song dag tu sdug bsngal drag po dang / /bde 'gro dag tu 'ang bde ba mang po myong / /
<p>165b</p>
<p>165b.1</p>gcig tu gnas pas bdag la 'di dag dga'/ /gang gi mngal du lan cig min par bdag /ma gnas pa'am bdag la gang ma gnas/ /sems can de na 'di ni gang yang med/ /de'i phyir thams cad gnyen du gyur pa yin/ /gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das la bdag dga'
<p>165b.2</p>ste/ /gang phyir 'di dag ched du bcom ldan 'das/ /shin tu yun ring bar ni skyo gyur na/ /des kyang bdag ni sems can rnams la dga'/ /'di ltar phan dang gnod pa byas pa las/ /bde ba dang ni sdug bsngal tshad med pa/ /gnyis ka'i rgyu ru 'gyur ba de phyir [(]yad [,]yang [)]/ /sems
<p>165b.3</p>can rnams ni bdag gi bla ma yin/ /'di nyid la ni gsod dang 'ching ba dang / /rdeg dang sdig sogs sdug bsngal myong ba gang / /de ni sems can 'tshe ba'i 'bras bu zhes/ /bde bar gshegs pa rnams kyis bka' stsal to/ /gzugs dang nad med dag gis gnod pa dang / / 
<p>165b.4</p>phongs dang rigs ngan tshe ni thung ba dang / /chung ma shi dang long bar gyur pa nyid/ /sems can gnod pa byas pa'i 'bras bu yin/ /mnar med pa yi bar gyi ngan song gi /gnas su sdug bsngal sna tshogs myong ba gang / /de dag thams cad rang nyid nyes pa yis/ /sems can rnams
<p>165b.5</p>la gnod pa byas pas yin/ /gang zhig 'di nyid la ni mchod byas mchod/ /grags dang yid 'ong nor rnams thob pa dag /yid 'ong yid du mi 'ong sems can la/ /mngon par phan dang 'tshe ba'i sgo nas so/ /nad med pa dang rigs ni phun sum tshogs/ /gzugs mdzes pa dang tshe ring
<p>165b.6</p>dbang phyug dang / /nor la sogs dang chung ma sbas pa ni/ /sems can phan pa byed pa'i 'bras bu yin/ /sems can rnams la dga' bar byed pa yis/ /rgyal srid rgyal srid che dang yang dag gi /rgyal srid 'khor los sgyur ba mchog nyid dang / /dbang po'i gnas ni 'thob par
<p>165b.7</p>'gyur ba yin/ /skyes bu sems can phan par byed pa yis/ /sangs rgyas go 'phang yang ni thob 'gyur na/ /gang zhig snying po med pa dman pa'i lha/ /thob pa 'di la ngo mtshar ci zhig yod/ /gal te sems can de dag med gyur na/ /'di ni gang gi ched du sbyin pa gtong / /gal te
<p>166a</p>
<p>166a.1</p>lus can rnams ni med gyur na/ /gang las 'dul ba'i tshul khrims thob par 'gyur/ /nyes pa byed pa yang ni gang zhig yin/ /gang gi ched du dpa' bo bzod pa sgom / /gang zhig mngon par 'dod pa thob bya'i phyir/ /su yi ched du brtson 'grus de de byed/ /
<p>166a.2</p>gal te lus can rnams ni med gyur na/ /ji ltar byams dang snying rje dga' ba dang / /btang snyoms dag la yang dag brten nas ni/ /bsam gtan snyoms 'jug bde ba thob par 'gyur/ /thar pa'i bde ba dngos dang dngos med shes/ /khams dang bsam pa bag la nyal du brjod/ /
<p>166a.3</p>kun nas nyon mongs rnam par byang ba dag /gal te de dag med na ji ltar shes/ /byang chub phyogs dang mthun pa'i chos rnams kyi / /rgyu ni ji ltar sems can rnams yin la / /de phyir rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'dod pa yis/ /sems can rnams ni bla ma bzhin du lta / /de ltar 'byung po
<p>166a.4</p>rnams ni bde chen gyi / /sgo ru sems bzhin par ni byed pa la/ /'gro ba na ni dka' ba'i rnam pa ni/ /mi bzod gang yin de la cung zad med/ /gang gi sems la sems can rnams/ /bdag nyid yin pa de ltar gnas/ /de la phyi rol dngos tshogs dang / /chung ma dag kyang mngon zhen
<p>166a.5</p>med/ /bdag nyid dang ni pha ma dang / /bu dang chung ma dag la yang / /gnod pa de 'dra khas blang gi /sems can rnams la gnod mi bya / /nyes pa drag po byed pa yi/ /sems can la bzod phan sems ldan/ /sems can rnams la gus brtan pa/ /nyes pa chung ngu 'ang mi byed do/ /
<p>166a.6</p>'di dag nyid la phan 'dod pa'i/ /brtson 'grus go cha gyon pa ni/ /'bras bu che la bskal stong du/ /dmyal ba'i mer yang gnas par spro/ /bdag gi skye dang 'jig dang rtogs pa la/ /ji lta ba dang ji snyed gnod pa yi/ /sems can de dag bsam gtan dbang gis ni/ /bla ma
<p>166a.7</p>dang ni bla mar rab tu sgom / /de ltar chos lnga po dag yod na ni/ /legs skyes rtsa can byang chub sems dpa' ni/ /'phags pa shes rab pha rol phyin pa yis/ /nges par gang pa yin par brjod par bya/ /gang zhig brten pas chen po nyid thob cing / /gnod pas dka' ba'i
<p>166b</p>
<p>166b.1</p>log par ltung ba thob/ /srog kyang yongs su btang bar byas nas kyang / /de dag dga' bar byas pa nyid du rigs/ /mang po gang dag brten pas grub pa ni/ /thob pa de ltar sems can de dag yin/ /sems can de dag las ni zhing gzhan pa'i/ /grub pa'i zhing ni 'gro ba na
<p>166b.2</p>yod min/ /'di dag yid bzhin nor bu ste/ /bum pa bzang yin 'dod 'jo'i ba/ /de'i phyir lha dang bla ma bzhin/ /de dag sten par byed pa yin/ /lung dang rigs pas yongs su bltas nas ni/ /sems can kun gyi bdag gi snyam rlom pa'i/ /dam pa'i lag tu dge
<p>166b.3</p>legs thams cad ni/ /yun mi ring bar 'byung bar 'gyur ba yin/ /'di ni thub pa chen po'i spyod pa ste/ /dpang bcas 'di la dpyad pa mi bya'o/ /ji srid 'di ni mngon du ma byas pa/ /de srid grub pa srid pa ma yin no/ /re zhig brtag par bya phyir ji skad du/ /bshad
<p>166b.4</p>pa 'di la 'bad pa gyis shig dang / /chen po nyid ni rgyu mtshan du gyur pa/ /yon tan rang nyid kyis ni thob par 'gyur/ /'di ni chen po nyid kyi lam/ /rigs ni sems can chen pos bsten/ /sems can kun la bde ster ba'i/ /'phags 'di yid bzhin nor bu yin/ /
<p>166b.5</p>rmi lam yid bzhin nor bu'i gtam slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //kha che'i paN+Di ta shrI ra tha dang / lo tsA ba dge slong grags 'byor shes rab kyis bsgyur//[ ]sbyin pa'i gtam/ @##/ /rgya gar skad du/ dA na pa ri ka thA/ bod skad
<p>166b.6</p>du/ sbyin pa'i gtam/ dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sbyin pa gter chen phyi bzhin 'brangs pa yin te chom rkun la sogs dbrog mi nus/ /sbyin pa sems kyi ser sna dang ni chags pa'i skyon gyi rdul rnams 'khru bar byed/ /sbyin pa 'khor ba'i lam dang ngal bsel
<p>166b.7</p>ba yin te bzhon pa bde blag can/ /sbyin pa bde dgur sbyor ba du ma dag gi sgo bzang gtan gyi mdza' bo mchog /'byor cing dag pa phun sum tshogs dang kun du bka' nyan yon tan rnams dang ni/ /sum cu rtsa gsum lha yul grong khyer la gnas byad gzugs mdzes pa'i yon tan rnams/ /ci dang
<p>167a</p>
<p>167a.1</p>ci 'dod de dag thams cad sbyin pa dag gis nges par thob 'gyur te/ /de ltar don ni yongs su brtags par gyur nas su dag sbyin pa sbyin mi byed/ /sbyin pa me dang chu dang chom rkun 'jigs pa'i 'khrug pa rnams kyis bskyod mi nus/ /sbyin pa sgrib pa zad byed
<p>167a.2</p>srid pa'i 'gro ba phyi bzhin 'brang ba'i mdza' chen yin/ /sbyin pa 'gro ba'i rgyun gyi yul rnams kun du srog chags rnams kyi 'jug pa yin/ /sbyin pa tshe rabs bgrang ba dag tu phyi bzhin 'brangs te ba phyir be'u 'brang ba bzhin/ /nor rnams kun gyi snying po blang ba dbang phyug rnams kyi gzhi ni
<p>167a.3</p>sbyin pa yin zhe'o/ /blo can legs par 'dod pa yis/ /legs par bsgrims te sbyin pa sbyin/ /'khor bar yongs su 'khyam pa na/ /sbyin pa ma gtogs gnyen med do/ /sbyin pa 'jig rten rgyan yin te/ /sbyin pa ngan 'gro zlog pa yin/ /sbyin pa mtho ris skas yin te/ /sbyin
<p>167a.4</p>pa zhi byed shis pa yin/ /'jig rten dag na rgyal po'i mchog /dpa' brtul dregs shing mthu che la/ /rgyal srid rgyas la dbang byed pa/ /bde 'byung sbyin pa byin las byung / /sum cu rtsa gsum gnas rnams na/ /brgya byin lha yi dbang byed pa/ /de yang phyin pa'i 'bras bu
<p>167a.5</p>mchog /dam pa yin zhes mkhas rnams smra/ /mtshan mchog sum cu gnyis mnga' ba/ /dri med gzi brjid mtshungs med pa/ /'khor ba'i rgya mtsho rgal ba yang / /sbyin pa la ni brten te 'byung / /lha yi 'jig rten skas kyang yin/ /thar pa'i mthar gyi sgo yang yin/ /
<p>167a.6</p>ngan song rnams las bzlog pa yin/ /phun sum tshogs kun rgyu yang yin/ /de yi phyir na mi rnams kyis/ /legs par bsgrims te sbyin pa sbyin/ /chags dang phrag dog la sogs pa/ /med par bsod nams bsags par gyis/ /sangs rgyas 'dra ba'i ston pa med/ /chos dang
<p>167a.7</p>'dra ba'i skyob pa med/ /dge 'dun 'dra ba'i zhing med de/ /de'i phyir gsum la dbul bar gyis/ /phrad par gyur pa'i mtha' ni 'bral bar 'gyur/ /phun sum tshogs pa'i mtha' ni ngan cing rgud/ /tshe 'di glog ltar 'gyur zhing 'jig la g.yo/ /de yi phyir na bag yod brtan por gyis/ /
<p>167b</p>
<p>167b.1</p>'jig rten 'di kun bde ba mngon par 'dod/ /skyes bu bde la longs spyod med par min/ /longs spyod sbyin las byung bar mkhyen nas ni/ /thub pas dang por sbyin pa'i gtam dag mdzad/ /slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa sbyin pa'i gtam rdzogs so// // @##/ /rgya gar
<p>167b.2</p>skad du/ b+hA ba saM krAn ta pa ri ka thA/ bod skad du/ srid pa las 'das pa'i gtam/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo / /dngos med dngos las mi skye ste/ /dngos med las kyang skye ma yin/ /dngos po rtag tu skye ba ste/ /dngos 'khrul nam mkha'i me tog bzhin/ /
<p>167b.3</p>mkha' dang 'dra ba'i chos yod na/ /gzhan ni mkha' dang 'dra ba skye/ /brten nas thams cad mkha' dang 'dra/ /de nas srid pa med pa can/ /ngo bo nyid kyis las med cing / /rgyu med 'bras bu yod ma yin/ /'di dag thams cad med pa ste/ /'jig rten pa med 'jig pa med/ /ma skyes
<p>167b.4</p>pa yi dngos po gang / /ji ltar gzhan zhig skyed par 'gyur/ /'jig rten dang por ma byung ste/ /'ga' zhig gis kyang sprul pa min / /zla ba seng ge'i grong khyer bzhin/ /'jig rten don med gyi na 'khyams / /'jig rten rnam par rtog las 'byung / /rnam rtog sems las yang dag
<p>167b.5</p>'byung / /sems ni lus la brten pa ste/ /de phyir lus ni rnam dpyad do/ /gzugs ni stong pa tshor ba rang bzhin med/ /'du shes med de 'du byed yod ma yin/ /'byung ba spangs nas sems dang sems byung med/ /de phyir lus ni rtog bral ngo bo yin/ /sems med chos rnams de dag
<p>167b.6</p>med/ /lus med khams rnams yod ma yin/ /gnyis su med pa'i las 'di ni/ /de nyid rig pa rnams kyis bstan/ /'di dag thams cad dmigs med par/ /gnyis su med par bstan pa yin/ /blo ni dmigs pa med byas nas/ /dmigs pa med par 'byung bar 'gyur/ /sbyin dang tshul khrims bzod brtson
<p>167b.7</p>'grus/ /bsam gtan la sogs brten byas nas/ /yun mi ring ba'i dus kyis ni/ /byang chub dam pa thob par 'gyur/ /thabs dang shes rab la gnas te/ /sems can rnams la brtse bar bya/ /myur ba kho nar thams cad mkhyen/ /thob par 'gyur bar the tshom med/ /'di dag thams
<p>168a</p>
<p>168a.1</p>cad ming tsam ste/ /'du shes tsam la rab tu gnas/ /rjod par byed las tha dad pa'i/ /brjod par bya ba yod ma yin/ /chos rnams thams cad ming med de/ /bdag med par yang yongs su gsal/ /yang dag min pa'i chos 'di dag /rnam par rtog pas kun nas bslang / /gang
<p>168a.2</p>gis stong pa zhes brtags pa'i/ /rtog pa de yang 'dis stong ngo / /mig gis gzugs rnams mthong bar ni/ /de nyid gsungs pas gang bshad pa/ /log par zhen pa'i 'jig rten la/ /kun rdzob bden par brjod pa yin/ /gang du tshogs par mthong ba ni/ /'dren pas ston par byed pa yin/ /blo dang
<p>168a.3</p>ldan pas don dam gyi/ /nye bar brtags pa'i sa de gsungs/ /mig gis gzugs ni mi mthong ste/ /yid kyis chos rnams mi rig go/ /'jig rten pa yi yul min gang / /'di ni mchog tu bden pa'o/ /mig med gzugs kyang yod min zhing / /snang ba yid la byed pa med/ /sems ni rmi lam bzhin
<p>168a.4</p>du 'khrul/ /thams cad yod min med pa'ang min/ /srid pa las 'das pa'i gtam slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //kha che'i paN+Di ta shrI ra tha dang / lo tsA ba dge slong grags 'byor shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o/ / @##/ /rgya gar skad du/ /sap+ta gu
<p>168a.5</p>Na pa ri ba da nA ka thA/ bod skad du/ /yon tan bdun yongs su brjod pa'i gtam/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /las ni du ma la brten pa'i/ /sna tshogs yon tan 'dod pa yis/ /'bang byas sa bon med par ni/ /myu gu skye ba yod ma yin/ /nyes med yon tan bsdu ba ni/ /sna tshogs
<p>168a.6</p>pa dag rnam bya ste/ /nyes pa dag ni gcig pu yis/ /yon tan mang po 'joms par byed/ /tshe ring de bzhin nad med dang / /gzugs dang skal ba bzang dang rigs/ /nor dang shes rab dag dang bdun/ /yon tan mdo sde dag las gsungs/ /de las bzlog pa nyes pa yin/ /de dag re res ji ltar
<p>168a.7</p>na/ /yon tan thams cad 'byung 'gyur ba/ /de ltar da ni bshad par bya/ /nad med gzugs dang skal ba bzang / /rigs nor shes rab phun sum tshogs/ /tshe ring ba ni med gyur na/ /gsad par phyin pa'i rgyan dang 'dra/ /tshe dang gzugs sogs yon tan ni/ /'di dag nad med mi ldan na/ /
<p>168b</p>
<p>168b.1</p>don med par ni nyams 'gyur te/ /ma ning bud med mchog yod mtshungs/ /yon tan ldan pa mthong na yang / /gzugs ngan skyo ba skye 'gyur te/ /yon tan phun tshogs rgyas par ni/ /rgyal po'i btsun mo mthong dang mtshungs/ /sngar bshad yon tan phun sum tshogs/ /skal ba ngan pas
<p>168b.2</p>mdongs 'brog pa/ /sdang ba'i gnas su gyur pa'i phyir/ /drang srong bran dang mtshungs par 'dod/ /yon tan dpal ldan dri ma med/ /rigs ngan la brten mya ngan gzhi/ /bram ze'i chung ma yon tan can/ /rigs ngan lag na gnas dang mtshungs/ /tshe dang nad med la sogs pa/ /sngar bshad
<p>168b.3</p>yon tan 'di dag ni/ /dbul bo la gnas bkur 'os min/ /dur khrod gnas kyi mi dang mtshungs/ /yon tan ji skad bshad phun tshogs/ /glen pa bdag nyid brlag don 'gyur/ /'od ma smyug ma'i chu shing gi /'bras bu phun tshogs lta bu yin/ /de ltar ji skad bshad yon tan/ /yan lag re re
<p>168b.4</p>ma tshang nyams/ /yi ge gcig ni ma tshang ba'i/ /rig pa 'bras bu med 'gyur mtshungs/ /yon tan longs rdzogs mdzes pa ni/ /yi ge tshad pa'i rig pa 'dra/ /sbyor ba grub las 'bras bu 'thob/ /ma tshang med pa 'byung bar 'gyur/ /de bas legs mdzes rdzogs pa yi/ /yon tan la ni 'bad
<p>168b.5</p>par gyis/ /'di dag rgyu ni gang yin pa/ /mdo bshad nga las rtogs par gyis/ /gsod par chung pa legs btang dang / /de bzhin srog gis phan btags shing / /srog chags 'tshe ba las ldog pas/ /tshe ring pa ni thob par 'gyur/ /nad pa'i bsnyen bkur byas sman pa/ /sman ni rab tu
<p>168b.6</p>byin pa dang / /srog chags bod pa dbyig sogs kyis/ /'tshe ba med las nad med yin/ /khro bo med la brten pa dang / /brgya byin pas ni gzugs bzang nyid/ /phrag dog med pa'i 'bras bu nyid/ /skal pa bzang por yongs su bshad/ /dam pa mchod cing bsnyen bkur byas/ /nga rgyal
<p>168b.7</p>spangs pas rigs mthor 'gyur/ /sbyin byed rku ba las ldog pas/ /longs spyod phun sum tshogs thob 'gyur/ /dge dang sdig pa gang yin zhes/ /yang dag dri la btson pa dang / /chos kyi bstan bcos byin pa yis/ /blo gros rgya chen thob par 'gyur/ /yon tan bdun yongs su
<p>169a</p>
<p>169a.1</p>brjod pa'i gtam/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta gang+gA ta ra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ / @##/ /rgya gar skad du/ shI
<p>169a.2</p>la pa ri ka thA/ bod skad du/ tshul khrims kyi gtam/ dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rgya mtsho dang ni glang rjes kyi/ /khyad par dag ni gang yin pa/ /sbyin pa dang ni tshul khrims kyi/ /khyad par dag ni de yin no/ /gang zhig dad pa'i sems kyis ni/ /lo brgyar sbyin pa byin pa bas/ /
<p>169a.3</p>gang zhig nyin gcig tshul khrims ni/ /bsrung ba de las khyad par 'phags/ /sbyin pa shan pa rnams dang ni/ /rigs ngan dag kyang sbyin par byed/ /gang yang rung bas tshul khrims ni/ /yongs su bsrung bar mi nus so/ /sbyin pa rab tu 'byor gyur kyang / /de ni sbyin bdag chen po min/ /tshul
<p>169a.4</p>khrims rnam par dag pa yis/ /sbyin bdag chen po yin par bshad/ /mgo bregs ba'am gtsug phud ldan par rgyu/ /tshul khrims chu yis ral pa khyab par 'chang / /cha lugs sna tshogs dag gis spyod gyur kyang / /gal te tshul khrims med na rgyu spyod yin/ /gang+gA bgrod ba chu bon dar song
<p>169a.5</p>ba'am/ /dbyangs can chu'am rdzing bur song ba'am/ /ne le shar ni sten par byed pa yang / /gal te tshul khrims kyis rgud la don med/ /ji ltar tshul khrims bla med ldan pa'i dri/ /dam pa mtho ris 'di na mi zad ldan/ /de ltar phreng ba'i dri ni khyab min cing / /de bzhin byug pa'i dri yang 'byung mi
<p>169a.6</p>'gyur/ /'di na bdag dga' gzhan du 'gro ba bde/ /grags dang dga' zhing kun gyis bkur ba ste/ /chos ldan 'bras bu de de mang po mthong / /tshul khrims 'bras bu drang srong chen pos gsungs/ /tshul khrims nad la sman pa'i mchog yin zhing / /mun pa'i sgron ma nyam thag la 
<p>169a.7</p>skyabs dang / /'jigs la srungs dang phongs la nye du dang / /'chi ba'i rgya mtsho mtha' med gzings gyur yin/ /gang zhig 'dul ba'i tshul khrims rnam 'jig tshe/ /skrag zhugs tshul khrims ldan pa yod ma yin/ /de bas 'jig rten gzhan mtha' rgal sems kyis/ /gang zhig 'gro
<p>169b</p>
<p>169b.1</p>'dod des ni tshul khrims srungs / /tshul khrims dri med ma lus ji bzhin gzhag / /shes rab zhi bas yid ni yongs smin 'gyur/ /de bas rga shi nad 'jigs rnam thar pa/ /gang zhig thob 'dod des ni tshul khrims srungs/ /tshul khrims kyi gtam slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad
<p>169b.2</p>pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po dza ran+d+ha na dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ /[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ shI la ka thA br-it+ti/ bod skad du/ tshul khrims kyi gtam gyi 'grel pa/ dkon mchog
<p>169b.3</p>gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang zhig bdud las rgyal zhing pha rol phyin drug rdzogs/ /brtse bas gzhan don mdzad pa de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gzhan dag drang bas min la rang nyid drang phyir ni/ /dam ba'i rjes su 'brangs la tshul khrims 'di nyid bshad/ /de bzhin du spyi'i don ni pha rol tu phyin
<p>169b.4</p>pa'i nang nas tshul khrims ni sa gzhi lta bu yin par dgongs nas/ de nyid sbyin pa las khyad par du 'phags par bsgrub pa'i phyir/ dpe'i sgo nas bstan pa ni/ /rgya mtsho dang ni glang rjes kyi/ /khyad par dag ni gang yin pa/ /sbyin pa dang ni tshul khrims kyi/ /khyad par dag ni de yin
<p>169b.5</p>no/ /zhes bya ba 'dis smos so/ /ni zhes bya ba ni nges par gzung ba'o/ /de zhes bya ba ni 'das ma thag pa'o/ /yin no zhes bya ba ni ngag rdzogs pa ste go bar zad do/ /de nyid tshul khrims kyi sgo nas rgyas par bstan pa'i phyir/ gang zhig ces bya ba la sogs pa smos so/ /de ji ltar mngon zhe na
<p>169b.6</p>lung dang rigs pa ste/ de la lung ni zla ba sgron ma las/ bskal pa bye ba gang+gA'i bye snyed du/ /sangs rgyas dag ni gang+gA'i bye snyed la/ /gdugs dang ba dan mar me'i phreng ba dang / /zas dang skom gyis dad sems mchod byas pas/ /gang gis dam pa'i chos ni 'jig pa'i tshe/ /de bzhin gshegs
<p>169b.7</p>pa'i bstan pa dgag pa ni/ /nyin zhig gcig tu bslab pa gcig bzung na/ /de bas bsod nams 'di ni khyad par 'phags/ /zhes 'byung ste/ rgyas par ni mdo nyid la blta bar bya'o/ /gzhan yang tshul khrims kyi 'bras bu ni mtho ris yin la sbyin pa'i 'bras bu ni 'byor pa yin
<p>170a</p>
<p>170a.1</p>te/ /rgyu de log na cig shos dang ldan du zin kyang ngan song gi 'gro ba dag ni bsod nams bsags pa'i rten du rung ngo snyam du bsams pa yin no/ /gang zhig dad pa'i sems kyis ni/ /zhes bya ba la gang zag gi yid ches pa la sogs pa'i sgo nas so/ /lo brgyar sbyin pa byin pa
<p>170a.2</p>bas/ /zhes bya ba ni mtshon pa ste/ dus yun ring por 'bad pa byas kyang zhes bya ba'i don to/ /gang zhig nyin gcig tshul khrims ni/ /zhes bya ba ni tshad 'jog pa ste/ dus mnyam par ni ma yin te/ tha na nyin gcig tsam zhes nges par bzung ba'o/ /bsrung ba de las khyad par
<p>170a.3</p>'phags/ /zhes bya ba ni bsrung ba'am 'bad pa'am ched du gnyer ba ste/ de gang la yod pa de la de skad ces bya'o/ /da ni de las lhag pa 'am khyad par 'phags pa ste/ mi mtshungs pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go/ /gzhan yang slob dpon gyis de nyid kyi rgyu mtshan bstan pa'i phyir ro/ /sbyin
<p>170a.4</p>pa shan pa rnams dang ni/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ rnams zhes bya ba'i sgra ni du ma ste/ /shan pa dang nya pa dang tshong pa la sogs pa thams cad la bya'o/ /rigs ngan rnams kyang ster bar byed/ /ces bya ba ni 'jig rten na tha chad du gyur pa gdol ba de dag tshul khrims kyis dben la sbyin
<p>170a.5</p>ba gtong bar byed do/ /gang yang rung bas tshul khrims ni/ /zhes bya bas ni skyes bu dam pa sems pa lus ngag dul ba gnyen po stobs dang ldan pa dag gis kyang ste/ gzhan lta ci smos zhes bya ba'i don to/ /yongs su srung bar mi nus so/ /zhes bya ba la de'i phyir tshul khrims khyad par du
<p>170a.6</p>'phags zhes bya ba'i tha tshig gi lhag ma'o/ /ji lta zhe na skyes bu dam pas kyang tshul khrims rin po che dang 'dra bar dri mas dben pa rdul phra mo dag gis ma gtses pa de lta bu ma byung bar du dka' ste/ bar chad mang ba'i phyir dang / snyigs ma'i sems can dag gis ga la nus snyam du
<p>170a.7</p>bsams pa yin no/ /yongs su'i sgra ni lung du ste khyab pa'am chub par bsgrub pa'i mthu med de zhes bya ba'i don to/ /rgyu mtshan gnyis pa bstan pa'i phyir/ sbyin pa rab tu 'byor gyur kyang / /zhes bya ba la don 'di yin te/ da lta sbyin pa la gnas pa 'am de'i 'bras bu la spyod pa ste ldan
<p>170b</p>
<p>170b.1</p>zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go/ /yang na sbyin pas zhes gsum pa'i sgrar blta bar bya'o/ /de ni sbyin bdag chen po min/ /zhes bya ba smos pa yin te/ tshul khrims kyis lus dag pa'i phyir rta cang shes la sogs pa dag yin no/ /tshul khrims rnam par dag pa yis/ /zhes bya ba ni de ltar
<p>170b.2</p>tshul khrims la gnas pas de'i 'bras bu la spyod pa ste/ rnam par dag pa dang ldan zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go/ /sbyin bdag chen po yin par bshad/ /zhes bya ba ni bdag nyid chen po ste/ tshul khrims kyis 'phangs pa'i phyir lha'i dbang po la sogs pa bzhin no/ /gal te 'o na sbyin pa dang
<p>170b.3</p>ldan pa sbyin bdag ma yin na/ 'o na mdo las tshul khrims dang mi ldan pa yang sbyin pa'i sa can de la sbyin bdag ces pa ji lta bu zhe na/ de ni sbyin bdag tsam yin yang sbyin bdag chen po ni ma yin te/ pha rol tu phyin pa gzhan gyis ma zin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'i don to/ /ji ltar sbyin
<p>170b.4</p>pa de mchog yin yang tshul khrims la ltos shing dman par bstan nas/ da ni tshul gzhan gyi sgo nas tshul khrims de nyid khyad par du 'phags pa bstan pa'i phyir/ mgo bo bregs pa'am gtsug phud ldan par rgyu/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ mgo bo bregs
<p>170b.5</p>pa ni skra bregs pa'am zhes bya'o/ /gtsug phud can ni thor gtsug ste kun du rgyu'i rtags yin no/ /de nyid ldan par zhes bya ba'i sgrar sbyar te des rgyu zhing gnas par byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go/ /tshul khrims chu yis ral pa khyab par 'chang / /zhes bya ba ni spyod pa'i tshul gzhag
<p>170b.6</p>ba ste/ /tshul khrims kyi ched du zhes bya'o/ /de nyid khyab pa'i ral pa'am ral pas khyab pa ste/ de 'chad ba gang yin pa de la de skad ces bya'o/ /cha lugs sna tshogs dag gis spyod gyur kyang / /zhes bya ba ni cha byad du ma dag gi sgo nas dpa' ba byas kyang zhes lhag ma dang ldan
<p>170b.7</p>par ston pa yin no/ /de ltar 'bad na don dang ldan nam snyam du bsams na/ gal te tshul khrims med na g.yo sgyus spyod/ /ces smos te/ gal te rtag pa'i mtha' bzung nas de yang tshul khrims med na ste/ thog ma nas ma thob pa'am/ thob kyang nyams shing zhig nas bdag nyid slu ba ste 'bad
<p>171a</p>
<p>171a.1</p>pa 'bras bu med ces bya ba'i don to/ /de ltar ci mngon zhe na/ dge slong la rab tu gces pa'i mdo las/ dper na sdong po bzang po la/ /yun rings yal ga 'khrungs pa bzhin/ /mi de rtags tsam yun rings na/ /kha na ma tho rtag 'phel dang / /sdig pa'i
<p>171a.2</p>las rnams 'phel bar bshad/ /ces 'byung ba'i don ni 'di dag yin te/ rgyas par ni mdo nyid du lta'o/ /de tsam du zad dam zhe na/ tshul khrims nyid khyad par du 'phags pa sgrub pa de'i 'thad pa gnyis pa bstan pa'i phyir/ gang+gA bgrod pa chu bo na dar sod ba'am/ /zhes bya ba la
<p>171a.3</p>sogs pa smos te/ 'di dag ni mtshon pa tsam ste/ des ni 'am zhes bsu ba mdzad/ /de bzhin du/ dbyangs can chu'am rdzing bur song ba'am/ /zhes bya ba ni dbyangs can gyi chu bo'am rdzing bur 'jug pa la sogs pa dag /ne le sha ni sten par byed pa yang / /zhes bya ba ni gang la ne
<p>171a.4</p>le sha yod pa der ro/ /yang zhes bya ba ni de dag kyang de bzhin du chur 'jug pa dang / mer 'jug pa dang / nyi ma la lta ba dang / zla ba la lta ba dang / g.yang la mchong ba dang / gsal shing la sogs pa la zhon pa 'di dag don dang bcas pa yin nam snyam pa la gal te tshul khrims kyis
<p>171a.5</p>rgud la don med ces gsungs te 'bad pa 'bras bu med ces bya bar snyegs so/ /des na bag chags ngan pa la bdag phyin ci log gi dbang gis lam gol par 'jug cing bde bar gshegs pa'i bka' la yang yid mi ches shing lam drang po la 'gror mi btub pa'i snying rje'i gnas yin no/ /
<p>171a.6</p>de bas na tshul khrims kyi nor 'di ni gru dang 'dra ba la 'phags pa'i nor gang gi nor las mchog yin la pha rol tu phyin pa drug gi nang na yang gtso bo yin te/ rin po che 'di gsum gyis sangs rgyas rnams kyis bsngags so snyam du bsams pa yin no/ /de ltar tshul khrims khyad par du 'phags
<p>171a.7</p>pa bsgrubs zin nas/ da ni 'di'i yon tan ston pa de nyid dpe'i sgo nas bstan pa'i phyir/ ji ltar tshul khrims bla med ldan pa'i dri/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ ji ltar zhes pa ni dri ba bkod pa ste/ de ltar zhes 'og ma dang 'brel lo/ /tshul khrims de bslab pa yin pa'i
<p>171b</p>
<p>171b.1</p>phyir ro/ /bla med ldan pa'i dri zhes bya ba ni gong na med pa de ldan pa'am de la gnas pa'i dri ni de'i dri ste rjed pa zhes bya ba'i don to/ /dam pa mtho ris 'di na mi zad ldan/ /zhes bya ba la dam pa ni mchog yin la mtho ris ni gnas bcu la sogs pa'o/ /de nyid la bde 'gro zhes kyang bya ste/ de'i
<p>171b.2</p>gnas sam rten 'di ni tshul khrims kyi dri mi zad pa ste/ drag cing mu med par smin zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go/ /de ltar phreng ba'i dri ni khyab min zhing / /zhes bya ba ni sdom brtson gyi dri de ltar me tog phreng ba la sogs pa'i dris ni khyab mi nus te/ dman zhing mthu med pa'i phyir ro/ /'o na sman sna
<p>171b.3</p>tshogs kyi sbyor ba'i byug pa dag gis nus sam zhe na/ de bzhin byug pa'i dri yang khyab mi 'gyur/ /zhes bya ba smos te/ tshul khrims kyi 'khor lo skye ba du mar mtho ris kyi skas la rgyu ba bzhin du/ byug pa dang dpag bsam gyi shing la sogs pa'i dris ni ga la nus zhes bya ba'i don
<p>171b.4</p>yin no/ /de ltar yon tan bstan nas de'i 'bras bu bstan pa'i phyir slob dpon gyis/ 'di na bdag dga' gzhan du 'gro ba bde/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ 'di na zhes bya ba ni sdom brtson gyi gzhi 'di na'o/ /bdag dga' zhes bya ba ni mtshon pa ste/ gang zag la la dag go/ /
<p>171b.5</p>gzhan du 'gro ba bde zhes bya ba ni gnas gzhan du ste/ 'jig rten pha rol la sogs par 'gro ba na sems bde bar 'gro ba ste de nyid rgyas par mdo dag las blta bar bya'o/ /grags dang dga' nyid kun gyis bkur ba ste/ /zhes bya ba la grags pa de ni 'jig rten du grags pa'o/ /dga'
<p>171b.6</p>ba ni bdag nyid dga' ba ste/ tshul khrims kyi dbang gis ni snying por mthong zhes bya ba smos te/ chos ldan zhes bya ba ni khrims ldan can yin pa'i phyir ro/ /kun gyis bkur ba ste zhes bya ba ni gang zag de la sems can mang po dag gis bkur zhing rim gro byed pa'o/ /de bzhin
<p>171b.7</p>du sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis kyang dgongs par 'gyur te/ de skad du slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis/ de tshe de la dge ba'i phyir/ /rgyal ba sras dang bcas rnams kyis/ /dge ba'i thugs kyis rtag par yang / /bu sdug 'dra bar dgongs par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs
<p>172a</p>
<p>172a.1</p>pa 'di nyid yin te/ de tsam du zad dam zhe na/ chos ldan 'bras bu de de mang por mthong / /zhes bya ba smos te/ chos ldan zhes bya ba ni khrims ldan no/ /'bras bu ni 'bras bu ste 'dod pa'i don yin pa'i phyir ro/ /de de mang por mthong zhes bya ba ni de dang de
<p>172a.2</p>dag ste/ gzhan dpag tu med do zhes bya ba'i don to/ /ji ltar zhe na/ tshul khrims 'bras bu drang srong chen pos gsungs/ /zhes bya ba ston te de'i 'bras bu ni lhag par yang drang srong chen pos gsungs te/ de ni che ba'i bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/ /de nas de nyid rgyas par ni sdang ba
<p>172a.3</p>dor zhing gus pa skyes pas bstan bcos dang mdo sde la blta bar bya'o/ /da ni 'bras bu de nyid gnyen po 'am dpe rnam pa drug gi sgo nas bstan pa'i phyir/ tshul khrims nad la sman pa'i mchog yin zhing / zhes bya ba smos te/ dper na shin tu yun rings nad kyis gdungs pa de dag la
<p>172a.4</p>sman pa mkhas pa dag gis nad kyi rgyu las phye nas sman bzang po dag gis sbyor ba bzhin du/ ngan 'gro sdug bsngal nad dang 'dra ba du ma dag gis gzir ba de dag la tshul khrims ni sman pa'i mchog yin te/ nad de dag las thar par byed pa'o/ /mun pa'i sgron ma nyam thag la skyabs dang / /zhes bya ba
<p>172a.5</p>la gzhan yang mun pa'i tshogs shin tu chen po dag la mar me la sogs pa chung ngu dag gis de dag thams cad sel ba de bzhin du ma rig pa'i mun pa'i tshogs dpag tu med pa dag la tshul khrims kyis dngos sam brgyud pa'i sgo nas sgron ma'i mchog yin no/ /de bzhin du sdug bsngal sna tshogs kyis nyam thag
<p>172a.6</p>pa de dag la tshul khrims ni skyabs kyi mchog yin no zhes bya ba'i don to/ 'jigs la bsrung dang phongs la nye du dang / /zhes bya ba mi dang mi ma yin pas 'jigs pa bsrung ba'i mchog yin zhing phongs shing rgud pa nye du la sogs pa lta bu ste/ tshul khrims zhes sbyar ro/ /'chi
<p>172a.7</p>ba'i rgya mtsho mtha' med gzigs gyur yin/ /zhes bya ba ni dper na rgya mtsho las 'gro ba na gzings la brten nas 'gro ba bzhin du tshul khrims ni 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho chen po la gzings dang 'dra ba'o/ /de dag la sogs pa phan yon dpag tu med pa mdo las bshad de/ tshul khrims
<p>172b</p>
<p>172b.1</p>yang dag pa'i mdo las/ de phyir ston pas tshul khrims rab bsngags bshad/ /tshul khrims ldan pa sangs rgyas 'byung dang phrad/ /tshul khrims ldan pa rgyan rnams kun gyi mchog /tshul khrims ldan pa dri dang byug pa yin/ /zhes 'byung ste rgyas par ni mdo nyid la blta'o/ /
<p>172b.2</p>de ltar tshul khrims rnam par dag pas sems la 'gyod pa med/ sems la 'gyod pa med pas sems dben zhing ting nge 'dzin las su rung ste/ de bas na rin po che dang 'dra ba 'di ni lam gyi mchog yin no snyam du bsams pa yin no/ /da ni 'bras bu'i sgo nas gang zag gi khyad par
<p>172b.3</p>bstan pa'i phyir/ gang zhig 'dul ba'i tshul khrims rnam 'jig tshe/ /skrag zhugs tshul khrims ldan pa yod ma yin/ /zhes bya ba smos te gang zhig ces bya ba ni gang zag go/ /'dul ba'i tshul khrims zhes bya ba ni 'dul ba las gsungs pa'i tshul khrims so/ /rnam 'jig tshe zhes pa ni
<p>172b.4</p>btang ba'i tshe ste med par 'gyur zhes bya ba'i don to/ /skrag zhugs zhes bya ba ni de'i dbang gis te 'jigs pa'o/ /tshul khrims ldan pa zhes pa ma nyams pa ste/ gang la yod pa de la de skad ces bya'o/ /yod ma yin zhes bya ba ni 'jigs pa'am bag khums pa med pa yin te/ tshul khrims
<p>172b.5</p>de'i dbang gis bdag nyid dga' bar ma bshad na 'jigs pa lta ga la srid ces bya ba'i don to/ /de ltar 'bras bu bshad zin nas de nyid bsrung bar gdams par 'dod nas/ /de bas 'jig rten gzhan mtha' rgal sems kyis/ /gang zhig bgrod 'dod des ni tshul khrims bsrung / /zhes
<p>172b.6</p>smos te de bas zhes bya ba ni de bas na'o/ /'jig rten gzhan mtha' zhes bya ba mtha' gzhan te/ de dag kyang sdug bsngal gyi gzhi yin pa'i phyir ro/ /rgal sems kyis zhes bya ba ni de las 'da' bar 'dod pa ste/ go cha bgos nas zhes bya ba'i don to/ /gang zhig ces bya ba ni gang zag ste skyes
<p>172b.7</p>bu'o/ /bgrod 'dod des zhes bya ba ni 'gro bar 'dod pa nges so/ /ni zhes bya ba'i sgra ni nges par gzung ba ste gang zhe na tshul khrims te/ de gnas pa'i ched du srungs shig ces brtse ba'i tshul gyis bsgo bar mdzad do/ /da ni tshul khrims de nyid bye brag tu bstan pa dang / zhar la shes
<p>173a</p>
<p>173a.1</p>rab kyi 'bras bu'i sgo nas gdams pa ni/ tshul khrims dri med ma lus ji bzhin gzhag /shes rab zhi bas yid ni yongs smin 'gyur/ /zhes bya ba smos te/ thams cad yin nam zhe na/ tshul khrims dri med ces bya ba ni rigs bdun la sogs pa sems pa ngo bo spong ba
<p>173a.2</p>bdun 'khor dang bcas pa de nyid srung zhing dag pa'o/ /ma lus pa ni lus pa med pa ste/ /ltung ba phra mo tsam la 'dzem pa'i phyir ro/ /ji bzhin gzhag ces bya ba ni ji skad bshad pa bzhin du gzhag cing gdams pa'o/ /tshul khrims kho nar zad dam ce na/ shes rab zhi zhes bya ba smos te/ 
<p>173a.3</p>shes rab zhi ba ni zhi gnas dang lhag mthong yin no/ /yid ces bya ba ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa ste/ chos mngon pa las rab tu grags pa'i phyir ro/ /yongs su smin 'gyur zhes bya ba ni las su rung ba ste khyad par can no/ /'di dag kyang mtshon pa ste de bzhin du gzhan du yang yin no/ /ji skad du slob dpon
<p>173a.4</p>shAn ta de bas/ bzod bya thos pa btsal bar bya/ /de nas gnas lugs gnas par bya/ /'di dag legs par bshad pa yin no/ /da ni de dag tshul khrims la rag lus pas mjug bsdu ba'i tshul gyis bstan pa ni/ de bas rga shi nad 'jigs rnam thar pa/ /gang zhig thob 'dod des ni tshul khrims
<p>173a.5</p>srungs/ /zhes bya ba smos te/ de bas zhes bya ba ni de bas na'o/ /rga 'chi nad 'jigs zhes bya ba ni ma rig pa la sogs pa ste/ rten 'brel yan lag bcu gnyis srid pa len pa'i tshul lo/ /rnam thar zhes bya ba ni de las ldog ste spong bar byed ces pa'i tha tshig go/ /gang zhig ces bya ba ni snga ma bzhin
<p>173a.6</p>no/ /thos 'dod zhes bya ba ni don du gnyer te/ bzod pa can gyi skyes bu thabs la mkhas pa des so/ /ji ste nges pa kho nar tshul khrims srungs te/ de bas ni zhes bya ba'i sgra smos te/ don dag bstan pa yin no snyam du bsams pa yin no/ /bdag 'dra mkhas pa'i don la mkhas par bsam
<p>173a.7</p>par mi nus kyang / /cung zad dman la phan phyir 'phags pa'i rjes 'brangs te/ /lo brgya brtse ba can gyi gtam la rnam bshad pas/ /nyes pa mang yod mkhas pa rnams la bzod par gsol/ /'di la bsod nams cung zad bdag gis bskrun nges ni/ /'gro ba rgyal ba thob nas
<p>173b</p>
<p>173b.1</p>de bzhin gzhan dag kyang / /myur du dbang phyug thob nas sa la gnas pa dang / /pha rol phyin drug thob nas 'gro ba'i don byed shog /tshul khrims kyi gtam gyi 'grel pa slob dpon gsal grags kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// // @##/ /rgya gar skad du/ saM b+hA ra pa
<p>173b.2</p>ri ka thA/ bod skad du/ tshogs kyi gtam/ gsung gi mnga' bdag 'jam pa'i dbyangs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bdag gis de ring bsod nams dang / /ye shes tshogs ni gang zhig gam/ /gzhan la phan pa gang bya zhes/ /byang chub sems dpa' yang yang bsam/ /bsod nams rang bzhin
<p>173b.3</p>ye shes che/ /tshogs ni gang gis rdzogs 'gyur dang / /ji ltar gzhan phan byed 'gyur pa/ / de ni legs par bshad par bya/ /gang gis lus dang srog dag ni/ /sems can kun la gtang bar bya/ /lus can kun la byams pa dang / /snying rje nyid kyis khyab par bya/ /sdig pa kun
<p>173b.4</p>gyi rnam smin ni/ /rang gi rgyud la mngon 'dod cing / /bsod nams kun la yi rang dang / / sangs rgyas bdag nyid che la bsam / /de ltar yang dang yang bya ba/ /'di ni cho ga gzhan yin no/ /byang chub sems ni sngon 'gro bas/ /rtsom pa kun kyang bya ba yin/ /de lta bu yi thabs de
<p>173b.5</p>yis/ /rtsom pa'i ngal ba med par yang / /bsod nams ye shes tshad med pa/ /yang dang yang du sogs par 'gyur/ /sems can rnams kyi longs spyod dang / /yongs su bskyab pa'i phyir dang ni/ /rang gi lus dang srog nyid ni/ /yid kyi rjes bzhin gtang bar bya/ /
<p>173b.6</p>bkres skom ngal dang tsha grang dang / /rlung dang char gyi gnyen po bzhin/ /mchog mchod pa las bdag nyid ni/ /'di na bde myong gang yin dang / /nyams dga' khang bzangs gzhir gnas dang / /gtsang zhing zhi ba'i gnas gtogs dang / /bde ba thob pa gang yin dang / /bsam gtan bde ba
<p>173b.7</p>thob pa yis/ /bde ba'i gnas skabs thob gang dang / /sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' dang / /dgra bcom shin tu sbyangs zhi nyid/ /de ni sems can thams cad la/ /bye brag med par nye bar bstabs / /phal cher mnyam par ma bzhag tshe/ /de ltar byams pa nyer bsten la/ /
<p>174a</p>
<p>174a.1</p>mnyam par gzhag tshe bdag gis rtogs/ /dga' dang shin tu sbyangs pa nyid/ /nyi ltar nyams su myong ba dag /de bzhin gzhan la lhag mos byas / /skye dgu 'di ni sdug bsngal gyi/ /chu bor nub dang de rgyu can/ /dan 'gro dang ni bde 'gro dag /brtse la 'bad
<p>174a.2</p>pas brtag par bya/ /de las kyang ni dmyal ba dag /sdug bsngal mi bzad mang po dang / /dus ring rgyun mi 'chad pa yi/ /gcad gshegs me yis gdungs pa dang / /'tshed cing btags pa las byung ba'i/ /shin tu nyam thag rab tu 'phel/ /thal chu lta bur rab 'tshed pa'i/ /
<p>174a.3</p>bsreg cing tsha rims 'dra nyam thag /dud 'gro phan tshun sdang dang srog /rang dbang med par gsad sogs kyis/ /rtag tu sdug bsngal gyis gdungs pas/ /phal cher dmyal ba dag dang mtshungs/ /yi dgas me lce'i phreng ba yis/ /bskor zhing skad gsang mthon por sgrogs/ /la
<p>174a.4</p>la kha na me 'bar gzhan/ /mgrin pa khab mig lto ri tsam/ /rtag tu bkres skom la sogs pas / /bsreg cing lus ni skams pa dang / /kha cig skyug ba za ba dang / /gzhan dag de yang rab rnyed dka'/ /ngan 'gro'i sdug bsngal ma lus pa/ /mi rnams la yang yod par snang / /sdug
<p>174a.5</p>bsngal gzir ba dmyal ba mtshungs/ /dbul bas gshin rje'i 'jig rten pa / /'di yi dud 'gro'i sdug bsngal yang / /mthu ldan stobs kyis mthu med pa/ /rnam par gnon cing 'tshe ba dag /chu bo lta bu nyid yin no/ /kha cig dbul ba las
<p>174a.6</p>gyur dang / /gzhan dag chog mi shes las byung / /yongs tshol sdug bsngal mi bzad dang / /thams cad 'khu zhing gsod pa yin/ /'dod spyod lha ni gang yin pa/ /de la'ang bde ba'i sems med de/ /'dod pa'i 'dod chags rims btab pa'i/ /nang gi me yis bsregs 'gyur
<p>174a.7</p>las / /gang zhig sems g.yeng gyur pa dag /de la bde ba ga la yod/ /g.yengs med sems la skad cig kyang / /dbang med pa ni ma yin pas/ /rnam g.yeng dkrugs ba'i bdag nyid can/ /nam yang zhi bar mi 'gyur te/ /rlung bcas 'bar bas khyab pa yis / /me ni shing
<p>174b</p>
<p>174b.1</p>dang bcas dang mtshungs/ /shin tu ngoms med tha mar ni/ /dbang med shin tu mya ngan byed/ /lha dang mi ni lha la dag /sdug pa'i chags pa dam du zhen/ /bsod nams sngon byas de dang des/ /'dod pa rmongs pas gdungs par 'gyur/ /de yang nyon mongs sna tshogs dang / /sdig pa'i las ni
<p>174b.2</p>rgyun mi 'chad/ /rnam par ltung ba'i mthar gnas pas/ /bag med gyur la brtse bya'i rigs/ /nad sos yun rings ma lon pa'i/ /nad pas mi 'phrod zos dang mtshungs/ /gang zhig gzugs can gzugs med pa/ /sdug bsngal sdug bsngal las 'das shing / /ting 'dzin bde pa'i bdag nyid
<p>174b.3</p>can/ /bskal par g.yo ba med par gnas/ /de yang shin tu nges grol min/ /de yang slar yang ltung bar 'gyur/ /ngan 'gro'i sdug bsngal rba klong las/ /'das pa lta bur 'byung 'gyur ba/ /'bad kyang ji ltar ring mo gnas/ /mkha' la lding ba bya dang mtshungs/ /byis pa'i stobs kyis
<p>174b.4</p>mda' 'phangs ltar/ /de ni ltung ba'i mtha' can yin/ /mar me ring du 'bar ba dag /skad cig re re 'jig pa ltar/ /'du byed yongs 'gyur zhes bya yi/ /sdug bsngal dag gis nye bar gtses/ /rga shi na ba'i chos can gyis / /nyon mongs nad na rgyu sogs kyis/ /gang phyir thams cad
<p>174b.5</p>gdungs pas na / /de phyir shin tu brtse bya rigs/ /srog chags kun gyi sdig pa rnams/ /thams cad bdag la smin par ni/ /de ltar sdig pa len byed cing / /'gro ba'i phongs pas sdug bsngal byas/ /sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' dang / /'phags pa dag dang 'gro ba yi/ / 
<p>174b.6</p>dus ni thams cad dag gi yang / /bsod nams kun la yi rang bya/ /tshogs ni shin tu bya dka' dang / /sangs rgyas chos ni bla med pa/ /'gro ba'i don gyi bya ba nyid/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyis rjes su bsam/ /mang du thos la mngon brtson dang / /ji bzhin don ni sems pa dang / /'gro
<p>174b.7</p>ba'i shes pa nye bsdus pa'ang / /rten 'brel yid la byed pa yis/ /'du byed tsam la skad cig ma/ /bya ba med la 'jug par bya/ /thams cad rten 'brel la bsam la/ /rtag tu bdag med goms pa yi/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes tshogs/ /don dam par ni 'phel bar
<p>175a</p>
<p>175a.1</p>'gyur/ /byang chub sems ni nyer 'phel bas/ /tshogs ni thams cad rdzogs par 'gyur/ /de ltar bsod nams ye shes kyis/ /rang bzhin chu bos 'gengs pa dag /'gro ba'i thar la gcig tu mkhas/ /byang chub lag pa'i mthil na gnas/ /sbyin dang
<p>175a.2</p>snyan par smra ba dang / /don spyod don ni mthun pa nyid/ /de ltar bsdu ba'i dngos po rnams/ /'gro la phan par byed pa nyid/ /de ni gang la sbyin pa byin/ /gang zhig la ni snyan smra ba'am / /don spyod pa ni byas 'gyur ba/ /gang la don mthun byas 'gyur zhes/ /de ltar rtag tu brtson pa yis/ / 
<p>175a.3</p>'gro ba'i don ni ci nus bya/ /gzhan kun bdag gir bya ba dang / /rang la gnas pa gzhan gyir bya/ /tshogs kyi gtam slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po gang gA ta ra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur
<p>175a.4</p>cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ aSh+Ta ak+Sha Na ka thA/ bod skad du/ mi khom pa brgyad kyi gtam/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'dir bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa'i chos gus par mnyan par bya ste/ 
<p>175a.5</p>phyis ni rjes su rnyed par mi 'gyur ro/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gang gi tshe 'dir mi khom pa brgyad las grol ba'i mi ni shin tu dkon no/ /mi khom pa brgyad po dag gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ dmyal ba dang / dud 'gro dang / yi dgas dang / mtha' khob tu skyes pa dang / lha tshe ring po dang / dbang po ma
<p>175a.6</p>tshang ba dang / log par lta ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mi 'byung ba ste/ de ltar mi khom pa brgyad po 'di dag ldan na/ mi ma thob pas grol ba'i chos dang ldan par mi 'gyur ro/ /de dag ji lta zhe na brjod par bya ste/ dmyal ba dang / dud 'gro dang / yi dgas dang / sha za'i lam la
<p>175a.7</p>phal cher gnas pas/ 'dir 'ga' zhig mi 'am lhar 'gyur gyi phal cher ni mi 'gyur ro/ /dge ba'i rtsa ba'i tshogs bsags pa ni dkon pa nyid de/ de 'ga' zhig gi gnya' shing gi bu gar rus sbal gyi mgrin pa chud pa bzhin no/ /rin po che'i tshogs thams cad kyi gling du gyur pa/ bkra mi
<p>175b</p>
<p>175b.1</p>shis pa'i dri ma thams cad 'khrud pa/ dam pa'i chos kyi mthar thug pa/ bskal pa grangs med par nges par 'byung ba/ sna tshogs pa la mkhas par byas pa/ sangs rgyas nyid kyi go 'phang thob cing nges par legs pa ni thob pa mchog tu dka'o/ /bdag nyid kyis dge ba mdun du snying por byas
<p>175b.2</p>te/ mi dge ba'i chos zhe sdang gis skyed pas gnyen po dge ba'i chos gtsor bya'o/ /ri'i chu ltar g.yo ba dang / rlung ltar mi gnas pa dang / kA shi'i me tog ltar 'thor zhing / g.yo ba dang / ston ka'i sprin dang / glog dang / tho rangs kyi mar me dang / pad+ma'i 'dab ma'i chu thigs
<p>175b.3</p>dang / dri za'i grong khyer dang / dar la bab pa'i sems ltar g.yo bas mi rnams la yid brtan par mi bya'o/ /de bas na 'di ltar bsgrub par bya ste/ me'i nang du zhugs pa ltar bdag legs so 'dod pas myur du nges par skyabs su 'gro bar bya'o/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar gnas
<p>175b.4</p>skabs thams cad du dge ba'i bshes gnyen du ma rnyed pa ni dkon no/ /gang gi tshe yang sos dang / thig nag dang / bsdus 'joms dang / ngu 'bod dang / ngu 'bod chen po dang / tsha ba dang / rab tu tsha ba dang / mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen po 'di rnams su skyes shing 'khrugs
<p>175b.5</p>pas sgyur zhing 'don pa dang / rdeg pa dang / sreg pa dang / 'ched pa dang / 'don cing gtub pa dang / za ba dang / gsod pa dang / 'ching ba dang / ngu zhing nga ro 'don pas smre zhing sdug bsngal sna tshogs shing sdug bsngal du mar bying ste/ chu bo rab med du nub cing / lo ma ral gri'i nags tshal
<p>175b.6</p>dang / tsher ma rnon po'i tshal dang / spu gris gtams pa'i lam dang / rim pa med par 'gro ba dang / lcags kyi thu lum 'bar ba za ba dang / /khro chu 'thung ba dang / sa gzhi 'bar bar 'dug pa dang / me'i phreng bas lus sreg pa ni bud shing rab tu 'bar ba bzhin no/ /yongs su skyur
<p>175b.7</p>zhing 'bros pa dang / brgyal ba dang / smre ba dang / rnam par 'joms pa dang / nyon mongs pas nga ro 'don cing mya ngan byed cing ngu ba dang / rnam pa sna tshogs pa'i gzugs du mas sdug bsngal brgya stong phrag mang po myong ngo / /de dag gang du ji ltar zhi bar 'gyur zhes kyang gsungs so/ /kyi hud
<p>176a</p>
<p>176a.1</p>zer ba dang / a chu zer ba dang / snying rje rje skad zer ba dang / ral gri rnon po thogs pa'i gshin rje gtum pos rdeg cing gtub pa dang / mnar med par skyes nas 'bar ba'i mes bsregs par de dag rab tu spangs nas chos kyi 'du shes ji ltar skye bar 'gyur/ de
<p>176a.2</p>bas na gus pas chos mnyan par bya ste/ phyis rjes su rnyed par mi 'gyur ro zhes bya'o/ /yang gang dag 'di ltar phan tshun za ba dang / ded pa dang skrag par byed pa dang / 'joms pa dang bcas shing za ba dang / ma la 'khrig pa spyod pa dang 'di lta ste/ sre mo dang / ku ra dang / ri dgas
<p>176a.3</p>dang / phag dang / ru ru dang / smi shi d+ha dang / gnag dang / spre'u dang / srin bu dang / phye ma leb dang / chu srin dang / ma he dang / glang po dang / glang dang / 'ug pa dang / bya rog dang / khrung khrung dang / bya rgod dang / khyi dang / wa dang / ce spyang dang / rnga mo dang / bong bu la sogs par
<p>176a.4</p>skyes nas/ phan 'dogs pa dang / blo gros dang rtogs pa dang / dran pa med cing blun por spyod pa dang / bgrod par bya ba dang / bgrod par mi bya ba la ltos pa med cing / dgra dang dgra ma yin pa mi shes shing / smra ba dang bral zhing rigs pa mi byed pa/ dpal dang bral ba'i lus dang
<p>176a.5</p>ldan pa de bas na/ de dag la yang chos kyi 'du shes ji ltar skye bar 'gyur/ mgo dang mgrin pa dang kha dang rgyab la lcags kyu dang / rdo ba dang / dbyig pa dang / gnya' shing la sogs pas nye bar sdug bsngal zhing / skrag cing 'bros pa dang / rnam par 'thor ba dang / rdeg 'chos pa
<p>176a.6</p>dang / 'gred pa dang / rnam pa sna tshogs pa'i ngo bo du mas sdug bsngal brgya phrag du ma nyams su myong ba/ de dag gang du ji ltar zhi bar 'gyur zhes gsungs so/ /dgun gyi dus su rlung drag po dang ba mo mi bzad pas 'joms shing / dbyar gyi dus su nyi ma'i 'od zer tsha bas gdungs
<p>176a.7</p>par byed pa dang / phan tshun bsnyems shing 'chi ba'i 'jigs pas 'jig rten rnams la rtag par skrag pa'i dud 'gro log par ltung ba'i srog chags la/ 'di ji ltar chos kyi 'du shes skye/ de bas na gus par chos mnyan par bya ste/ phyis rjes su rnyed par mi 'gyur zhes bya'o/ /yang gang gi
<p>176b</p>
<p>176b.1</p>tshe bkres pa dang / skom pas gdungs shing lus bsregs pa'i rnam pa lta bu dang / mgrin pa dang / rkan dang / lce dang / mchu rnams skams shing / snying dang / mig dang / lag pa dang / rkang pa dang / khrag dang / sha dang / rus pa dang / gzhungs pa dang / rgyu ma dang / 
<p>176b.2</p>nang khrol rnams phyung ba lta bur skams pa dang / mchil ma dang / skyug pa zas su za ba mes bsregs pa lta bu'i lus kyi rnam pa dang ldan pa/ snang ba med pa'i mun par gnas pa/ mi gtsang ba zos pas gos shing spags pa lo brgya phrag du mar zas skom dang bral ba/ nyon mongs
<p>176b.3</p>ba rab tu 'bar zhing gcig la gcig gnod pas skrag cing sdug bsngal ba/ shing dang bong ba dang dbyig pas rdeg pas skom bzhin du bsrungs pas/ rim par dbang med par skom pas sdug bsngal ba/ bsod nams dman pa/ gdong rang gi skras g.yogs pa/ dur khrod mi
<p>176b.4</p>bzad par gnas pa/ lo brgya stong phrag du mar sdug bsngal brgya stong phrag du ma nyams su myong ba/ de dag dus gang du ji ltar zhi bar 'gyur zhes kyang gsungs so/ /bkres pa dang skom pas skams shing / lus me 'bar ba drag po'i rnam pa dang ldan pa/ sgal bu rnams
<p>176b.5</p>nang khrol gyis stongs pas ri'i khrod lta bu/ nang khrol nyams pas g.yo ba dang bral ba/ kha khab kyi mig ltar phra ba/ skra'i tshogs chen po rtsub cing gyen du brdzes pa/ dge ba cung zad kyang med pas/ mi dge bas yi dgas kyi 'jig rten du skye ste/ de bas na gus par chos
<p>176b.6</p>mnyan par bya ste/ phyis rjes su rnyed par mi 'gyur ro zhes bya'o/ /yang gang gi tshe mtha' khob tu skyes par gyur pa de dag kyang rab tu dran pa dang / gcugs pa dang / blo gros dang / rtogs pa dang bral bas spyod cing lo brgyar yang ltos pa med do/ /de dag dus gang
<p>176b.7</p>gi tshe zhi bar 'gyur zhes kyang gsungs so/ /yang gang gi tshe mtha' na gnas pa dang / gle na gnas pa dang / ri khrod dang / shul sa dang / par sig pa dang / d+ha ka pa dang / mu kha 'jab pa dang / kur pa pa dang / kha sha ba dang / ra ma tha ba dang / bug na ba dang / ci ra
<p>177a</p>
<p>177a.1</p>tha ba dang / tang ka na ba dang / la sha ba na dang / hor dang / ha das ga ba dang / nad ldan pa dang / ya ma na ba dang / a tra ba dang / dra ci la ba dang / rna can ba dang / tsin pa na dang / mi tshangs pa la sogs pa'i yul du skyes pas/ gang du bcom ldan
<p>177a.2</p>'das kyis nyan thos dus thams cad du mi rgyu bar 'di ltar de dag ni skyes bu'i gzugs tsam rten pa yin te/ dud 'gro'i skye gnas su song ba ltar bya ba dang bya ba ma yin pa ni mi shes so/ /khyi lta bur za ba dang / skrag pa dang / 'dod pa spyod pa mkhas pa'i 'du shes tsam mo/ /gzhan
<p>177a.3</p>yang spong ba'i rtog pa tsam dang ldan pa dang / rkyen gyis khro ba dang / nga rgyal dang / phrag dog dang ldan par spyod pa de dag dus gang gi tshe zhi bar 'gyur zhes gsungs so/ /mtha' khob pa'i yul na gnas pa gang yin pa mtha' khob tu skyes pa dge ba dang mi dge ba'i sems
<p>177a.4</p>mi shes pa'i mun pa dang ldan pa mtha' khob pa'i yul na gnas pa gang yin pa/ thos pa dang / dul ba dang / dka' thub pa dang / shes pa dang / sbyin pa dang rab tu spyod pa med bas/ dud 'gro rnams dang 'dra bar shes par bya'o/ /'di ltar 'di lta bu dang bral zhing mi'i gzugs
<p>177a.5</p>tsam du zad de chos mnyan par ji ltar nus/ legs pa'i blo gros dang bral zhing mi bzad pa'i mun pa dang ldan pa yin no/ /de bas na chos mnyan pa la gus par bya ste/ phyis rjes su rnyed par mi 'gyur ro zhes bya'o/ /yang gang gi tshe 'di ltar man+da ra ba'i rtse mor gnas shing lus
<p>177a.6</p>rgyas shing dga' ba dang / /mdzes shing gsal ba 'dod pa grub cing phun sum tshogs pa bsdus pa mchog tu gyur pa/ pad+ma dang ut+pa la sna tshogs pa'i mchog dang / shing sna tshogs pa'i mchog dang / shing sna tshogs pa'i dri ma bsil ba sna tshogs pa'i bya dang / ngur ba'i skad snyan
<p>177a.7</p>pa sgrogs pa dang / chu'i rgyun du drag tu 'bab pa/ skyed mos tshal nyams dga' bas brgyan pa/ 'dod pa'i khams kyi mthar thug pa 'dod pa rtse gcig tu byed pa'i bya bas rtag tu g.yengs pas phyag 'tshal zhing rab tu 'khod pa ni rol zhing rtsed mo'i spyod pa sna tshogs pa byed cing / lta
<p>177b</p>
<p>177b.1</p>ba'i bde ba du ma nyams su myong ba de dag dus gang gi tshe zhi bar 'gyur zhes kyang gsungs so/ /mtho ris kyi bud med dang dga' bas mtshams sbyor zhing / g.yeng ba de dang de dag gis rtse zhing / man+dA ra'i lha mo dang rol cing glang po dang dpa' bo'i pad+ma'i rten pa la zhon nas sum cu rtsa gsum
<p>177b.2</p>pa'i lha'i dbang po dang skyed mos tshal du dga' bas bag med pas chags pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi gsung bdud rtsi la myong bar ji ltar byed de de bas chos nyan pa la gus par bya ste/ phyis rjes su rnyed par mi 'gyur ro zhes bya'o/ /de yul dbus su skyes kyang lta ba dang mnyan pa dang / 
<p>177b.3</p>myang ba dang dbang po ma tshang bas/ glang po lta bur brdas mtshon pa dang / 'jig rten pa'i bya ba rnams la yang bya ba'i blo dang bral ba/ gang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i zhi bar dus gang gi tshe yang 'gyur zhes kyang gsungs te/ thub pa'i dbang po'i gsung ji ltar dbang po dang bral
<p>177b.4</p>bas nyan par nus/ thos pa'i sgo med pas byams pa dang / snying rje don du gnyer ba las log par gyur pa/ mi'i brjod pa dang bral bar gyur pa/ rang nyid kyis nyes par spyod pas bslus pa/ sems kyi glang po lcags kyu med pas dregs pa ma thul bas yan pa yin te/ de bas na
<p>177b.5</p>chos gus par mnyan par bya ste phyis rjes su rnyed par mi 'gyur ro zhes bya'o/ /gal te yul dbus su skyes su zin kyang / yang dag pa'i lta ba'i mig log par lta bas g.yogs pa'i blos sangs rgyas yongs su spangs shing / rgyu dang 'bras bu thams cad la skur pa 'debs pa dge ba'i rtsa
<p>177b.6</p>ba'i chos thams cad la mngon par dga' ba dang bral ba/ nyes pa thams cad kyi stobs kyis nad la gso ba mi byed pa lta bu'i bsam pa phyin ci log gi bya ba byed pas dmyal ba nyid do/ /de dag dus gang gi tshe nye bar zhi bar 'gyur zhes kyang gsungs so/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ma yin/ /
<p>177b.7</p>'gro ba thar bar smin mdzad pas/ /gang dag yid kyi phug gnas pa'i/ /rmongs pa'i mun chen mi sel ba/ /me khyer dang 'dra'i mu stegs rnams/ /log lta'i yid ldan de dag gis/ /sel bar nus pa ma yin te/ /nyi bdun gyis kyang sel mi 'gyur/ /de bas na gus par chos mnyan
<p>178a</p>
<p>178a.1</p>par bya ste/ /phyis rjes su rnyed par mi 'gyur ro zhes bya'o/ /bcom ldan thugs ni rnam rgyas pa/ /sangs rgyas nyi ma ma byung bar/ /nyi ma med par pad+ma bzhin/ /zla ba ma shar bar du ni/ /ku mu da yi nags bzhin du/ /gdul bya yi ni pad+ma rnams/ /rab tu
<p>178a.2</p>rgyas par 'gyur ma yin/ /mun pa yis ni mig bsgribs pas/ /rgyal po yi ni lam bzhin dang / /gru skya med pa'i gru bzhin dang / /tshong dpon spangs pa'i zong thogs bzhin/ /byang chub phyogs kyi chos rnams kyi/ /gru la kun nas ma zhon par/ /de ni rtse gcig sems kyis
<p>178a.3</p>su/ /rnam par grol ba'i dga' mi myong / /khro bral bla ma thar la mos/ /'chi med grong khyer mchog lta ba/ /nyon mongs kun gyi gnyen po ni/ /skad cig gcig la dmigs pa yis/ /zhi ba'i bde ba'i lam la sbyor/ /'gro ba'i nam mkha'i che dkyil du/ /sangs rgyas nyi ma ma shar
<p>178a.4</p>bar/ /bsgom spangs gdul bya'i pad+ma la/ /ye shes nyi mas rgyas ma yin/ /ngan 'gro'i dus ni thams cad du/ /chos smra ba yis gsal byas pas/ /gang zhig 'di la brten pa yi/ /'gro de dge ba'i bshes kyis thul/ /mi rnams thob par gyur pa ni/ /ri rtse glog 'gyu ltar
<p>178a.5</p>g.yo zhing / /khyogs lta bur ni g.yo ba dang / /mi bzad mi khom brgyad kyi rtser/ /rab tu 'jigs pa'i gza' yis ni/ /med pa las ni thar gyur cing / /'khor ba'i rgya mtshor gnas pa yis/ /sangs rgyas gsung ni rang bzhin gyi/ /dam chos gru la ma zhon par/ /gang zhig pha
<p>178a.6</p>rol 'gro 'dod pa/ /blo gros shin tu dman pa yin/ /mi yi skye ba 'bras bu med/ /mi khom pa brgyad kyi gtam slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI a dzi ta b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya 'od kyis
<p>178a.7</p>bsgyur//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ su b+hA Shi ta rat+na ka raN+Da ka ka thA/ bod skad du/ legs par bshad pa rin po che za ma tog lta bu'i gtam/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang gis glang chen mchog 'dra'i sems ni lcags kyus
<p>178b</p>
<p>178b.1</p>ma yin ye shes lcags kyus btab nas thul/ /'dod chags mun pa'i dmag tshogs me yis ma yin ye shes me yis ma lus bsregs/ /bdud kyi stobs rnams mtshon chas ma yin blo gros rab zhi bzod pa'i mtshon gyis zlog /gus la bsgom pa zhi mdzad sangs rgyas mkhyen pa rab rgyas thub
<p>178b.2</p>dbang de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dka' ba brgya yis rnyed pa yi/ /mi rnams thob pa'i khom pa dkon/ /zlog pa med pa'i 'chi bdag ni/ /rtag tu mdun na gnas pas na/ /gang gis dul sbyin yang dag sdom/ /rgyags tshags mang po ma bsdogs pa/ /mi bzad 'khor ba'i mya ngan du/ /
<p>178b.3</p>'gro ba de dag sdug bsngal thob/ /mi rnams thob pa rnyed dka' ba/ /bar snang glog 'gyu lta bu yin/ /srid pa zad byed mkhas pa yis/ /srid pa rnams su phan pa byas/ /yang dag mi nyid thob pa ni/ /glog dang rbab ltar mi brtan pas/ /yid bzhin nor bu lta bu yi/ /bsod nams rjes su
<p>178b.4</p>skyes bus bstan/ /da ltar mi rnams thob pa ltar/ /gang gi mthu yis phyis kyang thob/ /bsod nams mchog ni gang yin pa/ /de ni bde ba'i rgyu yin te/ /gzugs dang gtong ba rigs mtho sogs/ /yon tan sna tshogs ldan par 'gyur/ /bsod nams de nyid mdza' bo gcig /
<p>178b.5</p>'khor ba kun du 'gro ba gnyen/ /de ltar 'dir ni bsod nams kyis/ /phyi phyir yon tan phun sum tshogs/ /gang tshe dpal gnas thob bsten pas/ /de bsngags 'jig rten bdag po nyid/ /phan pa'i phyogs su 'dren byed pa/ /bsod nams de nyid spel bar gyis/ /bsod nams che
<p>178b.6</p>gyis sdig dga' spongs/ /yul la g.yo ba yid kyi rta/ /rtag tu phyin ci log zhi gyis/ /dug stobs mi bzad 'chi sbrul gyis/ /sos ma bzung ba'i bar du ni/ /rtag tu khyed kyis thub dbang bzhin/ /gzhan phan la ni mngon dga' gyis/ /bsod nams la spro ba bskyed pa'i gtam ste dang
<p>178b.7</p>po'o// //rgya mtsho gnya' shing bu ga ru/ /rus sbal mgrin pa chud pa bzhin/ /yud tsam 'dzom pa ngo mtshar che/ /mi brtan 'di la yang dag soms/ /rab tu zhi ba'i grong khyer lam/ /ngan song 'jigs pa 'joms byed pa/ /de ni thub pa'i dbang pos gsungs/ /skad cig tsam
<p>179a</p>
<p>179a.1</p>yang thos par dka'/ /mi khom brgyad kyi nyes spangs mi/ /gang zhig dkon la bskal ba brgyas/ /de ltar bde thob mkhas pa yis/ /dam chos mnyan la 'dir 'bad bya/ /dmyal ba yi dgas 'gro ba dang / /dud 'gro dbang po ma tshang ba/ /'chi med bla ma mtha' khob
<p>179a.2</p>skyes/ /log par lta ba sel ba dang / /thub dbang gsung rab bdud rtsi ni/ /skyes bu mkhas pas 'thung nus pa/ /shes rab 'od mnga' thub dbang ni/ /ma shar bar du yod ma yin/ /de phyir bya min spangs nas ni/ /bdag gi bya ba kun shes pas/ /'phags mchog dam chos
<p>179a.3</p>mnyan par bya/ /chos 'di la ni gang 'bad pa/ /de la yon tan kun yod 'gyur/ /thub dbang gsung las rin chen 'byung / /mkhas pa 'di yis thog mar dga'/ /de ni gang gis thos pas kyang / /rtag tu stobs ldan brling pa yis/ /mun pa'i tshogs ni 'joms par byed/ /
<p>179a.4</p>bsams shing bsgoms na mthar thug gsal/ /'jigs bcas skye ba 'khor ba'i rgyun/ /nyon mongs ma lus rim gyis spongs/ /thams cad phun tshogs rtag pa'i gter/ /mi bzad 'khor ba'i rgyun 'joms shing / /bla na med pa'i dga' bde thob/ /thos pas 'dir yid dri ma med/ /
<p>179a.5</p>de ltar thub dbang gsung 'di soms/ /chos nyan pa la spro ba bskyed pa'i gtam ste gnyis pa'o// //gang zhig thob nas 'khor ba yi/ /pha rol phyin pa'i sa bon bskrun/ /byang chub dpal gyi sa bon mchog /yid bzhin nor bu las lhag pa'i/ /yon tan rgyun gyi mi rnams ni/ /
<p>179a.6</p>su zhig 'dir de 'bras med byed/ /gang zhig dge bas phyug pa'i mi/ /bskal pa grangs med kyis thob nas/ /'dir ni rmongs pas bsod nams gter/ /cung zad tsam yang mi sogs pa/ /de dag 'jig rten pha rol du/ /mi bzad mya ngan khang par 'jug /rin chen gling phyin tshong pa ni/ /lag
<p>179a.7</p>pa stong par rang khyim bzhin/ /dge bcu las kyi lam med par/ /phyi nas yang ni thob ma yin/ /mi ma thob par de bar ni/ /ci ltar de bde sdug bsngal nyid/ /de las pha rol slus yod min/ /de las mchog tu rmongs pa med/ /'di 'dra'i khom pa thob nas ni/ /bsod nams
<p>179b</p>
<p>179b.1</p>tshogs ni mi sogs pa/ /skad cig gcig las sdig spyad nas/ /mnar med par ni bskal par gnas/ /skye ba du mar sdig spyad pas/ /bde 'gro dka' lta ci zhig smos/ /rgya mtsho cher g.yeng gnya' shing gi /bu gar rus sbal mgrin chud ltar/ /mi ni shin tu thob dka' bar/ /
<p>179b.2</p>de skad bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs/ /mi'i skye bo dkon pa'i gtam ste gsum pa'o// //zas skom mal stan gos mchog dang / /phreng ba gnas dang rgyan rnams dang / /grags pa yon tan khyad 'phags pa/ /de kun sbyin las 'byung bar gsungs/ /ngag
<p>179b.3</p>snyan mdzes dang longs spyod ldan/ /khyad par 'phags gzugs yangs pa dang / /tshig snyan gzi ldan yid 'ong dag /grags dang nad med tshe dag ste/ /yid 'ong sdug pa de dang de/ /sbyin pa rnams kyi 'bras bu ste/ /rta dang dar dang glang po dang / /rnga yab gdugs dang me tog tshogs/ /
<p>179b.4</p>khang bzangs mdzes dang rol mor bcas/ /sgra snyan rol mo dang ldan zhing / /me tog phreng ldan bud med dang / /zas dang rin chen phreng ba gnas/ /gur gum grong yul lha yi gnas/ /rdzogs sangs nyid dang sangs rgyas te/ /sbyin pa dpag bsam ljon shing gi /'di dag 'bras bu yin
<p>179b.5</p>par gsungs/ /ut+pal sngon po'i 'dab ma 'jam/ /dkyus ring dri ma med pa dang / /bud med gang zhig mig 'grub cing / /rked pa 'og pag g.yo bar ldan/ /dmar zhing mdzes pa'i gos ldan zhing / /nu 'bur rgyas par rnam par g.yo/ /smin ma mdzes dang ldan de dag /de
<p>179b.6</p>dag ser sna'i sgo phye nas/ /sbyin pa btang las rgyas par 'gyur/ /mgul ba rnga mas brgyan pa'i rta/ /bzhon pa kha lo srabs kyi skyogs/ /mi dbang glang chen dregs zhon nas/ /gdugs bsgreng rgyan ldan 'khor bcas dang / /'gro ba thal mo sbyar byas nas/ /rtag tu mchod cing gsol
<p>179b.7</p>'debs pa/ /snga mar 'di 'dra sbyin ba yi/ /'bras bu yin par thub pas gsungs/ /gser gyi gdu bu rdo rjes spras/ /dpung rgyan cod pan rin chen bkod/ /sa bdag mu tig phreng bas brgyan/ /rtag tu seng ge'i khri la gnas/ /'bangs sogs btsun mo'i 'khor bsten cing / /
<p>180a</p>
<p>180a.1</p>rtsed mo rtse bas rnam rol pa/ /seng ge lta bu'i rnam rol de/ /sbyin 'bras yin par thub pas gsungs/ /khang bzangs gser dang rin chen spras/ /gdugs dang rgyal mtshan bsgreng bas brgyan/ /pi wang rdza rnga rig byad sgrogs/ /rin chen rnams kyis 'od 'bar
<p>180a.2</p>ba/ /brgya byin bde sogs dga' spyod cing / /lha mo'i tshogs kyi 'khor ldan de/ /snga mar 'di 'dra byin pa yi/ /'bras bu yin par thub pas gsungs/ /sbyin ba skye bo'i yid du 'ong / /mkhas pa'i tshogs kyis rtag tu brten/ /phyogs rnams dri med phreng bas khyab/ /snyan pas gnas ni de
<p>180a.3</p>dang der/ /'dir ni dri med nye bar gnas/ /lus dang bral nas lha rnams su/ /rnyog bral sna tshogs btung ba bsil/ /me tog sna tshogs mgo lcogs rgyas/ /dpag bsam gyi ni shing rnams skyes/ /tsan+dan la sogs kyis gang ba'i/ /skyed mos tshal ni mchog rnams su/ /yun ring du
<p>180a.4</p>ni sde spyod cing / /lha mo gzugs mchog ldan pa yis/ /bsnyen bkur mchog tu byed pa 'thob/ /sbyin pa zhes bya gter chen de/ /rkun sogs mi 'khyer rjes su 'brang / /sbyin pas sems kyi ser sna dang / /chags pa'i rdul gyi dri ma 'khru/ /'khor ba'i lam gyis dub pa sel/ /
<p>180a.5</p>sbyin pa bzhon ba bde ba ste/ /sbyin pa bde ba du ma'i rten/ /yang dag grogs mchog bde ba'i sgo/ /rked pa gser gyi ska rags ldan/ /ngag 'jam zur mig bzhin skyob mdzes/ /mig gi dkyus ring rna drung gsan/ /me tog phreng bas skra bcings mdzes/ /gang zhig rang 'khor yan lag
<p>180a.6</p>dang / /rkang gnyis 'gro ba mdzes pa yi/ /zas gtsang gi ni phun sum tshogs/ /de dag sbyin pa'i 'bras yin zhes/ /bdag nyid chen pos bka' stsal te/ /sa sa ka ri'i dum bu dang / ut+pal gyis bsgos dri zhim la/ /bkra shis gser gyi snod du blugs/ /ban du ka dang zangs mdog
<p>180a.7</p>'dra/ /btung ba chung ma mna' skyel zhing / /chung ma dang bcas yang yang 'thung / /dga' ba'i bsam pas smra ba de'i/ /rgyu ni sbyin mchog bkra shis yin/ /zhi ba'ang sbyin pa'i yon tan te/ /mdzes pa 'dod pa bdag cag gis/ /sbyin pa 'di la 'bad par gyis/ /srid gsum mi bzad
<p>180b</p>
<p>180b.1</p>'jigs chen la/ /sbyin las gzhan pa'i gnyen mchog med/ /sbyin pa'i gtam ste bzhi pa'o// //'gro ba gang zhig mdzes yid 'ong / /gzugs dang rigs dang gnyen dang stobs/ /bde bar mthong ba gang yin pa/ /bsod nams bzo bos de byed par/ /'di skad
<p>180b.2</p>mkhas pa rnams kyis bshad/ /gzhan phan byed pa'i skyes bu yis/ /bsod nams dang mnyam yod ma yin/ /rim pa sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa'i/ /rgyal mtshan dkar po mngon mtho btsugs/ /rta glang rkang thang shing rta yi/ /dpung gi tshogs kyis nges 'khrug cing / /yu ba sna tshogs
<p>180b.3</p>mdzes pa yi/ /rnga yab rnams kyis g.yob byed la/ /bsod nams lhag pa dbang sgyur zhing / /sa rnams la ni spyod byed de/ /dar dang kA shi du gu la/ /sna tshogs gos dang mu tig phreng / /gser dang nor bus yan lag brgyan/ /gang dag lha 'dra'i skyes bu dpal/ /
<p>180b.4</p>bsod nams bzhon pa la zhon nas/ /de bas yin par shes par gyis/ /shin tu tshe ring rigs btsun zhing / /lus mdzes nad kyi 'jigs pa med/ /nor mang g.yog 'khor phun sum tshogs/ /bsod nams rnam smin chen po yin/ /gang yang 'khor los sgyur ba mchog /bu ni dpa' bo stong
<p>180b.5</p>dang ldan/ /rgya mtsho'i mtshams kyi sa la dbang / /de dag bsod nams rin po che'i/ /'bras bu yangs pa chen po yin/ /sna tshogs pad+ma'i stan la 'dug /lha dang lha dbang rtag phyag 'tshal/ /brjid kyis 'khor rnams zil gyis gnon/ /tshangs pa'i 'jig rten snang byed pa/ /de dag nyid kyang
<p>180b.6</p>bsod nams las/ /gang la lha klu lha min grub/ /dri za gnod sbyin mi'am ci/ /mchog tu gyur pa'i tshogs rnams ni/ /rtag tu lha dbang mchod byed pa/ /de ni bsod nams rin po che'i/ /'bras bu yangs pa chen po yin/ /gzugs dang brtson 'grus bzo rnams ni/ /dbang med spangs nas
<p>180b.7</p>mi rnams ni/ /las kyi rlung gis mngags nas ni/ /'jig rten pha rol 'gro ba na/ /bsod nams gcig pu mchog yin te/ /rjes su 'gro zhing bde ba 'char/ /bsod nams gzhan gyis 'phrog mi nus/ /de phyir bsod nams gter gyi mchog /gang gi stobs kyis ri rab kyang / /phyogs dang
<p>181a</p>
<p>181a.1</p>phyogs su rnam 'thor ba'i/ /'jig pa'i bskal pa'i rlung rnams kyis/ /ded kyang bsod nams 'jig mi nus/ /'jig pa'i bskal pa'i chu yis ni/ /lcags kyang dbang med 'jig byed pa/ /rgya mtsho bzhi yi chu rnams kyis/ /bsod nams bzhu bar nus ma yin/ /'od
<p>181a.2</p>zer rab tsha gsal ba yi/ /nyi ma bdun shar me rnams kyis/ /sa rnams sreg par byed mod kyi/ /bsod nams gcig pu sreg ma yin/ /bsod nams kyi gtam ste lnga pa'o// //sangs rgyas sku gzugs bzhengs gsol pa/ /dang por mya ngan sel par byed/ /rtsod pa
<p>181a.3</p>kun spangs mthong na dga'/ /skal ldan gter tshogs dpal dang ldan/ /lus stobs ldan zhing snyan pa dang / /gzi brjid ldan zhing gzugs mdzes la/ /gsung rab kun la mkhas gyur cing / /dbang po'i rta ni thams cad thul/ /blo ldan stong dang ldan par 'gyur/ /bcom ldan
<p>181a.4</p>sku gzugs mchod rten la/ /phra rab rdul ni ji snyed song / /de snyed sa 'og sa steng 'dir/ /de snyed rgyal por nges par 'gyur/ /gzugs dang gzugs med ting 'dzin 'grub/ /thams cad bde bar ma lus spyod/ /tha mar skye rga'i rgud spangs nas/ /de dag byang chub go 'phang thob/ /
<p>181a.5</p>bde gshegs sku gzugs bzhengs gsol ba/ /mtshan bzang gis mtshan 'khor los sgyur/ /sum cu gnyis ldan lus mdzes thob/ /nyes pa'i dgra 'joms rgyal bar 'gyur/ /dbang po rnams ni ma tshang med/ /dpal ldan ngan 'gro rnams las ring / /mi yi rigs su skye 'gyur
<p>181a.6</p>zhing / /ngag ni btsan pa nyid du 'gyur/ /skye bar thos dang dran ldan brtan/ /mngon par 'dod par 'byung 'gyur zhing / /gnas la mngon par dad pa dang / /'dod chags sogs kyis gnod pa med/ /'di rgyal rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyis/ /khyad 'phags legs pa'i gzhung
<p>181a.7</p>la brten/ /gang 'di rgyal ba'i sku gzugs bzhengs/ /sangs rgyas sku 'am mchod rten nam/ /bzhengs byed srog dang ldan pa de/ /bran dang dbul por mi skye zhing / /mngag gzhug par min rigs dman min/ /dbang po rnams ni tshang bar 'gyur/ /sku gzugs kyi gtam ste drug
<p>181b</p>
<p>181b.1</p>pa'o// //dri zhim sna tshogs kyis bsgos pas/ /bde bar gshegs la khrus gsol ba/ /me tog dri yis yan lag mdzes/ /rab tu dga' ba'i yid kyis su/ /rol mo'i sgra ni snyan pa yis/ /dal gyis 'bab dang stegs 'grun brjid/ /gser gyi rang bzhin pad+ma yi/ /
<p>181b.2</p>ge sar rdul gyis khyab pa ru/ /khrus gsol gang zhig mchod byed pa/ /de dag rnyog pa thams cad kyi/ /dri ma bkrus nas thar pa thob/ /lha yi bu mo nu 'bur rgyas mthong zhing / /rked pa yangs pa la 'bab g.yo ba dang / /'dzam bu'i gser 'dra'i pad+ma'i ge sar gyi/ /rdul rnams
<p>181b.3</p>gtor ba yis ni dri zhim la/ /dal gyis 'bab pa'i nang du lha yi tshogs/ /rgyun du chu rnams la ni rtse byed pa/ /gang zhig dga' ba sna tshogs dri zhim chus/ /rje btsun khrus gsol pa yi 'bras de yin/ /gla rtsi ga bur tsan+dan gur kum bsgos/ /dri zhim chu ni yid 'ong ba/ /kha dog dkar ser
<p>181b.4</p>bye brag gis/ /yid 'ong thub pa khrus gsol 'dir/ /sems kyi dri ma spangs nas ni/ /de ni 'gro ba'i bla mar 'gyur/ /khrus kyi gtam ste bdun pa'o// //khrus byed lha yi bu mo mchog /rked ldan brla dang nu ma rgyas/ /'dab skyes mgo lcogs rgyas 'thor zhing / /lha
<p>181b.5</p>dbang dal 'bab khrus byed cing / /mdzes shes 'dod pas g.yo ba ni/ /'gro mchog yang yang mnyes byas yin/ /de ni spos chu rol mo dang / /bdug pa dang ni me tog phreng / /sbyin pa btang ba'i 'bras bu yin/ /gang zhig 'khor los sgyur rgyal la/ /mkha' la gur kum sprin tshogs dang / /
<p>181b.6</p>ga bur gyi ni chu rgyun dang / /ma la ya yi tsan+dan bzhin/ /rdza rnga pi wang rnga mchog gi /bde bar gshegs mchog mchod byed pa/ /lha dang mi yi sgra rnams thos/ /khyad 'phags lha yi rna ba thob/ /gur kum la sogs pa'i gtam ste brgyad pa'o// //rta glang rkang thang shing rta dang / /rin chen
<p>181b.7</p>sna bdun rnams dang ni/ /dpa' bo bu stong dang bcas par/ /mkha' la 'khor los sgyur 'gro zhing / /zla ba lta bu'i gdugs kyis ni/ /nyi ma'i 'od zer sgrib byed cing / /'bras bu mang la rgya che ba/ /gdugs phul ba las byung ba yin/ /bung ba yid 'ong sgra yis bskyod/ /me tog g.yo ba
<p>182a</p>
<p>182a.1</p>'khor bar bkod/ /kha dog sna tshogs dri zhim pa'i/ /me tog tshogs kyis ri mor bris/ /gdugs mdzes sna tshogs dar gyis brgyan/ /mchod rten rnams la phul ba yis/ /'khor los sgyur ba sa skyong ba/ /gling bzhi'i dbang phyug de yis 'thob/ /nyi
<p>182a.2</p>ma'i 'od zer gser gdugs thogs/ /dpal ldan dul ba'i glang po mchog /rin chen du mas brgyan pa zhon/ /rdzu 'phrul brgya byin dang 'gran pa'i/ /gling bzhi yi ni 'khor los sgyur/ /sa rnams ma lus skyong bar byed/ /de dag bde gshegs sku gdung la/ /me tog gdugs
<p>182a.3</p>phul 'bras bu yin/ /gdugs phul ba'i gtam ste dgu pa'o// //bde bar gshegs pa'i 'khrungs gnas dang / /de yi yid tsam bzhugs pa'i gnas/ /rab tu gsal ba'i 'gram gyur pa/ /nus pa kun gyis gdung snod sku/ /shin tu khyad 'phags gtsug tor
