<p>182a.4</p>mtho/ /sku gzugs bzhengs nas legs sbyangs la/ /skye bo gang gis sku bzhengs pa'i/ /nang du ring bsrel bcug byas na/ /kun nas brgya byin las 'phags pa'i/ /mi dbang gling bzhi rnams su ni/ /dpal dang ldan pas longs spyod nas/ /mtha' ru rnam dag go 'phang thob/ /rgyal
<p>182a.5</p>ba'i sku gdung bcug las yin/ /zla ba dang 'dra blta na sdug /smin ma legs shing mig dkyus ring / /mir skyes gser dang nor bur ldan/ /bzod cing des pa dang ldan pa/ /rgya mtshos gtugs pa'i sa rnams ni/ /skyong byed 'khor los sgyur rgyal yang / /de dag sangs rgyas sku gzugs
<p>182a.6</p>ni/ /ring bsrel dang bcas gus pas 'thob/ /ring bsrel gyi gtam ste bcu pa'o// //bde bar gshegs pa mchog rnams kyi/ /pho brang mchog ni brgyan byed pa/ /gser gyi mdog dang ldan 'gyur zhing / /nad rnams kun las grol bar 'gyur/ /lha dang mi
<p>182a.7</p>las khyad 'phags shing / /nyi ma'i 'khor lo lta bur mdzes/ /nor dang gser ni mang ba dang / /rgyal po'i rigs kyi rgyal bar 'gyur/ /'jig rten gsum gyis mchod pa yi/ /sangs rgyas la ni gang zhig 'dir/ /maN+Dal me tog bcas byed pa/ /'gro ba'i bdag po tshe ring zhing / /
<p>182b</p>
<p>182b.1</p>sna tshogs nad kyi 'jigs las grol/ /gang yin de yis skad cig thob/ /bde gshegs maN+Dal byed de dag /pha rol phyin drug thob 'gyur te/ /chu dang sa bsres btang sbyin pa/ /grog mo sogs sel tshul khrims te/ /bsres nas nyes pa bzod pa yin/ /'bad pa byed pa brtson 'grus
<p>182b.2</p>yin/ /skad cig de las rtse gcig tu/ /sems 'dzin byed pa bsam gtan yin/ /legs par gzob pa shes rab po/ /sna tshogs bsod nams kyis brgyan la/ /sa gzhi bris pa 'bul byed pa/ /lha yi bde ba thams cad dang / /longs spyod mchog dang ldan 'gyur zhing / /mir skyes gser
<p>182b.3</p>las lhag pa yi/ /kha dog dang ldan mdzes pa dang / /pad+ma'i mdog ltar yan lag tshang / /mig ni dkyus ring mdzes par 'gyur/ /maN+Dal gyi gtam ste bcu gcig pa'o// //pad+ma'i 'dab 'dra'i lag pa mdzes/ /'od gsal kha dog dri bzang ldan/ /ro zhim reg na bde ba
<p>182b.4</p>dang / /lha dang mi yi khang bzangs na/ /'od gsal gser gyi gzhong pa ru/ /lha yi bdud rtsis bkang za ba/ /de dag sangs rgyas la sogs pa'i/ /dge 'dun yul du lhags pa la/ /zhal zas drangs pa'i 'bras bu yin/ /rdo rje gdan la bzhugs nas ni/ /'dod pa'i dgra dang bcas pa yi/ /
<p>182b.5</p>tshogs ni byams pas nges 'pham mdzad/ /gang zhig mthar thug dka' ba'i yul/ /mtha' med par ni spyod 'gyur ba'i/ /nyon mongs dka' ba'i dgra las rgyal/ /phung po'i bdud kyang rab bcom nas/ /'chi bdag bdud la mnga' brnyes pa/ /zhal zas phul bar gyur pas yin/ /ro rnams
<p>182b.6</p>bro ba'i mchog dang ni/ /yan lag tshang zhing yongs rdzogs ldan/ /bde zhing dpal ldan stobs dang ldan/ /tshe dang stobs dang kha dog dang / /gzugs bzang ba dang ldan pa ni/ /mkhas pas zas mchog btang las byung / /stobs dang brtson 'grus ldan pa yi/ /rnam grangs las ni nges
<p>182b.7</p>par rgyal/ /yang dag dpal thob mi dbang gis/ /ro ldan kha zas longs spyod pa/ /rtag tu zas mchog sbyin des yin/ /zas kyi gtam ste bcu gnyis pa'o// //g.yo zhing ut+pal gyis bsgos pa/ /dri med pad+ma rA ga bzhin/ /yid 'ong gser gyi snod du blugs/ /
<p>183a</p>
<p>183a.1</p>dri zhim tsan+dan gyis bsgos mngar/ /yid du 'ong dang bdar zhing 'thung / /cung zad mig ni zangs mdog 'dra/ /glu len sgra dang nges ldan pa'i/ /mi mchog de rnams skom rnams ni/ /sbyin pa byin pa'i 'bras bu yin/ /in+d+ra nI la bai DUr+ya/ /rin chen mchog rnams
<p>183a.2</p>kyis spras pa'i/ /gser gyi snod ni gang yin par/ /lha gang lha yi bu mo ni/ /brang gi dkyil na nu ma ni/ /bum pa lta bu'i 'bur ldan pa'i/ /rab mdzes gcugs dang lhan cig tu/ /sbrang rtsi ltar mngar btung 'thung ba/ /yon tan ldan pa'i tshogs la ni/ /btung ba yid 'ong byin pa yi/ /
<p>183a.3</p>'bras bu yin par mkhas rnams gsungs/ /gang zhig kha dog dri zhim sogs/ /tshogs ldan skom pa'i sdug bsngal sel/ /bad kan rlung drag rab zhi byed/ /kha ra pi pi ling bsres tshod/ /tsan+dan lta bur tsha ba sel/ /zla ba'i 'od zer dang ldan pa'i/ /snod du blugs nas de dag gis/ /gus
<p>183a.4</p>par dge 'dun la phul bas/ /pha rol gyi ni skye gnas su/ /lha yi btung ba thob par 'gyur/ /mngar zhim mngar mchog gus pa yis/ /btung ba tshogs mchog la phul bas/ /lha dang mi yi gnas rnams su/ /lha yi bu mo mchog rnams dang / /yun ring btung ba lhan cig 'thung / /gang zhig
<p>183a.5</p>sa gnas mi rnams kyis/ /dang ba'i dad pa'i yid kyis ni/ /dge 'dun la ni btung ba mchog /dus la bab par drangs pa yis/ /'khor ba'i ri khrod gnas pa ni/ /rtag tu btung ba'ang zhim bzang thob/ /btung ba'i gtam ste bcu gsum pa'o// //gang zhig sngo ser ljang dmar
<p>183a.6</p>dkar/ /sna tshogs kha dog 'od bzang ba/ /mdzes gsal gos kyi phreng ba ni/ /yon tan mchog dang ldan pa yi/ /'jig rten bla ma la phul bas/ /bsngags pa'i gos mchog thob par 'gyur/ /gang zhig dge 'dun mchog sogs la/ /gang zhig dad dang gus pa yis/ /gos kyi phreng ba 'bul
<p>183a.7</p>byed pa/ /de ni ngo tsha shes gos dang / /mchog tu gyur pa'i chos kyi gos/ /nyon mongs gnyen po'i chos gos 'thob/ /kha dog sna tshogs kyis spras pa'i/ /sngon po ser po dkar po dang / /gzhan yang dmar po yid 'ong ba/ /shin tu mdzes pa'i gos dag dang / /chos gos phreng ba 'bul byed pa/ /
<p>183b</p>
<p>183b.1</p>bde 'gro yi ni bde bar 'gro/ /gzugs dang ldan zhing yid 'ong la/ /lha yi gos ni zad med dang / /ngo tsha shes pa'i gos kyis brgyan/ /bdag blo ngang gis mkhas pa dang / /de ni chos kyi dbang phyug 'gyur/ /gos kyi gtam ste bcu bzhi pa'o// //me tog bzang po dge 'dun la/ /
<p>183b.2</p>rab tu 'thor zhing mchod byed pa/ /brgya byin las lhag longs spyod ldan/ /pad+ma'i dbang po lta bur mdzes/ /mchog tu grags pa dang ldan zhing / /rtag tu de ni skad cig gis/ /dgra las rnam par rgyal bar 'gyur/ /sa rnams la ni spyod byed pa'i/ /rin chen mchog gi mir gyur pas/ /
<p>183b.3</p>spos mchog dang ni dri bzangs kyis/ /rgyal ba rnams la 'bul byed pa/ /lus kyi grags pa'i dri yis khyab/ /ut+pal sngo dang mnyam pa yi/ /mig ni dri med dkyus ring mdzes/ /bai DUr+ya dang mu tig dang / /rin po che yis yan lag brgyan/ /lus kun ku sha'i gos kyis g.yogs/ /skye ba kun
<p>183b.4</p>du mi yi mchog /gzugs dang ldan par gyur pa ni/ /dge 'dun dri bzang phul ba yin/ /sna tshogs pa yi sman rnams ni/ /de dag dge 'dun la phul bas/ /mdze la sogs pa'i nad rnams kyi/ /sdug bsngal mi bzad pa las grol/ /bzhin ni mdzes shing gser rnams dang / /mnyam zhing kha dog
<p>183b.5</p>yid du 'ong / /rgyal po yi ni 'tshe ba rnams/ /gang yin pa dang bral ba thob/ /me tog la sogs pa'i gtam ste bco lnga pa'o// //sa bdag 'khor los sgyur gang la/ /thal mo sbyar ba byas nas ni/ /mkhur ba rna rgyan mdzes ltung bas/ /gus ldan legs par spyi bo yis/ /lan mang du ni
<p>183b.6</p>phyag byed pa/ /de dag sangs rgyas phyag byed pa'i/ /'bras bu yin zhes mkhas rnams smra/ /skyes pa tsam gyis gtsor 'gyur pa'i/ /rtag tu mthon po'i rigs skye zhing / /rta dang glang pos rgyu byed pa/ /de dag bla ma 'phags pa la/ /legs par phyag ni byas pas yin/ /snyan pa yis ni khyab 'gyur
<p>183b.7</p>zhing / /nges par legs par 'dzin pa dang / /gsal bar byed pa'i 'od kyis ni/ /sdug bsngal thams cad spong byed cing / /nad ni thams cad 'joms par byed/ /'jig rten du ni bde 'gror nges/ /mi dbang gis ni rgyun du 'gyur/ /'bras bu dpal dang ldan pa yang / /thub dbang phyag byas
<p>184a</p>
<p>184a.1</p>pa las yin/ /'khor los sgyur rgyal stobs grags ldan/ /yan lag sum cu gnyis mtshan ldan/ /rgyal 'gyur sa stengs gtso bo de/ /sangs rgyas la ni phyag byas pa'i/ /'bras bu yin par blo ldan gsung / /de ltar yon tan tshogs shes pas/ /lus 'di 'jig
<p>184a.2</p>par shes nas ni/ /mkhas pas sangs rgyas phyag bya zhing / /lus kyi las ni legs par spyad/ /phyag gcig 'tshal bar gyur pa yis/ /'khor ba spong ba'i rgyu thob cing / /'khor ba'i 'jigs mthong gus pa yin/ /de ltar su zhig phyag mi byed/ /phyag gi gtam ste bcu drug pa'o// //
<p>184a.3</p>kr-iSh+Na sa ra ltar mdzes gzugs/ /stobs ldan 'jam zhing shin tu snum/ /dgun dus bsro khang gos bzang bgos/ /yid 'ong mdzes ma la 'khyud nas/ /mi dbang gang zhig rtse byed cing / /ro mchog sna tshogs ldan pa ni/ /rin chen snod blugs 'thung ba ni/ /de dag sgron ma phul ba yis/ /shin tu
<p>184a.4</p>'bras bu mngon yin par/ /yang dag rdzogs sangs rin chen gsungs/ /'bar zhing me lce rgyas dang ldan/ /khang pa'i nang du me 'bar gsal/ /dgun dus grang ba sel byed pa/ /snang ba thub pa'i dbang po ni/ /mchog tu gyur la phul ba yis/ /lha dang mi yi 'jig rten na/ /gsal zhing rab tu
<p>184a.5</p>'bar gyur dang / /dri za lha min mi'am ci/ /byad bzhin mdzes dang lhan cig tu/ /ston zla dang 'dra rab mdzes pa/ /sdug pa pang bar 'khyud nas ni/ /lus ni yid du 'ong ba dang / /mtho ris su ni spyod byed pa/ /de dag gang tshe 'phags tshogs la/ /snang ba dang bas phul ba yin/ /rkun ma las
<p>184a.6</p>rgyal bzhon par ldan/ /sa rnams ma lus rjes su skyong / /byad bzang gser gyis yan lag brgyan/ /de dag gis ni snang ba rnams/ /phul ba'i 'bras bu 'di dag yin/ /snang ba'i gtam ste bcu bdun pa'o// //ri rnams kyis ni bsgribs pa dang / /mchog tu ring na gnas
<p>184a.7</p>pa dang / /shin tu phra ba'i dngos po dang / /mtshan mo smag gis bsgribs pa dag /gang tshe lag mthil gnas pa ltar/ /dge slong ma 'gags pa yis mthong / /de ni bde bar gshegs pa la/ /zhugs mar phul ba'i 'bras bu yin/ /spyan gyis dngos kun gzigs pa'i phyir/ /bde gshegs
<p>184b</p>
<p>184b.1</p>mar me phul ba yis/ /sangs rgyas nyid ni mnyes zhes grags/ /phul ba bcom ldan gang zhe na/ /thub dbang dri med spyan la phul/ /ring dang phra dang bsgribs pa dang / /dpag tshad kyis chod mthong la ltos/ /rgyal la zhugs mar phul ba yi/ /de 'bras yin par thub pas gsungs/ /sa
<p>184b.2</p>bdag rgyal po gang yin pa/ /zla ba lta bu'i gzugs ldan pa/ /ut+pal lta bur mig dkyus ring / /gang zhig lha yi 'jig rten na/ /gser mdog 'od kyis snang ba ltar/ /rang gi 'od kyis snang byed pa'i/ /'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po ni/ /nor bu brgya phrag 'od gzer gyis/ /sa rnams rgyu zhing
<p>184b.3</p>snang byed pa/ /de dag shAkya seng ge la/ /gus par mar me phul ba yis/ /rgya cher 'phel bar 'gyur ba yin/ /lha gang 'jig rten gsal byed cing / /ut+pal lha yi mig ldan la/ /smin ma legs shing gser mchog ltar/ /mig stong dang ni ldan pa yi/ /brgya byin lha yi bdag po nyid/ /lha yi
<p>184b.4</p>stan la 'dug pa dang / /gang zhig 'dod bral tshangs pa ni/ /'od gsal lha mchog phyag byed cing / /lha yi shing rta g.yo byed pa/ /ston pa yi ni ring bsrel la/ /mar me'i phreng ba mis phul pa'i/ /'bras bu rgya chen gyur pa yin/ /mar me'i gtam ste bco brgyad pa'o// //mi dbang dus
<p>184b.5</p>ni thams cad du/ /nyams dga' ba yi khang bzangs mchog /rol mo'i gnas kyi nyams dga' bar/ /'tsho zhing rgyal ba'i sgra sgrogs par/ /btsun mo'i 'khor dang rol byed pa/ /grang ba sel ba'i khang pa ni/ /phyogs bzhi nas ni byon pa yi/ /dge 'dun bzhugs gnas phul ba yin/ /
<p>184b.6</p>thub pa 'phags pa'i dge 'dun bcas/ /gtsug lag khang gi don du ni/ /tshig gis rab tu bskul ba dang / /tshogs pa yis ni grogs byed cing / /nges par dus su 'gro byed pa/ /gnyid log pa'am langs pa na/ /bsod nams rgyun ni tshad med 'phel/ /shes rab rdo rje'i mtshon cha yis/ /
<p>184b.7</p>phyin ci log gi ri bcom nas/ /sa dang bcas pa'i khang bzangs 'gyur/ /dge 'dun la ni yo byad dang / /longs spyod bzang po dang bcas pa/ /gtsug lag khang ni gang zhig byed/ /rnam par rgyal ba'i khang bzangs ni/ /rin chen mchog gi rang bzhin gyi/ /rtsig pa ka ba dang ldan pa'i/ /mdzes
<p>185a</p>
<p>185a.1</p>ldan lhan cig dus kun du/ /de ni lha yi 'jig rten 'dir/ /yun ring du ni mngon par dga'/ /dpal dang ldan pa'i bla re dang / /sna tshogs kyi ni gos kyis spras/ /khang bzangs mchog ni 'od 'phro ba/ /yang dag gnas par gyur pa ni/ /yon tan tshogs ldan phul ba
<p>185a.2</p>yis/ /brgya byin gyi ni khang bzangs mchog /rnam par rgyal byed thob pa yin/ /gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa'i gtam ste bcu dgu pa'o// //khyogs dang stan ni mnyam pa ru/ /'bol stan la ni chung ma ni/ /nu ma rgyas dang lhan cig tu/ /mal stan la ni sa bdag
<p>185a.3</p>nyal/ /nyes pa'i tshogs spangs dam pa la/ /de yis mal stan phul ba yin/ /rkang rten dang bcas khri la ni/ /sna tshogs gos kyis brgyan la 'dug /dbyangs snyan rol mo dang mgrin bsdebs/ /rin chen rang bzhin stan la ni/ /dri zhim pas ni byugs pa yi/ /dad ldan mal stan
<p>185a.4</p>chen po la/ /dpung pa la ni mgo brten nas/ /yun ring lha yi khang pa ru/ /'jigs pa med par bde bar nyal/ /de dag mal cha stan rnams ni/ /dge 'dun rnams la phul ba yi/ /'di ni 'bras bu yin par bshad/ /ga pur tsan+dan a ka ru/ /lus byugs pa yi lha mo ni/ /nu ma zung ldan lus brten nas/ /gos
<p>185a.5</p>mchog 'bol stan la rtag nyal/ /de dag mchod rten rnams la ni/ /gdugs dang gos khri phul bas yin/ /mal cha dang stan gyi gtam ste nyi shu pa'o// //gling bzhi las ni rnam rgyal nas/ /stobs ldan brgya byin gnas yin te/ /nga las nu yis sum cu gsum/ /bdag
<p>185a.6</p>po'i stan phyed dbang byas nas/ /'dod pa'i bde ba'i dga' ba myong / /zhag bdun bar du dbyig rnams kyi/ /char ni khang par dpag med phab/ /de dag lhung bzed du gtor ba'i/ /sbyin pa chen po de yi ni/ /'bras bu ngo mtshar chen po yin/ /snod ni de dang de dag gis/ /rgyu bzhi dag
<p>185a.7</p>la brten pa yi/ /sdug bsngal la sogs bye brag gi /'bras bu tha dad tha dad 'gyur/ /de phyir mi dbang khyad 'phags rgyal/ /zla ba lta bu'i bzhin dang ni/ /ut+pal lta bu'i kha dog dang / /mi rnams nang du rtag par ni/ /dri med mig ldan ro stod yangs/ /dga' zhing stan dang mal cha
<p>185b</p>
<p>185b.1</p>dang / /zas dang snod du ldan pa ni/ /mi rnams sbyin pas yang dag 'thob/ /mi mchog gis ni nad pa dang / /dman pa dang ni dbul ba rnams/ /snying rje can gyis sbyin btang bas/ /dpal ldan yang dag khyad 'phags 'gro/ /mi dbang brgya byin dang mnyam rtse/ /dga' zhing bu dang bran
<p>185b.2</p>g.yog bcas/ /zla ba dang 'dra bzhin gyi mchog /mig yangs lus ni nyi ma bzhin/ /grags pa snyan pa dag dang ldan/ /mi dbang dgra yi stobs 'joms shing / /bde ba thams cad thob pa ni/ /de yis rang gi bla ma dang / /pha ma rnams la sbyin las byung / /gang zhig rta dang shing rta glang / /
<p>185b.3</p>zhon la skye bo'i tshogs phyag 'tshal/ /gser gyi yu ba dang ldan pa/ /zla ba'i dbyibs dang ldan pa yi/ /nyi ma'i 'od zer zlog byed thogs/ /mi dbang mchog tu gyur pa ste/ /'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po ni/ /sa rnams dbang phyug dang bcas pa'i/ /gang zhig rgyal por gyur pa ni/ /yang dag zhing
<p>185b.4</p>la de dag gis/ /sbyin pa'i sa bon sbyangs pa yi/ /yon tan mchog gi 'bras de yin/ /dman pa'i snod la sbyin pa yis/ /mang du byin yang 'bras bu nyung / /yur ma tshor ma'i skyon bcas dang / /rdo ba'i steng gi zhing rnams la/ /sa bon mang po btab pa bzhin/ /'dod chags zhe sdang gti
<p>185b.5</p>mug spangs/ /yon tan gyis brgyan zhing la sbyin/ /nyung ngu byin yang mang du 'byung / /n+ya gro d+ha yi sa bon bzhin/ /zhing gi gtam ste nyi shu gcig pa'o// //gang gis chos kyi sbyin byin zhing / /bri ba dang ni nyan pa dang / /rtag tu de dag sems nyid dang / /gal te yang dag sgom byed
<p>185b.6</p>na/ /skye ba dran pa rtag tu 'thob/ /gang zhig lha yi 'jig rten na/ /dpag bsam gyi ni shing gi mchog /don rnams thams cad 'grub byed pa/ /lha tshogs bde ba'i mchog gyur pa/ /de ni ba mchog byin pa yi/ /rgya che ba yi 'bras bu yin/ /gang zhig mngal du rdzogs par ni/ /gtsang zhing yid 'ong ro myang la/ /mar dang sbrang
<p>185b.7</p>rtsi stobs dang ni/ /gang zhig 'o ma 'thung tshe yang / /pad+ma'i ge sar mdangs ldan pa/ /khu 'jo'i dus gang yin par 'thung / /skyed rdzogs nas kyang de bzhin te/ /bdud rtsi'i mchog kyang 'thung byed pa/ /de ni ba mchog btang las byung / /seng ge'i khri ni rab dga' zhing / /mdzes pa gus
<p>186a</p>
<p>186a.1</p>pas chos la ni/ /rim pa bzhin du des phul bas/ /gzhig par mi nus rdo rje'i gnan/ /rab mchog seng ge'i khri la gzhugs/ /lha klu grub pa phyag 'tshal 'gyur/ /gser gyi snod du rtag tu der/ /ro ldan 'o ma blugs nas ni/ /mi yi mchog ni 'thung byed cing / /dpal ldan
<p>186a.2</p>phun sum tshogs pa dang / /pad+ma'i mdog ldan bud med rnyed/ /de ni ma he mchog btang yin/ /rtag tu nad pa nyam chung la/ /bzhon pa mchog ni sbyin pa dang / /bla ma rnams ni mnyes byas nas/ /btsun zhing mi rnams kyis bstod 'gyur/ /gser gyi chas kyis brgyan pa yi/ /rta ni yid du 'ong ba la/ /
<p>186a.3</p>mi mchog rtag tu zhon nas rgyu/ /shin tu ring ba'i yul rnams su/ /rdzu 'phrul gyis ni 'gro byed pa/ /bzhon pa mchog ni phyin pa yis/ /de lta bu yi mi ru 'gyur/ /do shal dang ni do shal phyed/ /'og pag dang ni ldan pa yi/ /yid 'ong lha mo rnams la rtse/ /sum cu gsum bdag dang 'gran pa/ /
<p>186a.4</p>ltos pa med par byin pa las/ /byung bar mkhas rnams rab tu bshad/ /bdud kyis zil gyis mi non cing / /legs par gsungs pa rtag tu ni/ /bdud rtsi lta bur mnyan par gyis/ /sa gzhi lta bur chos kyi yum/ /nyon mongs dgra ni spong bar byed/ /'khor ba'i bde ba nyams myong zhing / /
<p>186a.5</p>phun sum tshogs pa thams cad kyi/ /rab mchog nyid ni thob par 'gyur/ /dub pa'i dus ni thams cad du/ /mkhas pas gnas ni phul ba yis/ /mtho ris phyin nas rtag tu dga'/ /brgya byin dang ni lhan cig tu/ /rtag tu dga' ba myong bar byed/ /'dir ni skyed mos tshal phul bas/ /sna
<p>186a.6</p>tshogs pa yi shing rnams la/ /me tog dri zhim dang ldan zhing / /mngon par mtho ba'i mi thob nas/ /skyed mos tshal rnams longs spyod ldan/ /chu bo rgal bar dka' ba yi/ /gnas su zam pa 'dzugs byed pa/ /mi de longs spyod dang ldan pa'i/ /mtho ris gnas su 'gro bar 'gyur/ /gser
<p>186a.7</p>mdog lta bu'i lus dang ldan/ /nyams dga' rdzing bu byed pa'i mi/ /mtho ris gnas ni thob par 'gyur/ /'jig rten 'di ru mir gyur nas/ /rgyal po yi ni dga' bde thob/ /khron pa dang ni bu nyen khang / /sems can rnams ni rten pa dang / /than pa grang ba skyob gyur pa/ /byed pa'i
<p>186b</p>
<p>186b.1</p>mi mchog gang yin pa/ /lha yi bde ba myong bar 'gyur/ /nyi ma'i 'od zer tsha ba yis/ /shin tu sdug bsngal ldan pa la/ /gang zhig gdugs ni sbyin byed pa/ /gdugs dang 'dra bar de dag ni/ /dgra yi tshogs las rgyal 'gyur zhing / /rtag tu bde ba mchog dang ldan/ /mchil lham
<p>186b.2</p>rgyan gyis brgyan pa ni/ /sems can thams cad dag la ni/ /gus pa yis ni sbyin byed pa/ /de dag bzhon pa mchog rnams la/ /lha dang mi yi 'jig rten du/ /yun ring zhon par skye bar 'gyur/ /yon tan rnams ni sgrogs pa yis/ /rgyal ba mchog gi stod byed pa/ /thams cad
<p>186b.3</p>dag ni btud pa yis/ /lus kyis phyag ni 'tshal byed pa/ /bla mar brten pa'i rigs skye zhing / /de dag so sor rig pa 'thob/ /rdza rnga pi wang pa Ta has/ /bde bar gshegs mchog mchod byed pa/ /mir gyur nas ni dbyangs snyan la/ /sgra ni shin tu snyan par 'os/ /yid du 'ong ba'i
<p>186b.4</p>gzugs dang ldan/ /bde bar gshegs pa'i mchod rten la/ /dga' bas srog dang 'dzugs byed cing / /gdugs dang dril bu rnams dang ni/ /gdugs kyi phreng ba 'bul byed pa/ /de dag mir ni rgya che zhing / /dpal ni phun sum tshogs pa 'thob/ /mir gyur pa ni ma lus pa'i/ /bdag
<p>186b.5</p>po nyid ni stobs dang ldan/ /dpung rgyan mu tig rgyan ldan pa/ /sa rnams sbyin par btang ba las/ /yin pa ru ni mkhas pa 'chad/ /mchod rten dang ni rgyal ba yi/ /sku mchog rnams ni bzhengs byed pa/ /gdugs ldan sku gdung 'dzug byed pa/ /mtho ris yang dag 'dir thob nas/ /mi
<p>186b.6</p>rnams kyis ni bstod par 'gyur/ /gang zhig dang por sangs rgyas la/ /sa dang lci bas byugs nas ni/ /me tog 'bras bu zas skom phul/ /rtag tu mchod pa byed pa ni/ /rgyal po'i mchog ni thob par 'gyur/ /rgya chen mar me sna tshogs dang / /dri zhim me tog bdug pa dang / /bu ram
<p>186b.7</p>la sogs btung ba rnams/ /dge 'dun la ni 'bul byed pa/ /de yang nor dang ldan 'gyur zhing / /lha mi'i bde ba dag dang ldan/ /mchod rten gdung bcas gtsug lag khang / /mi gang 'bad pas nyen 'khor 'phyag /kun nas dri ma med byed pa/ /gser gyi kha dog 'dra bar 'gyur/ /rtag
<p>187a</p>
<p>187a.1</p>tu snang ba 'dul byed cing / /grang dus gos dang khang pa dang / /rgyan dang bu mo btung ba byin/ /skye gnas rnams su bde ldan 'gyur/ /sa stengs su ni tshe ring zhing / /thams cad nad las grol bar 'gyur/ /mnyam pa med pa'i bde ba thob/ /de dag rtag tu bde dang ldan/ /
<p>187a.2</p>lha yi bde ba sna tshogs pa/ /nyams su myong zhing 'byung 'gyur ba/ /srog gcod spangs pa las yin par/ /nges par mkhas pa rnams kyis bstan/ /gzhan mthong brnab sems mi byed pa/ /chom rkun las ni dben gyur cing / /rdzas ni yongs su srung bar byed/ /gser dang dpag med phun
<p>187a.3</p>tshogs thob/ /rkun ma brgya phrag dag gis ni/ /mi dbang las ni 'bral mi nus/ /chung ma gzhan la mi 'phyo zhing / /legs srung chung ma mnyam med rnyed/ /skye bar dgrar gyur cung zad med/ /'dir ni 'jig rten yid rton cing / /de la yid mi ches yod min/ /de dang der ni skye ba na/ /
<p>187a.4</p>ut+pal sngon po lta bur ni/ /dri ldan yid du 'ong ba'i gzugs/ /de ni mi 'gyur kha dri zhim/ /brdzun gyi tshig kyang smra ma yin/ /dam pa yi ni grogs ldan zhing / /mi dbang gis ni gus pas mchod/ /bu dang chung ma bran dang ni/ /longs spyod rgya ni chen po yis/ /dpag tu med pa'i bde thob pa/ /
<p>187a.5</p>rtag tu phra ma spangs pas yin/ /yid du 'ong zhing sgra snyan la/ /ngag ni snyan par 'os pa dang / /rtag tu shin tu mdzes pa dang / /mi rnams dang ni lha rnams su/ /de rgyal tshig ni rtsub mo dag /mi de yis ni spangs pas yin/ /chos don dben pa dga' ba yis/ /smra ba de ni 'jig rten gyi/ /rtag
<p>187a.6</p>tu mchog tu yid 'ong 'gyur/ /yang yang mchod pa de yis thob/ /rin chen mang dang bzhon pas phyug /mngon mtho 'jig rten sna tshogs pa'i/ /bde ba mtha' yas myong bar 'gyur/ /bdag gzhan chags pa spangs pa yis/ /de 'dir 'dod chags chung 'gyur zhing / /rtag tu longs
<p>187a.7</p>spyod rgya chen ldan/ /ngag la dbang zhes grags ldan 'gyur/ /rab tu mdzes pa nyid thob cing / /de ni rtag tu phyug cing bde/ /rgyal srid kyis mtho 'jig rten gyi/ /tshangs pa nyid ni thob 'gyur zhing / /yang dag byams pa'i sems ldan pa/ /dbang po yod pa'i mi ru skye/ /mtho ris thar 'bras
<p>187b</p>
<p>187b.1</p>bde ba thob/ /yang dag rdzogs dang mi de ldan/ /gang phyir 'di dag thams cad ni/ /yang dag lta ba mchog tu ni/ /dge ba'i rtsa ba'i 'bras bu yin/ /dad dang blo gros dang ldan pa'i/ /bsod nams kyi ni zhing mchog las/ /sa gsum bde ba rgya chen skye/ /de lta'i khyad par mi shes pas/ /
<p>187b.2</p>yon tan rin chen thams cad kyi/ /gter du gyur pa'i dad pa ni/ /rtag tu de yis brtan par bya/ /dad pa yis ni ma bzhin du/ /bde ba rnams ni bskyed par bya/ /de bas thog mar skyes bu yi/ /yid kyis legs par bsten par bya/ /'byung gnas dad pa spangs pa yis/ /dam chos rin
<p>187b.3</p>chen byang chub mchog /nges par gzung bar nus ma yin/ /rgyal po las ni nyams pa yis/ /longs spyod 'bras las nyams pa ltar/ /dad pa'i dbang po las nyams na/ /de bzhin 'bras rnams thob ma yin/ /de phyir skyes bu mkhas pa ni/ /'jig rten bde gshegs byed 'dod pas/ /
<p>187b.4</p>yid ni rab tu dad pa yis/ /rtag tu phan pa nyid du gyis/ /lhag mas nyes pa zhi ma yin/ /gzhan du dad pa dang ldan pa'i/ /nyes pa'i tshogs ni thams cad bsreg /dman zhing gos med rmongs pa dang / /lag pa na ni thod pa thogs/ /'jig rten 'di na slong ba snang / /sbyin ba med pa'i
<p>187b.5</p>'bras la ltos/ /tha dad khyim du slong zhing rgyu/ /rtag tu bkres par kun du 'khor/ /gang zhig lus las lag rkyong la/ /khyi dang 'dra bar ring na gnas/ /kun du 'jug cing slong ba la/ /phyir log nyung shas cha gcig kyang / /gang zhig kha zas mi ster ba/ /kha ni khab tsam lto ba ri/ /lus
<p>187b.6</p>skam skra yi gos kyis ni/ /nyi ma'i 'od zer snang min la/ /yi dgas skom gyis gdungs pa rnams/ /'bras de lag gis ma byin cing / /dus ma byin pa'i 'bras bur gsungs/ /sna tshogs bsdus pa'i gtam ste nyi shu gnyis pa'o// //bsod nams spro ba bskyed pa mnyan par
<p>187b.7</p>gyis/ /gtong dang bsod nams dkon pa ste/ /bde bar gshegs pa'i sku gzugs la/ /sku gdung rnams ni bcug byas na/ /khrus gsol gdugs ni 'degs pa dang / /maN+Dal zas dang skom rnams dang / /gos dang me tog la sogs dang / /snang ba dad ni mar me dang / /gtsug
<p>188a</p>
<p>188a.1</p>lag khang du mal stan dang / /zhing dang sna tshogs phul nas ni/ /bstod cing phyag ni 'tshal byed pa/ /'di 'dra du ma phun sum tshogs/ /gtam ni nyi shu rtsa gnyis kyis/ /yang yang sbyin pa'i bsngags pa brjod/ /mtsho ni sbrul gyis gang bzhin du/ /me tog lo ma
<p>188a.2</p>rgyas pa yi/ /ljon shing tsher ma dang bcas bzhin/ /thos dang dpyod dang rigs ldan zhing / /de lta bu yi bye brag can/ /tshul khrims la ni rgyab phyogs yin/ /dbul yang khrims ldan mchog yin gyi/ /yon tan rgyan dang bral ba yi/ /nor ldan rnams dang mtshungs ma yin/ /dbul yang
<p>188a.3</p>skyes bu dam pa rnams/ /de dag yon tan ro myang bas/ /bdud rtsi lta bur khyad par 'phags/ /yang dag dran bya bla ma bzhin/ /yon tan ldan 'phags gzi brjid ldan/ /nor rnams dang ni rgyan dang ni/ /de dag rgyal po rnams kyis ni/ /drung du nye bar mchod 'dod pas/ /tshul khrims
<p>188a.4</p>'di ni bsrung bar gyis/ /'jig rten bde ba rnams rgyal ba'i/ /'jigs dang zhe sdang bcas pa la/ /chos kyi bdag nyid blo byas te/ /bde ba mchog ni skyes bu yis/ /bde ba rgya chen mi 'phrogs pa/ /thob par 'dod pa de yis ni/ /tshul khrims nyid ni srung bar gyis/ /tshul khrims las
<p>188a.5</p>nyams 'dul zhing 'tshe/ /de yis 'jigs bcas nyams su myong / /tshul khrims ldan la de dag med/ /de nas 'jig rten pha rol du/ /mtha' yis gtugs shing 'gro ba na/ /bde ba'i yul rnams 'dod pa yin/ /de yi tshul khrims 'di nyid srung / /tshul khrims brten dang nges ldan na/ /
<p>188a.6</p>bde 'gro nyon mongs bdag nyid min/ /log par lta bas lam gol phyir/ /de phyir thar pa rab byung zhing / /rtags ldan mtho ris 'dod pa yis/ /de yis tshul khrims 'di nyid srungs/ /mi 'jig dbrog tu med pa'i rgyan/ /tshul khrims 'di yin bsrung bar gyis/ /tshul
<p>188a.7</p>khrims nor gyi mchog yin te/ /gzhan gyis dbrog cing rkur mi tshugs/ /tshul khrims brtan te 'chi ba na/ /gzhan du rjes 'brang lus ma yin/ /tshul khrims rjes su 'brang ba'i grogs/ /tshul khrims rgyan gyi mchog yin te/ /rgyan de la ni stor ba med/ /yid gcugs
<p>188b</p>
<p>188b.1</p>pa yi grogs po yin/ /tshul khrims lta bu'i phan byed med/ /tshul khrims yang dag nges pa'i gnyen/ /pha dang ma dang bu yin te/ /'dod pa ster ba tshul khrims te/ /mthu yis 'bras bu 'di sbyin byed/ /tshul khrims kyi gtam ste nyi shu gsum pa'o// //bskal pa
<p>188b.2</p>stong du bsags pa yi/ /sbyin dang bder gshegs mchod la sogs/ /legs spyad gang yin de kun yang / /khong khro gcig gis 'joms par byed/ /zhe sdang dang mnyam sdig pa med/ /bzod dang mnyam pa'i dka' thub med/ /de phyir 'bad pas bzod pa sgoms/ /sna
<p>188b.3</p>tshogs pa yi tshul gyis ni/ /zhi ba'i yid kyis ma bzung na/ /dga' dang bde ba myong ma yin/ /sdong ba'i zug rngu yid gnas la/ /gnyid med brtan pa yod ma yin/ /zhe sdang bral bar ma gyur na/ /ji srid 'tsho bar gnod dang bcas/ /khro ba gcig pu bcom pa yis/ /rnam par sdang ba
<p>188b.4</p>thams cad bcom/ /rtog pa'i bud shing la mched pa'i/ /khro ba'i me yis 'gro ba bsreg /dang por bdag nyid sreg byed la/ /gzhan dag sreg pa 'am yang na min/ /rgas pa yis ni gzugs bzhin dang / /khros dang mun pas mig dang ni/ /blo dang bral bas 'dod don ldan/ /de
<p>188b.5</p>bas khro ba 'joms par byed/ /dge ba'i las la 'di sbyar bya/ /bdag la gnod byed 'byung ba dang / /de las bzlog par bya snyam na/ /sdig ldan sems yin khror ci yod/ /mtshon sogs byed pa spangs nas ni/ /'phen pa ci zhig khro ru yod/ /rtsod byed zhe sdang yin pas na/ /de phyir
<p>188b.6</p>zhe sdang la sdang bsngags/ /bzod pa'i gtam ste nyi shu bzhi pa'o// //yon tan rin chen thams cad kyi/ /gter du gyur pa brtson 'grus te/ /nyon mongs rgya mtsho kun sgrol ba'i/ /rgya chen mchog ni brtson 'grus yin/ /brtson 'grus shing rta gang zhon pa/ /dngos po
<p>188b.7</p>bsams pas mi thob pa/ /de 'dra 'gro na yod ma yin/ /glang po rta dang rkang thang dang / /mda' dang mda' chen dgra sta dang / /mtshon cha yis ni g.yul 'gyed cing / /dgra bgegs mthar ni rgyal byed pa/ /'di de stobs dang ldan pa yi/ /brtson 'grus dpa' bo chen po yin/ /rgya
<p>189a</p>
<p>189a.1</p>mtsho chu srin tshogs gnas shing / /chu rlabs mthon por rim rgyu ba/ /brtson 'grus ldan pa'i dpa' bo yis/ /ba lang rjes bzhin 'gom par byed/ /rin thang med pa'i rin chen gyi/ /gter ni len par byed pa yin/ /'dod chags la sogs sbrul gdug rnams/ /lus la brtson
<p>189a.2</p>'grus can gyis spongs/ /khrims ldan skye bo dam pa ni/ /sems ni dri med khyad 'phags pas/ /mir ni yang dag mnyam gzhag 'dzin/ /ri rab mdzes pa'i rtse mo ru/ /blta na sdug pa'i lha mo la/ /pang du lag pas 'khyud pa yi/ /bde dang ldan zhing dga' bar byed/ /mkha' gnas lha ni gang yin
<p>189a.3</p>pas/ /gnyis gnyis ldan pa nges spangs nas/ /yang dag nyid kyi bde ba myong / /shin tu 'bras bu rgya che ba'i/ /bskyed pa'i rgyu ni brtson 'grus te/ /bstan pa la sbyor de sbyor byed/ /brtson 'grus kyi gtam ste nyi shu lnga pa'o// //nyon mongs dgra yi sde tshan rnams/ /bsam gtan
<p>189a.4</p>ldan pas zil mnan nas/ /yang dag byang chub dpal rnams thob/ /byang chub yan lag rab sbyin zhing / /'chi med skye ba'i rgyur gyur pa/ /'dod chags zhe sdang la sogs pa/ /nyes pa thams cad sel ba yi/ /rgyu ni bsam gtan yin pa ru/ /blo ldan de yis rab tu gsungs/ /nam mkha'
<p>189a.5</p>dang ni sems mnyam la/ /gser dang bong par mnyam pa yi/ /bsam gtan sgom byed skyes bu yi/ /yon tan rnams kyi rgyu ru gsungs/ /nyon mongs dgra tshogs las rgyal ba'i/ /dge ba'i stobs kyis bsgrub pa las/ /mtshan ni thams cad ldan pa yi/ /yang dag rdzogs pa'i byang
<p>189a.6</p>chub dpal/ /yon tan rab mchog bdag nyid can/ /dkon pa'i rigs pa thob par 'gyur/ /sems la ye shes chen po yis/ /dgra yi 'jigs pa rnams spangs nas/ /gang gis mi yi dbang po bskyed/ /bsam gtan gcig bu de rgyu ste/ /yon tan kun gyi gter yin pas/ /'phags
<p>189a.7</p>pa'i yon tan gyis phyug gsung / /rmongs pa'i mun pa sel mdzad cing / /rgyun gyis rtag pa'i ye shes kyis/ /rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi nyi ma dang / /mi rnams dang ni lha rnams kyi/ /bde rgyu bsam gtan rab mchog yin/ /bsam gtan gyi gtam ste nyi shu drug pa'o// //shes rab
<p>189b</p>
<p>189b.1</p>stobs dang bral na yang / /skyes bu'i gzugs brnyan 'ba' zhig ste/ /snying po spangs pa'i mthar thug par/ /ri mo bris pa'i gzugs dang mtshungs/ /blo ldan brtson 'grus yang ldan pa'i/ /blo ldan de la 'bras 'dod 'byung / /bla med bdag gsod pa yi dgra/ /skye ba du mas gang chod dang / /bdag
<p>189b.2</p>nyid skye bar 'gyur ba yis/ /rigs dang ming dang rus rnams dang / /dbus bzhin du ni mtha' bzung la/ /rnal 'byor pa yi shes pa 'jug /shes rab stobs kyis de shes gsungs/ /'jig rten rnams ni dri mi yi/ /rab rib tshogs ni sel byed pas/ /de bas blo de chos mchog yin/ /ye shes
<p>189b.3</p>snang ba skyed pa yis/ /mi rnams kyi ni nyes pa'i tshogs/ /rtag tu stongs par byed pa yin/ /dang por dbang po 'di bsgrub bya/ /yid kyis phra rab rnam shes shing / /rig pa thams cad gsal byed yin/ /shes rab de yang rtag par ni/ /stobs kyis dge ba skyed byed pa'i/ /rgyu yin
<p>189b.4</p>par ni rtag tu grags/ /bya ba'i rgya mtsho'i nang du ni/ /gdon mi za bar nub pa dang / /g.yul gyi nang du shes rab gtso/ /shes rab stobs kyis rnam rgyal thob/ /thos pa'i shes rab gang yin de/ /dge ba rnams kyi rgyu ru 'gyur/ /de ltar yon tan thams cad ni/ /sgrub par byed pa
<p>189b.5</p>yin pa'i phyir/ /gdon mi za bar shes rab sgrubs/ /shes rab med pa'i skyes bu ni/ /mi gsal tho rangs mar me bzhin/ /shes rab kyi gtam ste nyi shu bdun pa'o// //mtho ris thar pa'i yon tan ni/ /rin po che yi gter gyur pa/ /pha rol phyin pa drug 'di nyid/ /sa
<p>189b.6</p>gzhi bzhin du shes pa'i mis/ /bdag phan bsgrubs pa de yis ni/ /gzhan la phan par bya ba'i phyir/ /myur bar rtag par rgyun du 'bab/ /pha rol phyin pa'i gtam ste nyi shu brgyad pa'o// //legs par bshad pa rin po che za ma tog lta bu'i gtam snyan dngags
<p>189b.7</p>mkhan chen po slob dpon dpa' bos mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po ru dra dang / dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur/ /[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ tsa tu rbi paR+Ya ka thA/ bod skad du/ phyin ci log bzhi spang ba'i gtam/ 'jam dpal
<p>190a</p>
<p>190a.1</p>gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /skyes bu dam pa yid 'ong yul rnams yongs smod smra bar gyur pa na/ /de la yid 'byung skyo bar byed na khyed yid skyo bar cis mi byed/ /khyed kyi lus sdug de yang nyes mang de la smad par byas pa ni/ /yon tan mang yod de phyir bdag gi
<p>190a.2</p>tshig ni cung zad mnyan par gyis/ /'di ni rtag par gyur tam mi rtag gyur kyang ji srid gyur pa 'di ni bde ba'i don gyur tam/ /der ma gyur kyang gtsang bar gyur tam de med gyur kyang dbang yod gyur/ /rtag min bde ba'i rgyu min gtsang ba ma yin rang dbang can min na/ /ci phyir blo gros rab nyams khyed lus
<p>190a.3</p>nyes brgyar bcas la chags byed smros/ /ri bo mthon po'i rtse mo'i steng nas sa la lhung bar gyur pa yis/ /zhig par gyur tshe ci 'di bar snang la ni bde ba myong gyur ram/ /skyes nas brtsams te 'chi ba nyid phyir rtag tu rab tu rgyugs pa na/ /sems can rnams ni bar skabs gang du bde ba ji ltar thob
<p>190a.4</p>par 'gyur/ /gang gis sa 'og 'dzul te klu yi dbang po pad+ma'i rtsa ba ltar 'byin byed/ /gang gis mtho ris 'dzegs te dbang por bcas pa'i lha tshogs med par byed pa dang / /gang gis sa stengs 'phyan 'phyan ni ga dang ni ra gu na la btus 'gyur ba'i/ /'chi bdag des mi tshugs par gang du gnas nas
<p>190a.5</p>khyed ni 'jigs med 'gyur/ /yun ring 'tsho yang lus ni rgas pas rab tu rnyings pa nyid du 'gyur/ /tshe ni thung 'gyur tshe ni mod la 'chi bdag khar ni 'gro bar 'gyur/ /rga dang 'chi ba'i bar na phongs par bcas par gnas par gyur pa'i mi/ /nyam ngar lhung bas 'di dang 'di las bde ba thob par yod
<p>190a.6</p>mi 'gyur/ /byis pa rnams la brtse med rgan la gus par gyur pa cung zad med/ /gzhon nu ma la ngor lta phra mo med cing nyam thag rnams la brtse med pa/ /de ltar gzhung lugs med pa'i 'chi bdag gang yin de ni bdag la ni/ /dus la sdod ces gzhon lus sha rgyas sra bar khyed yid ma sems cig /
<p>190a.7</p>khyim drung gnas pa'i nor ni cung zad rkus zhes thos par gyur pa na/ /rang gi khyim dag bsrung bar bya snyam sems pa 'di ni rigs pa yin/ /mi ni khyem khyem dag nas nyin re drangs te khyer bar byed pa na/ /gshin rje la ci dogs med gyur tam 'gro ba mel tshe cis mi byed/ /ji ltar gsad bya'i me tog phreng
<p>190b</p>
<p>190b.1</p>btags sil krol mis bskor te/ /gsod sar khrid la gom pa re re bor bas 'chi nye'i sdug bsngal 'gyur/ /de bzhin longs spyod la gnas nyin re 'chi bdag drung du 'gro byed kyis/ /kye khyed 'byor pa dag gis yid ni dregs pa dag tu ma byed cig /'di ni mi rnams tshe ni mchog tu ring yang lo
<p>190b.2</p>brgya kho nar zad/ /de las kyang ni dang po byis pa tha mar rgas pas don mi byed/ /gnyid dang nad sogs dag gis de dus med par kun nas re ba 'joms/ /bde bar gnas pa'i mi nang 'gro ba'i tshe yi lhag ma ji tsam yod/ /sum cu rtsa gsum bdag po'i g.yul las rgyal ba'i rgyal po de rnams ni/ /
<p>190b.3</p>shes pa'i snang bas mun pa zad byas drang srong de yang shi bar 'gyur/ /gshin rjes zin par gyur tshe longs spyod kyis min bshes pa dag gis min/ /skyes bu rtsol bas zlog mi byed na 'dir ni mi rnams su la ji ltar skyabs su 'gro/ /bstan bcos klags dang bcas shing rig dang bzo yi bya ba dang
<p>190b.4</p>bcas dang / /yid rton grogs bcas sdug pa'i chung ma dang bcas drung gnas 'khor bcas pa'i/ /mi rnams 'chi bdag snying rje med pas sa stengs 'dir ni khyab 'gyur bas/ /med par byed na kun gyis ci bya ma yongs dge ba legs par gyis/ /e ma'o skyes bu rmongs rnams 'di na bde 'gror skyes
<p>190b.5</p>pa bzang zhes grags/ /rga dang 'chi dang na rnams kyis kyang 'di la brtse ba med par grags/ /gzhan las skyes pa'i sdug bsngal brgya phrag 'di dag skyes pa nyid byed de/ /rang gis bskyed nas bu ni gsod pa'i don du de dag la stod byed/ /sha ma'i rkyal par shin tu bsdams shing dbugs ma phyin
<p>190b.6</p>par nyam ngar gnas/ /mi gtsang khron par lto ba'i me yi tsha ba mi bzad pas bsregs nas/ /smra mi nus shing thos min bskyong ba'i dbang med nyal ba ma yin par/ /mi ni mngal du zla bcu nye ba'i bar du sdug bsngal nyams myong 'gyur/ /dka' ba dag gis byung nas nyi ma'i zer rnos mod la sreg
<p>190b.7</p>pa dang / tshad pa'i rlung gis bud shing sbrang bu mchu sbrang dag gis gnod pa dang / /nye du dgra bo dag gis lte ba bcad pas na tsha skyed byed dang / /mngal na gnas kyang bla yi snang ba dag tu gnas pa 'di mi rung / /lus kyi bya ba lag pa dag dang rkang pa bskyod pa tsam du zad/ /smra ba'i yul gyur
<p>191a</p>
<p>191a.1</p>thams cad la yang khyad par med par du bar byed/ /nyal ba'i tshe na gan rkyal gnas pas nyin dang mtshan mo 'da' bar byed/ /sa stengs dag na khu 'jo ba ltar sdug bsngal nyam thag ngas ma mthong / /'dug pa dag las ldang bar mi nus nyal dang 'greng dang 'gro bar bskyod mi nus/ /
<p>191a.2</p>'dug ste gnas dang lus mi brtan pas gom gcig 'gro bar nus ma yin/ /tshig gis rang don bstan par mi nus byed 'khrul lus dang ngag la ni/ /dbang byar med par srog 'dzin byed pas kyi hud na tshod 'das sdug bsngal/ /mngal na sdug bsngal mang po yun rings rjes myong gyur kyang mi
<p>191a.3</p>mthong la/ /'chi ba'i dus kyi gnas skabs skye bo 'dris pa'i mig gi yul ma yin/ /dregs ldan dga' bas bcom pa tshogs sar skyes pa bud med brgya phrag gis/ /mig ni 'ben du gyur pa mda' char 'bab pas nyam thag lta bu yin/ /skom pas kha skams tshe na bsil zhing dri zhim chu ni 'thung ba
<p>191a.4</p>dang / /bkres pas nyam thag pa na 'bras chan sha dang bcas pa za ba dang / /'dod chags me 'bar gyis gdungs tshe na chung ma dam du 'khyud nas byed pa yi/ /nad sel byed pa bde ba yin zhes skye bo phyin ci log par 'gyur/ /skyes bu zas nyung dag gis ring gyur zas mang dag la mngon dga' bas/ /dbugs
<p>191a.5</p>mi thon cing sdug bsngal gyur la mi mthun zas kyis 'chi bar byed/ /zas mi 'ju bas nad skyed 'gyur zhing zhu bas bkres pa nyid du 'gyur/ /kye ma zas zos gyur na sdug bsngal mi skyed skabs de yod ma yin/ /shing yag dag ni rab tu 'bar ba'i skabs su me las tha dad min/ /de ni 'jig rten dag gis kyi
<p>191a.6</p>hud me zhes zer zhing yongs su sdong / /de bzhin lus la sdug bsngal shin tu chen po nyams myong gnas skabs su/ /'di ni sdug bsngal lus 'di myong zhes khyad par med la 'jug mi byed/ /mi gtsang snom zhing srin bu'i tshogs ni brgya yis yongs su bskor gyur la/ /slad sa'i drod kyi dugs kyis mtshungs pa
<p>191a.7</p>med pa'i sdug bsngal nyams myong zhing / /snang ba med pa'i btson ra'i khyim nang lta bu'i ma yi lto na gnas/ /de bskyed pa na de yang de ltar min nam ci phyir khyod rig byed/ /ji ltar khyi dag rus skam sra la ro med pa la brkam par 'cha'/ /rang gi kha chu khrag gis gos la rnyi zhing zhim pa yin snyam sems/ /de
<p>191b</p>
<p>191b.1</p>bzhin lus zhes bya ba shin tu 'jigs su rung ba'i tshogs de la/ /rmongs rnams rang gi rtog pas yon tan brgya yis sgro btags dga' bar byed/ /sha rgyas mtho zhing zlum la nu ma'i blo yis kun nas 'khyud pa dang / /kha ni kha chus gang ba chang bcas snod ltar 'thung bar byed pa dang / reg pa'i sred pas
<p>191b.2</p>mi gtsang rlan pa'i lam la chags pas na/ /'gro ba rmongs pa chen pos ldongs pa dag la yid du mi 'ong ci zhig yod/ /'khru bas dri mas sbags dang dri zhim skud pas mi ro'i dri 'dra dang / /so rtsi 'cha' la brtson par byed pas kha ni dri mi zhim pa nyid/ /gos kyis kun nas dkris pas shin tu mi sdug yin
<p>191b.3</p>par 'di byed de/ /lus 'di 'jigs su rung bas bdag ni gzhon nu ma la smra zhing rton/ /yid brtan rung las nyan par mi byed bdag nyid kyis kyang rtog med pas/ /khyed la rna ba dang ni snying med pa zhes bya bar shin tu rigs/ /rlon byed 'jigs su rung zhing mi sdug lus kyi dri ni ma tshor ba/ /khyed la 'gro ba
<p>191b.4</p>sna med yin zhes kyang ni ci yi phyir mi smra/ /shin tu gtsang ba'i dar dang dri zhim me tog sbrang rtsi gur kum la/ /de dang de ni gang du reg na skad cig gis ni mi gtsang 'gyur/ /rma yi sgo dgu dag nas mi gtsang dri nga'i ljan ljin 'dzag 'gyur gang / /de la khyed ni skal bzang yin zhes 'dir ni rlom sems ji ltar byed/ /
<p>191b.5</p>phung po lnga po 'di la yul dang yul can nyid du brtags nas ni/ /bdag dang bdag gir med pa dag la nga dang nga yi nges byas pa/ /'jig rten rmongs pa 'di ni 'jig rten skom gyis gdungs pa mya ngam du/ /smig rgyu'i chu yi chu bur las byung snod du 'thung snyam sems dang mtshungs/ /bdag ni rtag pa yin zhing bde
<p>191b.6</p>dang sdug bsngal nyams su myong 'gyur la/ /lus kyi yul ni gcig pu dag la bdag gi zhes blo bskyed du zad/ /bu dang chung ma phyugs rnams zhes bya 'di dag las gzhan gyis bskyed pa/ /de la ji ltar bdag gi zhes rtsi 'dir ni gti mug stobs can yin/ /de ni rgyu las byung zhing gnas pa'ang rang gi rkyen gyi
<p>191b.7</p>dbang las byung / /dus kyis rgas shing tshe dang bsod nams zad la sogs pas 'chi bar 'gyur/ /skye la dbang byar ma yin rgas la ma yin shi la dbang med na/ /bdag gi chung ma zhes smra ngo tsha bar ni ji ltar de ma gyur/ /gang zhig rtag tu rang dbang gyur dang gang zhig bde ba nyid gyur pa/ /gang zhig
<p>192a</p>
<p>192a.1</p>skad cig tsam yang 'dor mi 'gyur ba de ni bdag gir bshad/ /lus 'di dbang byar med cing sdug bsngal dag kyang skyo bar 'dor gyur na/ /'di la rim pa gang zhig mthong na 'di la gang zhig mngon zhen 'gyur/ /mi rtag pa la rtag snyam sems la sdug bsngal ba la bder mngon dga'/ /mi gtsang lus
<p>192a.2</p>la gtsang ba nyid du shas cher zhen par byed pa dang / /bdag med pa la bdag ces 'dzin pa'i rdul rnams rnam par bsal nas ni/ /skye med 'gag med 'chi ba med cing rtag pa'i gnas ni 'bad pas mngon du gyis/ /phyin ci log bzhi 'gag par byed pa'i gtam/ /'di byas pa las bdag gis dge bsags pa/ /
<p>192a.3</p>gang yod des ni 'gro gsum ma lus pa/ /phyin ci log bzhi las ni yid grol shog /phyin ci log bzhi spang ba'i gtam slob dpon ma ti tsi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po bud+d+ha b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ /
<p>192a.4\] ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ ka lI yu ka pa ri ka thA/ bod skad du/ rtsod pa'i dus kyi gtam/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /tshul khrims las nyams thos pa'i nor bral 'dod pas 'di nyid cung zad mchod par byed/ /nyes med tshul khrims ldan la yon tan ro la rgyab
<p>192a.5</p>phyogs zhe sdang cung zad nyes pa rgod/ /rab byung rnams la khyim pas las bsgo de nas rab byung des kyang khyim pa mgu bar byed/ /ci spyad 'gro ba 'dir ni 'gro ba'i khyim du ma lus dus kyi snyigs ma zhugs pa yin/ /da ltar legs par spyod pa'i skye bo ngo tsha sdig pa can bsngags dga' bar 'gyur/ /slob dpon nor
<p>192a.6</p>rnams mchog tu sems pas 'joms phyir slob ma rnams ni zhum par gnas/ /'di na byis pa'i nye du'i 'khrul 'khor gyis bcings pa ni sun 'byin byed pa bzhin/ /da ltar rtsod pa'i dus na 'jig rten rnams la g.yo sgyu'i mtshon drag stobs dang ldan/ /bcud rnams sas 'thung dngos rnams stobs chung lha rnams char ni
<p>192a.7</p>'bebs mi byed/ /rlung rnams rab tu drag ldang lo tog rnams ni mi smin skye mi 'gyur/ /skyes la ser 'babs rnams rtsod pa'i dus kyis dbang sgyur 'bras bu med/ /dngos rnams mthu med dgos pa sgrub rnams nyams pa thob la brtag /'gro la nad 'phel sa ni de dag skye bo rnams kyis stongs/ /ljon pa'i nags tshal
<p>192b</p>
<p>192b.1</p>skom pas yal ga'i lag pa gyen du 'gred byed de/ /rtsod pa'i dus kyis bcom byas bzang po'i dus nub ri bo cho nges 'debs/ /yul bzang chags pa rnam spangs sa rnams su ni dus bzang yongs su zad/ /yon tan mkhas la mi bkur nor ldan rnams la mchod bya min par mchod/ /skye rmongs mchod byed gshin rjes 'jig rten sdu
<p>192b.2</p>bsngal des khrid gang gis bzlog /tshul khrims 'chal pa stobs ldan tshul khrims ldan pa bsdigs shing tshar gcod byed/ /sdig pa dga' ba'i stobs ldan g.yon can rnams kyis dam chos bsnub par 'gyur/ /gang zhig sdom pa la gnas brtan pa'i mchog la 'jug par byed pa nyung / /the tshom yod min drang srong bstan pa ring po
<p>192b.3</p>mi thogs nub par 'gyur/ /g.yul 'gyed rtsod pa du mas gos ltar sa g.yogs lo tog skyes la 'dod mi 'byung / /rlung rnams mi bzad ldang zhing de bzhin skye bo dam pa yang dag mchod mi byed/ /rgyal po dgra dang rkun ma'i 'jigs pas mi dag bag phebs nor rnams longs mi spyod/ /da ltar skye bo sdug bsngal bcas 'tsho 'gro ba rnams
<p>192b.4</p>la 'jigs pa 'byung / /gang zhig dus su char med gang du lam zhugs ser ba mi mthun du ma 'bab/ /gang zhig ba rnams 'o ma mi 'byung dus rnams 'khrugs shing sa las 'bru mi skye/ /sman rnams gang yin nus med de bzhin khyad par rnams ni rab tu nyams/ /yid ni nges bcom chos min rtsod pas dngos po 'di rnams nyes dang
<p>192b.5</p>bcas/ /rtsod pa'i dus 'dir chos spangs mi bzad pa la yang dag zhugs pas na/ /gang du dbang pos char phab ljon shing yal ga dag las me tog 'bras bu cung zad snang / /sa gzhi rlan pa dang bcas sa rnams gang yin pa las lo tog smin gyur pa/ /de kun tshul khrims brtul zhugs yang dag sdom ldan chos dang ldan pa'i
<p>192b.6</p>mthu/ /dus rnams 'khrul zhing sa la bcud rnams nub 'gyur nyi zla log par rgyu/ /chung ma khyo la gcugs pas 'brel pa'i sems med dman pa rnams ni mthon por 'gyur/ /rgyal po chos spangs nor rnams mchog tu don gnyer bu rnams pha la sdang / /kyi hud sdug bsngal rtsod pa'i dus ni nyer gnas bsod nams gnyer ba nags su
<p>192b.7</p>song / /chos dang rab byung dka' thub rnams 'bros bde ba rnams ni ring du song bar gyur/ /sa rnams 'bras bu nyung zhing rgyal po 'khrug byed mtshon gyis rgyal byed rnam par gnon/ /'jig rten bud med la dad bud med kyang g.yem bram ze rnams ni 'dod chen bcas/ /legs pa rnams nub skye ngan stobs ldan du ma rtsod pa'i dus
<p>193a</p>
<p>193a.1</p>su bzang po yi/ /dus song bde ba rnams 'das dus der sbyor ba'i skyes bu rnams kyang 'das/ /'dir yang dus mtha' de rnams mun bcas phug bzhin shes ma yin/ /legs spyad brgya phrag dri yis bsgos pa yi/ /skal ldan nub cing dus ni 'das par 'gyur/ /bad gzhon rtsa ba'i skud pa bzhin/ / 
<p>193a.2</p>dkar po'i chos rnams phra bar 'gyur/ /blo ldan skyes bu gtam mkhas dri mas rgod/ /'gro 'di dga' med dga' ston zin pa bzhin/ /bdag nyid chen po 'di ni yang dag 'gags/ /gang na yon tan rnams kyi stobs phra la/ /yon tan la bdud 'bab pas gcod byed cing / /skye bo smra ba la brten 'tsho bar
<p>193a.3</p>byed/ /rtsod pa'i dus kyi gtam slob dpon ma ti tsi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po a dzi ta shrI b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur ba'o//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ bi be ka ka thA/ bod skad du/ dben pa'i gtam/ byang chub
<p>193a.4</p>sems dpa' 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dka' thub rnyed pa'i bde ba 'dod rnams kyis/ /'chol bar spyod pa rnams ni mthong gyur pa/ /rab tu dben pa yang dag bsten pa yi/ /dge slong 'di skad tshig tu brjod pas smra/ /phongs pa spang phyir de bzhin gshegs pa yis/ /rab bsngags zhi ba'i
<p>193a.5</p>dbang bskur nyer blangs nas/ /dka' thub khyim dang 'dris pas rab chags pa'i/ /phongs nyid rgal dka' bying ba ji lta bur/ /'phags pa 'gran med shing drung gnas nas ni/ /'gro ba skye dang 'gag pa mthong bas na/ /zhi ba'i bde ba yongs smin tshe dge ba/ /mi las shin tu 'phags pa thob par 'gyur/ /sems kyi rnam par 'ching
<p>193a.6</p>ba gnyen po yi/ /stobs kyis bsal bas skye bral nags dag tu/ /rnal 'byor nyer zhi'i bdud rtsis tshim gyur pas/ /bde bar gnyid log pa dang sad par 'gyur/ /mtshan mo zla ba'i snang dang rab gsal ba'i/ /skar ma'i me tog bkram par nyer mchod nas/ /dgon par brten pa'i yid ni nges zhi ba'i/ /lhag par dga' ba dag ni skye bar 'gyur/ 
<p>193a.7</p>/gang du dge slong dben pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis/ /kha na ma tho med pa zhi 'gyur bde/ /gang du yo byad yang dag bsten chags pas/ /sems ni sna tshogs phongs pas gdungs par 'gyur/ /ji ltar chu shing smyug ma 'od ma dag /'bras bu 'byin nas rang nyid 'jig pa ston/ /de bzhin dka' thub khyim las rnam grol nas/ /bdag nyid zil gyis gnon la
<p>193b</p>
<p>193b.1</p>chags mthong 'gyur/ /sa yi rdul gyis gos pa'i ri dgas dag /rtswa dang 'dab nas tsam zhig sgrub byed ltar/ /sems ni dben par gzhol ba 'dod 'gyur gyi/ /gling bzhi'i phun tshogs rgya chen dag la'ang min/ /shing drung 'bab chu bstan pa'i dka' thub dag /yongs su 'dzin pa dag ni rnam spangs nas/ /rang sems tsam dang rab tu 'brel pa
<p>193b.2</p>yi/ /bde 'byung gang de rgyal po rnams la med/ /ljon shing sngon po'i rtse mo rlung dag gis/ /rnam g.yo phra la snyoms pa'i char 'bab pa'i/ /mi g.yo rnam brtags ri yi sul gnas ni/ /dge slong mtshan mo dge ba skyed par byed/ /rnyog can 'dod la 'dris pas 'phos pa yi/ /bdag bsnyen pa yi chags spangs ltos med cing / /skye bral nags gang
<p>193b.3</p>yin par dga' bya yi/ /dge slong gyur nas don med 'gyur mi bya/ /dge slong rtags ni bdag nyid gnod med par/ /nyer blangs gang zhig sgrub par mi byed cing / /dman la yongs su 'dzin pa'i 'dam bying ba/ /de ni 'tsho ba'i 'jig rten slu byed yin/ /chu dang rdo khu rtsa ba med pa yi/ /sa dbang 'dzegs nas mi bzad yang dag tu/ /rtog dang ldan
<p>193b.4</p>pas shi ba bzod bya yi/ /bslab pa yongs su nyams pas 'jug mi bya/ /rgya mtsho rnam par 'khrugs pa'i rlabs tshogs su/ /rin chen khur gyis gru dag nub pa bzhin/ /khyim dang 'dris pa'i rnyed chags khur dag gis/ /gang dag mchog brten rgya chen snub par byed/ /nags na brten pa'i zhi ba'i ri dgas ni/ /gzhon nu ma yi 'gro bas
<p>193b.5</p>dkrugs mtshon pa/ /gnyen po ji bzhin bdag nyid zhi 'dod rnams/ /sdom can rab tu dben nyid yang dag rtsom/ /yul gyi ro yi dug gis nyer gdung blo can dag /chags pa nyung ngu dag gis gdung gyur na/ /de dag yongs su spong la rtsod med pa'i/ /dka' thub kyi hud e ma'o rab nyams 'gyur/ /sdom can rkang pas 'gro zhing 'jog pa
<p>193b.6</p>ltar/ /de ltar 'dris pa 'dod pa 'phel 'gyur te/ /rang rlabs chab ngogs mngon brdabs 'jigs rung bas/ /sprin chen char gyis ya mu na bzhin no/ /dka' thub ji ltar dman pa dag la yang / /'dod lha'i dbang gis rjes su zhugs gyur pa/ /de ltar rang lag gis drang phun sum tshogs/ /rgyal chen khyim la khyim pa chags pa med/ /rang gi
<p>193b.7</p>khyim dang gdong dag mchi 'dzag pas/ /brlan pa'i gnyen dag spangs par gyur nas ni/ /dman pa gzhan gyi khyim la chags pa yi/ /rab byung 'di la shin tu ngo tsha med/ /thar pa 'dod gang rang khyim spangs nas ni/ /mi shes gzhan gyi khyim dag 'dod byed pa/ /rgya mtsho rnam par 'khrugs pa'i rlabs tshogs las/ /bdag nyid rgal nas glang rjes
<p>194a</p>
<p>194a.1</p>bying dang mtshungs/ /sdig pa spong byed de bzhin gshegs pa yis/ /gnang ba'i sgrub pa dag gis 'di brtags gang / /dman pa'i nor la 'dod pa'i sred pa yis/ /gzhan khyim la chags dri ma can du 'gyur/ /chu bo ni lu tsha yi me tog lhung ba'i dum bus mtha' mar bris/ /bye ma dkar po'i ngogs dang ngang pa ka dam pa
<p>194a.2</p>dag gnas/ /nags kyi glang chen khyu dag rtse bas tha dad 'thor rlabs can/ /dgon gnas brtul zhugs can la dga' ba rab tu skyed par byed/ /srid pa'i longs spyod don du gnyer ba'i yi dgas rnams bsal nas/ /ma brtsams yid 'ong bde ba bsten pa rnams kyi gnas skabs ni/ /pad+ma kha bye bzhin du dka' thub rang gi grags pa yis/ /
<p>194a.3</p>'jig rten yongs su dga' ba rab skyed kun du dpe las 'das/ /dka' thub ri dang nye ba'i shing rtsa rab yangs dang 'brel bar/ /gnas pa'i tshom bu mi snyoms lhod pa'i srubs bar la chags pa'i/ /ba mo'i dum bus gos pa tho rangs nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis/ /lag pa dag gis nyul ba bzhin du rnam par skems par byed/ /khang stong shing drung
<p>194a.4</p>rlung ni rgyu gyur kha ba'i tshogs chen 'bab/ /mdangs zad rab rtsub lo ma dag gis gdu bu bzhin bskor ba'i/ /'dod pa kun spangs shes rab rno ba'i brtul zhugs can dag la/ /mtshan mo rnam par skyo ba dag ni skyed par zad mi byed/ /shing gi lo ma'i tha ma la chags ba mo'i chu dag gi /dum bu nyi ma 'char tshe mdog nor bu dang 'dra/ /
<p>194a.5</p>thigs pa dag ni shing drung gnas pa'i dge slong la/ /'gro ba'i skye dang 'jig pa ji bzhin rab tu ston par byed/ /rab zhi'i bde ro shes pas 'khor los sgyur ba'i dpal 'byor kyang / /yongs su dpyad pas rnyings pa'i me tog phreng bzhin rnam spangs nas/ /lang tsho rang bzhin gyis g.yo ngang tshul can dag yol byas te/ /dgon par ri
<p>194a.6</p>dgas 'drar 'chi zhi ba'i sems ni brtan par bya/ /'dod pa la 'jen phyin ci log pa'i sems la ku mu ta'i/ /dum bu ltar dkar mi thod so dang 'brel pas nyer dgod dang / /rlung gis bud pa'i ro bsregs me yis nye 'khor shing bsregs pa'i/ /dur khrod dka' thub gcig pu la ni mtshan mo dga' ba skyed par byed/ /ljon
<p>194a.7</p>shing tshogs dang rgya ches ri yi rtsa ba sngor gyur cing / /rdo bas khyab dang bsil la rab dang ba yi chu 'dzag 'bab/ /rma bya rab dga' sgra yis khyab pa'i ri sul nang du ni/ /khyim du 'chi ba'i skyo ba'i sems ni rab tu dga' bar byed/ /'gro ba'i don ma byas pa'i 'chi bar 'gyur ba khyim dag la/ /dga' ba dag la dben pa mchog la slob
<p>194b</p>
<p>194b.1</p>byed sems can mchog /rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems ni rnyed gyur pha rol tshogs 'thob pa/ /srid pa'i dug gi sdong po'i rtsa ba brtan po 'byin par byed/ /nags tshig pa yi bya dang 'dra bar sdug bsngal brgya yi gzhir gyur pa'i/ /khyim gang yin pa yongs su spangs nas nags su 'gro byed pa/ /des ni srid pa'i gnyid rab bsal
<p>194b.2</p>ba 'gro ba kun gyi mgon/ /sangs rgyas rab tu mnyes par byed pa yin zhes de skad grags/ /margad sngon po dang 'dra ne'u gseng tshogs dag ni/ /shing rtsa nye bar bkod dang yal ga me tog gis bskor ba'i/ /zhi ba'i nags mtha' kye ma'o dge slong mchog gis spong byed pa/ /gsad phyir rngon pa'i glu yis drangs par gyur pa'i ri dgas
<p>194b.3</p>mtshungs/ /'phags pa'i bzhed pa bde bar gshegs pa'i lam gyi rjes 'brangs nas/ /nags dang 'dra bar khyim gyi rang gi don dag sgrub byed kyang / /rnam par 'tshe ba rang bzhin gyis med nags ni dben pa yis/ /sems kyi 'ching ba dag ni 'bad pa med par gcod par byed/ /'dod chags gang dag de la dgos par 'gyur bas kun 'phel zhing / 
<p>194b.4</p>/legs spyad thub pa'i bstan pa dag kyang nyams byas nas/ /me dpung rab tu 'bar ba rgal dka'i khongs ni mthar thug pa'i/ /ngan song dag tu dge slong bde chung la chags 'gro bar 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyes pa ma lus gdung ba zad byed sangs rgyas pa'i/ /legs par bshad pa khas blangs nas ni ngan 'gror ngan 'byin pa/ /ut+pal sngon po'i snying
<p>194b.5</p>po'i dri mchog dag dang chu dum bu/ /sar la bsil ldan rlung gis de dag ji ltar tshim par 'gyur/ /sa ra sa yi sgra ni rang bzhin snyan pa'i glu dbyangs dag /ldog pa med par sgrogs par gyur pas mchog rnams khyab gyur pas/ /brtul zhugs can gyis 'gro dang gnas pa dag las dub skyes dang / /lus lhod gyur pa'i
<p>194b.6</p>mtshan gyi gung thun gnyid dag sad par byed/ /rang gi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyis spras yongs su gnas pa yis/ /zla ba'i 'od zer tshogs kyi dpal 'joms shin tu zil gnon pas/ /dge ba'i rtsa ba nyer bsags skal ldan 'jig rten la gzigs shing / /rang byung 'phags pa mchog ni dgon pa de yang sten par
<p>194b.7</p>mdzad/ /ci ste gang zhig nang gi dgra las nges rgyal bya ba byas pa yi/ /ston pa 'jig rten mtha' gzigs de yang nags dag sten mdzad na/ /yang dag mi rtogs skye bo mi gtsang 'dam du bying gyur pa'i/ /sdom can zhi 'dod bde gshegs rjes su ci phyir 'jug mi byed/ /bdag tu log par 'dzin par gyur pas nyin dang mtshan/ /srin bus ji
<p>195a</p>
<p>195a.1</p>bzhin rnam rtog sdig can dag gis zos pas na/ /nyon mongs rnag gis nyer gos zhi ba'i chu yi bum pa yis/ /bkrus pa bzhin du sems ni skye ba med nags bsten par gyis/ /'bras bu'i lcid kyis yal ga gug pa'i tha ma lo ma yis/ /gsal gyur lcug ma me tog kha bye'i dga' byed rgyu ldan pa'i/ /nags kyi shing ni
<p>195a.2</p>dge slong phongs bral bsten pa la/ /mdza' bo bzhin du shin tu dbugs ni 'byin par byed/ /zla ba shar ba kha ba 'bab pa bsgrigs pas 'gog 'gyur ba'i/ /dgun gyi mtshan mo dag ni rab zhi bde ba 'dod rnams kyi/ /rnal 'byor rtswa yi stan la dga' ba dag la tho rangs dag /nags kyi shing na yib pa'i bya rnams 'dra bar byed/ /shing dang
<p>195a.3</p>nye ba'i ri yi rked du mi g.yo skyil krung bcas/ /me tog gis bskor rab dga'i rlung gis g.yo bar byed pa na/ /'gro gnyen srid gsum rnam rgyal dus na byang chub snying po yi/ /gdan la bzhugs bzhin sdom can mtshan mo rjes su sgrub par byed/ /dman pa'i 'gro ba'i sems kyis reg byas dregs pa'i chags pa dag /'dod bya don du
<p>195a.4</p>gnyer ba rnams kyis khyad par spangs nas ni/ /'phags pas rjes chags brtan pa mi snang 'ching ba 'jigs pa yi/ /'dod pa lhag ma med par dga' bzhin nags su zhi bar bya/ /skye dang 'chi dang na ba'i sdug bsngal mthar ni ma byas par/ /srid pa'i rgya mtsho dag tu bying 'gyur bag med ma byed cig /mthar byed kun gyi srog kyang 'phrog par
<p>195a.5</p>byed pa gang 'di ni/ /rgyun mi chad par 'gro la sta re'i so dag 'dar bar byed/ /sa 'dzin pa yi chu bo'i tshogs dag 'bab pa lta bu ni/ /chos kun gnas pa'i rang bzhin rjes su shes nas ni/ /ro la sems ldan gzhan las dam pas legs par 'gro ba yis/ /srid la chags bral rab zhi dga' ba dag la brten par gyis/ /smra ba tsam ni
<p>195a.6</p>nus su zin kyang tshig la gnas pa'ang grub med de/ /skyes bu tshig dang snying por byed pa ston gyi chu bral sprin dang mtshungs/ /gang phyir de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa 'di la sgrub pa snying po nyid/ /de phyir de nyid la 'jug blo gros yin bzo'i tshig la mkhas/ /kun nas nyon mongs dgra 'di yi/ /bdag nyid bran du gyur pa ste/ /de
<p>195a.7</p>bas bdag sems zhi byed cing / /rang nyid yongs su smra bar byed/ /dben pa'i gtam slob dpon chen pos 'tsho byin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o// //
